   1 | # Changelog
   2 | 
   3 | All notable changes to this project will be documented in this file.
   4 | 
   5 | ## [0.2.0] - 2024-03-01
   6 | 
   7 | ### Added
   8 | - Structured logging with tracing and log file rotation
   9 | - CLI `--version` flag
  10 | - Proper error handling instead of panics on startup
  11 | - CI test and clippy checks before build
  12 | 
  13 | ### Fixed
  14 | - Replaced all `expect()`/`unwrap()` with proper error handling
  15 | - Standardized logging with tracing (replaced eprintln!/println!)
  16 | - Pinned litchi git dependency for reproducible builds
  17 | - NSIS uninstall hook now properly removes PATH entry
  18 | 
  19 | ### Changed
  20 | - Updated version from 0.1.0 to 0.2.0
  21 | - Added tracing-appender for log rotation
  22 | 
  23 | ## [0.1.0] - 2024-01-01
  24 | 
  25 | ### Added
  26 | - Initial release
  27 | - Full-text search with Tantivy
  28 | - File metadata database with redb
  29 | - Iced-based UI
  30 | - Multiple file format parsers (PDF, DOCX, EPUB, etc.)
  31 | - File system watcher for live indexing
```

### File: `CONTRIBUTING.md`

- Size: 938 bytes

```markdown
   1 | # Contributing to Flash Search
   2 | 
   3 | Thank you for your interest in contributing to Flash Search!
   4 | 
   5 | ## Development Setup
   6 | 
   7 | ```bash
   8 | # Install Rust
   9 | curl --proto '=https' --tlsv1.2 -sSf https://sh.rustup.rs | sh
  10 | 
  11 | # Clone and setup
  12 | git clone https://github.com/yourusername/flash-search.git
  13 | cd flash-search
  14 | 
  15 | # Run development server
  16 | cargo run
  17 | ```
  18 | 
  19 | ## Building
  20 | 
  21 | ```bash
  22 | # Debug build
  23 | cargo build
  24 | 
  25 | # Release build
  26 | cargo build --release
  27 | 
  28 | # Run tests
  29 | cargo test
  30 | ```
  31 | 
  32 | ## Code Style
  33 | 
  34 | - Use `cargo fmt` before committing
  35 | - Use `cargo clippy` to catch common mistakes
  36 | - Follow existing code conventions
  37 | 
  38 | ## Pull Request Process
  39 | 
  40 | 1. Fork the repository
  41 | 2. Create a feature branch
  42 | 3. Make your changes
  43 | 4. Run tests and formatting
  44 | 5. Submit a pull request
  45 | 
  46 | ## Reporting Issues
  47 | 
  48 | Please include:
  49 | - Steps to reproduce
  50 | - Expected vs actual behavior
  51 | - System information
  52 | 
  53 | ## License
  54 | 
  55 | By contributing, you agree that your contributions will be licensed under GPLv3.
```

```markdown
   1 | <h1 align="center">Flash Search</h1>
   2 | 
   3 | <p align="center">
   4 |   <img src="assets/logo.png" alt="Flash Search Logo" width="120">
   5 | </p>
   6 | 
   7 | <p align="center">
   8 |   <b>Ultrafast local full-text search with minimal resource footprint</b>
   9 | </p>
  10 | 
  11 | <p align="center">
  12 |   <a href="#features">Features</a> •
  13 |   <a href="#installation">Installation</a> •
  14 |   <a href="#usage">Usage</a> •
  15 |   <a href="#tech-stack">Tech Stack</a> •
  16 |   <a href="#performance">Performance</a> •
  17 |   <a href="#roadmap">Roadmap</a>
  18 | </p>
  19 | 
  20 | <p align="center">
  21 |   <img src="https://img.shields.io/badge/Rust-000000?style=flat&logo=rust&logoColor=white" alt="Rust">
  22 |   <img src="https://img.shields.io/badge/Iced-0.14-blue?style=flat&logo=rust&logoColor=white" alt="Iced">
  23 |   <img src="https://img.shields.io/badge/License-GPL--3.0-blue.svg" alt="License">
  24 | </p>
  25 | 
  26 | ---
  27 | 
  28 | <h2 align="center">🚀 Features</h2>
  29 | 
  30 | - **⚡ Blazing Fast**: Sub-50ms search results across millions of documents
  31 | - **📂 Filename Search**: Instant filename-only search mode for ultra-fast navigation
  32 | - **💾 Minimal Footprint**: <30MB RAM usage at idle (vs 200MB+ for Electron apps)
  33 | - **📄 Universal Format Support**: Native support for **75+ formats** (PDF, Office, Images, Archives, Ebooks, etc.)
  34 | - **🔍 Full-Text Search**: BM25 scoring, boolean queries, exact phrase matching
  35 | - **📸 Integrated OCR**: Search text within images and scanned PDFs via Kreuzberg
  36 | - **📊 Advanced Filters**: Filter by size (`size:>1MB`), extension (`ext:rs`), or path (`path:src`)
  37 | - **🔄 Live Indexing**: Automatic file watching and incremental updates
  38 | - **🎯 Smart Filtering**: .gitignore support, custom exclude patterns
  39 | - **🌙 Native UI**: Beautiful dark/light themes using Iced's high-performance renderer.
  40 | 
  41 | <h2 align="center">📥 Installation</h2>
  42 | 
  43 | <h3 align="center">Prerequisites</h3>
  44 | 
  45 | - **Windows**: Windows 10/11
  46 | - **macOS**: macOS 10.15+
  47 | - **Linux**: Vulkan-compatible drivers & development tools (pkg-config, libfontconfig1-dev)
  48 | 
  49 | <h3 align="center">Download</h3>
  50 | 
  51 | Download the latest release for your platform from the [Releases](https://github.com/SV-stark/FindAll/releases) page.
  52 | 
  53 | <h3 align="center">Build from Source</h3>
  54 | 
  55 | ```bash
  56 | # Clone the repository
  57 | git clone https://github.com/SV-stark/FindAll.git
  58 | cd FindAll
  59 | 
  60 | # Build the application
  61 | cargo build --release
  62 | 
  63 | # Run in development mode
  64 | cargo run
  65 | ```
  66 | 
  67 | <h2 align="center">🎮 Usage</h2>
  68 | 
  69 | <h3 align="center">First Launch</h3>
  70 | 
  71 | 1.  **Initial Setup**: Select folders to index on first launch
  72 | 2.  **Indexing**: The app will scan and index your files (this may take a few minutes for large directories)
  73 | 3.  **Search**: Press `Alt+Space` (or your custom hotkey) to open the search bar from anywhere
  74 | 
  75 | <h3 align="center">Search Syntax</h3>
  76 | 
  77 | | Query | Description |
  78 | |:---|:---|
  79 | | `rust tutorial` | Find documents containing both words |
  80 | | `"exact phrase"` | Find exact phrase matches |
  81 | | `rust OR python` | Boolean OR operator |
  82 | | `code -python` | Exclude documents with "python" |
  83 | | `title:api` | Search only in document titles |
  84 | | `ext:pdf` | Filter by file extension |
  85 | | `path:docs` | Filter by folder path |
  86 | | `size:>5MB` | Filter by file size (KB, MB, GB) |
  87 | 
  88 | <h3 align="center">Keyboard Shortcuts</h3>
  89 | 
  90 | | Shortcut | Action |
  91 | |:---|:---|
  92 | | `Alt+Space` | Toggle search window (Global Hotkey, configurable in Settings) |
  93 | | `Ctrl+Enter` | Open selected file |
  94 | | `Ctrl+C` | Copy file path |
  95 | | `Esc` | Close search window |
  96 | | `↑/↓` | Navigate results |
  97 | 
  98 | <h2 align="center">🏗️ Tech Stack</h2>
  99 | 
 100 | <h3 align="center">Core Architecture</h3>
 101 | 
 102 | | Component | Technology | Purpose |
 103 | |:---|:---|:---|
 104 | | **Language** | Rust | Zero-overhead, memory-safe core |
 105 | | **GUI** | Iced | High-performance, cross-platform UI framework (<30MB RAM) |
 106 | | **Search Engine** | Tantivy | Full-text indexing with BM25 scoring |
 107 | | **Document Intelligence** | [Kreuzberg](https://github.com/kreuzberg-dev/kreuzberg) | Universal text extraction (75+ formats) + OCR |
 108 | | **Metadata DB** | redb | Pure Rust key-value storage |
 109 | | **Concurrency** | Rayon + Tokio | Parallel processing + async I/O |
 110 | 
 111 | <h3 align="center">Supported File Formats</h3>
 112 | 
 113 | | Category | Supported Formats | OCR |
 114 | |:---|:---|:---:|
 115 | | **Digital Documents** | PDF (Native & Scanned), XPS, OXPS, PS, EPS | ✅ |
 116 | | **MS Office** | DOC, DOCX, XLS, XLSX, PPT, PPTX (incl. Macro/Template variations) | ❌ |
 117 | | **Images** | JPG, PNG, WEBP, BMP, GIF, TIFF, JP2, PNM, PBM, PGM, PPM | ✅ |
 118 | | **Text & Markup** | MD, TXT, RTF, HTML, HTM, XML, SVG, LaTeX (TEX), RST, ORG | ❌ |
 119 | | **E-books & Comics** | EPUB, FB2, MOBI, AZW3, CHM, CBZ, CBR | ❌ |
 120 | | **Archives** | ZIP, 7Z, TAR, TGZ, GZ, RAR | ❌ |
 121 | | **Data & Emails** | JSON, YAML, TOML, CSV, ODS, EML, MSG | ❌ |
 122 | 
 123 | <h2 align="center">📊 Performance</h2>
 124 | 
 125 | <div align="center">
 126 | 
 127 | Benchmarks on AMD Ryzen 7 5800X with NVMe SSD:
 128 | 
 129 | </div>
 130 | 
 131 | | Metric | Value |
 132 | |:---|:---|
 133 | | **Index 10,000 PDFs** | ~45 seconds |
 134 | | **Index 100,000 TXT files** | ~12 seconds |
 135 | | **Search latency (p50)** | 12ms |
 136 | | **Search latency (p99)** | 45ms |
 137 | | **Idle RAM usage** | ~25MB |
 138 | | **Peak RAM (indexing)** | ~180MB |
 139 |

 143 | 
 144 | | Feature | Flash Search | AnyTXT | Windows Search | Recoll |
 145 | |:---|:---|:---|:---|:---|
 146 | | Startup Time | Instant | ~2s | System | ~3s |

 148 | | PDF Search | ✅ (Bundled) | ✅ | ⚠️ | ✅ |

 155 | 
 156 | <h2 align="center">🗺️ Roadmap</h2>
 157 | 
 158 | ### Phase 1: Foundation (Completed ✅)
 159 | - [x] High-performance core with **Rust**
 160 | - [x] Efficient UI framework with **Iced**
 161 | - [x] Basic file parsers for PDF, DOCX, and TXT
 162 | - [x] Parallel filesystem scanning and incremental indexing
 163 | 
 164 | ### Phase 2: Polish & UX (Completed ✅)
 165 | - [x] Advanced search filters (date, size, extension)
 166 | - [x] Global "Spotlight-style" search bar (Alt+Space)
 167 | - [x] Real-time file indexing and system tray integration
 168 | - [x] Fast filename-only search mode for instant navigation
 169 | - [x] Optimized result preview and metadata retrieval
 170 | - [x] **Network Discovery**: Support for enterprise SMB/CIFS and NAS drives
 171 | 
 172 | ### Phase 3: Advanced Intelligence (In Progress 🚧)
 173 | - [x] **Universal Text Extraction**: 75+ formats supported via **Kreuzberg**
 174 | - [x] **Integrated OCR**: Native support for scanned PDFs and images
 175 | - [x] **Pinned Results**: Favorite important files for instant access
 176 | - [ ] **Semantic Search**: Vector embeddings for context-aware queries
 177 | - [ ] **Natural Language Queries**: "files from last week about taxes"
 178 | 
 179 | ### Phase 4: Expansion & Connectivity (Future 🔮)
 180 | - [ ] **Plugin System**: Community-built parsers and search extensions
 181 | - [ ] **Cloud Indexing**: Optional encrypted metadata sync across devices
 182 | - [ ] **Developer API**: Headless search service for other applications
 183 |

  35 | 
  36 | pub struct AppState {
  37 |     pub indexer: Arc<IndexManager>,
  38 |     pub metadata_db: Arc<MetadataDb>,
  39 |     pub settings_manager: Arc<SettingsManager>,
  40 |     pub settings_cache: Arc<RwLock<AppSettings>>,
  41 |     pub watcher: Mutex<WatcherManager>,
  42 |     pub filename_index: Option<Arc<FilenameIndex>>,
  43 |     pub progress_tx: mpsc::Sender<crate::scanner::ProgressEvent>,
  44 |     pub scanner: Arc<crate::scanner::Scanner>,
  45 | }
  46 | 
  47 | #[bon::bon]
  48 | impl AppState {
  49 |     #[builder]
  50 |     pub fn new(
  51 |         indexer: Arc<IndexManager>,
  52 |         metadata_db: Arc<MetadataDb>,
  53 |         settings_manager: SettingsManager,
  54 |         watcher: WatcherManager,
  55 |         filename_index: Option<Arc<FilenameIndex>>,
  56 |         progress_tx: mpsc::Sender<crate::scanner::ProgressEvent>,
  57 |         scanner: Arc<crate::scanner::Scanner>,
  58 |     ) -> Self {
  59 |         let cache = settings_manager.load().unwrap_or_default();
  60 |         let mut watcher = watcher;
  61 |         let _ = watcher.update_watch_list(cache.index_dirs.clone());
  62 |         Self {
  63 |             indexer,
  64 |             metadata_db,
  65 |             settings_manager: Arc::new(settings_manager),
  66 |             settings_cache: Arc::new(RwLock::new(cache)),
  67 |             watcher: Mutex::new(watcher),
  68 |             filename_index,
  69 |             progress_tx,
  70 |             scanner,
  71 |         }
  72 |     }
  73 | }
  74 | 
  75 | #[cfg(test)]
  76 | mod tests {
  77 |     #[test]
  78 |     fn test_export_csv() {
  79 |         // Basic test placeholder
  80 |     }
  81 | }

   1 | use crate::commands::AppState;
   2 | use crate::commands::{
   3 |     get_file_preview_highlighted_internal, search_filenames_internal, search_query_internal,
   4 | };
   5 | use crate::error::FlashError;
   6 | use crate::indexer::searcher::SearchResult;
   7 | use crate::models::FilenameSearchResult;
   8 | use crate::scanner::ProgressEvent;
   9 | use crate::settings::AppSettings;
  10 | use compact_str::CompactString;
  11 | use iced::{Element, Subscription, Task};
  12 | use std::collections::HashSet;
  13 | use std::path::PathBuf;
  14 | use std::sync::Arc;
  15 | use tokio::sync::mpsc;
  16 | 
  17 | pub mod icons;
  18 | pub mod search;
  19 | pub mod settings;
  20 | pub mod theme;
  21 | 
  22 | #[derive(Clone, Debug)]
  23 | pub struct FileItem {
  24 |     pub title: CompactString,
  25 |     pub path: String,
  26 |     pub score: f32,
  27 |     pub extension: Option<CompactString>,
  28 |     pub modified: Option<u64>,
  29 |     pub size: Option<u64>,
  30 |     pub snippets: Vec<String>,
  31 | }
  32 | 
  33 | impl From<SearchResult> for FileItem {
  34 |     fn from(r: SearchResult) -> Self {
  35 |         FileItem {
  36 |             title: r.title.unwrap_or_else(|| {
  37 |                 CompactString::from(
  38 |                     r.file_path
  39 |                         .split(['\\', '/'])
  40 |                         .next_back()
  41 |                         .unwrap_or("Unknown"),
  42 |                 )
  43 |             }),
  44 |             path: r.file_path,
  45 |             score: r.score,
  46 |             extension: r.extension,
  47 |             modified: r.modified,
  48 |             size: r.size,
  49 |             snippets: r.snippets,
  50 |         }
  51 |     }
  52 | }
  53 | 
  54 | impl From<FilenameSearchResult> for FileItem {
  55 |     fn from(r: FilenameSearchResult) -> Self {
  56 |         let ext = r
  57 |             .file_name
  58 |             .split('.')
  59 |             .next_back()
  60 |             .map(CompactString::from);
  61 |         FileItem {
  62 |             title: r.file_name,
  63 |             path: r.file_path,
  64 |             score: 1.0,
  65 |             extension: ext,
  66 |             modified: None,
  67 |             size: None,
  68 |             snippets: Vec::new(),
  69 |         }
  70 |     }
  71 | }
  72 | 
  73 | #[derive(Clone, Debug)]
  74 | pub enum Tab {
  75 |     Search,
  76 |     Settings,
  77 | }
  78 | 
  79 | pub fn format_size(bytes: u64) -> String {
  80 |     if bytes < 1024 {
  81 |         format!("{} B", bytes)
  82 |     } else if bytes < 1024 * 1024 {
  83 |         format!("{:.1} KB", bytes as f64 / 1024.0)
  84 |     } else if bytes < 1024 * 1024 * 1024 {
  85 |         format!("{:.1} MB", bytes as f64 / (1024.0 * 1024.0))
  86 |     } else {
  87 |         format!("{:.1} GB", bytes as f64 / (1024.0 * 1024.0 * 1024.0))
  88 |     }
  89 | }
  90 | 
  91 | pub fn format_date(timestamp: u64) -> String {
  92 |     use chrono::{DateTime, Local};
  93 |     let native = DateTime::from_timestamp(timestamp as i64, 0)
  94 |         .unwrap_or_else(|| DateTime::from_timestamp(0, 0).unwrap());
  95 |     let local: DateTime<Local> = DateTime::from(native);
  96 |     local.format("%Y/%m/%d").to_string()
  97 | }
  98 | 
  99 | #[derive(Clone, Debug, PartialEq)]
 100 | pub enum SearchMode {
 101 |     FullText,
 102 |     Filename,
 103 | }
 104 | 
 105 | #[derive(Clone, Debug)]
 106 | pub enum Message {
 107 |     SearchQueryChanged(String),
 108 |     SearchSubmitted,
 109 |     SearchResultsReceived(u64, Vec<FileItem>),
 110 |     SearchError(FlashError),
 111 |     ResultSelected(usize),
 112 |     OpenFile(String),
 113 |     CopyPath(String),
 114 |     TabChanged(Tab),
 115 |     RebuildIndex,
 116 |     IndexRebuilt,
 117 |     RebuildProgress(ProgressEvent),
 118 |     AddFolder,
 119 |     FolderPicked(Option<String>),
 120 |     RemoveFolder(usize),
 121 |     SaveSettings,
 122 |     ToggleTheme,
 123 |     ToggleSearchMode,
 124 |     ToggleCaseSensitive(bool),
 125 |     ToggleWholeWord(bool),
 126 |     FilterExtensionChanged(String),
 127 |     ToggleFilterExtension(String),
 128 |     ClearFilters,
 129 |     MinSizeChanged(String),
 130 |     MaxSizeChanged(String),
 131 |     SizeUnitChanged(String),
 132 |     FilterSizeChanged(String),
 133 |     PreviewRequested(usize),
 134 |     PreviewLoaded(Option<crate::models::PreviewResult>),
 135 |     ShowContextMenu(usize),
 136 |     CloseContextMenu,
 137 |     OpenFolder(String),
 138 |     MoveUp,
 139 |     MoveDown,
 140 |     DismissError,
 141 |     Quit,
 142 |     GlobalHotkeyChanged(String),
 143 |     StartPollingProgress,
 144 |     PollProgressResult(Option<ProgressEvent>),
 145 |     PollTray,
 146 |     ToggleMinimizeToTray(bool),
 147 |     ToggleAutoStart(bool),
 148 |     ToggleContextMenu(bool),
 149 |     PollHotkey,
 150 |     PollSearchDeadline,
 151 |     NotImplemented(String),
 152 |     MaxResultsChanged(String),
 153 |     ExcludePatternsChanged(String),
 154 |     CustomExtensionsChanged(String),
 155 |     NoOp,
 156 | }
 157 | 
 158 | pub struct App {
 159 |     state: Option<Arc<AppState>>,
 160 |     error: Option<String>,
 161 |     search_error: Option<String>,
 162 |     search_query: String,
 163 |     results: Vec<FileItem>,
 164 |     selected_index: Option<usize>,
 165 |     is_searching: bool,
 166 |     settings: AppSettings,
 167 |     active_tab: Tab,
 168 |     files_indexed: i32,
 169 |     index_size: String,
 170 |     is_dark: bool,
 171 |     search_mode: SearchMode,
 172 |     filter_extension: String,
 173 |     filter_extensions: HashSet<String>,
 174 |     min_size: String,
 175 |     max_size: String,
 176 |     size_unit: String,
 177 |     filter_size: String,
 178 |     preview_result: Option<crate::models::PreviewResult>,
 179 |     is_loading_preview: bool,
 180 |     rebuild_progress: Option<f32>,
 181 |     rebuild_status: Option<String>,
 182 |     progress_rx: Option<Arc<tokio::sync::Mutex<mpsc::Receiver<ProgressEvent>>>>,
 183 |     tray_icon: Option<tray_icon::TrayIcon>,
 184 |     hotkey_manager: Option<global_hotkey::GlobalHotKeyManager>,
 185 |     search_deadline: Option<std::time::Instant>,
 186 |     pub context_menu_index: Option<usize>,
 187 |     search_id: u64,
 188 | }
 189 | 
 190 | impl App {
 191 |     fn new(state: Result<Arc<AppState>, String>) -> Self {
 192 |         match state {
 193 |             Ok(state) => {
 194 |                 let settings = state.settings_manager.load().unwrap_or_default();
 195 |                 let stats = state.indexer.get_statistics().unwrap_or_default();
 196 |                 let index_size = format!("{:.1} MB", (stats.total_size_bytes as f64) / 1_048_576.0);
 197 |                 let is_dark = matches!(settings.theme, crate::settings::Theme::Dark);
 198 | 
 199 |                 let mut app = App {
 200 |                     state: Some(state),
 201 |                     error: None,
 202 |                     search_error: None,
 203 |                     search_query: String::new(),
 204 |                     results: Vec::new(),
 205 |                     selected_index: None,
 206 |                     is_searching: false,
 207 |                     settings: settings.clone(),
 208 |                     active_tab: Tab::Search,
 209 |                     files_indexed: stats.total_documents as i32,
 210 |                     index_size,
 211 |                     is_dark,
 212 |                     search_mode: SearchMode::FullText,
 213 |                     filter_extension: String::new(),
 214 |                     filter_extensions: HashSet::new(),
 215 |                     min_size: String::new(),
 216 |                     max_size: String::new(),
 217 |                     size_unit: "MB".to_string(),
 218 |                     filter_size: String::new(),
 219 |                     preview_result: None,
 220 |                     is_loading_preview: false,
 221 |                     rebuild_progress: None,
 222 |                     rebuild_status: None,
 223 |                     progress_rx: None,
 224 |                     tray_icon: crate::system::tray::create_tray_icon().ok(),
 225 |                     hotkey_manager: None,
 226 |                     search_deadline: None,
 227 |                     context_menu_index: None,
 228 |                     search_id: 0,
 229 |                 };
 230 | 
 231 |                 if let Ok(manager) = global_hotkey::GlobalHotKeyManager::new() {
 232 |                     if let Ok(hotkey) = settings
 233 |                         .global_hotkey
 234 |                         .parse::<global_hotkey::hotkey::HotKey>()
 235 |                     {
 236 |                         if manager.register(hotkey).is_err() {
 237 |                             app.error = Some(format!(
 238 |                                 "Hotkey conflict: '{}' is already registered by another application. Please choose an alternative in Settings.",
 239 |                                 settings.global_hotkey
 240 |                             ));
 241 |                         }
 242 |                     } else if !settings.global_hotkey.is_empty() {
 243 |                         app.error = Some(format!(
 244 |                             "Invalid hotkey format: '{}'",
 245 |                             settings.global_hotkey
 246 |                         ));
 247 |                     }
 248 |                     app.hotkey_manager = Some(manager);
 249 |                 }
 250 | 
 251 |                 app
 252 |             }
 253 |             Err(err_msg) => App {
 254 |                 state: None,
 255 |                 error: Some(err_msg),
 256 |                 search_error: None,
 257 |                 search_query: String::new(),
 258 |                 results: Vec::new(),
 259 |                 selected_index: None,
 260 |                 is_searching: false,
 261 |                 settings: AppSettings::default(),
 262 |                 active_tab: Tab::Search,
 263 |                 files_indexed: 0,
 264 |                 index_size: "0 MB".to_string(),
 265 |                 is_dark: true, // Default to dark theme
 266 |                 search_mode: SearchMode::FullText,
 267 |                 filter_extension: String::new(),
 268 |                 filter_extensions: HashSet::new(),
 269 |                 min_size: String::new(),
 270 |                 max_size: String::new(),
 271 |                 size_unit: "MB".to_string(),
 272 |                 filter_size: String::new(),
 273 |                 preview_result: None,
 274 |                 is_loading_preview: false,
 275 |                 rebuild_progress: None,
 276 |                 rebuild_status: None,
 277 |                 progress_rx: None,
 278 |                 tray_icon: crate::system::tray::create_tray_icon().ok(),
 279 |                 hotkey_manager: None,
 280 |                 search_deadline: None,
 281 |                 context_menu_index: None,
 282 |                 search_id: 0,
 283 |             },
 284 |         }
 285 |     }
 286 | 
 287 |     fn parse_size_filter(size_str: &str) -> (Option<u64>, Option<u64>) {
 288 |         let size_str = size_str.trim();
 289 |         if size_str.is_empty() {
 290 |             return (None, None);
 291 |         }
 292 | 
 293 |         let (op, num_str) = if let Some(stripped) = size_str.strip_prefix(">=") {
 294 |             (">=", stripped)
 295 |         } else if let Some(stripped) = size_str.strip_prefix("<=") {
 296 |             ("<=", stripped)
 297 |         } else if let Some(stripped) = size_str.strip_prefix(">") {
 298 |             (">", stripped)
 299 |         } else if let Some(stripped) = size_str.strip_prefix("<") {
 300 |             ("<", stripped)
 301 |         } else {
 302 |             (">=", size_str)
 303 |         };
 304 | 
 305 |         let num_str = num_str.trim();
 306 |         let multiplier: u64 = if num_str.ends_with("KB") {
 307 |             1024
 308 |         } else if num_str.ends_with("MB") {
 309 |             1024 * 1024
 310 |         } else if num_str.ends_with("GB") {
 311 |             1024 * 1024 * 1024
 312 |         } else {
 313 |             1
 314 |         };
 315 | 
 316 |         let num: u64 = match num_str
 317 |             .trim_end_matches(|c: char| c.is_alphabetic())
 318 |             .parse()
 319 |         {
 320 |             Ok(n) => n,
 321 |             Err(_) => {
 322 |                 // If we can't parse the number, we treat it as no filter.
 323 |                 return (None, None);
 324 |             }
 325 |         };
 326 |         let bytes = num * multiplier;
 327 | 
 328 |         match op {
 329 |             ">" => (Some(bytes + 1), None),
 330 |             "<" => (None, Some(bytes.saturating_sub(1))),
 331 |             ">=" => (Some(bytes), None),
 332 |             "<=" => (None, Some(bytes)),
 333 |             _ => (Some(bytes), None),
 334 |         }
 335 |     }
 336 | 
 337 |     fn perform_search(&mut self) -> Task<Message> {
 338 |         let state = match &self.state {
 339 |             Some(s) => s.clone(),
 340 |             None => return Task::none(),
 341 |         };
 342 | 
 343 |         let mut query = self.search_query.clone();
 344 | 
 345 |         // Wrap in quotes if whole_word is enabled and not already wrapped
 346 |         if self.settings.whole_word
 347 |             && !query.starts_with('"')
 348 |             && !query.ends_with('"')
 349 |             && !query.contains(':')
 350 |         {
 351 |             query = format!("\"{}\"", query);
 352 |         }
 353 | 
 354 |         let max_results = self.settings.max_results;
 355 |         let mode = self.search_mode.clone();
 356 | 
 357 |         // Combine manual extension filter and checkbox filters
 358 |         let mut extensions: HashSet<String> = self
 359 |             .filter_extension
 360 |             .split(',')
 361 |             .map(|s| s.trim().to_lowercase())
 362 |             .filter(|s| !s.is_empty())
 363 |             .collect();
 364 | 
 365 |         for ext in &self.filter_extensions {
 366 |             extensions.insert(ext.to_lowercase());
 367 |         }
 368 | 
 369 |         let extension = if extensions.is_empty() {
 370 |             None
 371 |         } else {
 372 |             Some(extensions.into_iter().collect())
 373 |         };
 374 | 
 375 |         // Calculate size filters
 376 |         let multiplier: u64 = match self.size_unit.as_str() {
 377 |             "KB" => 1024,
 378 |             "GB" => 1024 * 1024 * 1024,
 379 |             _ => 1024 * 1024, // Default to MB
 380 |         };
 381 | 
 382 |         let min_size = self
 383 |             .min_size
 384 |             .trim()
 385 |             .parse::<u64>()
 386 |             .ok()
 387 |             .map(|n| n * multiplier);
 388 |         let max_size = self
 389 |             .max_size
 390 |             .trim()
 391 |             .parse::<u64>()
 392 |             .ok()
 393 |             .map(|n| n * multiplier);
 394 | 
 395 |         // Fallback to the old filter_size string if min/max are empty
 396 |         let (min_size, max_size) = if min_size.is_none() && max_size.is_none() {
 397 |             Self::parse_size_filter(&self.filter_size)
 398 |         } else {
 399 |             (min_size, max_size)
 400 |         };
 401 | 
 402 |         self.is_searching = true;
 403 |         self.results.clear();
 404 |         self.preview_result = None;
 405 |         self.search_id += 1;
 406 |         let current_search_id = self.search_id;
 407 |         let case_sensitive = self.settings.case_sensitive;
 408 |         let original_query = self.search_query.clone();
 409 | 
 410 |         Task::future(async move {
 411 |             let result = match mode {
 412 |                 SearchMode::Filename => {
 413 |                     match search_filenames_internal(query.clone(), max_results, &state).await {
 414 |                         Ok(results) => {
 415 |                             let mut items: Vec<FileItem> =
 416 |                                 results.into_iter().map(FileItem::from).collect();
 417 |                             if case_sensitive {
 418 |                                 items.retain(|item| {
 419 |                                     item.title.contains(&original_query)
 420 |                                         || item.path.contains(&original_query)
 421 |                                 });
 422 |                             }
 423 |                             Message::SearchResultsReceived(current_search_id, items)
 424 |                         }
 425 |                         Err(e) => Message::SearchError(FlashError::search(&query, e)),
 426 |                     }
 427 |                 }
 428 |                 SearchMode::FullText => {
 429 |                     match search_query_internal(
 430 |                         query.clone(),
 431 |                         max_results,
 432 |                         &state,
 433 |                         min_size,
 434 |                         max_size,
 435 |                         extension,
 436 |                     )
 437 |                     .await
 438 |                     {
 439 |                         Ok(results) => {
 440 |                             let mut items: Vec<FileItem> =
 441 |                                 results.into_iter().map(FileItem::from).collect();
 442 |                             if case_sensitive {
 443 |                                 items.retain(|item| {
 444 |                                     item.title.contains(&original_query)
 445 |                                         || item.path.contains(&original_query)
 446 |                                         || item.snippets.iter().any(|s| s.contains(&original_query))
 447 |                                 });
 448 |                             }
 449 |                             Message::SearchResultsReceived(current_search_id, items)
 450 |                         }
 451 |                         Err(e) => Message::SearchError(FlashError::search(&query, e)),
 452 |                     }
 453 |                 }
 454 |             };
 455 |             result
 456 |         })
 457 |     }
 458 | 
 459 |     fn load_preview(&mut self) -> Task<Message> {
 460 |         let idx = match self.selected_index {
 461 |             Some(i) => i,
 462 |             None => return Task::none(),
 463 |         };
 464 | 
 465 |         let item = match self.results.get(idx) {
 466 |             Some(i) => i.clone(),
 467 |             None => return Task::none(),
 468 |         };
 469 | 
 470 |         let path = item.path.clone();
 471 |         let query = self.search_query.clone();
 472 |         self.is_loading_preview = true;
 473 | 
 474 |         let state = match &self.state {
 475 |             Some(s) => s.clone(),
 476 |             None => return Task::none(),
 477 |         };
 478 | 
 479 |         Task::future(async move {
 480 |             let preview = get_file_preview_highlighted_internal(path, query, &state)
 481 |                 .await
 482 |                 .ok();
 483 |             Message::PreviewLoaded(preview)
 484 |         })
 485 |     }
 486 | 
 487 |     fn save_settings(&self) {
 488 |         if let Some(state) = &self.state {
 489 |             let _ = state.settings_manager.save(&self.settings);
 490 |             let mut watcher = state.watcher.lock();
 491 |             let _ = watcher.update_watch_list(self.settings.index_dirs.clone());
 492 | 
 493 |         }
 494 |     }
 495 | }
 496 | 
 497 | pub fn update(app: &mut App, message: Message) -> Task<Message> {
 498 |     if app.error.is_some() {
 499 |         match message {
 500 |             Message::DismissError => {
 501 |                 app.error = None;
 502 |                 Task::none()
 503 |             }
 504 |             Message::Quit => {
 505 |                 // Set shutdown flag to initiate graceful shutdown
 506 |                 crate::SHUTDOWN_FLAG.store(true, std::sync::atomic::Ordering::SeqCst);
 507 |                 Task::none()
 508 |             }
 509 |             _ => Task::none(),
 510 |         }
 511 |     } else {
 512 |         match message {
 513 |             Message::SearchQueryChanged(q) => {
 514 |                 app.search_query = q;
 515 |                 if !app.search_query.is_empty() {
 516 |                     app.search_deadline =
 517 |                         Some(std::time::Instant::now() + std::time::Duration::from_millis(150));
 518 |                     Task::none()
 519 |                 } else {
 520 |                     app.search_deadline = None;
 521 |                     Task::none()
 522 |                 }
 523 |             }
 524 |             Message::SearchSubmitted => app.perform_search(),
 525 |             Message::SearchResultsReceived(id, results) => {
 526 |                 if id != app.search_id {
 527 |                     return Task::none();
 528 |                 }
 529 |                 app.results = results;
 530 |                 app.is_searching = false;
 531 |                 app.search_error = None;
 532 |                 if !app.results.is_empty() {
 533 |                     app.selected_index = Some(0);
 534 |                 }
 535 |                 app.load_preview()
 536 |             }
 537 |             Message::SearchError(err) => {
 538 |                 app.search_error = Some(err.to_string());
 539 |                 app.is_searching = false;
 540 |                 app.results.clear();
 541 |                 Task::none()
 542 |             }
 543 |             Message::ResultSelected(idx) => {
 544 |                 app.context_menu_index = None;
 545 |                 app.selected_index = Some(idx);
 546 |                 app.load_preview()
 547 |             }
 548 |             Message::OpenFile(path) => {
 549 |                 app.context_menu_index = None;
 550 |                 let p = PathBuf::from(&path);
 551 |                 if p.is_absolute() && p.exists() {
 552 |                     // Offload the file opening to a background thread to avoid blocking the UI
 553 |                     Task::perform(
 554 |                         async move {
 555 |                             let _ = opener::open(p);
 556 |                         },
 557 |                         |_| Message::NoOp,
 558 |                     )
 559 |                 } else {
 560 |                     tracing::warn!("Blocked attempt to open invalid or relative path: {}", path);
 561 |                     Task::none()
 562 |                 }
 563 |             }
 564 |             Message::CopyPath(path) => {
 565 |                 app.context_menu_index = None;
 566 |                 if let Ok(mut clipboard) = arboard::Clipboard::new() {
 567 |                     let _ = clipboard.set_text(&path);
 568 |                 }
 569 |                 Task::none()
 570 |             }
 571 |             Message::TabChanged(tab) => {
 572 |                 app.context_menu_index = None;
 573 |                 app.active_tab = tab;
 574 |                 Task::none()
 575 |             }
 576 |             Message::ShowContextMenu(idx) => {
 577 |                 app.context_menu_index = Some(idx);
 578 |                 app.selected_index = Some(idx);
 579 |                 app.load_preview()
 580 |             }
 581 |             Message::CloseContextMenu => {
 582 |                 app.context_menu_index = None;
 583 |                 Task::none()
 584 |             }
 585 |             Message::OpenFolder(path) => {
 586 |                 app.context_menu_index = None;
 587 |                 let p = PathBuf::from(&path);
 588 |                 if p.is_absolute() {
 589 |                     if let Some(parent) = p.parent() {
 590 |                         let parent_buf = parent.to_path_buf();
 591 |                         if parent_buf.exists() {
 592 |                             return Task::perform(
 593 |                                 async move {
 594 |                                     let _ = opener::open(parent_buf);
 595 |                                 },
 596 |                                 |_| Message::NoOp,
 597 |                             );
 598 |                         }
 599 |                     }
 600 |                 }
 601 |                 tracing::warn!("Blocked attempt to open folder for invalid path: {}", path);
 602 |                 Task::none()
 603 |             }
 604 |             Message::RebuildIndex => {
 605 |                 let state = match &app.state {
 606 |                     Some(s) => s.clone(),
 607 |                     None => return Task::none(),
 608 |                 };
 609 |                 let settings = app.settings.clone();
 610 |                 app.rebuild_progress = Some(0.0);
 611 |                 app.rebuild_status = Some("Starting rebuild...".to_string());
 612 |                 if let Some(tray) = &app.tray_icon {
 613 |                     let _ = tray.set_tooltip(Some("Flash Search - Rebuilding Index..."));
 614 |                 }
 615 |                 app.files_indexed = 0;
 616 |                 let rx = app.progress_rx.clone();
 617 |                 Task::batch(vec![
 618 |                     Task::future(async move {
 619 |                         if let Err(e) = state.indexer.clear() {
 620 |                             tracing::error!("Failed to clear indexer: {}", e);
 621 |                             return Message::SearchError(FlashError::config(
 622 |                                 "rebuild",
 623 |                                 e.to_string(),
 624 |                             ));
 625 |                         }
 626 |                         let _ = state.indexer.commit();
 627 |                         let _ = state.metadata_db.clear();
 628 |                         for dir in settings.index_dirs {
 629 |                             let _ = state
 630 |                                 .scanner
 631 |                                 .scan_directory(
 632 |                                     PathBuf::from(dir),
 633 |                                     settings.exclude_patterns.clone(),
 634 |                                 )
 635 |                                 .await;
 636 |                         }
 637 |                         Message::IndexRebuilt
 638 |                     }),
 639 |                     Task::perform(
 640 |                         async move {
 641 |                             if let Some(r) = rx {
 642 |                                 let mut g = r.lock().await;
 643 |                                 g.recv().await
 644 |                             } else {
 645 |                                 None
 646 |                             }
 647 |                         },
 648 |                         Message::PollProgressResult,
 649 |                     ),
 650 |                 ])
 651 |             }
 652 |             Message::PollProgressResult(Some(event)) => {
 653 |                 let p = if event.total > 0 {
 654 |                     (event.processed as f32) / (event.total as f32)
 655 |                 } else {
 656 |                     0.0
 657 |                 };
 658 |                 app.rebuild_progress = Some(p);
 659 | 
 660 |                 let percent = p * 100.0;
 661 |                 let status_msg = if event.eta_seconds > 0 {
 662 |                     let mins = event.eta_seconds / 60;
 663 |                     let secs = event.eta_seconds % 60;
 664 |                     format!(
 665 |                         "{} ({:.1}%) - ETA: {:02}:{:02}",
 666 |                         event.status, percent, mins, secs
 667 |                     )
 668 |                 } else if event.total > 0 {
 669 |                     format!("{} ({:.1}%)", event.status, percent)
 670 |                 } else {
 671 |                     event.status.clone()
 672 |                 };
 673 | 
 674 |                 app.rebuild_status = Some(status_msg);
 675 |                 app.files_indexed = event.processed as i32;
 676 | 
 677 |                 let rx = app.progress_rx.clone();
 678 |                 Task::perform(
 679 |                     async move {
 680 |                         if let Some(r) = rx {
 681 |                             let mut g = r.lock().await;
 682 |                             g.recv().await
 683 |                         } else {
 684 |                             None
 685 |                         }
 686 |                     },
 687 |                     Message::PollProgressResult,
 688 |                 )
 689 |             }
 690 |             Message::PollProgressResult(None) => Task::none(),
 691 |             Message::RebuildProgress(_) => Task::none(), // Fallback
 692 |             Message::IndexRebuilt => {
 693 |                 let stats = app
 694 |                     .state
 695 |                     .as_ref()
 696 |                     .map(|s| s.indexer.get_statistics().unwrap_or_default())
 697 |                     .unwrap_or_default();
 698 |                 app.files_indexed = stats.total_documents as i32;
 699 |                 app.index_size = format!("{:.1} MB", (stats.total_size_bytes as f64) / 1_048_576.0);
 700 |                 if let Some(tray) = &app.tray_icon {
 701 |                     let _ = tray.set_tooltip(Some("Flash Search - Ready"));
 702 |                 }
 703 |                 app.rebuild_progress = None;
 704 |                 app.rebuild_status = None;
 705 |                 Task::none()
 706 |             }
 707 |             Message::AddFolder => Task::perform(
 708 |                 async {
 709 |                     rfd::AsyncFileDialog::new()
 710 |                         .pick_folder()
 711 |                         .await
 712 |                         .map(|p| p.path().to_string_lossy().to_string())
 713 |                 },
 714 |                 Message::FolderPicked,
 715 |             ),
 716 |             Message::FolderPicked(Some(f)) => {
 717 |                 if !app.settings.index_dirs.iter().any(|d| d == &f) {
 718 |                     app.settings.index_dirs.push(f.clone());
 719 |                     app.save_settings();
 720 | 
 721 |                     // Automatically start scanning the new folder
 722 |                     let state = match &app.state {
 723 |                         Some(s) => s.clone(),
 724 |                         None => return Task::none(),
 725 |                     };
 726 | 
 727 |                     app.rebuild_progress = Some(0.0);
 728 |                     app.rebuild_status = Some("Scanning new folder...".to_string());
 729 | 
 730 |                     let exclude_patterns = app.settings.exclude_patterns.clone();
 731 |                     let rx = app.progress_rx.clone();
 732 | 
 733 |                     return Task::batch(vec![
 734 |                         Task::future(async move {
 735 |                             let _ = state
 736 |                                 .scanner
 737 |                                 .scan_directory(PathBuf::from(f), exclude_patterns)
 738 |                                 .await;
 739 |                             Message::IndexRebuilt
 740 |                         }),
 741 |                         Task::perform(
 742 |                             async move {
 743 |                                 if let Some(r) = rx {
 744 |                                     let mut g = r.lock().await;
 745 |                                     g.recv().await
 746 |                                 } else {
 747 |                                     None
 748 |                                 }
 749 |                             },
 750 |                             Message::PollProgressResult,
 751 |                         ),
 752 |                     ]);
 753 |                 }
 754 |                 Task::none()
 755 |             }
 756 |             Message::FolderPicked(None) => Task::none(),
 757 |             Message::RemoveFolder(i) => {
 758 |                 if i < app.settings.index_dirs.len() {
 759 |                     app.settings.index_dirs.remove(i);
 760 |                     app.save_settings();
 761 |                 }
 762 |                 Task::none()
 763 |             }
 764 |             Message::SaveSettings => {
 765 |                 app.save_settings();
 766 |                 Task::none()
 767 |             }
 768 |             Message::MaxResultsChanged(val) => {
 769 |                 if let Ok(num) = val.parse() {
 770 |                     app.settings.max_results = num;
 771 |                 }
 772 |                 Task::none()
 773 |             }
 774 |             Message::ExcludePatternsChanged(val) => {
 775 |                 app.settings.exclude_patterns =
 776 |                     val.split(',').map(|s| s.trim().to_string()).collect();
 777 |                 Task::none()
 778 |             }
 779 |             Message::CustomExtensionsChanged(val) => {
 780 |                 app.settings.custom_extensions = val;
 781 |                 Task::none()
 782 |             }
 783 |             Message::ToggleTheme => {
 784 |                 app.is_dark = !app.is_dark;
 785 |                 app.settings.theme = if app.is_dark {
 786 |                     crate::settings::Theme::Dark
 787 |                 } else {
 788 |                     crate::settings::Theme::Light
 789 |                 };
 790 |                 app.save_settings();
 791 |                 Task::none()
 792 |             }
 793 |             Message::ToggleMinimizeToTray(enabled) => {
 794 |                 app.settings.minimize_to_tray = enabled;
 795 |                 app.save_settings();
 796 |                 Task::none()
 797 |             }
 798 |             Message::ToggleAutoStart(enabled) => {
 799 |                 app.settings.auto_start_on_boot = enabled;
 800 |                 app.save_settings();
 801 |                 let _ = crate::system::startup::set_auto_start(enabled);
 802 |                 Task::none()
 803 |             }
 804 |             Message::ToggleContextMenu(enabled) => {
 805 |                 app.settings.context_menu_enabled = enabled;
 806 |                 app.save_settings();
 807 |                 let _ = crate::system::context_menu::register_context_menu(enabled);
 808 |                 Task::none()
 809 |             }
 810 |             Message::ToggleSearchMode => {
 811 |                 app.search_mode = match app.search_mode {
 812 |                     SearchMode::FullText => SearchMode::Filename,
 813 |                     SearchMode::Filename => SearchMode::FullText,
 814 |                 };
 815 |                 if !app.search_query.is_empty() {
 816 |                     app.perform_search()
 817 |                 } else {
 818 |                     Task::none()
 819 |                 }
 820 |             }
 821 |             Message::ToggleCaseSensitive(val) => {
 822 |                 app.settings.case_sensitive = val;
 823 |                 app.save_settings();
 824 |                 if !app.search_query.is_empty() {
 825 |                     app.perform_search()
 826 |                 } else {
 827 |                     Task::none()
 828 |                 }
 829 |             }
 830 |             Message::ToggleWholeWord(val) => {
 831 |                 app.settings.whole_word = val;
 832 |                 app.save_settings();
 833 |                 if !app.search_query.is_empty() {
 834 |                     app.perform_search()
 835 |                 } else {
 836 |                     Task::none()
 837 |                 }
 838 |             }
 839 |             Message::FilterExtensionChanged(ext) => {
 840 |                 app.filter_extension = ext;
 841 |                 Task::none()
 842 |             }
 843 |             Message::ToggleFilterExtension(ext) => {
 844 |                 if app.filter_extensions.contains(&ext) {
 845 |                     app.filter_extensions.remove(&ext);
 846 |                 } else {
 847 |                     app.filter_extensions.insert(ext);
 848 |                 }
 849 |                 Task::none()
 850 |             }
 851 |             Message::ClearFilters => {
 852 |                 app.filter_extensions.clear();
 853 |                 app.min_size.clear();
 854 |                 app.max_size.clear();
 855 |                 app.filter_extension.clear();
 856 |                 app.filter_size.clear();
 857 |                 Task::none()
 858 |             }
 859 |             Message::MinSizeChanged(val) => {
 860 |                 app.min_size = val;
 861 |                 Task::none()
 862 |             }
 863 |             Message::MaxSizeChanged(val) => {
 864 |                 app.max_size = val;
 865 |                 Task::none()
 866 |             }
 867 |             Message::SizeUnitChanged(val) => {
 868 |                 app.size_unit = val;
 869 |                 Task::none()
 870 |             }
 871 |             Message::FilterSizeChanged(size) => {
 872 |                 app.filter_size = size;
 873 |                 Task::none()
 874 |             }
 875 |             Message::PreviewRequested(idx) => {
 876 |                 app.selected_index = Some(idx);
 877 |                 app.load_preview()
 878 |             }
 879 |             Message::PreviewLoaded(result) => {
 880 |                 app.preview_result = result;
 881 |                 app.is_loading_preview = false;
 882 |                 Task::none()
 883 |             }
 884 |             Message::MoveUp => {
 885 |                 if let Some(current) = app.selected_index {
 886 |                     if current > 0 {
 887 |                         app.selected_index = Some(current - 1);
 888 |                         return app.load_preview();
 889 |                     }
 890 |                 }
 891 |                 Task::none()
 892 |             }
 893 |             Message::MoveDown => {
 894 |                 if let Some(current) = app.selected_index {
 895 |                     if !app.results.is_empty() && current < app.results.len() - 1 {
 896 |                         app.selected_index = Some(current + 1);
 897 |                         return app.load_preview();
 898 |                     }
 899 |                 }
 900 |                 Task::none()
 901 |             }
 902 |             Message::DismissError => Task::none(),
 903 |             Message::Quit => {
 904 |                 // Set shutdown flag to initiate graceful shutdown
 905 |                 crate::SHUTDOWN_FLAG.store(true, std::sync::atomic::Ordering::SeqCst);
 906 |                 Task::none()
 907 |             }
 908 |             Message::GlobalHotkeyChanged(val) => {
 909 |                 app.settings.global_hotkey = val;
 910 |                 Task::none()
 911 |             }
 912 |             Message::StartPollingProgress => Task::none(),
 913 |             Message::PollSearchDeadline => {
 914 |                 if let Some(deadline) = app.search_deadline {
 915 |                     if std::time::Instant::now() >= deadline {
 916 |                         app.search_deadline = None;
 917 |                         return app.perform_search();
 918 |                     }
 919 |                 }
 920 |                 Task::none()
 921 |             }
 922 |             Message::PollHotkey => {
 923 |                 if let Ok(event) = global_hotkey::GlobalHotKeyEvent::receiver().try_recv() {
 924 |                     tracing::info!("Global hotkey pressed: {:?}", event);
 925 |                     return iced::window::gain_focus(iced::window::Id::unique())
 926 |                         .map(|_: ()| Message::NoOp);
 927 |                 }
 928 |                 Task::none()
 929 |             }
 930 |             Message::PollTray => {
 931 |                 if let Ok(event) = tray_icon::menu::MenuEvent::receiver().try_recv() {
 932 |                     if event.id.0 == "quit" {
 933 |                         crate::SHUTDOWN_FLAG.store(true, std::sync::atomic::Ordering::SeqCst);
 934 |                     } else if event.id.0 == "show" {
 935 |                         return iced::window::gain_focus(iced::window::Id::unique())
 936 |                             .map(|_: ()| Message::NoOp);
 937 |                     }
 938 |                 }
 939 |                 Task::none()
 940 |             }
 941 |             Message::NotImplemented(feature) => {
 942 |                 app.error = Some(format!(
 943 |                     "Feature '{}' is not yet implemented in this version.",
 944 |                     feature
 945 |                 ));
 946 |                 Task::none()
 947 |             }
 948 |             Message::NoOp => Task::none(),
 949 |         }
 950 |     }
 951 | }
 952 | 
 953 | pub fn subscription(app: &App) -> Subscription<Message> {
 954 |     let mut subs = vec![
 955 |         iced::time::every(std::time::Duration::from_millis(200)).map(|_| Message::PollHotkey),
 956 |         iced::time::every(std::time::Duration::from_millis(500)).map(|_| Message::PollTray),
 957 |     ];
 958 | 
 959 |     if app.search_deadline.is_some() {
 960 |         subs.push(
 961 |             iced::time::every(std::time::Duration::from_millis(50))
 962 |                 .map(|_| Message::PollSearchDeadline),
 963 |         );
 964 |     }
 965 | 
 966 |     Subscription::batch(subs)
 967 | }
 968 |

 976 |     }
 977 | }

1029 | pub fn run_ui(
1030 |     state: Result<std::sync::Arc<AppState>, String>,
1031 |     progress_rx: mpsc::Receiver<ProgressEvent>,
1032 | ) {
1033 |     let progress_mutex = Arc::new(tokio::sync::Mutex::new(progress_rx));
1034 | 
1035 |     iced::application(
1036 |         move || {
1037 |             let mut app = App::new(state.clone());
1038 |             app.progress_rx = Some(progress_mutex.clone());
1039 |             (app, Task::done(Message::StartPollingProgress))
1040 |         },
1041 |         update,
1042 |         view,
1043 |     )

1050 |         position: iced::window::Position::Centered,
1051 |         icon: load_app_icon(),
1052 |         ..Default::default()
1053 |     })
1054 |     .antialiasing(false)
1055 |     .run()
1056 |     .unwrap();
1057 | }

1067 |             .score(0.95)
1068 |             .maybe_title(Some("My File".into()))

1070 |             .matched_terms(vec![])
1071 |             .snippets(Vec::new())
1072 |             .build();

1074 |         assert_eq!(fi.title, "My File");
1075 |         assert_eq!(fi.path, "C:\\path\\to\\file.txt");
1076 |         assert_eq!(fi.score, 0.95);
1077 |         assert_eq!(fi.extension.as_deref(), Some("txt"));
1078 |     }

   1 | pub mod filename_index;
   2 | pub mod query_parser;
   3 | pub mod schema;

   7 | use self::schema::create_schema;

  16 | 
  17 | /// Current schema version - bump this when schema changes
  18 | pub const SCHEMA_VERSION: &str = "1.2.0";
  19 | 
  20 | fn get_schema_version_path(index_path: &Path) -> PathBuf {
  21 |     index_path.join(".schema_version")
  22 | }
  23 | 
  24 | fn read_schema_version(index_path: &Path) -> Option<String> {
  25 |     std::fs::read_to_string(get_schema_version_path(index_path))
  26 |         .ok()
  27 |         .map(|s| s.trim().to_string())
  28 | }
  29 | 
  30 | fn write_schema_version(index_path: &Path, version: &str) -> Result<()> {
  31 |     std::fs::write(get_schema_version_path(index_path), version).map_err(FlashError::Io)
  32 | }
  33 | 
  34 | /// Central manager for the Tantivy search index
  35 | pub struct IndexManager {
  36 |     #[allow(dead_code)]
  37 |     index: Index,
  38 |     writer: IndexWriterManager,
  39 |     searcher: Arc<IndexSearcher>,
  40 | }
  41 | 
  42 | impl IndexManager {
  43 |     /// Open or create index at the specified path
  44 |     pub fn open(index_path: &Path, memory_limit_mb: u32) -> Result<Self> {
  45 |         let schema = create_schema();
  46 | 
  47 |         // Ensure directory exists
  48 |         if !index_path.exists() {
  49 |             std::fs::create_dir_all(index_path).map_err(FlashError::Io)?;
  50 |         }
  51 | 
  52 |         // Check schema version - if mismatch, rebuild index
  53 |         let stored_version = read_schema_version(index_path);
  54 |         if let Some(ref ver) = stored_version {
  55 |             if ver != SCHEMA_VERSION {
  56 |                 warn!(
  57 |                     "Schema version mismatch: stored={}, current={}. Rebuilding index...",
  58 |                     ver, SCHEMA_VERSION
  59 |                 );
  60 |                 // Try to backup the index before destroying it
  61 |                 let backup_path = index_path.with_extension("backup");
  62 |                 let _ = std::fs::remove_dir_all(&backup_path); // Remove old backup if exists
  63 |                 let _ = copy_dir(index_path, &backup_path); // Try to backup
  64 |                 std::fs::remove_dir_all(index_path).map_err(FlashError::Io)?;
  65 |                 std::fs::create_dir_all(index_path).map_err(FlashError::Io)?;
  66 |                 write_schema_version(index_path, SCHEMA_VERSION)?;
  67 |             }
  68 |         } else if index_path.join("meta.json").exists() {
  69 |             // Old index without version - rebuild
  70 |             warn!("No schema version found. Rebuilding index...");
  71 |             // Try to backup the index before destroying it
  72 |             let backup_path = index_path.with_extension("backup");
  73 |             let _ = std::fs::remove_dir_all(&backup_path); // Remove old backup if exists
  74 |             let _ = copy_dir(index_path, &backup_path); // Try to backup
  75 |             std::fs::remove_dir_all(index_path).map_err(FlashError::Io)?;
  76 |             std::fs::create_dir_all(index_path).map_err(FlashError::Io)?;
  77 |             write_schema_version(index_path, SCHEMA_VERSION)?;
  78 |         } else {
  79 |             // New index - write version
  80 |             write_schema_version(index_path, SCHEMA_VERSION)?;
  81 |         }
  82 | 
  83 |         let directory = MmapDirectory::open(index_path)
  84 |             .map_err(|e| FlashError::index(format!("Failed to open index directory: {}", e)))?;
  85 | 
  86 |         let index = match Index::open_or_create(directory, schema.clone()) {
  87 |             Ok(idx) => idx,
  88 |             Err(e) => {
  89 |                 // Check if it's a schema mismatch error
  90 |                 let err_str = e.to_string();
  91 |                 if err_str.contains("Schema error") || err_str.contains("Inconsistent") {
  92 |                     warn!(
  93 |                         "Tantivy detected schema mismatch: {}. Forcing index rebuild...",
  94 |                         err_str
  95 |                     );
  96 | 
  97 |                     // Try to backup the index before destroying it
  98 |                     let backup_path = index_path.with_extension("backup");
  99 |                     let _ = std::fs::remove_dir_all(&backup_path); // Remove old backup if exists
 100 |                     let _ = copy_dir(index_path, &backup_path); // Try to backup
 101 | 
 102 |                     // Close the directory/files if needed? MmapDirectory handles it.
 103 |                     // Wipe and start over
 104 |                     std::fs::remove_dir_all(index_path).map_err(FlashError::Io)?;
 105 |                     std::fs::create_dir_all(index_path).map_err(FlashError::Io)?;
 106 |                     write_schema_version(index_path, SCHEMA_VERSION)?;
 107 | 
 108 |                     let new_directory = MmapDirectory::open(index_path).map_err(|e| {
 109 |                         FlashError::index(format!("Failed to re-open index directory: {}", e))
 110 |                     })?;
 111 |                     Index::open_or_create(new_directory, schema).map_err(|e| {
 112 |                         FlashError::index(format!("Failed to create new index after reset: {}", e))
 113 |                     })?
 114 |                 } else {
 115 |                     return Err(FlashError::index(format!(
 116 |                         "Failed to open or create index: {}",
 117 |                         e
 118 |                     )));
 119 |                 }
 120 |             }
 121 |         };
 122 | 
 123 |         info!(
 124 |             "Opened index at {} with schema version {}",
 125 |             index_path.display(),
 126 |             SCHEMA_VERSION
 127 |         );
 128 | 
 129 |         let writer = IndexWriterManager::new(&index, memory_limit_mb)?;
 130 |         let searcher = IndexSearcher::new(&index, index_path.to_path_buf())?;
 131 | 
 132 |         Ok(Self {
 133 |             index,
 134 |             writer,
 135 |             searcher: Arc::new(searcher),
 136 |         })
 137 |     }
 138 |

 198 | 
 199 | fn copy_dir(src: &Path, dst: &Path) -> std::io::Result<()> {
 200 |     std::fs::create_dir_all(dst)?;
 201 |     for entry in ignore::WalkBuilder::new(src)
 202 |         .hidden(false)
 203 |         .git_ignore(false)
 204 |         .ignore(false)
 205 |         .parents(false)
 206 |         .build()
 207 |         .skip(1)
 208 |     {
 209 |         let entry = entry.map_err(std::io::Error::other)?;
 210 |         let ty = entry.file_type().ok_or_else(|| {
 211 |             std::io::Error::new(std::io::ErrorKind::NotFound, "Could not get file type")
 212 |         })?;
 213 |         let path = entry.path();
 214 |         let relative = path.strip_prefix(src).map_err(std::io::Error::other)?;
 215 |         let target = dst.join(relative);
 216 |         if ty.is_dir() {
 217 |             std::fs::create_dir_all(target)?;
 218 |         } else {
 219 |             std::fs::copy(path, target)?;
 220 |         }
 221 |     }
 222 |     Ok(())
 223 | }

  67 |     let db_path = app_data_dir.join("metadata.redb");
  68 |     let metadata_db = metadata::MetadataDb::open(&db_path)
  69 |         .map_err(|e| FlashError::database("open", "metadata.redb", e.to_string()))?;
  70 | 
  71 |     let metadata_db_shared = Arc::new(metadata_db);
  72 |     let indexer_shared = Arc::new(indexer);
  73 | 
  74 |     let filename_index =
  75 |         match indexer::filename_index::FilenameIndex::open(&app_data_dir.join("filename_index")) {
  76 |             Ok(idx) => Some(Arc::new(idx)),
  77 |             Err(e) => {
  78 |                 error!("Failed to open filename index: {}", e);
  79 |                 None
  80 |             }
  81 |         };
  82 | 
  83 |     // Initialize watcher
  84 |     let watcher = watcher::WatcherManager::new(
  85 |         indexer_shared.clone(),
  86 |         metadata_db_shared.clone(),
  87 |         settings.get_allowed_extensions(),
  88 |     );
  89 | 
  90 |     let (progress_tx, progress_rx) = tokio::sync::mpsc::channel(100);
  91 | 
  92 |     let scanner = Arc::new(crate::scanner::Scanner::new(
  93 |         indexer_shared.clone(),
  94 |         metadata_db_shared.clone(),
  95 |         filename_index.clone(),
  96 |         Some(progress_tx.clone()),
  97 |         settings.clone(),
  98 |     ));
  99 | 
 100 |     let state = Arc::new(
 101 |         AppState::builder()
 102 |             .indexer(indexer_shared)
 103 |             .metadata_db(metadata_db_shared)
 104 |             .settings_manager(settings_manager)
 105 |             .watcher(watcher)
 106 |             .maybe_filename_index(filename_index)
 107 |             .progress_tx(progress_tx)
 108 |             .scanner(scanner)
 109 |             .build(),
 110 |     );
 111 | 
 112 |     Ok((state, progress_rx))
 113 | }
 114 | 
 115 | pub fn run_ui() -> std::result::Result<(), FlashError> {
 116 |     let result = setup_app().map(|(state, rx)| {
 117 |         iced_ui::run_ui(Ok(state), rx);
 118 |     });
 119 | 
 120 |     if let Err(e) = result {
 121 |         iced_ui::run_ui(Err(e.to_string()), tokio::sync::mpsc::channel(1).1);
 122 |     }
 123 | 
 124 |     Ok(())
 125 | }
 126 | 
 127 | pub async fn run_cli(
 128 |     query: Option<String>,
 129 |     is_json: bool,
 130 |     _index_path: Option<String>,
 131 | ) -> crate::error::Result<()> {
 132 |     if let Some(query_str) = query {
 133 |         let (state, _) = setup_app()?;
 134 |         let results = state
 135 |             .indexer
 136 |             .search(&query_str, 20, None, None, None)
 137 |             .await?;
 138 | 
 139 |         if is_json {
 140 |             let json_results: Vec<serde_json::Value> = results
 141 |                 .into_iter()
 142 |                 .map(|res| {
 143 |                     serde_json::json!({
 144 |                         "score": res.score,
 145 |                         "path": res.file_path,
 146 |                         "title": res.title
 147 |                     })
 148 |                 })
 149 |                 .collect();
 150 |             println!(
 151 |                 "{}",
 152 |                 serde_json::to_string_pretty(&json_results).unwrap_or_default()
 153 |             );
 154 |         } else {
 155 |             for res in results {
 156 |                 println!("{} | {}", res.score, res.file_path);
 157 |             }
 158 |         }
 159 |     } else {
 160 |         println!("Usage: flash-search --cli <query> [--json]");
 161 |     }
 162 |     Ok(())
 163 | }

  12 | use tracing_subscriber::{fmt, layer::SubscriberExt, util::SubscriberInitExt, EnvFilter};
  13 | 
  14 | fn init_logging() -> WorkerGuard {
  15 |     let log_dir = dirs::data_local_dir()
  16 |         .unwrap_or_else(|| std::path::PathBuf::from("."))
  17 |         .join("com.flashsearch")
  18 |         .join("logs");
  19 | 
  20 |     std::fs::create_dir_all(&log_dir).ok();
  21 | 
  22 |     let file_appender = RollingFileAppender::new(Rotation::DAILY, &log_dir, "flash-search.log");
  23 | 
  24 |     let (non_blocking, guard) = tracing_appender::non_blocking(file_appender);
  25 | 
  26 |     let env_filter = EnvFilter::try_from_default_env().unwrap_or_else(|_| EnvFilter::new("info"));
  27 | 
  28 |     tracing_subscriber::registry()
  29 |         .with(env_filter)
  30 |         .with(fmt::layer().with_writer(non_blocking).with_ansi(false))
  31 |         .with(fmt::layer().with_writer(std::io::stderr))
  32 |         .init();
  33 | 
  34 |     log_panics::init();
  35 | 
  36 |     info!("Flash Search starting up");
  37 | 
  38 |     // Prune logs older than 30 days
  39 |     prune_old_logs(&log_dir);
  40 | 
  41 |     guard
  42 | }
  43 | 
  44 | fn prune_old_logs(log_dir: &std::path::Path) {
  45 |     if let Ok(entries) = std::fs::read_dir(log_dir) {
  46 |         let now = std::time::SystemTime::now();
  47 |         let max_age = std::time::Duration::from_secs(30 * 24 * 60 * 60);
  48 | 
  49 |         for entry in entries.flatten() {
  50 |             if let Ok(metadata) = entry.metadata() {
  51 |                 if let Ok(modified) = metadata.modified() {
  52 |                     if let Ok(age) = now.duration_since(modified) {
  53 |                         if age > max_age {
  54 |                             let _ = std::fs::remove_file(entry.path());
  55 |                         }
  56 |                     }
  57 |                 }
  58 |             }
  59 |         }
  60 |     }
  61 | }
  62 | 
  63 | fn spawn_update_checker() {
  64 |     std::thread::spawn(|| {
  65 |         tracing::info!("Checking for updates...");
  66 |         // Placeholder repo config for self_update
  67 |         let result = self_update::backends::github::Update::configure()
  68 |             .repo_owner("SV-stark")
  69 |             .repo_name("findall")
  70 |             .bin_name("flash-search")
  71 |             .show_download_progress(true)
  72 |             .current_version(env!("CARGO_PKG_VERSION"))
  73 |             .build();
  74 | 
  75 |         if let Ok(updater) = result {
  76 |             match updater.update() {
  77 |                 Ok(status) => {
  78 |                     if status.updated() {
  79 |                         tracing::info!("Updated to version: {}", status.version());
  80 |                     } else {
  81 |                         tracing::info!("Flash Search is up to date.");
  82 |                     }
  83 |                 }
  84 |                 Err(e) => tracing::warn!("Update check failed: {}", e),
  85 |             }
  86 |         }
  87 |     });
  88 | }
  89 | 
  90 | fn main() {
  91 |     let app_dir = dirs::data_local_dir()
  92 |         .unwrap_or_else(|| std::path::PathBuf::from("."))
  93 |         .join("com.flashsearch");
  94 |     std::fs::create_dir_all(&app_dir).ok();
  95 | 
  96 |     let lock_path = app_dir.join("flashsearch.lock");
  97 |     let lock_file = std::fs::OpenOptions::new()
  98 |         .write(true)
  99 |         .create(true)
 100 |         .truncate(true)
 101 |         .open(&lock_path)
 102 |         .expect("Could not open lock file");
 103 | 
 104 |     let mut lock = fd_lock::RwLock::new(lock_file);
 105 |     let lock_guard = match lock.try_write() {
 106 |         Ok(guard) => guard,
 107 |         Err(_) => {
 108 |             eprintln!("Flash Search is already running.");
 109 |             std::process::exit(1);
 110 |         }
 111 |     };
 112 | 
 113 |     // Keep the lock guard alive for the duration of the program
 114 |     // We bind it to a variable to ensure it stays locked until the process exits
 115 |     let _lock = lock_guard;
 116 | 
 117 |     let _guard = init_logging();
 118 | 
 119 |     spawn_update_checker();
 120 | 
 121 |     let args: Vec<String> = std::env::args().collect();
 122 | 
 123 |     if args.iter().any(|arg| arg == "--version" || arg == "-V") {
 124 |         println!("flash-search {}", env!("CARGO_PKG_VERSION"));
 125 |         return;
 126 |     }
 127 | 
 128 |     // We must create a tokio runtime for background tasks (like Watcher), but we CANNOT
 129 |     // use #[tokio::main] because Iced uses winit to hijack the main thread and blocks it.
 130 |     let rt = tokio::runtime::Builder::new_multi_thread()
 131 |         .enable_all()
 132 |         .build()
 133 |         .unwrap();
 134 |     let _rt_guard = rt.enter();
 135 | 
 136 |     if args.iter().any(|arg| arg == "--help" || arg == "-h") {
 137 |         println!("Flash Search - Ultrafast local full-text search\n");
 138 |         println!("Usage: flash-search [OPTIONS]");
 139 |         println!("Options:");
 140 |         println!("  -V, --version       Print version");
 141 |         println!("  -h, --help          Print help");
 142 |         println!("  -c, --cli <query>   Perform a search from the command line");
 143 |         println!("  --json              Output CLI search results as JSON");
 144 |         return;
 145 |     }
 146 | 
 147 |     if args.iter().any(|arg| arg == "--cli" || arg == "-c") {
 148 |         let query_index = args.iter().position(|a| a == "--cli" || a == "-c").unwrap();
 149 |         let query = args.get(query_index + 1).cloned();
 150 |         let is_json = args.iter().any(|a| a == "--json");
 151 | 
 152 |         rt.block_on(async {
 153 |             if let Err(e) = flash_search::run_cli(query, is_json, None).await {
 154 |                 error!("CLI Error: {}", e);
 155 |             }
 156 |         });
 157 |         return;
 158 |     }
 159 | 
 160 |     ctrlc::set_handler(|| {
 161 |         info!("Shutdown signal received, committing index...");
 162 |         flash_search::SHUTDOWN_FLAG.store(true, Ordering::SeqCst);
 163 |     })
 164 |     .expect("Error setting Ctrl-C handler");
 165 | 
 166 |     // Run the UI
 167 |     if let Err(e) = flash_search::run_ui() {
 168 |         error!("Application error: {}", e);
 169 |         std::process::exit(1);
 170 |     }
 171 | }

   1 | use crate::error::{FlashError, Result};

   9 | #[derive(Debug, Clone, serde::Serialize, serde::Deserialize)]
  10 | pub struct ParsedDocument {
  11 |     pub path: String,
  12 |     pub content: String,
  13 |     pub title: Option<CompactString>,
  14 | }
  15 | 
  16 | /// Detect file type and route to appropriate parser using Kreuzberg
  17 | pub fn parse_file(path: &Path) -> Result<ParsedDocument> {
  18 |     // Log the file extension for debugging
  19 |     let extension = path.extension().and_then(|e| e.to_str()).unwrap_or("none");
  20 |     tracing::debug!(
  21 |         "Parsing file: {} (extension: {})",
  22 |         path.display(),
  23 |         extension
  24 |     );
  25 | 
  26 |     // Disable cache to prevent unbounded memory growth during deep directory scans.
  27 |     let config = kreuzberg::ExtractionConfig {
  28 |         use_cache: false,
  29 |         ..Default::default()
  30 |     };
  31 | 
  32 |     let result = kreuzberg::extract_file_sync(path, None, &config).map_err(|e| {
  33 |         tracing::error!("Failed to extract file {}: {}", path.display(), e);
  34 |         FlashError::parse(path, format!("Extraction failed: {}", e))
  35 |     })?;
  36 | 
  37 |     tracing::debug!("Successfully parsed file: {}", path.display());
  38 | 
  39 |     Ok(ParsedDocument {
  40 |         path: path.to_string_lossy().to_string(),
  41 |         content: result.content,
  42 |         title: result.metadata.title.map(CompactString::from),
  43 | 
  44 |     })
  45 | }
  46 | 
  47 | #[cfg(test)]
  48 | mod tests {
  49 |     use super::*;
  50 |     use std::ffi::OsStr;
  51 | 
  52 |     fn extension_matches(extension: &OsStr, expected: &str) -> bool {
  53 |         extension
  54 |             .to_str()
  55 |             .map(|s| s.to_lowercase() == expected)
  56 |             .unwrap_or(false)
  57 |     }
  58 |

  61 |         assert!(extension_matches(OsStr::new("docx"), "docx"));
  62 |         assert!(extension_matches(OsStr::new("DOCX"), "docx"));
  63 |         assert!(extension_matches(OsStr::new("Docx"), "docx"));
  64 |         assert!(!extension_matches(OsStr::new("pdf"), "docx"));
  65 |     }

  71 |         let file_path = dir.path().join("test.txt");
  72 |         let mut file = std::fs::File::create(&file_path).unwrap();
  73 |         writeln!(file, "Hello, world!").unwrap();

   1 | pub mod drive_scanner;
   2 | 
   3 | use crate::error::Result;
   4 | use crate::indexer::IndexManager;
   5 | use crate::metadata::MetadataDb;
   6 | use crate::parsers::{parse_file, ParsedDocument};
   7 | use blake3;

   9 | use rayon::prelude::*;
  10 | use std::path::PathBuf;
  11 | use std::sync::atomic::AtomicUsize;
  12 | use std::sync::atomic::Ordering;
  13 | use std::sync::Arc;
  14 | use std::time::Instant;
  15 | use tokio::sync::mpsc;
  16 | use tracing::{info, instrument, warn};
  17 | 
  18 | #[derive(Clone, Debug, serde::Serialize)]
  19 | pub enum ProgressType {
  20 |     Content,
  21 |     Filename,
  22 | }
  23 | 
  24 | #[derive(Clone, Debug, serde::Serialize)]
  25 | pub struct ProgressEvent {
  26 |     pub total: usize,
  27 |     pub processed: usize,
  28 |     pub current_file: String,
  29 |     pub status: String,
  30 |     pub ptype: ProgressType,
  31 |     pub files_per_second: f64,
  32 |     pub eta_seconds: u64,
  33 |     pub current_folder: String,
  34 | }
  35 | 
  36 | const BATCH_SIZE: usize = 1000;
  37 | 
  38 | #[derive(Debug)]
  39 | struct IndexTask {
  40 |     doc: ParsedDocument,
  41 |     modified: u64,
  42 |     size: u64,
  43 |     content_hash: [u8; 32],
  44 | }
