```rust
  46 | pub struct Scanner {
  47 |     indexer: Arc<IndexManager>,
  48 |     metadata_db: Arc<MetadataDb>,
  49 |     filename_index: Option<Arc<crate::indexer::filename_index::FilenameIndex>>,
  50 |     progress_tx: Option<mpsc::Sender<ProgressEvent>>,
  51 |     settings: crate::settings::AppSettings,
  52 | }
  53 | 
  54 | impl Scanner {
  55 |     pub fn new(
  56 |         indexer: Arc<IndexManager>,
  57 |         metadata_db: Arc<MetadataDb>,
  58 |         filename_index: Option<Arc<crate::indexer::filename_index::FilenameIndex>>,
  59 |         progress_tx: Option<mpsc::Sender<ProgressEvent>>,
  60 |         settings: crate::settings::AppSettings,
  61 |     ) -> Self {
  62 |         Self {
  63 |             indexer,
  64 |             metadata_db,
  65 |             filename_index,
  66 |             progress_tx,
  67 |             settings,
  68 |         }
  69 |     }
  70 | 
  71 |     fn get_scanner(&self) -> Box<dyn DriveScanner> {
  72 |         #[cfg(target_os = "windows")]
  73 |         {
  74 |             Box::new(drive_scanner::WindowsDriveScanner)
  75 |         }
  76 |         #[cfg(target_os = "macos")]
  77 |         {
  78 |             Box::new(drive_scanner::MacDriveScanner)
  79 |         }
  80 |         #[cfg(target_os = "linux")]
  81 |         {
  82 |             Box::new(drive_scanner::LinuxDriveScanner)
  83 |         }
  84 |         #[cfg(not(any(target_os = "windows", target_os = "macos", target_os = "linux")))]
  85 |         {
  86 |             Box::new(drive_scanner::DefaultDriveScanner)
  87 |         }
  88 |     }
  89 | 
  90 |     #[instrument(skip(self, tx))]
  91 |     pub fn watch_drive(
  92 |         &self,
  93 |         root: PathBuf,
  94 |         tx: mpsc::Sender<(PathBuf, crate::watcher::WatcherAction)>,
  95 |     ) -> Result<()> {
  96 |         let scanner = self.get_scanner();
  97 |         scanner.watch(root, tx)
  98 |     }
  99 | 
 100 |     #[instrument(skip(self, exclude_patterns), fields(root = %root.display()))]
 101 |     pub async fn scan_directory(&self, root: PathBuf, exclude_patterns: Vec<String>) -> Result<()> {
 102 |         info!("Starting directory scan for {}", root.display());
 103 | 
 104 |         let (path_tx, path_rx) = crossbeam_channel::unbounded::<PathBuf>();
 105 | 
 106 |         let root_clone = root.clone();
 107 |         let tx_clone = self.progress_tx.clone();
 108 |         let scanner = self.get_scanner();
 109 |         let total = Arc::new(AtomicUsize::new(0));
 110 |         let total_for_scan = total.clone();
 111 | 
 112 |         let walker_handle = tokio::task::spawn_blocking(move || {
 113 |             scanner.scan(
 114 |                 root_clone,
 115 |                 exclude_patterns,
 116 |                 path_tx,
 117 |                 tx_clone,
 118 |                 total_for_scan,
 119 |             )
 120 |         });
 121 | 
 122 |         // --- Stage 2: Content Indexing (Batched) ---
 123 |         // Parse files in parallel via Rayon, collect results via mpsc,
 124 |         // then batch-write to the index and metadata DB.
 125 |         let (task_tx, task_rx) = crossbeam_channel::bounded::<IndexTask>(BATCH_SIZE * 8);
 126 |         let metadata_db_for_parser = self.metadata_db.clone();
 127 |         let metadata_db_for_writer = self.metadata_db.clone();
 128 |         let indexer_clone = self.indexer.clone();
 129 |         let filename_index_clone = self.filename_index.clone();
 130 |         let progress_tx_clone = self.progress_tx.clone();
 131 |         let total_files = total.clone();
 132 | 
 133 |         // Configure Rayon thread pool based on settings limit
 134 |         let threads = self.settings.indexing_threads as usize;
 135 |         let pool = rayon::ThreadPoolBuilder::new()
 136 |             .num_threads(threads)
 137 |             .stack_size(8 * 1024 * 1024) // Increase stack size to 8MB to prevent overflow during parsing
 138 |             .build()
 139 |             .unwrap_or_else(|_| {
 140 |                 rayon::ThreadPoolBuilder::new()
 141 |                     .stack_size(8 * 1024 * 1024)
 142 |                     .build()
 143 |                     .unwrap()
 144 |             });
 145 |         let file_size_limit_mb = self.settings.index_file_size_limit_mb;
 146 |         let allowed_extensions = Arc::new(self.settings.get_allowed_extensions());
 147 |         let allowed_extensions_clone = allowed_extensions.clone();
 148 | 
 149 |         // --- Stage 2a: Parallel parsing (Rayon) → sends IndexTask into channel ---
 150 |         let parser_handle = tokio::task::spawn_blocking(move || {
 151 |             info!("Stage 2a: Parallel Parsing ({} threads)", threads);
 152 | 
 153 |             pool.install(|| {
 154 |                 let mut chunk = Vec::with_capacity(200);
 155 |                 for path in path_rx.into_iter() {
 156 |                     chunk.push(path);
 157 |                     if chunk.len() >= 200 {
 158 |                         Scanner::process_chunk(
 159 |                             &chunk,
 160 |                             &metadata_db_for_parser,
 161 |                             file_size_limit_mb,
 162 |                             &allowed_extensions_clone,
 163 |                             &task_tx,
 164 |                         );
 165 |                         chunk.clear();
 166 |                     }
 167 |                 }
 168 |                 if !chunk.is_empty() {
 169 |                     Scanner::process_chunk(
 170 |                         &chunk,
 171 |                         &metadata_db_for_parser,
 172 |                         file_size_limit_mb,
 173 |                         &allowed_extensions_clone,
 174 |                         &task_tx,
 175 |                     );
 176 |                 }
 177 |             });
 178 |             // task_tx is dropped here, closing the channel
 179 |         });
 180 | 
 181 |         // --- Stage 2b: Sequential batch writer (single thread) ---
 182 |         let writer_handle = tokio::task::spawn_blocking(move || {
 183 |             info!("Stage 2b: Batch Writing");
 184 |             let start = Instant::now();
 185 |             let mut doc_batch: Vec<(crate::parsers::ParsedDocument, u64, u64)> =
 186 |                 Vec::with_capacity(BATCH_SIZE);
 187 |             let mut meta_batch: Vec<(String, u64, u64, [u8; 32])> = Vec::with_capacity(BATCH_SIZE);
 188 |             let mut processed: usize = 0;
 189 | 
 190 |             for task in task_rx.iter() {
 191 |                 // Add to filename index
 192 |                 if let Some(f_index) = &filename_index_clone {
 193 |                     let path = std::path::Path::new(&task.doc.path);
 194 |                     if let Some(name) = path.file_name().and_then(|n| n.to_str()) {
 195 |                         let _ = f_index.add_file(&task.doc.path, name);
 196 |                     }
 197 |                 }
 198 | 
 199 |                 // Clone path before moving doc
 200 |                 let doc_path = task.doc.path.clone();
 201 |                 doc_batch.push((task.doc, task.modified, task.size));
 202 |                 meta_batch.push((doc_path, task.modified, task.size, task.content_hash));
 203 |                 processed += 1;
 204 | 
 205 |                 // Flush batch when full
 206 |                 if doc_batch.len() >= BATCH_SIZE {
 207 |                     let _ = indexer_clone.add_documents_batch(&doc_batch);
 208 |                     let _ = indexer_clone.commit();
 209 |                     indexer_clone.invalidate_cache();
 210 |                     let _ = metadata_db_for_writer.batch_update_metadata(&meta_batch);
 211 |                     doc_batch.clear();
 212 |                     meta_batch.clear();
 213 |                 }
 214 | 
 215 |                 // Progress update
 216 |                 if processed % 10 == 0 {
 217 |                     let current_total = total_files.load(Ordering::Relaxed);
 218 |                     let elapsed = start.elapsed().as_secs_f64();
 219 |                     let rate = if elapsed > 0.0 {
 220 |                         processed as f64 / elapsed
 221 |                     } else {
 222 |                         0.0
 223 |                     };
 224 | 
 225 |                     // Batch summary every 1000 files
 226 |                     if processed % 1000 == 0 {
 227 |                         info!(
 228 |                             "Indexed {} / {} files ({:.1} files/s)",
 229 |                             processed, current_total, rate
 230 |                         );
 231 |                     }
 232 | 
 233 |                     if let Some(tx) = &progress_tx_clone {
 234 |                         let _ = tx.try_send(ProgressEvent {
 235 |                             ptype: ProgressType::Content,
 236 |                             current_file: "".to_string(),
 237 |                             current_folder: "".to_string(),
 238 |                             processed,
 239 |                             total: current_total,
 240 |                             status: "Indexing contents...".to_string(),
 241 |                             eta_seconds: if rate > 0.0 {
 242 |                                 (current_total.saturating_sub(processed) as f64 / rate) as u64
 243 |                             } else {
 244 |                                 0
 245 |                             },
 246 |                             files_per_second: rate,
 247 |                         });
 248 |                     }
 249 |                 }
 250 |             }
 251 | 
 252 |             // Flush remaining items (B1: always commit at end)
 253 |             if !doc_batch.is_empty() {
 254 |                 let _ = indexer_clone.add_documents_batch(&doc_batch);
 255 |                 let _ = indexer_clone.commit();
 256 |                 indexer_clone.invalidate_cache();
 257 |                 let _ = metadata_db_for_writer.batch_update_metadata(&meta_batch);
 258 |             }
 259 | 
 260 |             // Final progress
 261 |             if let Some(tx) = &progress_tx_clone {
 262 |                 let _ = tx.try_send(ProgressEvent {
 263 |                     ptype: ProgressType::Content,
 264 |                     current_file: "".to_string(),
 265 |                     current_folder: "".to_string(),
 266 |                     processed,
 267 |                     total: processed,
 268 |                     status: "All files indexed".to_string(),
 269 |                     eta_seconds: 0,
 270 |                     files_per_second: 0.0,
 271 |                 });
 272 |             }
 273 | 
 274 |             info!(
 275 |                 "Indexed {} files in {:.2}s",
 276 |                 processed,
 277 |                 start.elapsed().as_secs_f64()
 278 |             );
 279 |         });
 280 | 
 281 |         // Wait for all stages to complete
 282 |         let _ = walker_handle
 283 |             .await
 284 |             .map_err(|e| crate::error::FlashError::index(format!("Walk task failed: {}", e)))?;
 285 |         parser_handle
 286 |             .await
 287 |             .map_err(|e| crate::error::FlashError::index(format!("Parse task failed: {}", e)))?;
 288 |         writer_handle
 289 |             .await
 290 |             .map_err(|e| crate::error::FlashError::index(format!("Write task failed: {}", e)))?;
 291 | 
 292 |         // Commit filename index to disk
 293 |         if let Some(f_index) = &self.filename_index {
 294 |             let _ = f_index.commit();
 295 |         }
 296 | 
 297 |         Ok(())
 298 |     }
 299 | 
 300 |     fn process_chunk(
 301 |         chunk: &[PathBuf],
 302 |         metadata_db: &Arc<MetadataDb>,
 303 |         file_size_limit_mb: u32,
 304 |         allowed_extensions: &std::collections::HashSet<String>,
 305 |         task_tx: &crossbeam_channel::Sender<IndexTask>,
 306 |     ) {
 307 |         let limit_bytes = (file_size_limit_mb as u64) * 1024 * 1024;
 308 |         let mut batch_entries = Vec::with_capacity(chunk.len());
 309 |         let mut valid_paths = Vec::with_capacity(chunk.len());
 310 | 
 311 |         for path in chunk {
 312 |             // Check file extension
 313 |             if let Some(ext) = path.extension().and_then(|e| e.to_str()) {
 314 |                 if !allowed_extensions.contains(&ext.to_lowercase()) {
 315 |                     continue;
 316 |                 }
 317 |             } else {
 318 |                 // If the file doesn't have an extension, we skip it by default
 319 |                 continue;
 320 |             }
 321 | 
 322 |             let metadata = match std::fs::metadata(path) {
 323 |                 Ok(m) => m,
 324 |                 Err(_) => continue,
 325 |             };
 326 | 
 327 |             let size = metadata.len();
 328 |             if size > limit_bytes {
 329 |                 warn!(
 330 |                     "Skipping large file: {} ({} bytes > limit of {} bytes)",
 331 |                     path.display(),
 332 |                     size,
 333 |                     limit_bytes
 334 |                 );
 335 |                 continue;
 336 |             }
 337 | 
 338 |             let modified = metadata
 339 |                 .modified()
 340 |                 .unwrap_or(std::time::SystemTime::UNIX_EPOCH)
 341 |                 .duration_since(std::time::SystemTime::UNIX_EPOCH)
 342 |                 .unwrap_or_default()
 343 |                 .as_secs();
 344 | 
 345 |             batch_entries.push((path.to_string_lossy().to_string(), modified, size));
 346 |             valid_paths.push((path.clone(), modified, size));
 347 |         }
 348 | 
 349 |         if batch_entries.is_empty() {
 350 |             return;
 351 |         }
 352 | 
 353 |         let needs_reindex = metadata_db
 354 |             .batch_needs_reindex(&batch_entries)
 355 |             .unwrap_or_else(|_| vec![true; batch_entries.len()]);
 356 | 
 357 |         let paths_to_parse: Vec<_> = valid_paths
 358 |             .into_iter()
 359 |             .enumerate()
 360 |             .filter(|(i, _)| needs_reindex[*i])
 361 |             .map(|(_, data)| data)
 362 |             .collect();
 363 | 
 364 |         paths_to_parse
 365 |             .into_par_iter()
 366 |             .for_each(|(path, modified, size)| {
 367 |                 if let Ok(parsed) = parse_file(&path) {
 368 |                     let content_hash = blake3::hash(parsed.content.as_bytes()).into();
 369 |                     let _ = task_tx.send(IndexTask {
 370 |                         doc: parsed,
 371 |                         modified,
 372 |                         size,
 373 |                         content_hash,
 374 |                     });
 375 |                 } else {
 376 |                     warn!("Failed to parse file {:?}", path);
 377 |                 }
 378 |             });
 379 |     }
 380 | }
 381 |

 384 |     use super::*;
 385 |     use crate::indexer::IndexManager;
 386 |     use crate::metadata::MetadataDb;
 387 |     use crate::settings::AppSettings;
```

```rust
   1 | use std::io::Result;
   2 | 
   3 | fn main() -> Result<()> {
   4 |     #[cfg(windows)]
   5 |     {
   6 |         use std::path::Path;
   7 |         let icon_path = Path::new("assets/icon.ico");
   8 |         let logo_path = Path::new("assets/logo.png");
   9 |         
  10 |         // Generate icon if it doesn't exist (or is empty) and logo exists
  11 |         if (!icon_path.exists() || std::fs::metadata(icon_path).map(|m| m.len()).unwrap_or(0) == 0) 
  12 |             && logo_path.exists() {
  13 |             println!("cargo:warning=Generating icon from logo.png...");
  14 |             if let Ok(img) = image::open(logo_path) {
  15 |                 // Resize to 256x256 for a high-quality icon that isn't massive
  16 |                 let resized = img.resize(256, 256, image::imageops::FilterType::Lanczos3);
  17 |                 if let Err(e) = resized.save_with_format(icon_path, image::ImageFormat::Ico) {
  18 |                     println!("cargo:warning=Failed to save icon.ico: {}", e);
  19 |                 } else {
  20 |                     println!("cargo:warning=Successfully generated icon.ico");
  21 |                 }
  22 |             } else {
  23 |                 println!("cargo:warning=Failed to open assets/logo.png");
  24 |             }
  25 |         }
  26 | 
  27 |         if icon_path.exists() && std::fs::metadata(icon_path).map(|m| m.len()).unwrap_or(0) > 0 {
  28 |             let mut res = winres::WindowsResource::new();
  29 |             res.set_icon(icon_path.to_str().unwrap());
  30 |             res.compile()?;
  31 |         } else {
  32 |             println!("cargo:warning=No valid icon found at assets/icon.ico - skipping embedding");
  33 |         }
  34 |     }
  35 |     
  36 |     Ok(())
  37 | }
```

```rust
   1 | #[cfg(target_os = "windows")]
   2 | pub fn set_auto_start(enable: bool, app_name: &str, exe_path: &str) -> Result<(), String> {
   3 |     use winreg::enums::{HKEY_CURRENT_USER, KEY_ALL_ACCESS};
   4 |     use winreg::RegKey;
   5 | 
   6 |     let hkcu = RegKey::predef(HKEY_CURRENT_USER);
   7 |     let run_key = hkcu
   8 |         .open_subkey_with_flags(
   9 |             r"Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Run",
  10 |             KEY_ALL_ACCESS,
  11 |         )
  12 |         .map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;
  13 | 
  14 |     if enable {
  15 |         run_key
  16 |             .set_value(app_name, &exe_path)
  17 |             .map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;
  18 |     } else {
  19 |         let _ = run_key.delete_value(app_name);
  20 |     }
  21 |     Ok(())
  22 | }
  23 | 
  24 | #[cfg(target_os = "windows")]
  25 | pub fn is_auto_start_enabled(app_name: &str) -> Result<bool, String> {
  26 |     use winreg::enums::HKEY_CURRENT_USER;
  27 |     use winreg::RegKey;
  28 | 
  29 |     let hkcu = RegKey::predef(HKEY_CURRENT_USER);
  30 |     let run_key = hkcu
  31 |         .open_subkey(r"Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Run")
  32 |         .map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;
  33 | 
  34 |     match run_key.get_value::<String, _>(app_name) {
  35 |         Ok(_) => Ok(true),
  36 |         Err(_) => Ok(false),
  37 |     }
  38 | }
  39 |
```

```rust
  67 | pub fn add_search_history_internal(query: String, state: &Arc<AppState>) -> Result<(), String> {
  68 |     let mut cache = state.settings_cache.write();
  69 | 
  70 |     let mut history = cache.search_history.clone().unwrap_or_default();
  71 | 
  72 |     let mut found = false;
  73 |     for item in &mut history {
  74 |         if item.query == query {
  75 |             item.frequency += 1;
  76 |             item.last_used = std::time::SystemTime::now()
  77 |                 .duration_since(std::time::SystemTime::UNIX_EPOCH)
  78 |                 .unwrap()
  79 |                 .as_secs();
  80 |             found = true;
  81 |             break;
  82 |         }
  83 |     }
  84 | 
  85 |     if !found {
  86 |         history.insert(
  87 |             0,
  88 |             crate::settings::SearchHistoryItem {
  89 |                 query,
  90 |                 frequency: 1,
  91 |                 last_used: std::time::SystemTime::now()
  92 |                     .duration_since(std::time::SystemTime::UNIX_EPOCH)
  93 |                     .unwrap()
  94 |                     .as_secs(),
  95 |             },
  96 |         );
  97 |     }
  98 | 
  99 |     history.sort_by(|a, b| b.frequency.cmp(&a.frequency));
 100 |     history.truncate(50);
 101 | 
 102 |     cache.search_history = Some(history);
 103 |     state
 104 |         .settings_manager
 105 |         .save(&cache)
 106 |         .map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;
 107 | 
 108 |     Ok(())
 109 | }

 127 | pub fn pin_file_internal(path: String, state: &Arc<AppState>) -> Result<(), String> {
 128 |     let mut cache = state.settings_cache.write();
 129 | 
 130 |     if !cache.pinned_files.contains(&path) {
 131 |         cache.pinned_files.push(path);
 132 |         state
 133 |             .settings_manager
 134 |             .save(&cache)
 135 |             .map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;
 136 |     }
 137 |     Ok(())
 138 | }
 139 | 
 140 | pub fn unpin_file_internal(path: String, state: &Arc<AppState>) -> Result<(), String> {
 141 |     let mut cache = state.settings_cache.write();
 142 | 
 143 |     cache.pinned_files.retain(|p| p != &path);
 144 |     state
 145 |         .settings_manager
 146 |         .save(&cache)
 147 |         .map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;
 148 |     Ok(())
 149 | }
 150 | 
 151 | pub fn get_pinned_files_internal(state: &Arc<AppState>) -> Result<Vec<String>, String> {
 152 |     Ok(state.settings_cache.read().pinned_files.clone())
 153 | 
 154 | }
```

```rust
   3 | pub fn get_home_dir_internal() -> Result<String, String> {
   4 |     dirs::home_dir()
   5 |         .map(|p| p.to_string_lossy().to_string())
   6 |         .ok_or_else(|| "Could not determine home directory".to_string())

   8 | 
   9 | pub fn open_folder_internal(path: String) -> Result<(), String> {
  10 |     #[cfg(target_os = "windows")]
  11 |     {
  12 |         use std::process::Command;
  13 |         Command::new("explorer")
  14 |             .arg("/select,")
  15 |             .arg(path)
  16 |             .spawn()
  17 |             .map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;
  18 |         Ok(())
  19 |     }
  20 |     #[cfg(not(target_os = "windows"))]
  21 |     {
  22 |         let path = std::path::PathBuf::from(path);
  23 |         if let Some(parent) = path.parent() {
  24 |             opener::reveal(parent).map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;
  25 |         }
  26 |         Ok(())
  27 |     }
  28 | }
  29 | 
  30 | pub async fn select_folder_internal() -> Result<Option<String>, String> {
  31 |     let handle = rfd::AsyncFileDialog::new()
  32 |         .set_title("Select Folder to Index")
  33 |         .pick_folder()
  34 |         .await;
  35 |     Ok(handle.map(|h| h.path().to_string_lossy().to_string()))
  36 | }
  37 | 
  38 | pub fn copy_to_clipboard_internal(text: String) -> Result<(), String> {
  39 |     use arboard::Clipboard;
  40 |     let mut clipboard = Clipboard::new().map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;
  41 |     clipboard.set_text(text).map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;
  42 |     Ok(())
  43 | }
  44 | 
  45 | pub async fn export_results_internal(
  46 |     results: Vec<SearchResult>,
  47 |     format: String,
  48 | ) -> Result<(), String> {
  49 |     let mut dialog = rfd::AsyncFileDialog::new()
  50 |         .set_title("Export Search Results")
  51 |         .set_file_name(format!("flash_search_results.{}", format));
  52 | 
  53 |     if format == "csv" {
  54 |         dialog = dialog.add_filter("CSV File", &["csv"]);
  55 |     } else if format == "json" {
  56 |         dialog = dialog.add_filter("JSON File", &["json"]);
  57 |     }
  58 | 
  59 |     if let Some(handle) = dialog.save_file().await {
  60 |         let path = handle.path().to_string_lossy().to_string();
  61 |         if format == "csv" {
  62 |             crate::commands::export_results_csv(&results, &path)?;
  63 |         } else if format == "json" {
  64 |             crate::commands::export_results_json(&results, &path)?;
  65 |         }
  66 |     }
  67 | 
  68 |     Ok(())
  69 | }
```

```rust
   1 | use std::path::PathBuf;
   2 | use thiserror::Error;
   3 | 
   4 | pub use anyhow::Context;
   5 | 
   6 | #[derive(Error, Debug)]
   7 | pub enum FlashError {
   8 |     #[error("IO error: {0}")]
   9 |     Io(std::io::Error),
  10 | 
  11 |     #[error("Parse error in {path}: {cause}")]
  12 |     Parse { path: PathBuf, cause: String },
  13 | 
  14 |     #[error("Index error: {msg}")]
  15 |     Index { msg: String, field: Option<String> },
  16 | 
  17 |     #[error("Database error: {operation} on {key}: {cause}")]
  18 |     Database {
  19 |         operation: String,
  20 |         key: String,
  21 |         cause: String,
  22 |     },
  23 | 
  24 |     #[error("Unsupported file format: {format}")]
  25 |     UnsupportedFormat { format: String, extension: String },
  26 | 
  27 |     #[error("File corrupted or encrypted: {path}")]
  28 |     CorruptedFile { path: PathBuf, operation: String },
  29 | 
  30 |     #[error("Search error: query '{query}' failed: {cause}")]
  31 |     Search { query: String, cause: String },
  32 | 
  33 |     #[error("Config error: {key}: {cause}")]
  34 |     Config { key: String, cause: String },
  35 | 
  36 |     #[error("Archive error: {archive_type} - {operation}: {cause}")]
  37 |     Archive {
  38 |         archive_type: String,
  39 |         operation: String,
  40 |         cause: String,
  41 |     },
  42 | 
  43 |     #[error("Lock poisoned: {lock_name}")]
  44 |     PoisonedLock { lock_name: String },
  45 | 
  46 |     #[error("Not found: {resource} '{identifier}'")]
  47 |     NotFound {
  48 |         resource: String,
  49 |         identifier: String,
  50 |     },
  51 |     #[error("{context}: {source}")]
  52 |     WithContext {
  53 |         context: String,
  54 |         source: Box<FlashError>,
  55 |     },
  56 | }
  57 | 
  58 | impl Clone for FlashError {
  59 |     fn clone(&self) -> Self {
  60 |         match self {
  61 |             Self::Io(e) => Self::Io(std::io::Error::new(e.kind(), e.to_string())),
  62 |             Self::Parse { path, cause } => Self::Parse {
  63 |                 path: path.clone(),
  64 |                 cause: cause.clone(),
  65 |             },
  66 |             Self::Index { msg, field } => Self::Index {
  67 |                 msg: msg.clone(),
  68 |                 field: field.clone(),
  69 |             },
  70 |             Self::Database {
  71 |                 operation,
  72 |                 key,
  73 |                 cause,
  74 |             } => Self::Database {
  75 |                 operation: operation.clone(),
  76 |                 key: key.clone(),
  77 |                 cause: cause.clone(),
  78 |             },
  79 |             Self::UnsupportedFormat { format, extension } => Self::UnsupportedFormat {
  80 |                 format: format.clone(),
  81 |                 extension: extension.clone(),
  82 |             },
  83 |             Self::CorruptedFile { path, operation } => Self::CorruptedFile {
  84 |                 path: path.clone(),
  85 |                 operation: operation.clone(),
  86 |             },
  87 |             Self::Search { query, cause } => Self::Search {
  88 |                 query: query.clone(),
  89 |                 cause: cause.clone(),
  90 |             },
  91 |             Self::Config { key, cause } => Self::Config {
  92 |                 key: key.clone(),
  93 |                 cause: cause.clone(),
  94 |             },
  95 |             Self::Archive {
  96 |                 archive_type,
  97 |                 operation,
  98 |                 cause,
  99 |             } => Self::Archive {
 100 |                 archive_type: archive_type.clone(),
 101 |                 operation: operation.clone(),
 102 |                 cause: cause.clone(),
 103 |             },
 104 |             Self::PoisonedLock { lock_name } => Self::PoisonedLock {
 105 |                 lock_name: lock_name.clone(),
 106 |             },
 107 |             Self::NotFound {
 108 |                 resource,
 109 |                 identifier,
 110 |             } => Self::NotFound {
 111 |                 resource: resource.clone(),
 112 |                 identifier: identifier.clone(),
 113 |             },
 114 |             Self::WithContext { context, source } => Self::WithContext {
 115 |                 context: context.clone(),
 116 |                 source: source.clone(),
 117 |             },
 118 |         }
 119 |     }
 120 | }
 121 | 
 122 | impl From<std::io::Error> for FlashError {
 123 |     fn from(e: std::io::Error) -> Self {
 124 |         FlashError::Io(e)
 125 |     }
 126 | }
 127 | 
 128 | pub trait Contextualize<T> {
 129 |     fn context(self, msg: &str) -> std::result::Result<T, FlashError>;
 130 | }
 131 | 
 132 | impl<T, E: Into<FlashError>> Contextualize<T> for std::result::Result<T, E> {
 133 |     fn context(self, msg: &str) -> std::result::Result<T, FlashError> {
 134 |         self.map_err(|e| FlashError::WithContext {
 135 |             context: msg.to_string(),
 136 |             source: Box::new(e.into()),
 137 |         })
 138 |     }
 139 | }
 140 | 
 141 | pub type Result<T> = std::result::Result<T, FlashError>;
 142 | 
 143 | // Helper constructors for common error patterns
 144 | impl FlashError {
 145 |     pub fn parse<P: Into<PathBuf>, S: Into<String>>(path: P, cause: S) -> Self {
 146 |         Self::Parse {
 147 |             path: path.into(),
 148 |             cause: cause.into(),
 149 |         }
 150 |     }
 151 | 
 152 |     pub fn index<S: Into<String>>(msg: S) -> Self {
 153 |         Self::Index {
 154 |             msg: msg.into(),
 155 |             field: None,
 156 |         }
 157 |     }
 158 | 
 159 |     pub fn index_field<S: Into<String>>(field: S, msg: S) -> Self {
 160 |         Self::Index {
 161 |             msg: msg.into(),
 162 |             field: Some(field.into()),
 163 |         }
 164 |     }
 165 | 
 166 |     pub fn database<S: Into<String>, S2: Into<String>>(operation: S, key: S, cause: S2) -> Self {
 167 |         Self::Database {
 168 |             operation: operation.into(),
 169 |             key: key.into(),
 170 |             cause: cause.into(),
 171 |         }
 172 |     }
 173 | 
 174 |     pub fn unsupported_format<S: Into<String>>(format: S, extension: S) -> Self {
 175 |         Self::UnsupportedFormat {
 176 |             format: format.into(),
 177 |             extension: extension.into(),
 178 |         }
 179 |     }
 180 | 
 181 |     pub fn corrupted_file<P: Into<PathBuf>, S: Into<String>>(path: P, operation: S) -> Self {
 182 |         Self::CorruptedFile {
 183 |             path: path.into(),
 184 |             operation: operation.into(),
 185 |         }
 186 |     }
 187 | 
 188 |     pub fn search<S1: Into<String>, S2: Into<String>>(query: S1, cause: S2) -> Self {
 189 |         Self::Search {
 190 |             query: query.into(),
 191 |             cause: cause.into(),
 192 |         }
 193 |     }
 194 | 
 195 |     pub fn config<S1: Into<String>, S2: Into<String>>(key: S1, cause: S2) -> Self {
 196 |         Self::Config {
 197 |             key: key.into(),
 198 |             cause: cause.into(),
 199 |         }
 200 |     }
 201 | 
 202 |     pub fn archive<S1: Into<String>, S2: Into<String>, S3: Into<String>>(
 203 |         archive_type: S1,
 204 |         operation: S2,
 205 |         cause: S3,
 206 |     ) -> Self {
 207 |         Self::Archive {
 208 |             archive_type: archive_type.into(),
 209 |             operation: operation.into(),
 210 |             cause: cause.into(),
 211 |         }
 212 |     }
 213 | 
 214 |     pub fn poisoned_lock<S: Into<String>>(lock_name: S) -> Self {
 215 |         Self::PoisonedLock {
 216 |             lock_name: lock_name.into(),
 217 |         }
 218 |     }
 219 | 
 220 |     pub fn not_found<S: Into<String>>(resource: S, identifier: S) -> Self {

 222 |             resource: resource.into(),
 223 |             identifier: identifier.into(),
 224 |         }
 225 |     }
 226 | }
```

```rust
   8 |     let csv_path = temp_dir.path().join("results.csv");
   9 | 
  10 |     let results = vec![
  11 |         SearchResult {
  12 |             file_path: "/path/to/file1.txt".to_string(),

  16 |             snippet: Some("content...".to_string()),
  17 |         },
  18 |         SearchResult {
  19 |             file_path: "/path/to/file2.txt".to_string(),
  20 |             title: Some("File 2".to_string()),
  21 |             score: 1.2,
  22 |             matched_terms: vec![],
  23 |             snippet: None,
  24 |         },
  25 |     ];
  26 | 
  27 |     crate::commands::export_results_csv(&results, csv_path.to_str().unwrap()).unwrap();
  28 | 
  29 |     let content = std::fs::read_to_string(csv_path).unwrap();
  30 |     assert!(content.contains("Score,File Path,Title"));
  31 |     assert!(content.contains("1.5,/path/to/file1.txt,File 1"));
  32 |     assert!(content.contains("1.2,/path/to/file2.txt,File 2"));
  33 | }
```

```rust
   1 | use iced::widget::{text, Text};
   2 | use iced::Element;
   3 | 
   4 | pub const FONT: iced::Font = iced::Font::with_name("lucide");
   5 | 
   6 | // Load the pre-built Lucide font from assets
   7 | pub const FONT_BYTES: &[u8] = include_bytes!("../../assets/lucide.ttf");
   8 | 
   9 | /// Icon name to Unicode character mapping for Lucide font
  10 | pub fn get_icon_char(name: &str) -> char {
  11 |     match name {
  12 |         "magnifying-glass" | "search" => '\u{e151}',
  13 |         "magnifying-glass-plus" => '\u{e1b6}',
  14 |         "magnifying-glass-minus" => '\u{e1b7}',
  15 |         "gear" | "settings" => '\u{e154}',
  16 |         "trash" => '\u{e18d}',
  17 |         "file" => '\u{e0c0}',
  18 |         "file-text" | "text" => '\u{e0cc}',
  19 |         "folder" => '\u{e0d7}',
  20 |         "folder-open" => '\u{e247}',
  21 |         "info" => '\u{e0f9}',
  22 |         "warning" => '\u{e193}',
  23 |         "check" => '\u{e06c}',
  24 |         "x" => '\u{e1b2}',
  25 |         "plus" => '\u{e13d}',
  26 |         "minus" => '\u{e11c}',
  27 |         "arrow-right" => '\u{e049}',
  28 |         "arrow-left" => '\u{e048}',
  29 |         "arrow-up" => '\u{e04a}',
  30 |         "arrow-down" => '\u{e042}',
  31 |         "download" => '\u{e0b2}',
  32 |         "copy" => '\u{e09e}',
  33 |         "database" => '\u{e0ad}',
  34 |         "star" => '\u{e176}',
  35 |         _ => {
  36 |             eprintln!("icon '{}' not found", name);
  37 |             '\u{003f}' // Question mark as fallback
  38 |         }
  39 |     }
  40 | }
  41 | 
  42 | /// Helper function to create an iced Text widget containing the given icon unicode.
  43 | pub fn icon<'a>(name: &str) -> Text<'a> {
  44 |     text(get_icon_char(name).to_string()).font(FONT)
  45 | }
  46 | 
  47 | /// For the old `load_icon` helper signature
  48 | pub fn load_icon<'a>(name: &str) -> Element<'a, super::Message> {
  49 |     icon(name).size(16).into()
  50 | }
```

```rust
 329 | 
 330 | fn highlight_text<'a>(content: &'a str, terms: &[String]) -> Element<'a, Message> {
 331 |     if terms.is_empty() || content.is_empty() {
 332 |         return text(content).size(14).into();
 333 |     }
 334 | 
 335 |     let lower_content = content.to_lowercase();
 336 |     let mut matches = Vec::new();
 337 | 
 338 |     for term in terms {
 339 |         if term.is_empty() {
 340 |             continue;
 341 |         }
 342 |         let lower_term = term.to_lowercase();
 343 |         let mut start = 0;
 344 |         while let Some(idx) = lower_content[start..].find(&lower_term) {
 345 |             let abs_idx = start + idx;
 346 |             matches.push((abs_idx, abs_idx + term.len()));
 347 |             start = abs_idx + term.len();
 348 |         }
 349 |     }
 350 | 
 351 |     if matches.is_empty() {
 352 |         return text(content).size(14).into();
 353 |     }
 354 | 
 355 |     matches.sort_by_key(|m| m.0);
 356 |     let mut merged: Vec<(usize, usize)> = Vec::new();
 357 |     for m in matches {
 358 |         if let Some(last) = merged.last_mut() {
 359 |             if m.0 <= last.1 {
 360 |                 last.1 = last.1.max(m.1);
 361 |                 continue;
 362 |             }
 363 |         }
 364 |         merged.push(m);
 365 |     }
 366 | 
 367 |     let mut spans: Vec<iced::widget::text::Span<'a, Message>> = Vec::new();
 368 |     let mut current = 0;
 369 | 
 370 |     for (start, end) in merged {
 371 |         if start > current {
 372 |             spans.push(span(&content[current..start]).size(14));
 373 |         }
 374 |         spans.push(
 375 |             span(&content[start..end])
 376 |                 .size(14)
 377 |                 .font(Font {
 378 |                     weight: font::Weight::Bold,
 379 |                     ..Font::default()
 380 |                 })
 381 |                 .color(iced::Color::from_rgb8(234, 179, 8)), // Highlight color (yellow)
 382 |         );
 383 |         current = end;
 384 |     }
 385 | 
 386 |     if current < content.len() {
 387 |         spans.push(span(&content[current..]).size(14));
 388 |     }
 389 | 
 390 |     rich_text(spans).into()
 391 | }
 392 | 
 393 | fn parse_snippet<'a>(content: &'a str) -> Element<'a, Message> {
 394 |     let mut spans: Vec<iced::widget::text::Span<'a, Message>> = Vec::new();
 395 |     let mut current_pos = 0;
 396 | 
 397 |     while let Some(start) = content[current_pos..].find("<b>") {
 398 |         let absolute_start = current_pos + start;
 399 | 
 400 |         if absolute_start > current_pos {
 401 |             spans.push(span(&content[current_pos..absolute_start]).size(12));
 402 |         }
 403 | 
 404 |         current_pos = absolute_start + 3; // length of <b>
 405 | 
 406 |         if let Some(end) = content[current_pos..].find("</b>") {
 407 |             let absolute_end = current_pos + end;
 408 |             spans.push(
 409 |                 span(&content[current_pos..absolute_end])
 410 |                     .size(12)
 411 |                     .font(Font {
 412 |                         weight: font::Weight::Bold,
 413 |                         ..Font::default()
 414 |                     })
 415 |                     .color(iced::Color::from_rgb8(234, 179, 8)),
 416 |             );
 417 |             current_pos = absolute_end + 4; // length of </b>
 418 |         } else {
 419 |             spans.push(span(&content[current_pos..]).size(12).font(Font {
 420 |                 weight: font::Weight::Bold,
 421 |                 ..Font::default()
 422 |             }));
 423 |             current_pos = content.len();
 424 |             break;
 425 |         }
 426 |     }
 427 | 
 428 |     if current_pos < content.len() {
 429 |         spans.push(span(&content[current_pos..]).size(12));
 430 |     }
 431 | 
 432 |     if spans.is_empty() {
 433 |         return text(content).size(12).into();
 434 |     }
 435 | 
 436 |     rich_text(spans).into()
 437 | }

 439 | fn right_panel(app: &App) -> Element<'_, Message> {
 440 |     let preview_tabs = container(
 441 |         row![
 442 |             button(text("Preview").size(12)).style(theme::nav_button(true)),
 443 |             Space::new().width(Length::Fill),
 444 |             load_icon("text"),
 445 |         ]
 446 |         .padding(Padding::new(8.0))
 447 |         .align_y(Alignment::Center),
 448 |     )
 449 |     .style(theme::table_header_container)
 450 |     .width(Length::Fill);
 451 | 
 452 |     let preview_content: Element<'_, Message> = if app.is_loading_preview {
 453 |         container(text("Loading preview...").style(theme::dim_text_style()))
 454 |             .center_x(Length::Fill)
 455 |             .center_y(Length::Fill)
 456 |             .into()
 457 |     } else if let Some(preview_result) = &app.preview_result {
 458 |         let highlighted_text =
 459 |             highlight_text(&preview_result.content, &preview_result.matched_terms);
 460 | 
 461 |         container(scrollable(
 462 |             container(highlighted_text).padding(Padding::new(20.0)),
 463 |         ))
 464 |         .into()
 465 |     } else {
 466 |         container(text("Select a file to preview").style(theme::dim_text_style()))
 467 |             .center_x(Length::Fill)
 468 |             .center_y(Length::Fill)
 469 |             .into()
 470 |     };
 471 | 
 472 |     container(column![
 473 |         preview_tabs,
 474 |         container(preview_content).height(Length::Fill),
 475 |         hits_panel(app),
 476 |     ])
 477 |     .width(Length::FillPortion(3))
 478 |     .height(Length::Fill)
 479 |     .into()
 480 | }
 481 | 
 482 | fn hits_panel(app: &App) -> Element<'_, Message> {
 483 |     let result = app.selected_index.and_then(|i| app.results.get(i));
 484 | 
 485 |     let hits_content: Element<'_, Message> = if let Some(res) = result {
 486 |         if res.snippets.is_empty() || res.snippets.iter().all(|s| s.is_empty()) {
 487 |             container(text("No preview context available").style(theme::muted_text_style()))
 488 |                 .width(Length::Fill)
 489 |                 .height(Length::Fill)
 490 |                 .center_x(Length::Fill)
 491 |                 .center_y(Length::Fill)
 492 |                 .into()
 493 |         } else {
 494 |             scrollable(
 495 |                 column(
 496 |                     res.snippets
 497 |                         .iter()
 498 |                         .enumerate()
 499 |                         .map(|(i, s)| hit_row(i + 1, s))
 500 |                         .collect::<Vec<_>>(),
 501 |                 )
 502 |                 .spacing(8)
 503 |                 .padding(8),
 504 |             )
 505 |             .height(Length::Fill)
 506 |             .into()
 507 |         }
 508 |     } else {
 509 |         container(text("Select a file to see context hits").style(theme::muted_text_style()))
 510 |             .width(Length::Fill)
 511 |             .height(Length::Fill)
 512 |             .center_x(Length::Fill)
 513 |             .center_y(Length::Fill)
 514 |             .into()
 515 |     };
 516 | 
 517 |     let header_text = if let Some(res) = result {
 518 |         format!(
 519 |             "Context Highlights for '{}' in {}",
 520 |             app.search_query, res.title
 521 |         )
 522 |     } else {
 523 |         "Search Hits".to_string()
 524 |     };
 525 | 
 526 |     container(column![
 527 |         container(
 528 |             row![
 529 |                 text(header_text).size(13).font(Font {
 530 |                     weight: font::Weight::Bold,
 531 |                     ..Font::default()
 532 |                 }),
 533 |                 Space::new().width(Length::Fill),
 534 |                 text(format!(
 535 |                     "{} total",
 536 |                     result.map(|r| r.snippets.len()).unwrap_or(0)
 537 |                 ))
 538 |                 .size(11)
 539 |                 .style(theme::muted_text_style()),
 540 |             ]
 541 |             .align_y(Alignment::Center)
 542 |             .padding(Padding::new(8.0))
 543 |         )
 544 |         .style(theme::header_container)
 545 |         .width(Length::Fill),
 546 |         hits_content,
 547 |     ])
 548 |     .style(theme::sidebar_container)
 549 |     .width(Length::Fill)
 550 |     .height(Length::Fixed(220.0))
 551 |     .into()
 552 | }
 553 | 
 554 | fn hit_row(_idx: usize, content: &str) -> Element<'_, Message> {
 555 |     container(
 556 |         row![
 557 |             text(format!("{}.", _idx))
 558 |                 .size(12)
 559 |                 .font(Font {
 560 |                     weight: font::Weight::Bold,
 561 |                     ..Font::default()
 562 |                 })
 563 |                 .style(theme::dim_text_style()),
 564 |             container(parse_snippet(content)).width(Length::Fill),
 565 |         ]
 566 |         .spacing(12)
 567 |         .align_y(Alignment::Start),
 568 |     )
 569 |     .padding(Padding::new(8.0))
 570 |     .style(theme::hit_highlight_container)
 571 |     .width(Length::Fill)
 572 |     .into()
 573 | }
 574 | 
 575 | fn status_bar(app: &App) -> Element<'_, Message> {
 576 |     let mut status_row = row![
 577 |         text(format!("{} files indexed", app.files_indexed)).size(11),
 578 |         Space::new().width(Length::Fixed(16.0)),
 579 |         text(&app.index_size).size(11),
 580 |         Space::new().width(Length::Fill),
 581 |     ];
 582 | 
 583 |     if let Some(p) = app.rebuild_progress {
 584 |         status_row = status_row
 585 |             .push(container(iced::widget::progress_bar(0.0..=1.0, p)).width(Length::Fixed(100.0)));
 586 |         status_row = status_row.push(Space::new().width(Length::Fixed(8.0)));
 587 |     }
 588 | 
 589 |     if let Some(status) = &app.rebuild_status {
 590 |         status_row = status_row.push(text(status).size(11));
 591 |     }
 592 | 
 593 |     container(status_row.padding(Padding {
 594 |         top: 4.0,
 595 |         bottom: 4.0,
 596 |         left: 16.0,
 597 |         right: 16.0,
 598 |     }))
 599 |     .style(theme::top_bar_container)
 600 |     .width(Length::Fill)
 601 |     .into()
 602 | }
 603 | 
 604 | fn extension_checkbox<'a>(ext: &'a str, app: &App) -> Element<'a, Message> {
 605 |     checkbox(app.filter_extensions.contains(ext))
 606 |         .label(ext)
 607 |         .on_toggle(move |_| Message::ToggleFilterExtension(ext.to_string()))
 608 |         .size(14)
 609 |         .text_size(11)
 610 |         .into()
 611 | }
 612 | 
 613 | fn size_unit_button<'a>(unit: &'a str, app: &App) -> Element<'a, Message> {
 614 |     let is_active = app.size_unit == unit;
 615 |     button(text(unit).size(10))
 616 |         .on_press(Message::SizeUnitChanged(unit.to_string()))
 617 |         .style(move |t: &iced::Theme, s| {
 618 |             if is_active {
 619 |                 theme::primary_button()(t, s)
 620 |             } else {
 621 |                 theme::secondary_button()(t, s)
 622 |             }
 623 |         })
 624 |         .padding(Padding::new(4.0))
 625 |         .into()
 626 | }
```

### File: `src\indexer\filename_index.rs`

- Size: 9586 bytes
- Modified: SystemTime { intervals: 134186262857983497 }

```rust
   1 | use crate::error::Result;
   2 | use compact_str::CompactString;
   3 | use fst::automaton::Subsequence;
   4 | use fst::{IntoStreamer, Streamer};
   5 | use parking_lot::RwLock;
   6 | use serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};
   7 | use std::path::Path;
   8 | use std::sync::Arc;
   9 | 
  10 | #[derive(
  11 |     Serialize, Deserialize, Debug, Clone, rkyv::Archive, rkyv::Serialize, rkyv::Deserialize,
  12 | )]
  13 | pub struct FilenameEntry {
  14 |     pub path: String,
  15 |     pub name: CompactString,
  16 | }
  17 | 
  18 | #[derive(Serialize, Deserialize, Debug, Clone)]
  19 | pub struct FilenameSearchResult {
  20 |     pub file_path: String,
  21 |     pub file_name: CompactString,
  22 | }
  23 | 
  24 | #[derive(Serialize, Deserialize, Debug, Clone)]
  25 | pub struct FilenameIndexStats {
  26 |     pub total_files: usize,
  27 |     pub index_size_bytes: u64,
  28 | }
  29 | 
  30 | /// File extension for the binary index file
  31 | const INDEX_FILENAME: &str = "filenames.bin";
  32 | /// Legacy JSON filename for migration
  33 | const LEGACY_INDEX_FILENAME: &str = "filenames.json";
  34 | 
  35 | pub struct FilenameIndex {
  36 |     entries: Arc<RwLock<Vec<FilenameEntry>>>,
  37 |     data_path: std::path::PathBuf,
  38 |     fst_map: Arc<RwLock<Arc<[u8]>>>,
  39 | }
  40 | 
  41 | impl FilenameIndex {
  42 |     pub fn open(data_path: &Path) -> Result<Self> {
  43 |         let data_path = data_path.to_path_buf();
  44 | 
  45 |         let entries = if data_path.exists() {
  46 |             // Try rkyv first, then fall back to legacy JSON
  47 |             let bin_path = data_path.join(INDEX_FILENAME);
  48 |             let json_path = data_path.join(LEGACY_INDEX_FILENAME);
  49 | 
  50 |             if bin_path.exists() {
  51 |                 match std::fs::read(&bin_path) {
  52 |                     Ok(bytes) => {
  53 |                         // Ensure byte alignment for rkyv
  54 |                         let mut aligned_bytes = rkyv::util::AlignedVec::<16>::new();
  55 |                         aligned_bytes.extend_from_slice(&bytes);
  56 | 
  57 |                         match rkyv::access::<rkyv::Archived<Vec<FilenameEntry>>, rkyv::rancor::Error>(
  58 |                             &aligned_bytes,
  59 |                         ) {
  60 |                             Ok(archived) => {
  61 |                                 let entries: Vec<FilenameEntry> =
  62 |                                     rkyv::deserialize::<Vec<FilenameEntry>, rkyv::rancor::Error>(
  63 |                                         archived,
  64 |                                     )
  65 |                                     .unwrap_or_default();
  66 |                                 tracing::info!(
  67 |                                     "Loaded {} filenames from rkyv index",
  68 |                                     entries.len()
  69 |                                 );
  70 |                                 entries
  71 |                             }
  72 |                             Err(e) => {
  73 |                                 tracing::warn!("Failed to parse rkyv filename index: {}", e);
  74 |                                 Vec::new()
  75 |                             }
  76 |                         }
  77 |                     }
  78 |                     Err(_) => Vec::new(),
  79 |                 }
  80 |             } else if json_path.exists() {
  81 |                 // Migrate from legacy JSON
  82 |                 match std::fs::read_to_string(&json_path) {
  83 |                     Ok(content) => match serde_json::from_str::<Vec<FilenameEntry>>(&content) {
  84 |                         Ok(entries) => {
  85 |                             tracing::info!(
  86 |                                 "Migrated {} filenames from legacy JSON index",
  87 |                                 entries.len()
  88 |                             );
  89 |                             // Save as rkyv immediately and remove JSON
  90 |                             Self::save_to_disk_sync(&entries, &data_path);
  91 |                             let _ = std::fs::remove_file(&json_path);
  92 |                             entries
  93 |                         }
  94 |                         Err(e) => {
  95 |                             tracing::warn!("Failed to parse legacy JSON filename index: {}", e);
  96 |                             Vec::new()
  97 |                         }
  98 |                     },
  99 |                     Err(_) => Vec::new(),
 100 |                 }
 101 |             } else {
 102 |                 Vec::new()
 103 |             }
 104 |         } else {
 105 |             Vec::new()
 106 |         };
 107 | 
 108 |         let fst_map = Arc::new(RwLock::new(Arc::from(Self::build_fst(&entries))));
 109 | 
 110 |         Ok(Self {
 111 |             entries: Arc::new(RwLock::new(entries)),
 112 |             data_path,
 113 |             fst_map,
 114 |         })
 115 |     }
 116 | 
 117 |     pub fn add_file(&self, path: &str, name: &str) -> Result<()> {
 118 |         let entry = FilenameEntry {
 119 |             path: path.to_string(),
 120 |             name: CompactString::from(name),
 121 |         };
 122 | 
 123 |         let entries = self.entries.clone();
 124 | 
 125 |         {
 126 |             let mut guard = entries.write();
 127 |             guard.push(entry);
 128 | 
 129 |             if guard.len() % 1000 == 0 {
 130 |                 let data = guard.clone();
 131 |                 let data_path = self.data_path.clone();
 132 |                 std::thread::spawn(move || {
 133 |                     Self::save_to_disk_sync(&data, &data_path);
 134 |                 });
 135 |             }
 136 |         }
 137 | 
 138 |         Ok(())
 139 |     }
 140 | 
 141 |     pub fn commit(&self) -> Result<()> {
 142 |         let entries = self.entries.clone();
 143 | 
 144 |         {
 145 |             let guard = entries.read();
 146 |             let data_path = self.data_path.clone();
 147 |             let data: Vec<_> = guard
 148 |                 .iter()
 149 |                 .map(|e| FilenameEntry {
 150 |                     path: e.path.clone(),
 151 |                     name: e.name.clone(),
 152 |                 })
 153 |                 .collect();
 154 | 
 155 |             {
 156 |                 let mut fst_guard = self.fst_map.write();
 157 |                 *fst_guard = Arc::from(Self::build_fst(&data));
 158 |             }
 159 | 
 160 |             std::thread::spawn(move || {
 161 |                 Self::save_to_disk_sync(&data, &data_path);
 162 |             });
 163 |         }
 164 | 
 165 |         Ok(())
 166 |     }
 167 | 
 168 |     fn build_fst(entries: &[FilenameEntry]) -> Vec<u8> {
 169 |         let mut items: Vec<(String, u64)> = entries
 170 |             .iter()
 171 |             .enumerate()
 172 |             .map(|(i, e)| (format!("{}\0{}", e.name.to_lowercase(), i), i as u64))
 173 |             .collect();
 174 |         items.sort_by(|a, b| a.0.cmp(&b.0));
 175 | 
 176 |         let mut build = fst::MapBuilder::memory();
 177 |         for (k, v) in items {
 178 |             let _ = build.insert(k, v);
 179 |         }
 180 |         build.into_inner().unwrap_or_default()
 181 |     }
 182 | 
 183 |     /// Save entries to disk using rkyv (consolidated from bincode)
 184 |     fn save_to_disk_sync(entries: &Vec<FilenameEntry>, data_path: &std::path::Path) {
 185 |         match rkyv::to_bytes::<rkyv::rancor::Error>(entries) {
 186 |             Ok(bytes) => {
 187 |                 let _ = std::fs::write(data_path.join(INDEX_FILENAME), bytes.as_slice());
 188 |             }
 189 |             Err(e) => {
 190 |                 tracing::warn!("Failed to serialize filename index: {}", e);
 191 |             }
 192 |         }
 193 |     }
 194 | 
 195 |     pub fn search(&self, query: &str, limit: usize) -> Result<Vec<FilenameSearchResult>> {
 196 |         let fst_guard = self.fst_map.read();
 197 |         if fst_guard.is_empty() {
 198 |             return Ok(Vec::new());
 199 |         }
 200 | 
 201 |         // FST Map - use reference borrow from the guard to avoid trait bound issues with Arc
 202 |         let map = match fst::Map::new(&**fst_guard) {
 203 |             Ok(m) => m,
 204 |             Err(_) => return Ok(Vec::new()),
 205 |         };
 206 | 
 207 |         // Fuzzy / Subsequence matching
 208 |         let query_lower = query.to_lowercase();
 209 |         let aut = Subsequence::new(&query_lower);
 210 | 
 211 |         let mut stream = map.search(aut).into_stream();
 212 | 
 213 |         let entries_lock = self.entries.read();
 214 | 
 215 |         let mut results = Vec::new();
 216 |         while let Some((_, v)) = stream.next() {
 217 |             if results.len() >= limit {
 218 |                 break;
 219 |             }
 220 |             if let Some(entry) = entries_lock.get(v as usize) {
 221 |                 results.push(FilenameSearchResult {
 222 |                     file_path: entry.path.clone(),
 223 |                     file_name: entry.name.clone(),
 224 |                 });
 225 |             }
 226 |         }
 227 | 
 228 |         Ok(results)
 229 |     }
 230 | 
 231 |     pub fn clear(&self) -> Result<()> {
 232 |         let entries = self.entries.clone();
 233 | 
 234 |         {
 235 |             let mut guard = entries.write();
 236 |             guard.clear();
 237 |             let data_path = self.data_path.clone();
 238 |             std::thread::spawn(move || {
 239 |                 let _ = std::fs::remove_file(data_path.join(INDEX_FILENAME));
 240 |                 let _ = std::fs::remove_file(data_path.join(LEGACY_INDEX_FILENAME));
 241 |             });
 242 |         }
 243 | 
 244 |         Ok(())
 245 |     }
 246 | 
 247 |     pub fn get_stats(&self) -> Result<FilenameIndexStats> {
 248 |         let entries = self.entries.clone();
 249 | 
 250 |         let entries = entries.read();
 251 | 
 252 |         let size: u64 = entries
 253 |             .iter()
 254 |             .map(|e| e.path.len() as u64 + e.name.len() as u64 + 32)
 255 |             .sum();
 256 | 
 257 |         Ok(FilenameIndexStats {
 258 |             total_files: entries.len(),
 259 |             index_size_bytes: size,
 260 |         })
 261 |     }
 262 | 
 263 |     pub fn rebuild_index(&self, paths: Vec<(String, String)>) -> Result<()> {
 264 |         let entries = self.entries.clone();
 265 |         let data_path = self.data_path.clone();
 266 | 
 267 |         {
 268 |             let mut guard = entries.write();
 269 |             *guard = paths
 270 |                 .into_iter()
 271 |                 .map(|(path, name)| FilenameEntry {
 272 |                     path,
 273 |                     name: CompactString::from(name),
 274 |                 })
 275 |                 .collect();
 276 | 
 277 |             let data: Vec<_> = guard
 278 |                 .iter()
 279 |                 .map(|e| FilenameEntry {
 280 |                     path: e.path.clone(),
 281 |                     name: e.name.clone(),
 282 |                 })
 283 |                 .collect();
 284 | 
 285 |             {
 286 |                 let mut fst_guard = self.fst_map.write();
 287 |                 *fst_guard = Arc::from(Self::build_fst(&data));
 288 |             }
 289 | 
 290 |             std::thread::spawn(move || {
 291 |                 Self::save_to_disk_sync(&data, &data_path);
 292 |             });
 293 |         }
 294 | 
 295 |         Ok(())
 296 |     }
 297 | }
```

```rust
   1 | use regex::Regex;
   2 | use std::sync::OnceLock;
   3 | 
   4 | static OPERATOR_REGEX: OnceLock<Regex> = OnceLock::new();
   5 | 
   6 | /// Parsed query with operators and search terms
   7 | #[derive(Debug, Clone)]
   8 | pub struct ParsedQuery {
   9 |     /// The original text query (for Tantivy)
  10 |     pub text_query: String,
  11 |     /// Extension filter (e.g., "pdf", "docx")
  12 |     pub extension: Option<String>,
  13 |     /// Path filter (search in specific path)
  14 |     pub path_filter: Option<String>,
  15 |     /// Title filter
  16 |     pub title_filter: Option<String>,
  17 |     /// Size filters
  18 |     pub min_size: Option<u64>,
  19 |     pub max_size: Option<u64>,
  20 |     /// Whether fuzzy matching is enabled
  21 |     pub fuzzy: bool,
  22 | }
  23 | 
  24 | impl ParsedQuery {
  25 |     pub fn new(query: &str) -> Self {
  26 |         Self::parse(query)
  27 |     }
  28 | 
  29 |     fn parse(input: &str) -> Self {
  30 |         let mut extension = None;
  31 |         let mut path_filter = None;
  32 |         let mut title_filter = None;
  33 |         let mut min_size = None;
  34 |         let mut max_size = None;
  35 |         let fuzzy = true;
  36 | 
  37 |         // Parse operators
  38 |         // ext:pdf, path:docs, title:report, size:>1MB, size:<10MB, exact:"phrase"
  39 |         let operator_regex = OPERATOR_REGEX.get_or_init(|| {
  40 |             Regex::new(
  41 |                 r#"(?i)(ext|path|title|size):(?:([<>]?)(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)(MB|KB|GB|B)?|"([^"]*)"|(\S+))"#,
  42 |             )
  43 |             .unwrap()
  44 |         });
  45 | 
  46 |         let mut remaining = input.to_string();
  47 | 
  48 |         // Process all operators
  49 |         for cap in operator_regex.captures_iter(input) {
  50 |             let operator = cap
  51 |                 .get(1)
  52 |                 .map(|m| m.as_str().to_lowercase())
  53 |                 .unwrap_or_default();
  54 |             let value = cap
  55 |                 .get(5)
  56 |                 .map(|m| m.as_str().to_string()) // Quoted value
  57 |                 .or_else(|| cap.get(6).map(|m| m.as_str().to_string())) // Unquoted value
  58 |                 .unwrap_or_default();
  59 | 
  60 |             match operator.as_str() {
  61 |                 "ext" => {
  62 |                     extension = Some(value.trim_start_matches('.').to_lowercase());
  63 |                     if let Some(m) = cap.get(0) {
  64 |                         remaining = remaining.replace(m.as_str(), "");
  65 |                     }
  66 |                 }
  67 |                 "path" => {
  68 |                     path_filter = Some(value.to_lowercase());
  69 |                     if let Some(m) = cap.get(0) {
  70 |                         remaining = remaining.replace(m.as_str(), "");
  71 |                     }
  72 |                 }
  73 |                 "title" => {
  74 |                     title_filter = Some(value.to_lowercase());
  75 |                     if let Some(m) = cap.get(0) {
  76 |                         remaining = remaining.replace(m.as_str(), "");
  77 |                     }
  78 |                 }
  79 |                 "size" => {
  80 |                     // Handle size operators
  81 |                     if let Some(op) = cap.get(2) {
  82 |                         let op = op.as_str();
  83 |                         if let Some(num_str) = cap.get(3) {
  84 |                             if let Ok(num) = num_str.as_str().parse::<f64>() {
  85 |                                 let multiplier = cap
  86 |                                     .get(4)
  87 |                                     .map(|m| match m.as_str().to_uppercase().as_str() {
  88 |                                         "GB" => 1024 * 1024 * 1024,
  89 |                                         "MB" => 1024 * 1024,
  90 |                                         "KB" => 1024,
  91 |                                         _ => 1,
  92 |                                     })
  93 |                                     .unwrap_or(1);
  94 | 
  95 |                                 let bytes = (num * multiplier as f64) as u64;
  96 |                                 match op {
  97 |                                     ">" => min_size = Some(bytes),
  98 |                                     "<" => max_size = Some(bytes),
  99 |                                     _ => {}
 100 |                                 }
 101 |                             }
 102 |                         }
 103 |                     } else if let Ok(size_val) = value.parse::<u64>() {
 104 |                         // Exact size match (treat as minimum for practical purposes)
 105 |                         min_size = Some(size_val);
 106 |                         max_size = Some(size_val + 1);
 107 |                     }
 108 |                     if let Some(m) = cap.get(0) {
 109 |                         remaining = remaining.replace(m.as_str(), "");
 110 |                     }
 111 |                 }
 112 |                 _ => {}
 113 |             }
 114 |         }
 115 | 
 116 |         // Clean up remaining text for full-text search
 117 |         let text_query = remaining
 118 |             .split_whitespace()
 119 |             .collect::<Vec<_>>()
 120 |             .join(" ")
 121 |             .trim()
 122 |             .to_string();
 123 | 
 124 |         Self {
 125 |             text_query: if text_query.is_empty() {
 126 |                 "*".to_string()
 127 |             } else {
 128 |                 text_query
 129 |             },
 130 |             extension,
 131 |             path_filter,
 132 |             title_filter,
 133 |             min_size,
 134 |             max_size,
 135 |             fuzzy,
 136 |         }
 137 |     }
 138 | 
 139 |     /// Check if a path matches the extension filter
 140 |     pub fn matches_extension(&self, path: &str) -> bool {
 141 |         if let Some(ref ext) = self.extension {
 142 |             let path_lower = path.to_lowercase();
 143 |             path_lower.ends_with(&format!(".{}", ext))
 144 |         } else {
 145 |             true
 146 |         }
 147 |     }
 148 | 
 149 |     /// Check if a path matches the path filter
 150 |     pub fn matches_path(&self, path: &str) -> bool {
 151 |         if let Some(ref filter) = self.path_filter {
 152 |             path.to_lowercase().contains(filter)
 153 |         } else {
 154 |             true
 155 |         }
 156 |     }
 157 | 
 158 |     /// Check if a title matches the title filter
 159 |     pub fn matches_title(&self, title: Option<&str>) -> bool {
 160 |         if let Some(ref filter) = self.title_filter {
 161 |             if let Some(t) = title {
 162 |                 t.to_lowercase().contains(filter)
 163 |             } else {
 164 |                 false
 165 |             }
 166 |         } else {
 167 |             true
 168 |         }
 169 |     }
 170 | }
 171 | 
 172 | /// Extract search terms for highlighting from a query
 173 | pub fn extract_highlight_terms(query: &str) -> Vec<String> {
 174 |     let parsed = ParsedQuery::new(query);
 175 | 
 176 |     let mut terms: Vec<String> = parsed
 177 |         .text_query
 178 |         .split_whitespace()
 179 |         .filter(|t| *t != "*")
 180 |         .map(|t| t.to_lowercase())
 181 |         .collect();
 182 | 
 183 |     if terms.is_empty() && parsed.text_query == "*" {
 184 |         terms.push("*".to_string());
 185 |     }
 186 | 
 187 |     // Also add title filter terms
 188 |     if let Some(title) = parsed.title_filter {
 189 |         terms.push(title);
 190 |     }
 191 | 
 192 |     terms
 193 | }
```

```rust
   1 | use tantivy::schema::*;
   2 | 
   3 | /// Create Tantivy schema optimized for file search
   4 | pub fn create_schema() -> Schema {
   5 |     let mut schema_builder = Schema::builder();
   6 | 
   7 |     // File path - stored for retrieval, indexed for exact matches
   8 |     schema_builder.add_text_field("file_path", STRING | STORED);
   9 | 
  10 |     // Content - indexed for search AND stored for fast preview retrieval
  11 |     // Storing content allows fast previews without re-parsing files
  12 |     let text_options = TextOptions::default().set_indexing_options(
  13 |         TextFieldIndexing::default()
  14 |             .set_tokenizer("default")
  15 |             .set_index_option(IndexRecordOption::WithFreqsAndPositions),
  16 |     );
  17 |     schema_builder.add_text_field("content", text_options);
  18 | 
  19 |     // Title - stored for display, indexed for search
  20 |     schema_builder.add_text_field("title", TEXT | STORED);
  21 | 
  22 |     // Modified timestamp - indexed for sorting
  23 |     schema_builder.add_date_field("modified", FAST | INDEXED);
  24 | 
  25 |     // File size - indexed for range queries
  26 |     schema_builder.add_u64_field("size", FAST | INDEXED);
  27 | 
  28 |     // File extension - indexed as keyword for fast filtering
  29 |     schema_builder.add_text_field("extension", STRING | STORED);
  30 | 
  31 |     schema_builder.build()
  32 | }
```

```rust
  67 | impl QueryCache {

  69 |         Self {
  70 |             cache: Cache::builder()

  72 |                 .time_to_live(Duration::from_secs(CACHE_TTL_SECS))
  73 |                 .build(),
  74 |         }

  77 |     pub(crate) fn get(&self, key: &CacheKey) -> Option<Vec<SearchResult>> {
  78 |         self.cache.get(key).map(|cached| cached.results)

 102 | /// Manages searching the Tantivy index
 103 | pub struct IndexSearcher {
 104 |     reader: IndexReader,
 105 |     query_parser: QueryParser,
 106 |     path_field: Field,
 107 |     title_field: Field,
 108 |     size_field: Field,
```
