```rust
 114 | 
 115 | impl IndexSearcher {
 116 |     pub fn new(index: &Index, index_path: std::path::PathBuf) -> Result<Self> {
 117 |         let schema = index.schema();
 118 | 
 119 |         // Pre-warm the reader by loading index into memory on startup
 120 |         // This ensures first search is fast (no initial load latency)
 121 |         let reader = index
 122 |             .reader_builder()
 123 |             .reload_policy(ReloadPolicy::OnCommitWithDelay)
 124 |             .try_into()
 125 |             .map_err(|e| FlashError::search("create_index_reader", e.to_string()))?;
 126 | 
 127 |         // Pre-warm: load the index reader
 128 |         if let Err(e) = reader.reload() {
 129 |             tracing::warn!("Failed to pre-warm index reader: {}", e);
 130 |         }
 131 | 
 132 |         // Get field references once to avoid repeated lookups
 133 |         let path_field = schema
 134 |             .get_field("file_path")
 135 |             .map_err(|_| FlashError::index_field("file_path", "Field not found in schema"))?;
 136 |         let title_field = schema
 137 |             .get_field("title")
 138 |             .map_err(|_| FlashError::index_field("title", "Field not found in schema"))?;
 139 |         let size_field = schema
 140 |             .get_field("size")
 141 |             .map_err(|_| FlashError::index_field("size", "Field not found in schema"))?;
 142 |         let content_field = schema
 143 |             .get_field("content")
 144 |             .map_err(|_| FlashError::index_field("content", "Field not found in schema"))?;
 145 |         let extension_field = schema
 146 |             .get_field("extension")
 147 |             .map_err(|_| FlashError::index_field("extension", "Field not found in schema"))?;
 148 | 
 149 |         // Search across content, title, and file_path fields
 150 |         let default_fields: Vec<Field> = ["content", "title", "file_path"]
 151 |             .iter()
 152 |             .filter_map(|field_name| schema.get_field(field_name).ok())
 153 |             .collect();
 154 | 
 155 |         let mut query_parser = QueryParser::for_index(index, default_fields);
 156 |         query_parser.set_conjunction_by_default();
 157 | 
 158 |         Ok(Self {
 159 |             reader,
 160 |             query_parser,
 161 |             path_field,
 162 |             title_field,
 163 |             size_field,
 164 |             content_field,
 165 |             extension_field,
 166 |             cache: QueryCache::new(),
 167 |             index_path,
 168 |         })
 169 |     }
 170 | 
 171 |     /// Search the index and return top results with optional filters
 172 |     pub async fn search(
 173 |         self: &std::sync::Arc<Self>,
 174 |         query: &str,
 175 |         limit: usize,
 176 |         min_size: Option<u64>,
 177 |         max_size: Option<u64>,
 178 |         file_extensions: Option<&[String]>,
 179 |     ) -> Result<Vec<SearchResult>> {
 180 |         let query_owned = query.to_string();
 181 |         let extensions_owned = file_extensions.map(|e| e.to_vec());
 182 |         // Arc::clone is O(1) — no heap allocation, just an atomic refcount bump
 183 |         let this = std::sync::Arc::clone(self);
 184 | 
 185 |         tokio::task::spawn_blocking(move || {
 186 |             this.search_sync(
 187 |                 &query_owned,
 188 |                 limit,
 189 |                 min_size,
 190 |                 max_size,
 191 |                 extensions_owned.as_deref(),
 192 |             )
 193 |         })
 194 |         .await
 195 |         .map_err(|e| FlashError::search(query, format!("Search task failed: {}", e)))?
 196 |     }
 197 | 
 198 |     /// Synchronous search implementation
 199 |     pub fn search_sync(
 200 |         &self,
 201 |         query: &str,
 202 |         limit: usize,
 203 |         min_size: Option<u64>,
 204 |         max_size: Option<u64>,
 205 |         file_extensions: Option<&[String]>,
 206 |     ) -> Result<Vec<SearchResult>> {
 207 |         use super::query_parser::{extract_highlight_terms, ParsedQuery};
 208 | 
 209 |         // Create cache key
 210 |         let cache_key = CacheKey {
 211 |             query: query.to_string(),
 212 |             limit,
 213 |             min_size,
 214 |             max_size,
 215 |             extensions: file_extensions.map(|e| e.to_vec()),
 216 |         };
 217 | 
 218 |         // Check cache first
 219 |         if let Some(cached) = self.cache.get(&cache_key) {
 220 |             return Ok(cached);
 221 |         }
 222 | 
 223 |         let parsed = ParsedQuery::new(query);
 224 |         let highlight_terms = extract_highlight_terms(query);
 225 | 
 226 |         let searcher = self.reader.searcher();
 227 | 
 228 |         // Helper to run query with all filters
 229 |         #[allow(clippy::type_complexity)]
 230 |         let run_query = |text_query: Box<dyn tantivy::query::Query>| -> Result<(
 231 |             Box<dyn tantivy::query::Query>,
 232 |             Vec<(f32, tantivy::DocAddress)>,
 233 |         )> {
 234 |             let mut combine: Vec<(Occur, Box<dyn tantivy::query::Query>)> =
 235 |                 vec![(Occur::Must, text_query)];
 236 | 
 237 |             if min_size.is_some() || max_size.is_some() {
 238 |                 let lower = Term::from_field_u64(self.size_field, min_size.unwrap_or(0));
 239 |                 let upper = Term::from_field_u64(self.size_field, max_size.unwrap_or(u64::MAX));
 240 |                 let range = RangeQuery::new(Bound::Included(lower), Bound::Included(upper));
 241 |                 combine.push((Occur::Must, Box::new(range)));
 242 |             }
 243 | 
 244 |             if let Some(extensions) = file_extensions {
 245 |                 if !extensions.is_empty() {
 246 |                     let extension_queries: Vec<_> = extensions
 247 |                         .iter()
 248 |                         .map(|ext| {
 249 |                             let ext_lower = ext.to_lowercase();
 250 |                             let term =
 251 |                                 tantivy::Term::from_field_text(self.extension_field, &ext_lower);
 252 |                             tantivy::query::TermQuery::new(term, IndexRecordOption::Basic)
 253 |                         })
 254 |                         .collect();
 255 | 
 256 |                     if !extension_queries.is_empty() {
 257 |                         let extension_bool_query = tantivy::query::BooleanQuery::new(
 258 |                             extension_queries
 259 |                                 .into_iter()
 260 |                                 .map(|q| {
 261 |                                     (Occur::Should, Box::new(q) as Box<dyn tantivy::query::Query>)
 262 |                                 })
 263 |                                 .collect(),
 264 |                         );
 265 |                         combine.push((Occur::Must, Box::new(extension_bool_query)));
 266 |                     }
 267 |                 }
 268 |             }
 269 | 
 270 |             let final_query: Box<dyn tantivy::query::Query> = if combine.len() == 1 {
 271 |                 combine.remove(0).1
 272 |             } else {
 273 |                 Box::new(BooleanQuery::new(combine))
 274 |             };
 275 | 
 276 |             let top_docs = searcher
 277 |                 .search(&*final_query, &TopDocs::with_limit(limit))
 278 |                 .map_err(|e| FlashError::search(query, e.to_string()))?;
 279 | 
 280 |             Ok((final_query, top_docs))
 281 |         };
 282 | 
 283 |         // TIER 1: Exact search
 284 |         let exact_query = self
 285 |             .query_parser
 286 |             .parse_query(&parsed.text_query)
 287 |             .unwrap_or_else(|_| Box::new(tantivy::query::AllQuery));
 288 |         let (mut final_query, mut top_docs) = run_query(exact_query)?;
 289 | 
 290 |         // TIER 2: Fuzzy Fallback
 291 |         static PHRASE_REGEX: std::sync::OnceLock<regex::Regex> = std::sync::OnceLock::new();
 292 |         let phrase_regex = PHRASE_REGEX.get_or_init(|| regex::Regex::new(r#""([^"]+)""#).unwrap());
 293 | 
 294 |         if top_docs.len() < limit
 295 |             && !phrase_regex.is_match(&parsed.text_query)
 296 |             && !parsed.text_query.trim().is_empty()
 297 |         {
 298 |             let fuzzy_query = self.build_fuzzy_query(&parsed.text_query)?;
 299 |             let (fuzzy_final_query, fuzzy_docs) = run_query(fuzzy_query)?;
 300 | 
 301 |             // Prefer highlighting based on the more permissive fuzzy query
 302 |             final_query = fuzzy_final_query;
 303 | 
 304 |             let seen: std::collections::HashSet<tantivy::DocAddress> =
 305 |                 top_docs.iter().map(|(_, addr)| *addr).collect();
 306 | 
 307 |             // Use itertools to chain and filter unique documents
 308 |             top_docs = top_docs
 309 |                 .into_iter()
 310 |                 .chain(
 311 |                     fuzzy_docs
 312 |                         .into_iter()
 313 |                         .filter(|(_, addr)| !seen.contains(addr)),
 314 |                 )
 315 |                 .take(limit)
 316 |                 .sorted_by(|a, b| b.0.partial_cmp(&a.0).unwrap_or(std::cmp::Ordering::Equal))
 317 |                 .collect();
 318 |         }
 319 | 
 320 |         let mut results = Vec::with_capacity(top_docs.len().min(limit));
 321 | 
 322 |         // Create snippet generator once outside the loop
 323 |         let snippet_generator =
 324 |             SnippetGenerator::create(&searcher, &*final_query, self.content_field)?;
 325 | 
 326 |         for (score, doc_address) in top_docs {
 327 |             let retrieved_doc: TantivyDocument = searcher.doc(doc_address).map_err(|e| {
 328 |                 FlashError::search(query, format!("Failed to retrieve document: {}", e))
 329 |             })?;
 330 | 
 331 |             let file_path = retrieved_doc
 332 |                 .get_first(self.path_field)
 333 |                 .and_then(|f| f.as_str())
 334 |                 .map(|s: &str| s.to_string())
 335 |                 .unwrap_or_default();
 336 | 
 337 |             let title = retrieved_doc
 338 |                 .get_first(self.title_field)
 339 |                 .and_then(|f| f.as_str())
 340 |                 .map(|s: &str| CompactString::from(s));
 341 | 
 342 | 
 343 |             let extension = retrieved_doc
 344 |                 .get_first(self.extension_field)
 345 |                 .and_then(|f| f.as_str())
 346 |                 .map(|s: &str| CompactString::from(s));
 347 | 
 348 | 
 349 |             // Get fast fields for size and modified
 350 |             let size = searcher
 351 |                 .segment_reader(doc_address.segment_ord)
 352 |                 .fast_fields()
 353 |                 .u64("size")
 354 |                 .ok()
 355 |                 .map(|f| f.values.get_val(doc_address.doc_id));
 356 | 
 357 |             let modified = searcher
 358 |                 .segment_reader(doc_address.segment_ord)
 359 |                 .fast_fields()
 360 |                 .date("modified")
 361 |                 .ok()
 362 |                 .map(|f| {
 363 |                     let date = f.values.get_val(doc_address.doc_id);
 364 |                     date.into_timestamp_secs() as u64
 365 |                 });
 366 | 
 367 |             // Generates snippets and replaces HTML tags.
 368 |             // NOTE: Offloading full rendering to UI.
 369 |             let snippet = snippet_generator.snippet_from_doc(&retrieved_doc);
 370 |             let snippet_text = snippet
 371 |                 .to_html()
 372 |                 .replace("<b>", "")
 373 |                 .replace("</b>", "")
 374 |                 .replace("&lt;", "<")
 375 |                 .replace("&gt;", ">")
 376 |                 .replace("&amp;", "&");
 377 | 
 378 |             let snippets = if snippet_text.is_empty() {
 379 |                 vec![]
 380 |             } else {
 381 |                 vec![snippet_text]
 382 |             };
 383 | 
 384 |             results.push(
 385 |                 SearchResult::builder()
 386 |                     .file_path(file_path)
 387 |                     .maybe_title(title)
 388 |                     .score(score)
 389 |                     .maybe_modified(modified)
 390 |                     .maybe_size(size)
 391 |                     .maybe_extension(extension)
 392 |                     .matched_terms(highlight_terms.clone())
 393 |                     .snippets(snippets)
 394 |                     .build(),
 395 |             );
 396 | 
 397 |             if results.len() >= limit {
 398 |                 break;
 399 |             }
 400 |         }
 401 | 
 402 |         // Cache the results
 403 |         self.cache.insert(cache_key, results.clone());
 404 | 
 405 |         Ok(results)
 406 |     }
 407 | 
 408 |     /// Build a fuzzy query for better typo tolerance
 409 |     fn build_fuzzy_query(&self, text_query: &str) -> Result<Box<dyn tantivy::query::Query>> {
 410 |         // Check if it's a phrase query (contains quoted strings)
 411 |         static PHRASE_REGEX: OnceLock<regex::Regex> = OnceLock::new();
 412 |         let phrase_regex = PHRASE_REGEX.get_or_init(|| regex::Regex::new(r#""([^"]+)""#).unwrap());
 413 | 
 414 |         if phrase_regex.is_match(text_query) {
 415 |             // For phrase queries, use the query parser with phrase support
 416 |             return Ok(Box::new(
 417 |                 self.query_parser
 418 |                     .parse_query(text_query)
 419 |                     .map_err(|e| FlashError::search(text_query, e.to_string()))?,
 420 |             ));
 421 |         }
 422 | 
 423 |         // For regular queries, build a fuzzy query with OR for each term
 424 |         let terms: Vec<&str> = text_query.split_whitespace().collect();
 425 | 
 426 |         if terms.is_empty() || (terms.len() == 1 && terms[0] == "*") {
 427 |             // Match all
 428 |             return Ok(Box::new(tantivy::query::AllQuery));
 429 |         }
 430 | 
 431 |         if terms.len() == 1 {
 432 |             // Single term - try exact first, then fuzzy across all relevant fields
 433 |             let term_text = terms[0];
 434 |             let mut subqueries: Vec<(Occur, Box<dyn tantivy::query::Query>)> = Vec::new();
 435 | 
 436 |             for field in [self.content_field, self.title_field, self.path_field] {
 437 |                 let term = Term::from_field_text(field, term_text);
 438 |                 let exact = tantivy::query::TermQuery::new(
 439 |                     term.clone(),
 440 |                     tantivy::schema::IndexRecordOption::Basic,
 441 |                 );
 442 |                 let fuzzy = FuzzyTermQuery::new(term, 2, true);
 443 |                 subqueries.push((Occur::Should, Box::new(exact)));
 444 |                 subqueries.push((Occur::Should, Box::new(fuzzy)));
 445 |             }
 446 | 
 447 |             Ok(Box::new(BooleanQuery::new(subqueries)))
 448 |         } else {
 449 |             // Multiple terms - build fuzzy query for each with AND logic
 450 |             let mut and_subqueries: Vec<(Occur, Box<dyn tantivy::query::Query>)> = Vec::new();
 451 | 
 452 |             for term_text in terms {
 453 |                 let mut term_subqueries: Vec<(Occur, Box<dyn tantivy::query::Query>)> = Vec::new();
 454 |                 for field in [self.content_field, self.title_field, self.path_field] {
 455 |                     let term = Term::from_field_text(field, term_text);
 456 |                     let exact = tantivy::query::TermQuery::new(
 457 |                         term.clone(),
 458 |                         tantivy::schema::IndexRecordOption::Basic,
 459 |                     );
 460 |                     let fuzzy = FuzzyTermQuery::new(term, 2, true);
 461 |                     term_subqueries.push((Occur::Should, Box::new(exact)));
 462 |                     term_subqueries.push((Occur::Should, Box::new(fuzzy)));
 463 |                 }
 464 |                 and_subqueries.push((Occur::Must, Box::new(BooleanQuery::new(term_subqueries))));
 465 |             }
 466 | 
 467 |             Ok(Box::new(BooleanQuery::new(and_subqueries)))
 468 |         }
 469 |     }
 470 | 
 471 |     /// Invalidate the search cache (call after index updates)
 472 |     pub fn invalidate_cache(&self) {
 473 |         self.cache.invalidate();
 474 |     }
 475 | 
 476 |     /// Get recent files using Tantivy's fast fields
 477 |     pub fn get_recent_files(&self, limit: usize) -> Result<Vec<SearchResult>> {
 478 |         let searcher = self.reader.searcher();
 479 |         let top_docs = searcher
 480 |             .search(
 481 |                 &tantivy::query::AllQuery,
 482 |                 &TopDocs::with_limit(limit)
 483 |                     .order_by_fast_field::<u64>("modified", tantivy::Order::Desc),
 484 |             )
 485 |             .map_err(|e| FlashError::search("recent files", e.to_string()))?;
 486 | 
 487 |         let mut results = Vec::with_capacity(top_docs.len().min(limit));
 488 | 
 489 |         for (_date, doc_address) in top_docs {
 490 |             let retrieved_doc: TantivyDocument = searcher.doc(doc_address).map_err(|e| {
 491 |                 FlashError::search(
 492 |                     "recent files",
 493 |                     format!("Failed to retrieve document: {}", e),
 494 |                 )
 495 |             })?;
 496 | 
 497 |             let file_path = retrieved_doc
 498 |                 .get_first(self.path_field)
 499 |                 .and_then(|f| f.as_str())
 500 |                 .map(|s: &str| s.to_string())
 501 |                 .unwrap_or_default();
 502 | 
 503 |             let title = retrieved_doc
 504 |                 .get_first(self.title_field)
 505 |                 .and_then(|f| f.as_str())
 506 |                 .map(|s: &str| CompactString::from(s));
 507 | 
 508 | 
 509 |             let extension = retrieved_doc
 510 |                 .get_first(self.extension_field)
 511 |                 .and_then(|f| f.as_str())
 512 |                 .map(|s: &str| CompactString::from(s));
 513 | 
 514 | 
 515 |             // Get fast fields for size and modified
 516 |             let size = searcher
 517 |                 .segment_reader(doc_address.segment_ord)
 518 |                 .fast_fields()
 519 |                 .u64("size")
 520 |                 .ok()
 521 |                 .map(|f| f.values.get_val(doc_address.doc_id));
 522 | 
 523 |             let modified = searcher
 524 |                 .segment_reader(doc_address.segment_ord)
 525 |                 .fast_fields()
 526 |                 .date("modified")
 527 |                 .ok()
 528 |                 .map(|f| {
 529 |                     let date = f.values.get_val(doc_address.doc_id);
 530 |                     date.into_timestamp_secs() as u64
 531 |                 });
 532 | 
 533 |             results.push(
 534 |                 SearchResult::builder()
 535 |                     .file_path(file_path)
 536 |                     .maybe_title(title)
 537 |                     .score(1.0)
 538 |                     .maybe_modified(modified)
 539 |                     .maybe_size(size)
 540 |                     .maybe_extension(extension)
 541 |                     .matched_terms(vec![])
 542 |                     .snippets(vec![])
 543 |                     .build(),
 544 |             );
 545 |         }
 546 | 
 547 |         // Reverse because order_by_fast_field might sort ascending? We'll test it.
 548 |         // Actually Tantivy sorts in ascending order by default.
 549 |         results.reverse();
 550 | 
 551 |         Ok(results)
 552 |     }
 553 | 
 554 |     /// Get statistics about the index
 555 |     pub fn get_statistics(&self) -> Result<IndexStatistics> {
 556 |         let searcher = self.reader.searcher();
 557 |         let total_docs = searcher.num_docs() as usize;
 558 | 
 559 |         let mut total_size = 0;
 560 |         if let Ok(entries) = std::fs::read_dir(&self.index_path) {
 561 |             for entry in entries.flatten() {
 562 |                 if let Ok(metadata) = entry.metadata() {
 563 |                     if metadata.is_file() {
 564 |                         total_size += metadata.len();
 565 |                     }
 566 |                 }
 567 |             }
 568 |         }
 569 | 
 570 |         Ok(IndexStatistics {
 571 |             total_documents: total_docs,
 572 |             total_size_bytes: total_size,
 573 |             last_updated: Some(jiff::Zoned::now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S").to_string()),
 574 |         })
 575 |     }
 576 | }

 583 |     fn test_cache_key_equality() {
 584 |         let key1 = CacheKey {
 585 |             query: "test".to_string(),
 586 |             limit: 10,
 587 |             min_size: None,
 588 |             max_size: None,
 589 |             extensions: None,
 590 |         };
 591 |         let key2 = CacheKey {
 592 |             query: "test".to_string(),
 593 |             limit: 10,
 594 |             min_size: None,
 595 |             max_size: None,
 596 |             extensions: None,
 597 |         };
 598 |         assert_eq!(key1, key2);
 599 | 
 600 |         let key3 = CacheKey {
 601 |             query: "diff".to_string(),
 602 |             ..key1.clone()
 603 |         };
 604 |         assert_ne!(key1, key3);
 605 |     }

 610 |         let key = CacheKey {
 611 |             query: "test".to_string(),
 612 |             limit: 10,
 613 |             min_size: None,
 614 |             max_size: None,
 615 |             extensions: None,
 616 |         };
 617 |         let results = vec![SearchResult::builder()
 618 |             .file_path("path".to_string())
 619 |             .score(1.0)
 620 |             .matched_terms(vec!["test".to_string()])
 621 |             .snippets(vec!["snippet".to_string()])
 622 |             .build()];
 623 |         cache.insert(key.clone(), results.clone());
 624 |         let cached = cache.get(&key);
 625 |         assert!(cached.is_some());
 626 |         assert_eq!(cached.unwrap().len(), 1);
```

```rust
   1 | use crate::error::{FlashError, Result};
   2 | use crate::parsers::ParsedDocument;
   3 | use parking_lot::Mutex;
   4 | use tantivy::schema::{Field, Schema};
   5 | use tantivy::{Index, IndexWriter, TantivyDocument};
   6 | use tracing::info;
   7 | 
   8 | /// Manages writing documents to the Tantivy index with batch support
   9 | pub struct IndexWriterManager {
  10 |     writer: Mutex<IndexWriter>,
  11 |     #[allow(dead_code)]
  12 |     schema: Schema,
  13 |     path_field: Field,
  14 |     content_field: Field,
  15 |     title_field: Field,
  16 |     modified_field: Field,
  17 |     size_field: Field,
  18 |     extension_field: Field,
  19 | }
  20 | 
  21 | impl IndexWriterManager {
  22 |     /// Calculate optimal heap size based on system resources
  23 |     /// Returns heap size in bytes (min 32MB, max 256MB)
  24 |     fn calculate_heap_size() -> usize {
  25 |         // Get system memory info (using sysinfo crate would be better, but this is lightweight)
  26 |         let available_memory = std::env::var("FLASH_SEARCH_MEMORY_MB")
  27 |             .ok()
  28 |             .and_then(|s| s.parse::<usize>().ok())
  29 |             .map(|mb| mb * 1_000_000)
  30 |             .unwrap_or_else(|| {
  31 |                 // Default calculation: use 5% of system memory, capped at 256MB
  32 |                 // This is a heuristic - in production, use sysinfo to get actual memory
  33 |                 let mut sys = sysinfo::System::new_with_specifics(
  34 |                     sysinfo::RefreshKind::nothing()
  35 |                         .with_memory(sysinfo::MemoryRefreshKind::everything()),
  36 |                 );
  37 |                 sys.refresh_memory();
  38 |                 let system_memory = sys.total_memory() as usize;
  39 | 
  40 |                 (system_memory / 20).clamp(32_000_000, 256_000_000)
  41 |             });
  42 | 
  43 |         available_memory.clamp(32_000_000, 256_000_000)
  44 |     }
  45 | 
  46 |     pub fn new(index: &Index, _memory_limit_mb: u32) -> Result<Self> {
  47 |         let schema = index.schema();
  48 | 
  49 |         // Configure with adaptive heap size based on system resources
  50 |         let heap_size = Self::calculate_heap_size();
  51 |         info!(
  52 |             "Tantivy index writer heap size: {} MB",
  53 |             heap_size / 1_000_000
  54 |         );
  55 | 
  56 |         let writer = index
  57 |             .writer(heap_size)
  58 |             .map_err(|e| FlashError::index(format!("Failed to create index writer: {}", e)))?;
  59 | 
  60 |         let path_field = schema
  61 |             .get_field("file_path")
  62 |             .map_err(|_| FlashError::index_field("file_path", "Field not found in schema"))?;
  63 |         let content_field = schema
  64 |             .get_field("content")
  65 |             .map_err(|_| FlashError::index_field("content", "Field not found in schema"))?;
  66 |         let title_field = schema
  67 |             .get_field("title")
  68 |             .map_err(|_| FlashError::index_field("title", "Field not found in schema"))?;
  69 |         let modified_field = schema
  70 |             .get_field("modified")
  71 |             .map_err(|_| FlashError::index_field("modified", "Field not found in schema"))?;
  72 |         let size_field = schema
  73 |             .get_field("size")
  74 |             .map_err(|_| FlashError::index_field("size", "Field not found in schema"))?;
  75 |         let extension_field = schema
  76 |             .get_field("extension")
  77 |             .map_err(|_| FlashError::index_field("extension", "Field not found in schema"))?;
  78 | 
  79 |         Ok(Self {
  80 |             writer: Mutex::new(writer),
  81 |             schema,
  82 |             path_field,
  83 |             content_field,
  84 |             title_field,
  85 |             modified_field,
  86 |             size_field,
  87 |             extension_field,
  88 |         })
  89 |     }
  90 | 
  91 |     /// Add a single document to the index
  92 |     /// Note: For better performance, use add_documents_batch for multiple docs
  93 |     pub fn add_document(&self, doc: &ParsedDocument, modified: u64, size: u64) -> Result<()> {
  94 |         let tantivy_doc = self.create_tantivy_document(doc, modified, size);
  95 | 
  96 |         #[allow(unused_mut)]
  97 |         let mut writer = self.writer.lock();
  98 | 
  99 |         writer
 100 |             .add_document(tantivy_doc)
 101 |             .map_err(|e| FlashError::index(format!("Failed to add document: {}", e)))?;
 102 | 
 103 |         Ok(())
 104 |     }
 105 | 
 106 |     /// Add multiple documents in a single lock acquisition (much more efficient)
 107 |     pub fn add_documents_batch(&self, docs: &[(ParsedDocument, u64, u64)]) -> Result<()> {
 108 |         if docs.is_empty() {
 109 |             return Ok(());
 110 |         }
 111 | 
 112 |         #[allow(unused_mut)]
 113 |         let mut writer = self.writer.lock();
 114 | 
 115 |         for (doc, modified, size) in docs {
 116 |             let tantivy_doc = self.create_tantivy_document(doc, *modified, *size);
 117 |             writer
 118 |                 .add_document(tantivy_doc)
 119 |                 .map_err(|e| FlashError::index(format!("Failed to add document: {}", e)))?;
 120 |         }
 121 | 
 122 |         Ok(())
 123 |     }
 124 | 
 125 |     /// Create a Tantivy document from ParsedDocument
 126 |     #[inline]
 127 |     fn create_tantivy_document(
 128 |         &self,
 129 |         doc: &ParsedDocument,
 130 |         modified: u64,
 131 |         size: u64,
 132 |     ) -> TantivyDocument {
 133 |         let mut document = TantivyDocument::default();
 134 | 
 135 |         document.add_text(self.path_field, &doc.path);
 136 |         document.add_text(self.content_field, &doc.content);
 137 | 
 138 |         if let Some(ref title) = doc.title {
 139 |             document.add_text(self.title_field, title);
 140 |         }
 141 | 
 142 |         let modified_date = tantivy::DateTime::from_timestamp_secs(modified as i64);
 143 |         document.add_date(self.modified_field, modified_date);
 144 |         document.add_u64(self.size_field, size);
 145 | 
 146 |         // Index file extension for fast filtering
 147 |         if let Some(ext) = std::path::Path::new(&doc.path)
 148 |             .extension()
 149 |             .and_then(|e| e.to_str())
 150 |         {
 151 |             document.add_text(self.extension_field, ext.to_lowercase());
 152 |         }
 153 | 
 154 |         document
 155 |     }
 156 | 
 157 |     /// Remove a document from the index
 158 |     pub fn remove_document(&self, path: &str) -> Result<()> {
 159 |         #[allow(unused_mut)]
 160 |         let mut writer = self.writer.lock();
 161 | 
 162 |         let term = tantivy::Term::from_field_text(self.path_field, path);
 163 |         writer.delete_term(term);
 164 | 
 165 |         Ok(())
 166 |     }
 167 | 
 168 |     /// Delete all documents from the index
 169 |     pub fn delete_all_documents(&self) -> Result<()> {
 170 |         #[allow(unused_mut)]
 171 |         let mut writer = self.writer.lock();
 172 | 
 173 |         writer
 174 |             .delete_all_documents()
 175 |             .map_err(|e| FlashError::index(format!("Failed to delete all documents: {}", e)))?;
 176 | 
 177 |         Ok(())
 178 |     }
 179 | 
 180 |     /// Commit pending changes to disk
 181 |     pub fn commit(&self) -> Result<()> {
 182 |         #[allow(unused_mut)]
 183 |         let mut writer = self.writer.lock();
 184 | 
 185 |         writer
 186 |             .commit()
 187 |             .map_err(|e| FlashError::index(format!("Failed to commit index: {}", e)))?;
 188 | 
 189 |         Ok(())
 190 |     }
 191 | }
```

```rust
  62 |     pub fn open(db_path: &Path) -> Result<Self> {
  63 |         let db = match Database::create(db_path) {
  64 |             Ok(db) => Arc::new(db),
  65 |             Err(e) => {
  66 |                 tracing::warn!("Failed to open metadata database: {}. Forcing reset...", e);
  67 |                 let _ = std::fs::remove_file(db_path);
  68 |                 Arc::new(Database::create(db_path).map_err(|e| {
  69 |                     FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
  70 |                 })?)
  71 |             }
  72 |         };
  73 | 
  74 |         // Create table if it doesn't exist
  75 |         // Wrap this in a closure to easily catch errors and retry
  76 |         let init_table = |db: &Database| -> Result<()> {
  77 |             let txn = db.begin_write().map_err(|e| {
  78 |                 FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())

  85 |             txn.commit().map_err(|e| {
  86 |                 FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
  87 |             })
  88 |         };
  89 | 
  90 |         if let Err(e) = init_table(&db) {
  91 |             tracing::warn!(
  92 |                 "Failed to initialize database tables: {}. Wiping and recreating...",
  93 |                 e
  94 |             );
  95 |             drop(db); // Ensure file is not locked
  96 |             let _ = std::fs::remove_file(db_path);

  99 |                 FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())

 105 |                     "files_table",
 106 |                     format!("Retry failed: {}", e),
 107 |                 )
 108 |             })?;
 109 | 
 110 |             return Ok(Self {
 111 |                 db,
 112 |                 metrics: Arc::new(ConnectionMetrics::default()),
 113 |             });
 114 |         }

 117 |             db,
 118 |             metrics: Arc::new(ConnectionMetrics::default()),

 140 |     /// Check if file needs reindexing based on modification time and hash
 141 |     pub fn needs_reindex(&self, path: &Path, modified: u64, size: u64) -> Result<bool> {
 142 |         let txn = self.db.begin_read().map_err(|e| {
 143 |             FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
 144 |         })?;
 145 | 
 146 |         let table = txn.open_table(FILES_TABLE).map_err(|e| {
 147 |             FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
 148 |         })?;
 149 | 
 150 |         let path_str = path.to_str().unwrap_or("");
 151 | 
 152 |         let result = match table
 153 |             .get(path_str)
 154 |             .map_err(|e| FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string()))?
 155 |         {
 156 |             Some(metadata) => {
 157 |                 let bytes = metadata.value();
 158 |                 self.metrics.read_operations.fetch_add(1, Ordering::Relaxed);
 159 |                 self.metrics
 160 |                     .bytes_read
 161 |                     .fetch_add(bytes.len() as u64, Ordering::Relaxed);
 162 |                 // Zero-copy read and validate with byte alignment
 163 |                 let mut aligned_bytes = rkyv::util::AlignedVec::<16>::new();
 164 |                 aligned_bytes.extend_from_slice(bytes);
 165 | 
 166 |                 if let Ok(meta) = rkyv::access::<rkyv::Archived<FileMetadata>, rkyv::rancor::Error>(
 167 |                     &aligned_bytes,
 168 |                 ) {
 169 |                     meta.modified != modified || meta.size != size
 170 |                 } else {
 171 |                     true // Reindex if validation fails
 172 |                 }
 173 |             }
 174 |             None => true, // File not indexed yet
 175 |         };
 176 | 
 177 |         Ok(result)
 178 |     }

 265 |             })?;

 268 |             // Safer to just open it again to ensure it exists empty.

 311 |     /// Batch update metadata for multiple files (much more efficient)
 312 |     /// Updates all files in a single transaction to minimize I/O overhead
 313 |     pub fn batch_update_metadata(
 314 |         &self,
 315 |         entries: &[(String, u64, u64, [u8; 32])], // (path, modified, size, hash)
 316 |     ) -> Result<usize> {
 317 |         if entries.is_empty() {
 318 |             return Ok(0);
 319 |         }
 320 | 
 321 |         let txn = self.db.begin_write().map_err(|e| {
 322 |             FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
 323 |         })?;
 324 | 
 325 |         let indexed_at = SystemTime::now()
 326 |             .duration_since(SystemTime::UNIX_EPOCH)
 327 |             .unwrap_or_default()
 328 |             .as_secs();
 329 | 
 330 |         let mut total_bytes_written = 0u64;
 331 | 
 332 |         {
 333 |             let mut table = txn.open_table(FILES_TABLE).map_err(|e| {
 334 |                 FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
 335 |             })?;
 336 | 
 337 |             for (path, modified, size, content_hash) in entries {
 338 |                 let metadata = FileMetadata {
 339 |                     path: path.clone(),
 340 |                     modified: *modified,
 341 |                     size: *size,
 342 |                     content_hash: *content_hash,
 343 |                     indexed_at,
 344 |                 };
 345 | 
 346 |                 let bytes = rkyv::to_bytes::<rkyv::rancor::Error>(&metadata).map_err(|e| {
 347 |                     FlashError::database(
 348 |                         "database_operation",
 349 |                         "files_table",
 350 |                         format!("Serialization error: {}", e),
 351 |                     )
 352 |                 })?;
 353 | 
 354 |                 total_bytes_written += bytes.len() as u64;
 355 |                 total_bytes_written += path.len() as u64;
 356 | 
 357 |                 table.insert(path.as_str(), bytes.as_slice()).map_err(|e| {
 358 |                     FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
 359 |                 })?;
 360 |             }
 361 |         }
 362 | 
 363 |         txn.commit().map_err(|e| {
 364 |             FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
 365 |         })?;
 366 | 
 367 |         // Update metrics
 368 |         self.metrics
 369 |             .write_operations
 370 |             .fetch_add(1, Ordering::Relaxed);
 371 |         self.metrics
 372 |             .bytes_written
 373 |             .fetch_add(total_bytes_written, Ordering::Relaxed);
 374 | 
 375 |         Ok(entries.len())
 376 |     }
 377 | 
 378 |     /// Batch check which files need reindexing
 379 |     /// Returns a vector of booleans indicating if each file needs reindexing
 380 |     pub fn batch_needs_reindex(
 381 |         &self,
 382 |         entries: &[(String, u64, u64)], // (path, modified, size)
 383 |     ) -> Result<Vec<bool>> {
 384 |         if entries.is_empty() {
 385 |             return Ok(vec![]);
 386 |         }
 387 | 
 388 |         let txn = self.db.begin_read().map_err(|e| {
 389 |             FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
 390 |         })?;
 391 | 
 392 |         let table = txn.open_table(FILES_TABLE).map_err(|e| {
 393 |             FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
 394 |         })?;
 395 | 
 396 |         let results: Vec<bool> = entries
 397 |             .iter()
 398 |             .map(|(path, modified, size)| {
 399 |                 match table.get(path.as_str()) {
 400 |                     Ok(Some(metadata)) => {
 401 |                         let bytes = metadata.value();
 402 |                         if let Ok(meta) =
 403 |                             rkyv::access::<rkyv::Archived<FileMetadata>, rkyv::rancor::Error>(bytes)
 404 |                         {
 405 |                             meta.modified != *modified || meta.size != *size
 406 |                         } else {
 407 |                             true
 408 |                         }
 409 |                     }
 410 |                     Ok(None) => true, // File not indexed yet
 411 |                     Err(e) => {
 412 |                         // Log error but assume safe to reindex rather than silently reindexing
 413 |                         tracing::warn!("Error reading metadata for '{}': {}", path, e);
 414 |                         true
 415 |                     }
 416 |                 }
 417 |             })
 418 |             .collect();
 419 | 
 420 |         Ok(results)
 421 |     }
 422 | 
 423 |     /// Get recently modified files sorted by modification time
 424 |     /// Uses a bounded min-heap to avoid loading all files into memory.
 425 |     pub fn get_recent_files(&self, limit: usize) -> Result<Vec<RecentFileEntry>> {
 426 |         let txn = self.db.begin_read().map_err(|e| {
 427 |             FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
 428 |         })?;
 429 | 
 430 |         let table = txn.open_table(FILES_TABLE).map_err(|e| {
 431 |             FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
 432 |         })?;
 433 | 
 434 |         // Use a min-heap to keep the top `limit` most recent files.
 435 |         // We store (modified, path, size) and the heap is ordered by modified (smallest at top).
 436 |         use std::collections::BinaryHeap;
 437 |         // We define a wrapper struct to have a min-heap based on modified time.
 438 |         // Since BinaryHeap is a max-heap, we invert the order by using Reverse.
 439 |         let mut heap: BinaryHeap<Reverse<(u64, String, u64)>> = BinaryHeap::new();
 440 | 
 441 |         for entry in table
 442 |             .iter()
 443 |             .map_err(|e| FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string()))?
 444 |         {
 445 |             let (k, v) = entry.map_err(|e| {
 446 |                 FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
 447 |             })?;
 448 |             let bytes = v.value();
 449 |             let modified = if let Ok(meta) =
 450 |                 rkyv::access::<rkyv::Archived<FileMetadata>, rkyv::rancor::Error>(bytes)
 451 |             {
 452 |                 meta.modified.to_native()
 453 |             } else {
 454 |                 0
 455 |             };
 456 |             let path = k.value().to_string();
 457 |             let size = if let Ok(meta) =
 458 |                 rkyv::access::<rkyv::Archived<FileMetadata>, rkyv::rancor::Error>(bytes)
 459 |             {
 460 |                 meta.size.to_native()
 461 |             } else {
 462 |                 0
 463 |             };
 464 | 
 465 |             // Push the entry into the heap
 466 |             heap.push(Reverse((modified, path, size)));
 467 | 
 468 |             // If heap exceeds limit, remove the least recent (smallest modified)
 469 |             if heap.len() > limit {
 470 |                 heap.pop();
 471 |             }
 472 |         }
 473 | 
 474 |         // Extract the files from the heap.
 475 |         // They are in arbitrary order (heap order). We want them sorted by modified descending.
 476 |         let mut files: Vec<(String, u64, u64)> = heap
 477 |             .into_iter()
 478 |             .map(|Reverse(tuple)| {
 479 |                 let (modified, path, size) = tuple;
 480 |                 (path, modified, size)
 481 |             })
 482 |             .collect();
 483 | 
 484 |         // Sort by modified descending
 485 |         files.sort_by(|a, b| b.1.cmp(&a.1));
 486 | 
 487 |         // Convert to the expected format (without titles for now, can be enhanced)
 488 |         Ok(files
 489 |             .into_iter()
 490 |             .map(|(path, modified, size)| (path, None, modified, size))
 491 |             .collect())
 492 |     }
 493 | }
```

### File: `src\parsers\memory_map.rs`

- Size: 2073 bytes
- Modified: SystemTime { intervals: 134168914525145568 }

```rust
   1 | use crate::error::{FlashError, Result};
   2 | use memmap2::Mmap;
   3 | use std::fs::File;
   4 | use std::io::Read;
   5 | use std::path::Path;
   6 | 
   7 | const MMAP_THRESHOLD: u64 = 1024 * 1024; // 1MB
   8 | const MAX_FILE_SIZE: u64 = 100 * 1024 * 1024; // 100MB
   9 | 
  10 | pub fn read_file(path: &Path) -> Result<Vec<u8>> {
  11 |     let metadata = std::fs::metadata(path).map_err(FlashError::Io)?;
  12 | 
  13 |     let file_size = metadata.len();
  14 | 
  15 |     if file_size > MAX_FILE_SIZE {
  16 |         return Err(FlashError::parse(
  17 |             path,
  18 |             format!(
  19 |                 "File too large: {} bytes (max: {})",
  20 |                 file_size, MAX_FILE_SIZE
  21 |             ),
  22 |         ));
  23 |     }
  24 | 
  25 |     if file_size > MMAP_THRESHOLD {
  26 |         read_with_mmap(path)
  27 |     } else {
  28 |         read_with_buffer(path)
  29 |     }
  30 | }
  31 | 
  32 | pub fn read_file_as_string(path: &Path) -> Result<String> {
  33 |     let bytes = read_file(path)?;
  34 |     String::from_utf8(bytes).map_err(|e| FlashError::parse(path, format!("Invalid UTF-8: {}", e)))
  35 | }
  36 | 
  37 | fn read_with_buffer(path: &Path) -> Result<Vec<u8>> {
  38 |     let mut file = File::open(path).map_err(FlashError::Io)?;
  39 |     let mut bytes = Vec::new();
  40 |     file.read_to_end(&mut bytes).map_err(FlashError::Io)?;
  41 |     Ok(bytes)
  42 | }
  43 | 
  44 | fn read_with_mmap(path: &Path) -> Result<Vec<u8>> {
  45 |     let file = File::open(path)
  46 |         .map_err(|e| FlashError::parse(path, format!("Failed to open file: {}", e)))?;
  47 | 
  48 |     // SAFETY: Memory mapping a file is unsafe because another process could modify it
  49 |     // while we are reading, potentially violating Rust's memory safety guarantees.
  50 |     // For a local desktop search engine, this risk is acceptable and typically results
  51 |     // in a process crash rather than an exploitable vulnerability.
  52 |     let mmap = unsafe { Mmap::map(&file).map_err(|e| FlashError::Io(std::io::Error::other(e)))? };
  53 | 
  54 |     Ok(mmap.to_vec())
  55 | }
  56 | 
  57 | pub fn is_mmap_applicable(path: &Path) -> bool {
  58 |     std::fs::metadata(path)
  59 |         .map(|m| m.len() > MMAP_THRESHOLD)
  60 |         .unwrap_or(false)
  61 | }
  62 | 
  63 | pub fn get_file_size(path: &Path) -> Result<u64> {
  64 |     std::fs::metadata(path)
  65 |         .map(|m| m.len())
  66 |         .map_err(FlashError::Io)
  67 | }
```

```rust
   1 | #[cfg(target_os = "windows")]
   2 | mod windows_usn {
   3 |     use crate::error::{FlashError, Result};
   4 |     use crate::scanner::{ProgressEvent, ProgressType};
   5 |     use compact_str::CompactString;
   6 |     use smallvec::SmallVec;

  14 |     use windows::Win32::Storage::FileSystem::{

  17 |     };
  18 |     use windows::Win32::System::Ioctl::{
  19 |         FSCTL_ENUM_USN_DATA, FSCTL_QUERY_USN_JOURNAL, FSCTL_READ_USN_JOURNAL, MFT_ENUM_DATA_V0,
  20 |         READ_USN_JOURNAL_DATA_V0, USN_JOURNAL_DATA_V0, USN_RECORD_V2,
  21 |     };
  22 |     use windows::Win32::System::IO::DeviceIoControl;
  23 | 
  24 |     #[derive(Debug)]
  25 |     struct DirInfo {
  26 |         name: CompactString,
  27 |         parent_frn: u64,
  28 |     }
  29 | 
  30 |     pub fn scan_volume(
  31 |         root: &Path,
  32 |         path_tx: crossbeam_channel::Sender<PathBuf>,
  33 |         progress_tx: Option<mpsc::Sender<ProgressEvent>>,
  34 |         total_count: Arc<AtomicUsize>,
  35 |     ) -> Result<()> {
  36 |         let drive_letter = root.to_string_lossy();
  37 |         let volume_path = format!("\\\\.\\{}", &drive_letter[..2]);
  38 |         let mut volume_wide: Vec<u16> = volume_path.encode_utf16().collect();
  39 |         volume_wide.push(0);
  40 | 
  41 |         unsafe {
  42 |             let handle = CreateFileW(
  43 |                 windows::core::PCWSTR(volume_wide.as_ptr()),
  44 |                 GENERIC_READ.0,
  45 |                 FILE_SHARE_READ | FILE_SHARE_WRITE,
  46 |                 None,
  47 |                 OPEN_EXISTING,
  48 |                 FILE_FLAG_BACKUP_SEMANTICS,
  49 |                 None,
  50 |             )
  51 |             .map_err(|e| FlashError::index(format!("Failed to open volume handle: {}", e)))?;
  52 | 
  53 |             let result = iterate_mft(
  54 |                 handle,
  55 |                 &drive_letter[..3],
  56 |                 path_tx,
  57 |                 progress_tx,
  58 |                 total_count,
  59 |             );
  60 |             let _ = CloseHandle(handle);
  61 |             result
  62 |         }
  63 |     }
  64 | 
  65 |     unsafe fn iterate_mft(
  66 |         handle: HANDLE,
  67 |         drive_root: &str,
  68 |         path_tx: crossbeam_channel::Sender<PathBuf>,
  69 |         progress_tx: Option<mpsc::Sender<ProgressEvent>>,
  70 |         total_count: Arc<AtomicUsize>,
  71 |     ) -> Result<()> {
  72 |         let mut journal_data = USN_JOURNAL_DATA_V0::default();
  73 |         let mut bytes_returned = 0u32;
  74 | 
  75 |         DeviceIoControl(
  76 |             handle,
  77 |             FSCTL_QUERY_USN_JOURNAL,
  78 |             None,
  79 |             0,
  80 |             Some(&mut journal_data as *mut _ as *mut _),
  81 |             std::mem::size_of::<USN_JOURNAL_DATA_V0>() as u32,
  82 |             Some(&mut bytes_returned),
  83 |             None,
  84 |         )
  85 |         .map_err(|e| FlashError::index(format!("Query USN Journal failed: {}", e)))?;
  86 | 
  87 |         let mut mft_enum_data = MFT_ENUM_DATA_V0 {
  88 |             StartFileReferenceNumber: 0,
  89 |             LowUsn: 0,
  90 |             HighUsn: journal_data.NextUsn,
  91 |         };
  92 | 
  93 |         let mut dir_map: HashMap<u64, DirInfo> = HashMap::with_capacity(100_000);
  94 |         let mut files: Vec<(CompactString, u64)> = Vec::with_capacity(500_000);
  95 |         let mut buffer = [0u8; 65536];
  96 | 
  97 |         info!("Enumerating MFT records...");
  98 | 
  99 |         loop {
 100 |             let mut bytes_returned = 0u32;
 101 |             let success = DeviceIoControl(
 102 |                 handle,
 103 |                 FSCTL_ENUM_USN_DATA,
 104 |                 Some(&mft_enum_data as *const _ as *const _),
 105 |                 std::mem::size_of::<MFT_ENUM_DATA_V0>() as u32,
 106 |                 Some(buffer.as_mut_ptr() as *mut _),
 107 |                 buffer.len() as u32,
 108 |                 Some(&mut bytes_returned),
 109 |                 None,
 110 |             );
 111 | 
 112 |             if success.is_err() || bytes_returned < 8 {
 113 |                 break;
 114 |             }
 115 | 
 116 |             let next_usn = *(buffer.as_ptr() as *const i64);
 117 |             mft_enum_data.StartFileReferenceNumber = next_usn as u64;
 118 | 
 119 |             let mut offset = 8;
 120 |             while offset < bytes_returned as usize {
 121 |                 let record = &*(buffer.as_ptr().add(offset) as *const USN_RECORD_V2);
 122 | 
 123 |                 // Skip system files to clean up the output and increase performance
 124 |                 if (record.FileAttributes & FILE_ATTRIBUTE_SYSTEM.0) == 0 {
 125 |                     let name_ptr =
 126 |                         buffer.as_ptr().add(offset + record.FileNameOffset as usize) as *const u16;
 127 |                     let name_len = (record.FileNameLength / 2) as usize;
 128 |                     let name = CompactString::from_utf16_lossy(std::slice::from_raw_parts(
 129 |                         name_ptr, name_len,
 130 |                     ));
 131 | 
 132 |                     let frn = record.FileReferenceNumber;
 133 |                     let parent_frn = record.ParentFileReferenceNumber;
 134 |                     let is_dir = (record.FileAttributes & 0x00000010) != 0; // FILE_ATTRIBUTE_DIRECTORY
 135 | 
 136 |                     if is_dir {
 137 |                         dir_map.insert(frn, DirInfo { name, parent_frn });
 138 |                     } else {
 139 |                         files.push((name, parent_frn));
 140 |                     }
 141 |                 }
 142 | 
 143 |                 offset += record.RecordLength as usize;
 144 |             }
 145 |         }
 146 | 
 147 |         info!(
 148 |             "MFT Enumeration finished. Reconstructing paths for {} files...",
 149 |             files.len()
 150 |         );
 151 | 
 152 |         let mut count = 0;
 153 | 
 154 |         for (name, mut current_parent) in files {
 155 |             let mut path_parts: SmallVec<[&str; 16]> = SmallVec::new();
 156 |             path_parts.push(name.as_str());
 157 | 
 158 |             let mut depth = 0;
 159 |             let mut valid_path = true;
 160 | 
 161 |             // Trace back to root. In NTFS, root's parent is itself. FRN 5 is typically root.
 162 |             while depth < 50 {
 163 |                 if let Some(parent_info) = dir_map.get(&current_parent) {
 164 |                     path_parts.push(parent_info.name.as_str());
 165 |                     if current_parent == parent_info.parent_frn {
 166 |                         break; // Reached root
 167 |                     }
 168 |                     current_parent = parent_info.parent_frn;
 169 |                     depth += 1;
 170 |                 } else {
 171 |                     // Parent not found, orphaned or root not in map
 172 |                     valid_path = false;
 173 |                     break;
 174 |                 }
 175 |             }
 176 | 
 177 |             if valid_path {
 178 |                 let mut full_path = PathBuf::from(drive_root);
 179 |                 for part in path_parts.iter().rev() {
 180 |                     // Skip if it's the drive root name itself being reported
 181 |                     if !part.is_empty() && !part.contains(':') {
 182 |                         full_path.push(part);
 183 |                     }
 184 |                 }
 185 | 
 186 |                 let _ = path_tx.send(full_path.clone());
 187 |                 count += 1;
 188 | 
 189 |                 if count % 2000 == 0 {
 190 |                     total_count.store(count, Ordering::Relaxed);
 191 |                     if let Some(tx) = &progress_tx {
 192 |                         let _ = tx.try_send(ProgressEvent {
 193 |                             ptype: ProgressType::Filename,
 194 |                             current_file: name.to_string(),
 195 |                             current_folder: "".to_string(),
 196 |                             processed: count,
 197 |                             total: 0,
 198 |                             status: format!("Reconstructing MFT: {} files", count),
 199 |                             eta_seconds: 0,
 200 |                             files_per_second: 0.0,
 201 |                         });
 202 |                     }
 203 |                 }
 204 |             }
 205 |         }
 206 | 
 207 |         total_count.store(count, Ordering::Relaxed);
 208 |         Ok(())
 209 |     }

 211 |     pub fn watch_volume(
 212 |         root: &Path,
 213 |         tx: tokio::sync::mpsc::Sender<(PathBuf, crate::watcher::WatcherAction)>,
 214 |     ) -> Result<()> {
 215 |         let drive_letter = root.to_string_lossy();
 216 |         let volume_path = format!("\\\\.\\{}", &drive_letter[..2]);
 217 |         let mut volume_wide: Vec<u16> = volume_path.encode_utf16().collect();
 218 |         volume_wide.push(0);
 219 | 
 220 |         let drive_root_str = drive_letter[..3].to_string();
 221 | 
 222 |         std::thread::spawn(move || {
 223 |             unsafe {
 224 |                 let handle = CreateFileW(
 225 |                     windows::core::PCWSTR(volume_wide.as_ptr()),
 226 |                     GENERIC_READ.0,
 227 |                     FILE_SHARE_READ | FILE_SHARE_WRITE,
 228 |                     None,
 229 |                     OPEN_EXISTING,
 230 |                     FILE_FLAG_BACKUP_SEMANTICS,
 231 |                     None,
 232 |                 )
 233 |                 .unwrap_or(HANDLE(std::ptr::null_mut()));
 234 | 
 235 |                 if handle == HANDLE(std::ptr::null_mut()) {
 236 |                     error!("Failed to open handle for USN monitoring.");
 237 |                     return;
 238 |                 }
 239 | 
 240 |                 let mut journal_data = USN_JOURNAL_DATA_V0::default();
 241 |                 let mut bytes_returned = 0u32;
 242 | 
 243 |                 let success = DeviceIoControl(
 244 |                     handle,
 245 |                     FSCTL_QUERY_USN_JOURNAL,
 246 |                     None,
 247 |                     0,
 248 |                     Some(&mut journal_data as *mut _ as *mut _),
 249 |                     std::mem::size_of::<USN_JOURNAL_DATA_V0>() as u32,
 250 |                     Some(&mut bytes_returned),
 251 |                     None,
 252 |                 );
 253 | 
 254 |                 if success.is_err() {
 255 |                     let _ = CloseHandle(handle);
 256 |                     return;
 257 |                 }
 258 | 
 259 |                 const USN_REASON_FILE_DELETE: u32 = 0x00000200;
 260 | 
 261 |                 let mut read_data = READ_USN_JOURNAL_DATA_V0 {
 262 |                     StartUsn: journal_data.NextUsn,
 263 |                     ReasonMask: 0xFFFFFFFF,
 264 |                     ReturnOnlyOnClose: 1, // Only get events when file is closed (finished writing)
 265 |                     Timeout: 0,
 266 |                     BytesToWaitFor: 0,
 267 |                     UsnJournalID: journal_data.UsnJournalID,
 268 |                 };
 269 | 
 270 |                 let mut buffer = [0u8; 8192];
 271 | 
 272 |                 loop {
 273 |                     let mut bytes_returned = 0u32;
 274 |                     let success = DeviceIoControl(
 275 |                         handle,
 276 |                         FSCTL_READ_USN_JOURNAL,
 277 |                         Some(&read_data as *const _ as *const _),
 278 |                         std::mem::size_of::<READ_USN_JOURNAL_DATA_V0>() as u32,
 279 |                         Some(buffer.as_mut_ptr() as *mut _),
 280 |                         buffer.len() as u32,
 281 |                         Some(&mut bytes_returned),
 282 |                         None,
 283 |                     );
 284 | 
 285 |                     if success.is_ok() && bytes_returned >= 8 {
 286 |                         let next_usn = *(buffer.as_ptr() as *const i64);
 287 |                         read_data.StartUsn = next_usn;
 288 | 
 289 |                         let mut offset = 8;
 290 |                         while offset < bytes_returned as usize {
 291 |                             let record = &*(buffer.as_ptr().add(offset) as *const USN_RECORD_V2);
 292 | 
 293 |                             if (record.FileAttributes & FILE_ATTRIBUTE_SYSTEM.0) == 0 {
 294 |                                 let name_ptr =
 295 |                                     buffer.as_ptr().add(offset + record.FileNameOffset as usize)
 296 |                                         as *const u16;
 297 |                                 let name_len = (record.FileNameLength / 2) as usize;
 298 |                                 let name = String::from_utf16_lossy(std::slice::from_raw_parts(
 299 |                                     name_ptr, name_len,
 300 |                                 ));
 301 | 
 302 |                                 // Simplified path: In a full impl, we'd use the FRN map.
 303 |                                 // For now, we only support top-level changes or
 304 |                                 // we'd need to keep the fs_map in memory.
 305 |                                 // As a compromise for this prototype, we'll try to get the path
 306 |                                 // by using the parent FRN if we have a way to cache it.
 307 |                                 let mut changed_path = PathBuf::from(&drive_root_str);
 308 |                                 changed_path.push(name);
 309 | 
 310 |                                 let action = if (record.Reason & USN_REASON_FILE_DELETE) != 0 {
 311 |                                     crate::watcher::WatcherAction::Remove
 312 |                                 } else {
 313 |                                     crate::watcher::WatcherAction::Index
 314 |                                 };
 315 | 
 316 |                                 let _ = tx.blocking_send((changed_path, action));
 317 |                             }
 318 | 
 319 |                             offset += record.RecordLength as usize;
 320 |                         }
 321 |                     } else {
 322 |                         std::thread::sleep(std::time::Duration::from_millis(500));
 323 |                     }
 324 |                 }
 325 |             }
 326 |         });
 327 | 
 328 |         Ok(())
 329 |     }
 330 | }

 366 | use crate::error::Result;
 367 | use crate::scanner::{ProgressEvent, ProgressType};
 368 | use ignore::WalkBuilder;
 369 | use std::path::PathBuf;
 370 | use std::sync::atomic::{AtomicUsize, Ordering};
 371 | use std::sync::Arc;
 372 | use tokio::sync::mpsc;
 373 | use tracing::{info, warn};
 374 | 
 375 | pub trait DriveScanner: Send + Sync {
 376 |     fn scan(
 377 |         &self,
 378 |         root: PathBuf,
 379 |         exclude_patterns: Vec<String>,
 380 |         path_tx: crossbeam_channel::Sender<PathBuf>,
 381 |         progress_tx: Option<mpsc::Sender<ProgressEvent>>,
 382 |         total_count: Arc<AtomicUsize>,
 383 |     ) -> Result<()>;
 384 | 
 385 |     // Real-time hook for whole drives
 386 |     fn watch(
 387 |         &self,
 388 |         _root: std::path::PathBuf,
 389 |         _tx: tokio::sync::mpsc::Sender<(std::path::PathBuf, crate::watcher::WatcherAction)>,
 390 |     ) -> Result<()> {
 391 |         // Default no-op
 392 |         Ok(())
 393 |     }
 394 | }
 395 | 
 396 | pub struct DefaultDriveScanner;
 397 | 
 398 | impl DriveScanner for DefaultDriveScanner {
 399 |     fn scan(
 400 |         &self,
 401 |         root: PathBuf,
 402 |         exclude_patterns: Vec<String>,
 403 |         path_tx: crossbeam_channel::Sender<PathBuf>,
 404 |         progress_tx: Option<mpsc::Sender<ProgressEvent>>,
 405 |         total_count: Arc<AtomicUsize>,
 406 |     ) -> Result<()> {
 407 |         let mut builder = WalkBuilder::new(&root);
 408 | 
 409 |         let mut override_builder = ignore::overrides::OverrideBuilder::new(&root);
 410 |         for pattern in &exclude_patterns {
 411 |             let ignore_pattern = format!("!{}", pattern);
 412 |             if let Err(e) = override_builder.add(&ignore_pattern) {
 413 |                 warn!("Invalid exclude pattern '{}': {}", pattern, e);
 414 |             }
 415 |         }
 416 |         if let Ok(overrides) = override_builder.build() {
 417 |             builder.overrides(overrides);
 418 |         }
 419 | 
 420 |         builder.follow_links(true).standard_filters(false);
 421 |         builder.max_depth(Some(20));
 422 | 
 423 |         info!("Starting DefaultDriveScanner for {}", root.display());
 424 |         let walker = builder.build_parallel();
 425 | 
 426 |         walker.run(|| {
 427 |             let path_tx = path_tx.clone();
 428 |             let progress_tx = progress_tx.clone();
 429 |             let total = total_count.clone();
 430 |             Box::new(move |entry| {
 431 |                 if let Ok(entry) = entry {
 432 |                     if entry.file_type().map(|ft| ft.is_file()).unwrap_or(false) {
 433 |                         let path = entry.path().to_path_buf();
 434 |                         let _ = path_tx.send(path);
 435 |                         let count = total.fetch_add(1, Ordering::Relaxed);
 436 | 
 437 |                         if count % 100 == 0 {
 438 |                             if let Some(tx) = &progress_tx {
 439 |                                 let _ = tx.try_send(ProgressEvent {
 440 |                                     ptype: ProgressType::Filename,
 441 |                                     current_file: entry.file_name().to_string_lossy().to_string(),
 442 |                                     current_folder: "".to_string(),
 443 |                                     processed: count,
 444 |                                     total: 0,
 445 |                                     status: "Scanning filenames...".to_string(),
 446 |                                     eta_seconds: 0,
 447 |                                     files_per_second: 0.0,
 448 |                                 });
 449 |                             }
 450 |                         }
 451 |                     }
 452 |                 }
 453 |                 ignore::WalkState::Continue
 454 |             })
 455 |         });
 456 | 
 457 |         let final_count = total_count.load(Ordering::Relaxed);
 458 |         if let Some(tx) = &progress_tx {
 459 |             let _ = tx.try_send(ProgressEvent {
 460 |                 ptype: ProgressType::Filename,
 461 |                 current_file: "".to_string(),
 462 |                 current_folder: "".to_string(),
 463 |                 processed: final_count,
 464 |                 total: final_count,
 465 |                 status: "Filename scan complete".to_string(),
 466 |                 eta_seconds: 0,
 467 |                 files_per_second: 0.0,
 468 |             });
 469 |         }
 470 | 
 471 |         Ok(())
 472 |     }
 473 | }
 474 | 
 475 | #[cfg(target_os = "windows")]
 476 | pub struct WindowsDriveScanner;
 477 | 
 478 | #[cfg(target_os = "windows")]
 479 | impl DriveScanner for WindowsDriveScanner {
 480 |     fn scan(
 481 |         &self,
 482 |         root: PathBuf,
 483 |         exclude_patterns: Vec<String>,
 484 |         path_tx: crossbeam_channel::Sender<PathBuf>,
 485 |         progress_tx: Option<mpsc::Sender<ProgressEvent>>,
 486 |         total_count: Arc<AtomicUsize>,
 487 |     ) -> Result<()> {
 488 |         let root_str = root.to_string_lossy();
 489 |         let is_unc = root_str.starts_with("\\\\");
 490 |         let is_root = root.parent().is_none() || root_str.len() <= 3;
 491 | 
 492 |         let mut is_local_drive = true;
 493 |         if is_root && !is_unc {
 494 |             unsafe {
 495 |                 let drive_root = format!("{}\\", &root_str[..2]);
 496 |                 let mut wide_root: Vec<u16> = drive_root.encode_utf16().collect();
 497 |                 wide_root.push(0);
 498 | 
 499 |                 let drive_type = windows::Win32::Storage::FileSystem::GetDriveTypeW(
 500 |                     windows::core::PCWSTR(wide_root.as_ptr()),
 501 |                 );
 502 | 
 503 |                 if drive_type == 3 {
 504 |                     // DRIVE_REMOTE
 505 |                     is_local_drive = false;
 506 |                 }
 507 |             }
 508 |         }
 509 | 
 510 |         if is_root && !is_unc && is_local_drive && root.exists() {
 511 |             info!(
 512 |                 "Whole local drive detected, attempting MFT scan for {:?}",
 513 |                 root
 514 |             );
 515 |             if let Err(e) = windows_usn::scan_volume(
 516 |                 &root,
 517 |                 path_tx.clone(),
 518 |                 progress_tx.clone(),
 519 |                 total_count.clone(),
 520 |             ) {
 521 |                 warn!("MFT scan failed, falling back to parallel walk: {}", e);
 522 |             } else {
 523 |                 return Ok(());
 524 |             }
 525 |         } else if is_unc || !is_local_drive {
 526 |             info!(
 527 |                 "Network/Remote drive detected, using parallel fallback scanner for {:?}",
 528 |                 root
 529 |             );
 530 |         }
 531 | 
 532 |         let fallback = DefaultDriveScanner;
 533 |         fallback.scan(root, exclude_patterns, path_tx, progress_tx, total_count)
 534 |     }
 535 | 
 536 |     fn watch(
 537 |         &self,
 538 |         root: PathBuf,
 539 |         tx: tokio::sync::mpsc::Sender<(PathBuf, crate::watcher::WatcherAction)>,
 540 |     ) -> Result<()> {
 541 |         let root_str = root.to_string_lossy();
 542 |         let is_unc = root_str.starts_with("\\\\");
 543 |         let is_root = root.parent().is_none() || root_str.len() <= 3;
 544 | 
 545 |         let mut is_local_drive = true;
 546 |         if is_root && !is_unc {
 547 |             unsafe {
 548 |                 let drive_root = format!("{}\\", &root_str[..2]);
 549 |                 let mut wide_root: Vec<u16> = drive_root.encode_utf16().collect();
 550 |                 wide_root.push(0);
 551 | 
 552 |                 let drive_type = windows::Win32::Storage::FileSystem::GetDriveTypeW(
 553 |                     windows::core::PCWSTR(wide_root.as_ptr()),
 554 |                 );
 555 | 
 556 |                 if drive_type == 3 {
 557 |                     // DRIVE_REMOTE
 558 |                     is_local_drive = false;
 559 |                 }
 560 |             }
 561 |         }
 562 | 
 563 |         if is_root && !is_unc && is_local_drive && root.exists() {
 564 |             windows_usn::watch_volume(&root, tx)
 565 |         } else {
 566 |             // For network drives and subdirectories, watcher.rs handles standard notify events
 567 |             Ok(())
 568 |         }
 569 |     }
 570 | }
 571 | 
 572 | #[cfg(target_os = "macos")]
 573 | pub struct MacDriveScanner;
 574 | 
 575 | #[cfg(target_os = "macos")]
 576 | impl DriveScanner for MacDriveScanner {
 577 |     fn scan(
 578 |         &self,
 579 |         root: PathBuf,
 580 |         exclude_patterns: Vec<String>,
 581 |         path_tx: crossbeam_channel::Sender<PathBuf>,
 582 |         progress_tx: Option<mpsc::Sender<ProgressEvent>>,
 583 |         total_count: Arc<AtomicUsize>,
 584 |     ) -> Result<()> {
 585 |         let _ = macos_fsevents::scan_volume(&root);
 586 |         let fallback = DefaultDriveScanner;
 587 |         fallback.scan(root, exclude_patterns, path_tx, progress_tx, total_count)
 588 |     }
 589 | }
 590 | 
 591 | #[cfg(target_os = "linux")]
 592 | pub struct LinuxDriveScanner;
 593 | 
 594 | #[cfg(target_os = "linux")]
 595 | impl DriveScanner for LinuxDriveScanner {
 596 |     fn scan(
 597 |         &self,
 598 |         root: PathBuf,
 599 |         exclude_patterns: Vec<String>,
 600 |         path_tx: crossbeam_channel::Sender<PathBuf>,
 601 |         progress_tx: Option<mpsc::Sender<ProgressEvent>>,
 602 |         total_count: Arc<AtomicUsize>,
 603 |     ) -> Result<()> {
 604 |         let _ = linux_fanotify::scan_volume(&root);
 605 |         let fallback = DefaultDriveScanner;
 606 |         fallback.scan(root, exclude_patterns, path_tx, progress_tx, total_count)
```

```rust
 185 | impl AppSettings {
 186 |     pub fn get_allowed_extensions(&self) -> std::collections::HashSet<String> {
 187 |         let mut exts = std::collections::HashSet::new();
 188 |         for ext in COMMON_EXTENSIONS {
 189 |             exts.insert(ext.to_string());
 190 |         }
 191 |         for custom in self.custom_extensions.split(',') {
 192 |             let trimmed = custom.trim().trim_start_matches('.').to_lowercase();
 193 |             if !trimmed.is_empty() {
 194 |                 exts.insert(trimmed);
 195 |             }
 196 |         }
 197 |         exts
 198 |     }
 199 | }

 201 | impl SettingsManager {
 202 |     pub fn new(app_data_dir: &Path) -> Self {
 203 |         Self {
 204 |             path: app_data_dir.join("settings.json"),
 205 |         }
 206 |     }
 207 | 
 208 |     pub fn load(&self) -> Result<AppSettings> {
 209 |         let builder = Config::builder()
 210 |             // Start with default settings
 211 |             .add_source(ConfigFile::from_str(
 212 |                 &serde_json::to_string(&AppSettings::default()).unwrap(),
 213 |                 config::FileFormat::Json,
 214 |             ))
 215 |             // Add settings from file if it exists
 216 |             .add_source(ConfigFile::from(self.path.clone()).required(false))
 217 |             // Override with environment variables (e.g., FLASH_SEARCH_THEME=dark)
 218 |             .add_source(Environment::with_prefix("FLASH_SEARCH").separator("_"));
 219 | 
 220 |         match builder.build() {
 221 |             Ok(config) => config
 222 |                 .try_deserialize()
 223 |                 .map_err(|e| FlashError::config("parse_settings", e.to_string())),
 224 |             Err(e) => Err(FlashError::config("build_config", e.to_string())),
 225 |         }
 226 |     }
 227 | 
 228 |     pub fn save(&self, settings: &AppSettings) -> Result<()> {
 229 |         let content = serde_json::to_string_pretty(settings)
 230 |             .map_err(|e| FlashError::config("serialize_settings", e.to_string()))?;
 231 | 
 232 |         let tmp_path = self.path.with_extension("tmp");
 233 |         fs::write(&tmp_path, content).map_err(FlashError::Io)?;
 234 |         fs::rename(&tmp_path, &self.path).map_err(FlashError::Io)
 235 |     }
 236 | }
 237 |
```

```rust
  10 | #[cfg(target_os = "windows")]
  11 | pub fn register_context_menu(enable: bool) -> Result<()> {
  12 |     use std::env;
  13 |     use winreg::enums::HKEY_CURRENT_USER;
  14 |     use winreg::RegKey;
  15 | 
  16 |     let hkcu = RegKey::predef(HKEY_CURRENT_USER);
  17 |     let path = r#"Software\Classes\Directory\shell\FlashSearch"#;
  18 | 
  19 |     if enable {
  20 |         let (key, _) = hkcu
  21 |             .create_subkey(path)
  22 |             .map_err(|e| FlashError::config("context_menu", e.to_string()))?;
  23 | 
  24 |         key.set_value("", &"Search with Flash Search")
  25 |             .map_err(|e| FlashError::config("context_menu", e.to_string()))?;
  26 | 
  27 |         let icon_path = env::current_exe().unwrap_or_default();
  28 |         key.set_value("Icon", &icon_path.to_str().unwrap_or_default())
  29 |             .map_err(|e| FlashError::config("context_menu", e.to_string()))?;
  30 | 
  31 |         let (command_key, _) = key
  32 |             .create_subkey("command")
  33 |             .map_err(|e| FlashError::config("context_menu", e.to_string()))?;
  34 | 
  35 |         let command = format!("\"{}\" \"%%1\"", icon_path.to_str().unwrap_or_default());
  36 |         command_key
  37 |             .set_value("", &command)
  38 |             .map_err(|e| FlashError::config("context_menu", e.to_string()))?;
  39 |     } else {
  40 |         let _ = hkcu.delete_subkey_all(path);
  41 |     }
  42 |     Ok(())
```

```rust
   8 |     let image = image::load_from_memory_with_format(icon_data, ImageFormat::Png)

  25 |         .with_id("com.flashsearch")
  26 |         .with_menu(Box::new(tray_menu))
  27 |         .with_tooltip("Flash Search")
```
