```markdown
   1 | # Advanced Features Reference
   2 | 
   3 | Kreuzberg provides powerful advanced features for customization, semantic processing, and integration with external systems.
   4 | 
   5 | ## Plugin System
   6 | 
   7 | The plugin system allows you to extend Kreuzberg's extraction pipeline with custom post-processors, validators, and OCR backends. Plugins run within the extraction pipeline and have direct access to extraction results.
   8 | 
   9 | ### Custom Post-Processors
  10 | 
  11 | Post-processors enrich extraction results after document parsing. They run non-destructively—if a post-processor fails, the extraction succeeds anyway (errors are logged).
  12 | 
  13 | === "Python"
  14 | 
  15 |     ```python
  16 |     from kreuzberg import register_post_processor, ExtractionResult
  17 | 
  18 |     class MetadataEnricher:
  19 |         def name(self) -> str:
  20 |             return "metadata_enricher"
  21 | 
  22 |         def process(self, result: ExtractionResult) -> ExtractionResult:
  23 |             result.metadata["processed_by"] = "metadata_enricher"
  24 |             result.metadata["char_count"] = len(result.content)
  25 |             return result
  26 | 
  27 |         def processing_stage(self) -> str:
  28 |             # "early", "middle", or "late"
  29 |             return "middle"
  30 | 
  31 |         def initialize(self) -> None:
  32 |             print("Initializing metadata enricher")
  33 | 
  34 |         def shutdown(self) -> None:
  35 |             print("Shutting down metadata enricher")
  36 | 
  37 |     register_post_processor(MetadataEnricher())
  38 | 
  39 |     # Now use extraction with the registered processor
  40 |     from kreuzberg import extract_file_sync
  41 |     result = extract_file_sync("document.pdf")
  42 |     print(result.metadata["char_count"])
  43 |     ```
  44 | 
  45 | === "TypeScript"
  46 | 
  47 |     ```typescript
  48 |     import { registerPostProcessor, ExtractionResult } from '@kreuzberg/node';
  49 | 
  50 |     const enricher = {
  51 |         name(): string {
  52 |             return "metadata_enricher";
  53 |         },
  54 | 
  55 |         async process(result: ExtractionResult): Promise<ExtractionResult> {
  56 |             result.metadata.processed_by = "metadata_enricher";
  57 |             result.metadata.char_count = result.content.length;
  58 |             return result;
  59 |         },
  60 | 
  61 |         processingStage?(): "early" | "middle" | "late" {
  62 |             return "middle";
  63 |         },
  64 | 
  65 |         async initialize?(): Promise<void> {
  66 |             console.log("Initializing metadata enricher");
  67 |         },
  68 | 
  69 |         async shutdown?(): Promise<void> {
  70 |             console.log("Shutting down metadata enricher");
  71 |         }
  72 |     };
  73 | 
  74 |     registerPostProcessor(enricher);
  75 | 
  76 |     // Now use extraction with the registered processor
  77 |     const result = await extractFile("document.pdf");
  78 |     console.log(result.metadata.char_count);
  79 |     ```
  80 | 
  81 | ### Custom Validators
  82 | 
  83 | Validators perform quality checks on extraction results. Unlike post-processors, validator failures cause the entire extraction to fail. Use validators to enforce quality standards.
  84 | 
  85 | === "Python"
  86 | 
  87 |     ```python
  88 |     from kreuzberg import register_validator, ExtractionResult, ValidationError
  89 | 
  90 |     class MinimumContentValidator:
  91 |         def name(self) -> str:
  92 |             return "min_content_validator"
  93 | 
  94 |         def validate(self, result: ExtractionResult) -> None:
  95 |             if len(result.content) < 100:
  96 |                 raise ValidationError("Extracted content too short (< 100 chars)")
  97 | 
  98 |         def priority(self) -> int:
  99 |             # Higher priority runs first (0-1000, default 50)
 100 |             return 100
 101 | 
 102 |         def should_validate(self, result: ExtractionResult) -> bool:
 103 |             # Only validate PDFs
 104 |             return "pdf" in result.mime_type.lower()
 105 | 
 106 |         def initialize(self) -> None:
 107 |             pass
 108 | 
 109 |         def shutdown(self) -> None:
 110 |             pass
 111 | 
 112 |     register_validator(MinimumContentValidator())
 113 | 
 114 |     # Extraction will fail if content < 100 chars
 115 |     result = extract_file_sync("document.pdf")
 116 |     ```
 117 | 
 118 | === "TypeScript"
 119 | 
 120 |     ```typescript
 121 |     import { registerValidator, ExtractionResult } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 122 | 
 123 |     const validator = {
 124 |         name(): string {
 125 |             return "min_content_validator";
 126 |         },
 127 | 
 128 |         async validate(result: ExtractionResult): Promise<void> {
 129 |             if (result.content.length < 100) {
 130 |                 throw new Error("Extracted content too short (< 100 chars)");
 131 |             }
 132 |         },
 133 | 
 134 |         priority?(): number {
 135 |             return 100;
 136 |         },
 137 | 
 138 |         shouldValidate?(result: ExtractionResult): boolean {
 139 |             return result.mimeType.toLowerCase().includes("pdf");
 140 |         },
 141 | 
 142 |         async initialize?(): Promise<void> {},
 143 | 
 144 |         async shutdown?(): Promise<void> {}
 145 |     };
 146 | 
 147 |     registerValidator(validator);
 148 | 
 149 |     // Extraction will fail if content < 100 chars
 150 |     const result = await extractFile("document.pdf");
 151 |     ```
 152 | 
 153 | ### Custom OCR Backends
 154 | 
 155 | Implement custom OCR engines by registering an OCR backend. This allows integration with proprietary or specialized OCR solutions.
 156 | 
 157 | === "Python"
 158 | 
 159 |     ```python
 160 |     from kreuzberg import register_ocr_backend
 161 | 
 162 |     class CustomOcrBackend:
 163 |         def name(self) -> str:
 164 |             return "custom_ocr"
 165 | 
 166 |         def supported_languages(self) -> list[str]:
 167 |             return ["eng", "deu", "fra", "spa"]
 168 | 
 169 |         def process_image(self, image_bytes: bytes, language: str) -> dict:
 170 |             # image_bytes: raw image data
 171 |             # language: ISO 639-3 code (e.g., "eng", "deu")
 172 | 
 173 |             # Call your OCR engine here
 174 |             # text = my_ocr_engine.recognize(image_bytes, language)
 175 | 
 176 |             return {
 177 |                 "content": "Extracted text from image",
 178 |                 "metadata": {"confidence": 0.95, "language": language},
 179 |                 "tables": []
 180 |             }
 181 | 
 182 |         def process_file(self, path: str, language: str) -> dict:
 183 |             # Optional: custom file processing
 184 |             # Called when extracting OCR from a file path
 185 |             with open(path, "rb") as f:
 186 |                 image_bytes = f.read()
 187 |             return self.process_image(image_bytes, language)
 188 | 
 189 |         def initialize(self) -> None:
 190 |             # Load models, initialize engine
 191 |             pass
 192 | 
 193 |         def shutdown(self) -> None:
 194 |             # Clean up resources
 195 |             pass
 196 | 
 197 |         def version(self) -> str:
 198 |             return "1.0.0"
 199 | 
 200 |     register_ocr_backend(CustomOcrBackend())
 201 | 
 202 |     # Use in extraction config
 203 |     from kreuzberg import ExtractionConfig, OcrConfig, extract_file_sync
 204 | 
 205 |     config = ExtractionConfig(
 206 |         ocr=OcrConfig(backend="custom_ocr", language="eng")
 207 |     )
 208 |     result = extract_file_sync("scanned.pdf", config=config)
 209 |     ```
 210 | 
 211 | === "TypeScript"
 212 | 
 213 |     ```typescript
 214 |     import { registerOcrBackend, ExtractionConfig, extractFile } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 215 | 
 216 |     const backend = {
 217 |         name(): string {
 218 |             return "custom_ocr";
 219 |         },
 220 | 
 221 |         supportedLanguages(): string[] {
 222 |             return ["eng", "deu", "fra", "spa"];
 223 |         },
 224 | 
 225 |         async processImage(
 226 |             imageBytes: Uint8Array | string,
 227 |             language: string
 228 |         ): Promise<{
 229 |             content: string;
 230 |             mime_type: string;
 231 |             metadata: Record<string, unknown>;
 232 |             tables: unknown[];
 233 |         }> {
 234 |             const buffer = typeof imageBytes === "string"
 235 |                 ? Buffer.from(imageBytes, "base64")
 236 |                 : Buffer.from(imageBytes);
 237 | 
 238 |             // Call your OCR engine
 239 |             // const text = await myOcrEngine.recognize(buffer, language);
 240 | 
 241 |             return {
 242 |                 content: "Extracted text from image",
 243 |                 mime_type: "text/plain",
 244 |                 metadata: { confidence: 0.95, language },
 245 |                 tables: []
 246 |             };
 247 |         },
 248 | 
 249 |         async initialize?(): Promise<void> {
 250 |             // Load models, initialize engine
 251 |         },
 252 | 
 253 |         async shutdown?(): Promise<void> {
 254 |             // Clean up resources
 255 |         }
 256 |     };
 257 | 
 258 |     registerOcrBackend(backend);
 259 | 
 260 |     // Use in extraction config
 261 |     const config: ExtractionConfig = {
 262 |         ocr: { backend: "custom_ocr", language: "eng" }
 263 |     };
 264 |     const result = await extractFile("scanned.pdf", null, config);
 265 |     ```
 266 | 
 267 | ## Embeddings
 268 | 
 269 | Generate vector embeddings for text chunks using ONNX-based models. Embeddings enable semantic search, clustering, and similarity operations on extracted content.
 270 | 
 271 | **Requirements:** ONNX Runtime 1.22.x or later
 272 | 
 273 | === "Python"
 274 | 
 275 |     ```python
 276 |     from kreuzberg import (
 277 |         ExtractionConfig, ChunkingConfig, EmbeddingConfig,
 278 |         EmbeddingModelType, list_embedding_presets,
 279 |         get_embedding_preset, extract_file_sync
 280 |     )
 281 | 
 282 |     # List available embedding presets
 283 |     presets = list_embedding_presets()
 284 |     print(f"Available presets: {presets}")  # ['balanced', 'compact', 'large']
 285 | 
 286 |     # Get details about a preset
 287 |     preset_info = get_embedding_preset("balanced")
 288 |     print(f"Model: {preset_info.model_name}")
 289 |     print(f"Dimensions: {preset_info.dimensions}")
 290 |     print(f"Recommended chunk size: {preset_info.chunk_size}")
 291 | 
 292 |     # Method 1: Use preset (recommended)
 293 |     config = ExtractionConfig(
 294 |         chunking=ChunkingConfig(
 295 |             max_chars=512,
 296 |             max_overlap=100,
 297 |             embedding=EmbeddingConfig(
 298 |                 model=EmbeddingModelType.preset("balanced"),
 299 |                 normalize=True,
 300 |                 batch_size=32
 301 |             )
 302 |         )
 303 |     )
 304 | 
 305 |     # Method 2: Use specific fastembed model
 306 |     config = ExtractionConfig(
 307 |         chunking=ChunkingConfig(
 308 |             embedding=EmbeddingConfig(
 309 |                 model=EmbeddingModelType.fastembed(
 310 |                     model="BAAI/bge-small-en-v1.5",
 311 |                     dimensions=384
 312 |                 ),
 313 |                 normalize=True
 314 |             )
 315 |         )
 316 |     )
 317 | 
 318 |     # Method 3: Use custom ONNX model from HuggingFace
 319 |     config = ExtractionConfig(
 320 |         chunking=ChunkingConfig(
 321 |             embedding=EmbeddingConfig(
 322 |                 model=EmbeddingModelType.custom(
 323 |                     model_id="sentence-transformers/all-MiniLM-L6-v2",
 324 |                     dimensions=384
 325 |                 ),
 326 |                 cache_dir="/path/to/model/cache"
 327 |             )
 328 |         )
 329 |     )
 330 | 
 331 |     result = extract_file_sync("document.pdf", config=config)
 332 | 
 333 |     # Access embeddings in chunks
 334 |     for chunk in result.chunks:
 335 |         embedding = chunk.embedding  # list[float] or None
 336 |         print(f"Chunk: {chunk.content[:50]}...")
 337 |         print(f"Embedding dimensions: {len(embedding) if embedding else 0}")
 338 |     ```
 339 | 
 340 | === "TypeScript"
 341 | 
 342 |     ```typescript
 343 |     import {
 344 |         ExtractionConfig, ChunkingConfig,
 345 |         listEmbeddingPresets, getEmbeddingPreset,
 346 |         extractFile
 347 |     } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 348 | 
 349 |     // List available embedding presets
 350 |     const presets = listEmbeddingPresets();
 351 |     console.log(`Available presets: ${presets}`);  // ['balanced', 'compact', 'large']
 352 | 
 353 |     // Get details about a preset
 354 |     const preset = getEmbeddingPreset("balanced");
 355 |     console.log(`Model: ${preset.modelName}`);
 356 |     console.log(`Dimensions: ${preset.dimensions}`);
 357 |     console.log(`Recommended chunk size: ${preset.chunkSize}`);
 358 | 
 359 |     // Method 1: Use preset (recommended)
 360 |     const config: ExtractionConfig = {
 361 |         chunking: {
 362 |             maxChars: 512,
 363 |             maxOverlap: 100,
 364 |             embedding: {
 365 |                 model: { type: 'preset', name: 'balanced' },
 366 |                 normalize: true,
 367 |                 batchSize: 32
 368 |             }
 369 |         }
 370 |     };
 371 | 
 372 |     // Method 2: Use specific fastembed model
 373 |     const config2: ExtractionConfig = {
 374 |         chunking: {
 375 |             embedding: {
 376 |                 model: {
 377 |                     type: 'fastembed',
 378 |                     model: 'BAAI/bge-small-en-v1.5',
 379 |                     dimensions: 384
 380 |                 },
 381 |                 normalize: true
 382 |             }
 383 |         }
 384 |     };
 385 | 
 386 |     // Method 3: Use custom ONNX model
 387 |     const config3: ExtractionConfig = {
 388 |         chunking: {
 389 |             embedding: {
 390 |                 model: {
 391 |                     type: 'custom',
 392 |                     modelId: 'sentence-transformers/all-MiniLM-L6-v2',
 393 |                     dimensions: 384
 394 |                 },
 395 |                 cacheDir: '/path/to/model/cache'
 396 |             }
 397 |         }
 398 |     };
 399 | 
 400 |     const result = await extractFile("document.pdf", null, config);
 401 | 
 402 |     // Access embeddings in chunks
 403 |     if (result.chunks) {
 404 |         for (const chunk of result.chunks) {
 405 |             const embedding = chunk.embedding;  // number[] | null
 406 |             console.log(`Chunk: ${chunk.content.substring(0, 50)}...`);
 407 |             console.log(`Embedding dimensions: ${embedding?.length ?? 0}`);
 408 |         }
 409 |     }
 410 |     ```
 411 | 
 412 | ## Keyword Extraction
 413 | 
 414 | Extract important keywords and phrases from documents using YAKE (Yet Another Keyword Extractor) or RAKE (Rapid Automatic Keyword Extraction) algorithms.
 415 | 
 416 | === "Python"
 417 | 
 418 |     ```python
 419 |     from kreuzberg import (
 420 |         ExtractionConfig, KeywordConfig, KeywordAlgorithm,
 421 |         YakeParams, RakeParams, extract_file_sync
 422 |     )
 423 | 
 424 |     # YAKE algorithm (unsupervised, good for general use)
 425 |     config = ExtractionConfig(
 426 |         keywords=KeywordConfig(
 427 |             algorithm=KeywordAlgorithm.Yake,
 428 |             max_keywords=15,
 429 |             min_score=0.1,
 430 |             ngram_range=(1, 3),
 431 |             language="en",
 432 |             yake_params=YakeParams(window_size=2)
 433 |         )
 434 |     )
 435 | 
 436 |     # RAKE algorithm (co-occurrence based)
 437 |     config = ExtractionConfig(
 438 |         keywords=KeywordConfig(
 439 |             algorithm=KeywordAlgorithm.Rake,
 440 |             max_keywords=10,
 441 |             min_score=0.0,
 442 |             language="en",
 443 |             rake_params=RakeParams(
 444 |                 min_word_length=3,
 445 |                 max_words_per_phrase=3
 446 |             )
 447 |         )
 448 |     )
 449 | 
 450 |     result = extract_file_sync("document.pdf", config=config)
 451 | 
 452 |     # Access extracted keywords
 453 |     if result.keywords:
 454 |         for keyword in result.keywords:
 455 |             print(f"Text: {keyword.text}")
 456 |             print(f"Score: {keyword.score}")
 457 |             print(f"Algorithm: {keyword.algorithm}")
 458 |     ```
 459 | 
 460 | === "TypeScript"
 461 | 
 462 |     ```typescript
 463 |     import {
 464 |         ExtractionConfig, KeywordConfig,
 465 |         extractFile
 466 |     } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 467 | 
 468 |     // YAKE algorithm
 469 |     const config: ExtractionConfig = {
 470 |         keywords: {
 471 |             algorithm: "yake",
 472 |             maxKeywords: 15,
 473 |             minScore: 0.1,
 474 |             ngramRange: [1, 3],
 475 |             language: "en",
 476 |             yakeParams: {
 477 |                 windowSize: 2
 478 |             }
 479 |         }
 480 |     };
 481 | 
 482 |     // RAKE algorithm
 483 |     const config2: ExtractionConfig = {
 484 |         keywords: {
 485 |             algorithm: "rake",
 486 |             maxKeywords: 10,
 487 |             minScore: 0.0,
 488 |             language: "en",
 489 |             rakeParams: {
 490 |                 minWordLength: 3,
 491 |                 maxWordsPerPhrase: 3
 492 |             }
 493 |         }
 494 |     };
 495 | 
 496 |     const result = await extractFile("document.pdf", null, config);
 497 | 
 498 |     // Access extracted keywords
 499 |     if (result.keywords) {
 500 |         for (const keyword of result.keywords) {
 501 |             console.log(`Text: ${keyword.text}`);
 502 |             console.log(`Score: ${keyword.score}`);
 503 |             console.log(`Algorithm: ${keyword.algorithm}`);
 504 |         }
 505 |     }
 506 |     ```
 507 | 
 508 | ## Language Detection
 509 | 
 510 | Automatically detect the language(s) in documents using ISO 639-1 language codes.
 511 | 
 512 | === "Python"
 513 | 
 514 |     ```python
 515 |     from kreuzberg import (
 516 |         ExtractionConfig, LanguageDetectionConfig,
 517 |         extract_file_sync
 518 |     )
 519 | 
 520 |     # Enable language detection
 521 |     config = ExtractionConfig(
 522 |         language_detection=LanguageDetectionConfig(
 523 |             enabled=True,
 524 |             min_confidence=0.8,
 525 |             detect_multiple=False
 526 |         )
 527 |     )
 528 | 
 529 |     result = extract_file_sync("multilingual.pdf", config=config)
 530 | 
 531 |     # Access detected languages
 532 |     if result.detected_languages:
 533 |         for lang_code in result.detected_languages:
 534 |             print(f"Detected language: {lang_code}")  # e.g., "en", "de", "fr"
 535 |     ```
 536 | 
 537 | === "TypeScript"
 538 | 
 539 |     ```typescript
 540 |     import {
 541 |         ExtractionConfig, LanguageDetectionConfig,
 542 |         extractFile
 543 |     } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 544 | 
 545 |     const config: ExtractionConfig = {
 546 |         languageDetection: {
 547 |             enabled: true,
 548 |             minConfidence: 0.8,
 549 |             detectMultiple: false
 550 |         }
 551 |     };
 552 | 
 553 |     const result = await extractFile("multilingual.pdf", null, config);
 554 | 
 555 |     // Access detected languages
 556 |     if (result.detectedLanguages) {
 557 |         for (const langCode of result.detectedLanguages) {
 558 |             console.log(`Detected language: ${langCode}`);  // e.g., "en", "de", "fr"
 559 |         }
 560 |     }
 561 |     ```
 562 | 
 563 | ## Token Reduction
 564 | 
 565 | Reduce the number of tokens in extracted content for cost optimization when working with LLM APIs. Higher modes are more aggressive but may lose more information.
 566 | 
 567 | === "Python"
 568 | 
 569 |     ```python
 570 |     from kreuzberg import (
 571 |         ExtractionConfig, TokenReductionConfig,
 572 |         extract_file_sync
 573 |     )
 574 | 
 575 |     # Light token reduction
 576 |     config = ExtractionConfig(
 577 |         token_reduction=TokenReductionConfig(
 578 |             mode="light",
 579 |             preserve_important_words=True
 580 |         )
 581 |     )
 582 | 
 583 |     # Moderate reduction
 584 |     config = ExtractionConfig(
 585 |         token_reduction=TokenReductionConfig(
 586 |             mode="moderate",
 587 |             preserve_important_words=True
 588 |         )
 589 |     )
 590 | 
 591 |     # Aggressive reduction
 592 |     config = ExtractionConfig(
 593 |         token_reduction=TokenReductionConfig(
 594 |             mode="aggressive",
 595 |             preserve_important_words=True
 596 |         )
 597 |     )
 598 | 
 599 |     # Maximum reduction
 600 |     config = ExtractionConfig(
 601 |         token_reduction=TokenReductionConfig(
 602 |             mode="maximum",
 603 |             preserve_important_words=True
 604 |         )
 605 |     )
 606 | 
 607 |     result = extract_file_sync("document.pdf", config=config)
 608 |     print(f"Reduced content length: {len(result.content)}")
 609 |     ```
 610 | 
 611 | === "TypeScript"
 612 | 
 613 |     ```typescript
 614 |     import {
 615 |         ExtractionConfig, TokenReductionConfig,
 616 |         extractFile
 617 |     } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 618 | 
 619 |     const config: ExtractionConfig = {
 620 |         tokenReduction: {
 621 |             mode: "moderate",
 622 |             preserveImportantWords: true
 623 |         }
 624 |     };
 625 | 
 626 |     const result = await extractFile("document.pdf", null, config);
 627 |     console.log(`Reduced content length: ${result.content.length}`);
 628 |     ```
 629 | 
 630 | **Token Reduction Modes:**
 631 | - `off`: No reduction (default)
 632 | - `light`: Remove extra whitespace and redundant punctuation
 633 | - `moderate`: Also remove common filler words and some formatting
 634 | - `aggressive`: Also remove longer stopwords and collapse similar phrases
 635 | - `maximum`: Maximum reduction while preserving semantic content
 636 | 
 637 | ## Page Extraction
 638 | 
 639 | Extract and track per-page content separately. Useful for multi-page documents where you need page-level granularity.
 640 | 
 641 | === "Python"
 642 | 
 643 |     ```python
 644 |     from kreuzberg import (
 645 |         ExtractionConfig, PageConfig,
 646 |         extract_file_sync
 647 |     )
 648 | 
 649 |     config = ExtractionConfig(
 650 |         pages=PageConfig(
 651 |             extract_pages=True,
 652 |             insert_page_markers=True,
 653 |             marker_format="\n\n<!-- PAGE {page_num} -->\n\n"
 654 |         )
 655 |     )
 656 | 
 657 |     result = extract_file_sync("multi_page.pdf", config=config)
 658 | 
 659 |     # Access per-page content
 660 |     if result.pages:
 661 |         for page in result.pages:
 662 |             print(f"Page {page.page_number}:")
 663 |             print(f"Content: {page.content[:100]}...")
 664 |             print(f"Tables: {len(page.tables)}")
 665 |             print(f"Images: {len(page.images)}")
 666 |     ```
 667 | 
 668 | === "TypeScript"
 669 | 
 670 |     ```typescript
 671 |     import {
 672 |         ExtractionConfig, PageExtractionConfig,
 673 |         extractFile
 674 |     } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 675 | 
 676 |     const config: ExtractionConfig = {
 677 |         pages: {
 678 |             extractPages: true,
 679 |             insertPageMarkers: true,
 680 |             markerFormat: "\n\n<!-- PAGE {page_num} -->\n\n"
 681 |         }
 682 |     };
 683 | 
 684 |     const result = await extractFile("multi_page.pdf", null, config);
 685 | 
 686 |     // Access per-page content
 687 |     if (result.pages) {
 688 |         for (const page of result.pages) {
 689 |             console.log(`Page ${page.pageNumber}:`);
 690 |             console.log(`Content: ${page.content.substring(0, 100)}...`);
 691 |             console.log(`Tables: ${page.tables.length}`);
 692 |             console.log(`Images: ${page.images.length}`);
 693 |         }
 694 |     }
 695 |     ```
 696 | 
 697 | ## Element-Based Output
 698 | 
 699 | Extract semantic elements instead of unified content. This format is compatible with the Unstructured library and provides structured access to different content types (titles, headings, text, tables, images, etc.).
 700 | 
 701 | === "Python"
 702 | 
 703 |     ```python
 704 |     from kreuzberg import ExtractionConfig, ResultFormat, extract_file_sync
 705 | 
 706 |     config = ExtractionConfig(
 707 |         result_format="element_based"
 708 |     )
 709 | 
 710 |     result = extract_file_sync("document.pdf", config=config)
 711 | 
 712 |     # Access semantic elements
 713 |     if result.elements:
 714 |         for element in result.elements:
 715 |             print(f"Type: {element.element_type}")  # title, heading, narrative_text, etc.
 716 |             print(f"Text: {element.text}")
 717 |             if element.metadata.get("page_number"):
 718 |                 print(f"Page: {element.metadata['page_number']}")
 719 |     ```
 720 | 
 721 | === "TypeScript"
 722 | 
 723 |     ```typescript
 724 |     import { ExtractionConfig, extractFile } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 725 | 
 726 |     const config: ExtractionConfig = {
 727 |         resultFormat: "element_based"
 728 |     };
 729 | 
 730 |     const result = await extractFile("document.pdf", null, config);
 731 | 
 732 |     // Access semantic elements
 733 |     if (result.elements) {
 734 |         for (const element of result.elements) {
 735 |             console.log(`Type: ${element.elementType}`);
 736 |             console.log(`Text: ${element.text}`);
 737 |             if (element.metadata.pageNumber) {
 738 |                 console.log(`Page: ${element.metadata.pageNumber}`);
 739 |             }
 740 |         }
 741 |     }
 742 |     ```
 743 | 
 744 | **Element Types:**
 745 | - `title`: Document or section title
 746 | - `heading`: Section headings
 747 | - `narrative_text`: Regular paragraph text
 748 | - `list_item`: Items in bullet/numbered lists
 749 | - `table`: Table structures
 750 | - `image`: Images or figures
 751 | - `page_break`: Page boundaries
 752 | - `code_block`: Code snippets
 753 | - `block_quote`: Quoted text
 754 | - `footer`: Footer content
 755 | - `header`: Header content
 756 | 
 757 | ## Djot Content
 758 | 
 759 | Output extracted content in Djot markup format (a lighter alternative to Markdown with enhanced structure).
 760 | 
 761 | === "Python"
 762 | 
 763 |     ```python
 764 |     from kreuzberg import ExtractionConfig, OutputFormat, extract_file_sync
 765 | 
 766 |     config = ExtractionConfig(
 767 |         output_format="djot"
 768 |     )
 769 | 
 770 |     result = extract_file_sync("document.pdf", config=config)
 771 |     print(result.content)  # Djot-formatted content
 772 | 
 773 |     # Access structured Djot content
 774 |     if result.djot_content:
 775 |         print(f"Plain text: {result.djot_content['plain_text']}")
 776 |         print(f"Blocks: {result.djot_content['blocks']}")
 777 |         print(f"Links: {result.djot_content['links']}")
 778 |         print(f"Images: {result.djot_content['images']}")
 779 |         print(f"Footnotes: {result.djot_content['footnotes']}")
 780 |     ```
 781 | 
 782 | === "TypeScript"
 783 | 
 784 |     ```typescript
 785 |     import { ExtractionConfig, extractFile } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 786 | 
 787 |     const config: ExtractionConfig = {
 788 |         outputFormat: "djot"
 789 |     };
 790 | 
 791 |     const result = await extractFile("document.pdf", null, config);
 792 |     console.log(result.content);  // Djot-formatted content
 793 | 
 794 |     // Access structured Djot content (if available)
 795 |     if (result.djotContent) {
 796 |         console.log(`Plain text: ${result.djotContent.plain_text}`);
 797 |         console.log(`Blocks: ${result.djotContent.blocks}`);
 798 |         console.log(`Links: ${result.djotContent.links}`);
 799 |         console.log(`Images: ${result.djotContent.images}`);
 800 |         console.log(`Footnotes: ${result.djotContent.footnotes}`);
 801 |     }
 802 |     ```
 803 | 
 804 | ## API Server
 805 | 
 806 | Run Kreuzberg as an HTTP API server for integration with external services.
 807 | 
 808 | ```bash
 809 | # Start server on default port 8000
 810 | kreuzberg serve
 811 | 
 812 | # Custom host and port
 813 | kreuzberg serve --host 0.0.0.0 --port 9000
 814 | 
 815 | # Enable CORS and other options
 816 | kreuzberg serve --host localhost --port 8000
 817 | ```
 818 | 
 819 | **API Endpoints:**
 820 | 
 821 | - `POST /extract` - Extract from uploaded file
 822 | - `POST /batch` - Batch extraction
 823 | - `POST /detect` - Detect MIME type
 824 | 
 825 | **Example:**
 826 | 
 827 | ```bash
 828 | curl -X POST -F "file=@document.pdf" http://localhost:8000/extract
 829 | ```
 830 | 
 831 | ## MCP Server
 832 | 
 833 | Run Kreuzberg as a Model Context Protocol server for integration with Claude and other AI models.
 834 | 
 835 | ```bash
 836 | # Start MCP server with stdio transport
 837 | kreuzberg mcp --transport stdio
 838 | 
 839 | # Start MCP server with HTTP transport
 840 | kreuzberg mcp --transport http --host 127.0.0.1 --port 8001
 841 | ```
 842 | 
 843 | The MCP server exposes extraction functions to AI models, allowing them to process documents directly.
 844 | 
 845 | ## Security Limits
 846 | 
 847 | Set resource limits to prevent abuse and control memory/file size consumption.
 848 | 
 849 | === "Python"
 850 | 
 851 |     ```python
 852 |     from kreuzberg import ExtractionConfig, extract_file_sync
 853 | 
 854 |     config = ExtractionConfig(
 855 |         security_limits={
 856 |             "max_file_size": 100_000_000,      # 100 MB
 857 |             "max_archive_files": 1000,
 858 |             "max_text_length": 10_000_000,     # 10 MB of text
 859 |             "max_pages": 10000,
 860 |             "max_concurrent_extractions": 4
 861 |         }
 862 |     )
 863 | 
 864 |     result = extract_file_sync("document.pdf", config=config)
 865 |     ```
 866 | 
 867 | === "TypeScript"
 868 | 
 869 |     ```typescript
 870 |     import { ExtractionConfig, extractFile } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 871 | 
 872 |     const config: ExtractionConfig = {
 873 |         securityLimits: {
 874 |             max_file_size: 100_000_000,        // 100 MB
 875 |             max_archive_files: 1000,
 876 |             max_text_length: 10_000_000,       // 10 MB of text
 877 |             max_pages: 10000,
 878 |             max_concurrent_extractions: 4
 879 |         }
 880 |     };
 881 | 
 882 |     const result = await extractFile("document.pdf", null, config);
 883 |     ```
 884 | 
 885 | **Common Limits:**
 886 | - `max_file_size`: Maximum input file size in bytes
 887 | - `max_archive_files`: Maximum files in archives (zip, tar, etc.)
 888 | - `max_text_length`: Maximum extracted text length
 889 | - `max_pages`: Maximum number of pages to process
 890 | - `max_concurrent_extractions`: Maximum concurrent extraction operations
 891 | 
 892 | ## Caching
 893 | 
 894 | Extraction results are cached by default to improve performance on repeated extractions of identical documents. Control caching behavior through configuration.
 895 | 
 896 | === "Python"
 897 | 
 898 |     ```python
 899 |     from kreuzberg import ExtractionConfig, extract_file_sync
 900 | 
 901 |     # Enable caching (default)
 902 |     config = ExtractionConfig(use_cache=True)
 903 |     result = extract_file_sync("document.pdf", config=config)
 904 | 
 905 |     # Disable caching for a specific extraction
 906 |     config = ExtractionConfig(use_cache=False)
 907 |     result = extract_file_sync("document.pdf", config=config)
 908 |     ```
 909 | 
 910 | === "TypeScript"
 911 | 
 912 |     ```typescript
 913 |     import { ExtractionConfig, extractFile } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 914 | 
 915 |     // Enable caching (default)
 916 |     const config: ExtractionConfig = { useCache: true };
 917 |     const result = await extractFile("document.pdf", null, config);
 918 | 
 919 |     // Disable caching
 920 |     const config2: ExtractionConfig = { useCache: false };
 921 |     const result2 = await extractFile("document.pdf", null, config2);
 922 |     ```
 923 | 
 924 | **CLI Cache Management:**
 925 | 
 926 | ```bash
 927 | # View cache statistics
 928 | kreuzberg cache stats
 929 | 
 930 | # Clear all cached results
 931 | kreuzberg cache clear
 932 | ```
 933 | 
 934 | Caching is transparent and automatic—same input produces cached output instantly on subsequent extractions.
```

### File: `skills\kreuzberg\references\cli-reference.md`

- Size: 10505 bytes
- Modified: SystemTime { intervals: 134176840057557836 }

```markdown
   1 | # Kreuzberg CLI Reference
   2 | 
   3 | Comprehensive command-line interface for the Kreuzberg document intelligence library.
   4 | 
   5 | ## Installation
   6 | 
   7 | Install from crates.io:
   8 | 
   9 | ```bash
  10 | cargo install kreuzberg-cli
  11 | ```
  12 | 
  13 | Or download pre-built binaries from [GitHub Releases](https://github.com/lukasmwirth/kreuzberg/releases).
  14 | 
  15 | ## Commands
  16 | 
  17 | ### extract
  18 | 
  19 | Extract text and structure from a single document.
  20 | 
  21 | ```bash
  22 | kreuzberg extract <path> [FLAGS]
  23 | ```
  24 | 
  25 | **Positional Arguments**
  26 | 
  27 | - `<path>` — Path to the document file
  28 | 
  29 | **Flags**
  30 | 
  31 | - `-c, --config <path>` — Path to config file (TOML, YAML, or JSON). Auto-discovers `kreuzberg.{toml,yaml,json}` in current and parent directories if omitted.
  32 | - `--config-json <json>` — Inline JSON configuration (merged after config file, before CLI flags).
  33 | - `--config-json-base64 <base64>` — Base64-encoded JSON configuration.
  34 | - `-m, --mime-type <type>` — MIME type hint (auto-detected if not provided).
  35 | - `-f, --format <text|json>` — CLI output format (default: `text`). Controls how results display, not extraction content format.
  36 | - `--output-format <plain|markdown|djot|html>` — Extraction content format (default: `plain`). Controls format of extracted content.
  37 | - `--ocr <bool>` — Enable OCR processing.
  38 | - `--force-ocr <bool>` — Force OCR even if text extraction succeeds.
  39 | - `--no-cache <bool>` — Disable caching.
  40 | - `--chunk <bool>` — Enable text chunking.
  41 | - `--chunk-size <n>` — Chunk size in characters.
  42 | - `--chunk-overlap <n>` — Chunk overlap in characters.
  43 | - `--quality <bool>` — Enable quality processing.
  44 | - `--detect-language <bool>` — Enable language detection.
  45 | 
  46 | **Examples**
  47 | 
  48 | ```bash
  49 | # Extract with default settings
  50 | kreuzberg extract document.pdf
  51 | 
  52 | # Extract with OCR enabled
  53 | kreuzberg extract scanned.pdf --ocr true
  54 | 
  55 | # Extract with specific output format
  56 | kreuzberg extract doc.docx --output-format markdown
  57 | 
  58 | # Extract with inline JSON config
  59 | kreuzberg extract file.pdf --config-json '{"ocr":{"backend":"tesseract"}}'
  60 | 
  61 | # Extract with base64-encoded config
  62 | kreuzberg extract file.pdf --config-json-base64 eyJvY3IiOnsiYmFja2VuZCI6InRlc3NlcmFjdCJ9fQ==
  63 | 
  64 | # Extract and output as JSON
  65 | kreuzberg extract doc.pdf --format json
  66 | 
  67 | # Extract with chunking
  68 | kreuzberg extract large-doc.pdf --chunk true --chunk-size 2000 --chunk-overlap 200
  69 | ```
  70 | 
  71 | ### batch
  72 | 
  73 | Batch extract from multiple documents in parallel.
  74 | 
  75 | ```bash
  76 | kreuzberg batch <paths...> [FLAGS]
  77 | ```
  78 | 
  79 | **Positional Arguments**
  80 | 
  81 | - `<paths...>` — One or more document file paths
  82 | 
  83 | **Flags**
  84 | 
  85 | - `-c, --config <path>` — Path to config file (TOML, YAML, or JSON). Auto-discovers `kreuzberg.{toml,yaml,json}` in current and parent directories if omitted.
  86 | - `--config-json <json>` — Inline JSON configuration (merged after config file, before CLI flags).
  87 | - `--config-json-base64 <base64>` — Base64-encoded JSON configuration.
  88 | - `-f, --format <text|json>` — CLI output format (default: `json`). Controls how results display, not extraction content format.
  89 | - `--output-format <plain|markdown|djot|html>` — Extraction content format (default: `plain`). Controls format of extracted content.
  90 | - `--ocr <bool>` — Enable OCR processing.
  91 | - `--force-ocr <bool>` — Force OCR even if text extraction succeeds.
  92 | - `--no-cache <bool>` — Disable caching.
  93 | - `--quality <bool>` — Enable quality processing.
  94 | 
  95 | **Notes**
  96 | 
  97 | - Batch command defaults to JSON output format (unlike `extract` which defaults to text).
  98 | - Does not support chunking parameters (`--chunk`, `--chunk-size`, `--chunk-overlap`).
  99 | - Does not support `--mime-type` or `--detect-language` flags.
 100 | 
 101 | **Examples**
 102 | 
 103 | ```bash
 104 | # Batch extract multiple PDFs
 105 | kreuzberg batch document1.pdf document2.pdf document3.pdf
 106 | 
 107 | # Batch extract with glob patterns (shell expansion)
 108 | kreuzberg batch *.pdf
 109 | 
 110 | # Batch extract with custom output format
 111 | kreuzberg batch doc1.pdf doc2.pdf --output-format markdown
 112 | 
 113 | # Batch extract with OCR
 114 | kreuzberg batch scanned*.pdf --ocr true
 115 | 
 116 | # Batch extract with text output format
 117 | kreuzberg batch files*.docx --format text
 118 | ```
 119 | 
 120 | ### detect
 121 | 
 122 | Identify MIME type of a file.
 123 | 
 124 | ```bash
 125 | kreuzberg detect <path> [FLAGS]
 126 | ```
 127 | 
 128 | **Positional Arguments**
 129 | 
 130 | - `<path>` — Path to the file
 131 | 
 132 | **Flags**
 133 | 
 134 | - `-f, --format <text|json>` — Output format (default: `text`)
 135 | 
 136 | **Examples**
 137 | 
 138 | ```bash
 139 | # Detect MIME type (text output)
 140 | kreuzberg detect unknown-file.bin
 141 | 
 142 | # Detect MIME type (JSON output)
 143 | kreuzberg detect file.xyz --format json
 144 | ```
 145 | 
 146 | ### version
 147 | 
 148 | Display version information.
 149 | 
 150 | ```bash
 151 | kreuzberg version [FLAGS]
 152 | ```
 153 | 
 154 | **Flags**
 155 | 
 156 | - `-f, --format <text|json>` — Output format (default: `text`)
 157 | 
 158 | **Examples**
 159 | 
 160 | ```bash
 161 | # Show version as text
 162 | kreuzberg version
 163 | 
 164 | # Show version as JSON
 165 | kreuzberg version --format json
 166 | ```
 167 | 
 168 | ### cache
 169 | 
 170 | Manage extraction cache.
 171 | 
 172 | #### cache stats
 173 | 
 174 | Display cache statistics.
 175 | 
 176 | ```bash
 177 | kreuzberg cache stats [FLAGS]
 178 | ```
 179 | 
 180 | **Flags**
 181 | 
 182 | - `--cache-dir <path>` — Cache directory (default: `.kreuzberg` in current directory)
 183 | - `-f, --format <text|json>` — Output format (default: `text`)
 184 | 
 185 | **Examples**
 186 | 
 187 | ```bash
 188 | # Show cache stats
 189 | kreuzberg cache stats
 190 | 
 191 | # Show cache stats as JSON
 192 | kreuzberg cache stats --format json
 193 | 
 194 | # Show stats for specific cache directory
 195 | kreuzberg cache stats --cache-dir /tmp/my-cache
 196 | ```
 197 | 
 198 | #### cache clear
 199 | 
 200 | Clear all cached extractions.
 201 | 
 202 | ```bash
 203 | kreuzberg cache clear [FLAGS]
 204 | ```
 205 | 
 206 | **Flags**
 207 | 
 208 | - `--cache-dir <path>` — Cache directory (default: `.kreuzberg` in current directory)
 209 | - `-f, --format <text|json>` — Output format (default: `text`)
 210 | 
 211 | **Examples**
 212 | 
 213 | ```bash
 214 | # Clear cache
 215 | kreuzberg cache clear
 216 | 
 217 | # Clear specific cache directory
 218 | kreuzberg cache clear --cache-dir /tmp/my-cache
 219 | ```
 220 | 
 221 | ### serve
 222 | 
 223 | Start the API server (requires `api` feature).
 224 | 
 225 | ```bash
 226 | kreuzberg serve [FLAGS]
 227 | ```
 228 | 
 229 | **Flags**
 230 | 
 231 | - `-H, --host <host>` — Host to bind to (e.g., `127.0.0.1` or `0.0.0.0`). CLI arg overrides config file and environment variables.
 232 | - `-p, --port <port>` — Port to bind to. CLI arg overrides config file and environment variables.
 233 | - `-c, --config <path>` — Path to config file (TOML, YAML, or JSON). Auto-discovers `kreuzberg.{toml,yaml,json}` in current and parent directories if omitted.
 234 | 
 235 | **Configuration Precedence**
 236 | 
 237 | 1. CLI arguments (`--host`, `--port`)
 238 | 2. Environment variables (`KREUZBERG_HOST`, `KREUZBERG_PORT`)
 239 | 3. Config file (`[server]` section)
 240 | 4. Built-in defaults (`127.0.0.1:8000`)
 241 | 
 242 | **Examples**
 243 | 
 244 | ```bash
 245 | # Start server with defaults
 246 | kreuzberg serve
 247 | 
 248 | # Start server on specific host and port
 249 | kreuzberg serve --host 0.0.0.0 --port 3000
 250 | 
 251 | # Start server with config file
 252 | kreuzberg serve --config kreuzberg.toml
 253 | 
 254 | # Start server (environment variables override defaults)
 255 | KREUZBERG_HOST=192.168.1.100 KREUZBERG_PORT=8080 kreuzberg serve
 256 | ```
 257 | 
 258 | ### mcp
 259 | 
 260 | Start the Model Context Protocol (MCP) server (requires `mcp` feature).
 261 | 
 262 | ```bash
 263 | kreuzberg mcp [FLAGS]
 264 | ```
 265 | 
 266 | **Flags**
 267 | 
 268 | - `-c, --config <path>` — Path to config file (TOML, YAML, or JSON). Auto-discovers `kreuzberg.{toml,yaml,json}` in current and parent directories if omitted.
 269 | - `--transport <stdio|http>` — Transport mode (default: `stdio`)
 270 | - `--host <host>` — HTTP host for http transport (default: `127.0.0.1`)
 271 | - `--port <port>` — HTTP port for http transport (default: `8001`)
 272 | 
 273 | **Examples**
 274 | 
 275 | ```bash
 276 | # Start MCP server with stdio transport
 277 | kreuzberg mcp
 278 | 
 279 | # Start MCP server with HTTP transport
 280 | kreuzberg mcp --transport http
 281 | 
 282 | # Start MCP server on custom HTTP host/port
 283 | kreuzberg mcp --transport http --host 0.0.0.0 --port 9000
 284 | 
 285 | # Start MCP server with config file
 286 | kreuzberg mcp --config kreuzberg.toml
 287 | ```
 288 | 
 289 | ## Configuration
 290 | 
 291 | ### File Format
 292 | 
 293 | Configuration files support three formats with automatic detection:
 294 | 
 295 | - **TOML** — `.toml` extension (recommended)
 296 | - **YAML** — `.yaml` or `.yml` extension
 297 | - **JSON** — `.json` extension
 298 | 
 299 | ### Configuration Precedence
 300 | 
 301 | Settings are applied in order from highest to lowest priority:
 302 | 
 303 | 1. **Individual CLI flags** (e.g., `--ocr true`, `--output-format markdown`)
 304 | 2. **Inline JSON config** (`--config-json` or `--config-json-base64`)
 305 | 3. **Config file** (explicit `--config path.toml` or auto-discovered)
 306 | 4. **Default values** (built-in library defaults)
 307 | 
 308 | ### Auto-Discovery
 309 | 
 310 | When no config file is specified, Kreuzberg searches for configuration in this order:
 311 | 
 312 | 1. `kreuzberg.toml` in current directory
 313 | 2. `kreuzberg.yaml` in current directory
 314 | 3. `kreuzberg.json` in current directory
 315 | 4. Parent directories (same search pattern, up to filesystem root)
 316 | 
 317 | ### Example Configuration
 318 | 
 319 | ```toml
 320 | # Top-level extraction options
 321 | use_cache = true
 322 | enable_quality_processing = true
 323 | force_ocr = false
 324 | output_format = "markdown"
 325 | 
 326 | # OCR settings
 327 | [ocr]
 328 | backend = "tesseract"
 329 | language = "eng"
 330 | 
 331 | # Chunking settings
 332 | [chunking]
 333 | max_chars = 2000
 334 | max_overlap = 200
 335 | 
 336 | # Language detection
 337 | [language_detection]
 338 | enabled = true
 339 | 
 340 | # Server configuration (for serve command)
 341 | [server]
 342 | host = "127.0.0.1"
 343 | port = 8000
 344 | ```
 345 | 
 346 | ## Exit Codes
 347 | 
 348 | - `0` — Success
 349 | - Non-zero — Error (see stderr for details)
 350 | 
 351 | ## Error Handling
 352 | 
 353 | The CLI validates input and provides clear error messages:
 354 | 
 355 | - **File not found** — Verify path exists and is readable
 356 | - **Invalid MIME type** — Ensure file is accessible and format is supported
 357 | - **Invalid JSON** — Check `--config-json` syntax
 358 | - **Invalid config file** — Verify TOML/YAML/JSON format
 359 | - **Invalid chunk parameters** — Ensure chunk-size > 0 and overlap < chunk-size
 360 | 
 361 | ## Environment Variables
 362 | 
 363 | - `RUST_LOG` — Set logging level (e.g., `RUST_LOG=debug`)
 364 | - `KREUZBERG_HOST` — Server bind host (used by `serve` command)
 365 | - `KREUZBERG_PORT` — Server bind port (used by `serve` command)
 366 | 
 367 | ## Common Patterns
 368 | 
 369 | ### Extract with Custom Configuration
 370 | 
 371 | ```bash
 372 | kreuzberg extract document.pdf \
 373 |   --output-format markdown \
 374 |   --ocr true \
 375 |   --quality true
 376 | ```
 377 | 
 378 | ### Batch Process with Config File
 379 | 
 380 | ```bash
 381 | kreuzberg batch *.pdf --config extraction-config.toml
 382 | ```
 383 | 
 384 | ### CI/CD Integration
 385 | 
 386 | ```bash
 387 | # Extract to JSON for downstream processing
 388 | kreuzberg extract file.pdf --format json | jq '.content'
 389 | 
 390 | # Batch process with error handling
 391 | kreuzberg batch docs/*.pdf --format json || exit 1
 392 | ```
 393 | 
 394 | ### Performance Tuning
 395 | 
 396 | ```bash
 397 | # Disable cache for temporary processing
 398 | kreuzberg extract file.pdf --no-cache true
 399 | 
 400 | # Enable chunking for large documents
 401 | kreuzberg extract large-file.pdf \
 402 |   --chunk true \
 403 |   --chunk-size 5000 \
 404 |   --chunk-overlap 500
 405 | ```
 406 | 
 407 | ## Debugging
 408 | 
 409 | Enable detailed logging:
 410 | 
 411 | ```bash
 412 | RUST_LOG=debug kreuzberg extract document.pdf
 413 | ```
 414 | 
 415 | Check cache statistics:
 416 | 
 417 | ```bash
 418 | kreuzberg cache stats --format json
 419 | ```
 420 | 
 421 | Detect file MIME type:
 422 | 
 423 | ```bash
 424 | kreuzberg detect unknown-file --format json
 425 | ```
```
