```markdown
   1 | # Configuration Reference
   2 | 
   3 | Kreuzberg uses a hierarchical configuration system supporting multiple formats and auto-discovery mechanisms. This reference covers all available configuration options, field names across programming languages, and loading strategies.
   4 | 
   5 | ## Supported Formats
   6 | 
   7 | Kreuzberg configurations can be defined in three formats:
   8 | 
   9 | - **TOML** (recommended): `kreuzberg.toml`
  10 | - **YAML**: `kreuzberg.yaml`
  11 | - **JSON**: `kreuzberg.json`
  12 | 
  13 | All formats support the same schema and configuration options.
  14 | 
  15 | ## Auto-Discovery
  16 | 
  17 | When no configuration file is explicitly specified, Kreuzberg searches for configuration files in the following order:
  18 | 
  19 | 1. Current working directory: `kreuzberg.toml`, `kreuzberg.yaml`, `kreuzberg.json`
  20 | 2. Parent directories (recursively up the tree, same file name pattern)
  21 | 
  22 | The first matching configuration file is loaded.
  23 | 
  24 | ## Programmatic Loading
  25 | 
  26 | ### Python
  27 | 
  28 | ```python
  29 | from kreuzberg import ExtractionConfig
  30 | 
  31 | # Load from explicit path
  32 | config = ExtractionConfig.from_file("kreuzberg.toml")
  33 | 
  34 | # Auto-discover configuration
  35 | config = ExtractionConfig.discover()
  36 | ```
  37 | 
  38 | ### Node.js / TypeScript
  39 | 
  40 | ```typescript
  41 | import { ExtractionConfig } from '@kreuzberg/node';
  42 | 
  43 | // Load from explicit path
  44 | const config = ExtractionConfig.fromFile('kreuzberg.toml');
  45 | 
  46 | // Auto-discover configuration
  47 | const config = ExtractionConfig.discover();
  48 | ```
  49 | 
  50 | ### CLI
  51 | 
  52 | ```bash
  53 | # Explicit configuration file
  54 | kreuzberg extract --config kreuzberg.toml document.pdf
  55 | 
  56 | # Auto-discovery (searches default locations)
  57 | kreuzberg extract document.pdf
  58 | ```
  59 | 
  60 | ## Configuration Schema
  61 | 
  62 | The complete TOML schema with all available sections and options:
  63 | 
  64 | ### Top-Level Options
  65 | 
  66 | ```toml
  67 | use_cache = true
  68 | enable_quality_processing = true
  69 | force_ocr = false
  70 | output_format = "markdown"
  71 | result_format = "text"
  72 | max_concurrent_extractions = 4
  73 | ```
  74 | 
  75 | | Option | Type | Default | Description |
  76 | |--------|------|---------|-------------|
  77 | | `use_cache` | boolean | `true` | Enable caching of extraction results |
  78 | | `enable_quality_processing` | boolean | `true` | Enable post-processing for output quality |
  79 | | `force_ocr` | boolean | `false` | Force OCR processing even for searchable PDFs |
  80 | | `output_format` | string | `"markdown"` | Output format (markdown, html, text) |
  81 | | `result_format` | string | `"text"` | Result format for structured output |
  82 | | `max_concurrent_extractions` | integer | `4` | Maximum concurrent document extractions |
  83 | 
  84 | ### OCR Configuration
  85 | 
  86 | ```toml
  87 | [ocr]
  88 | backend = "tesseract"
  89 | language = "eng"
  90 | ```
  91 | 
  92 | | Option | Type | Default | Description |
  93 | |--------|------|---------|-------------|
  94 | | `backend` | string | `"tesseract"` | OCR backend (currently tesseract) |
  95 | | `language` | string | `"eng"` | ISO 639-3 language code (eng, deu, fra, etc.) |
  96 | 
  97 | #### Tesseract Configuration
  98 | 
  99 | ```toml
 100 | [ocr.tesseract_config]
 101 | psm = 3
 102 | oem = 3
 103 | min_confidence = 0.0
 104 | output_format = "text"
 105 | enable_table_detection = false
 106 | table_min_confidence = 0.5
 107 | table_column_threshold = 50
 108 | table_row_threshold_ratio = 0.5
 109 | use_cache = true
 110 | ```
 111 | 
 112 | | Option | Type | Default | Description |
 113 | |--------|------|---------|-------------|
 114 | | `psm` | integer | `3` | Page Segmentation Mode (0-13) |
 115 | | `oem` | integer | `3` | OCR Engine Mode (0-3) |
 116 | | `min_confidence` | float | `0.0` | Minimum OCR confidence threshold (0.0-1.0) |
 117 | | `output_format` | string | `"text"` | Output format from OCR |
 118 | | `enable_table_detection` | boolean | `false` | Enable table detection during OCR |
 119 | | `table_min_confidence` | float | `0.5` | Minimum confidence for table cells |
 120 | | `table_column_threshold` | integer | `50` | Pixel threshold for column detection |
 121 | | `table_row_threshold_ratio` | float | `0.5` | Row height ratio threshold |
 122 | | `use_cache` | boolean | `true` | Cache OCR results |
 123 | 
 124 | #### Tesseract Preprocessing
 125 | 
 126 | ```toml
 127 | [ocr.tesseract_config.preprocessing]
 128 | target_dpi = 300
 129 | auto_rotate = true
 130 | deskew = true
 131 | denoise = true
 132 | contrast_enhance = true
 133 | binarization_method = "otsu"
 134 | invert_colors = false
 135 | ```
 136 | 
 137 | | Option | Type | Default | Description |
 138 | |--------|------|---------|-------------|
 139 | | `target_dpi` | integer | `300` | Target DPI for preprocessing |
 140 | | `auto_rotate` | boolean | `true` | Automatically detect and correct page rotation |
 141 | | `deskew` | boolean | `true` | Correct skewed pages |
 142 | | `denoise` | boolean | `true` | Remove noise from images |
 143 | | `contrast_enhance` | boolean | `true` | Enhance image contrast |
 144 | | `binarization_method` | string | `"otsu"` | Method for image binarization |
 145 | | `invert_colors` | boolean | `false` | Invert image colors if needed |
 146 | 
 147 | ### PDF Options
 148 | 
 149 | ```toml
 150 | [pdf_options]
 151 | extract_images = true
 152 | extract_metadata = true
 153 | 
 154 | [pdf_options.hierarchy]
 155 | enabled = true
 156 | k_clusters = 6
 157 | include_bbox = true
 158 | ocr_coverage_threshold = 0.5
 159 | ```
 160 | 
 161 | | Option | Type | Default | Description |
 162 | |--------|------|---------|-------------|
 163 | | `extract_images` | boolean | `true` | Extract images from PDF documents |
 164 | | `extract_metadata` | boolean | `true` | Extract PDF metadata |
 165 | | `hierarchy.enabled` | boolean | `true` | Enable PDF hierarchy extraction (v4.0.0+) |
 166 | | `hierarchy.k_clusters` | integer | `6` | Number of clusters for hierarchy detection |
 167 | | `hierarchy.include_bbox` | boolean | `true` | Include bounding boxes in hierarchy |
 168 | | `hierarchy.ocr_coverage_threshold` | float | `0.5` | OCR coverage threshold for hierarchy (0.0-1.0) |
 169 | 
 170 | ### Image Processing
 171 | 
 172 | ```toml
 173 | [images]
 174 | extract_images = true
 175 | target_dpi = 300
 176 | max_image_dimension = 4096
 177 | auto_adjust_dpi = true
 178 | min_dpi = 72
 179 | max_dpi = 600
 180 | ```
 181 | 
 182 | | Option | Type | Default | Description |
 183 | |--------|------|---------|-------------|
 184 | | `extract_images` | boolean | `true` | Extract images from documents |
 185 | | `target_dpi` | integer | `300` | Target DPI for image processing |
 186 | | `max_image_dimension` | integer | `4096` | Maximum image dimension in pixels |
 187 | | `auto_adjust_dpi` | boolean | `true` | Automatically adjust DPI based on image size |
 188 | | `min_dpi` | integer | `72` | Minimum DPI threshold |
 189 | | `max_dpi` | integer | `600` | Maximum DPI threshold |
 190 | 
 191 | ### Chunking Configuration
 192 | 
 193 | ```toml
 194 | [chunking]
 195 | max_chars = 1000
 196 | max_overlap = 200
 197 | 
 198 | [chunking.embedding]
 199 | batch_size = 32
 200 | normalize = true
 201 | show_download_progress = true
 202 | cache_dir = "~/.cache/kreuzberg/embeddings"
 203 | 
 204 | [chunking.embedding.model]
 205 | type = "preset"
 206 | name = "balanced"
 207 | ```
 208 | 
 209 | | Option | Type | Default | Description |
 210 | |--------|------|---------|-------------|
 211 | | `max_chars` | integer | `1000` | Maximum characters per chunk |
 212 | | `max_overlap` | integer | `200` | Overlap between consecutive chunks |
 213 | | `embedding.batch_size` | integer | `32` | Batch size for embedding generation |
 214 | | `embedding.normalize` | boolean | `true` | Normalize embeddings to unit length |
 215 | | `embedding.show_download_progress` | boolean | `true` | Show progress when downloading models |
 216 | | `embedding.cache_dir` | string | `"~/.cache/kreuzberg/embeddings"` | Directory for caching embeddings |
 217 | | `embedding.model.type` | string | `"preset"` | Model type: preset, fastembed, or custom |
 218 | | `embedding.model.name` | string | `"balanced"` | Preset model name (balanced, fast, accurate, multilingual) |
 219 | | `embedding.model.model` | string | | FastEmbed model identifier |
 220 | | `embedding.model.model_id` | string | | Custom HuggingFace model ID |
 221 | | `embedding.model.dimensions` | integer | | Embedding dimensions |
 222 | 
 223 | ### Keywords Configuration
 224 | 
 225 | ```toml
 226 | [keywords]
 227 | algorithm = "yake"
 228 | max_keywords = 10
 229 | min_score = 0.0
 230 | ngram_range = [1, 3]
 231 | language = "en"
 232 | ```
 233 | 
 234 | | Option | Type | Default | Description |
 235 | |--------|------|---------|-------------|
 236 | | `algorithm` | string | `"yake"` | Keyword extraction algorithm (yake or rake) |
 237 | | `max_keywords` | integer | `10` | Maximum keywords to extract |
 238 | | `min_score` | float | `0.0` | Minimum relevance score for keywords |
 239 | | `ngram_range` | array | `[1, 3]` | N-gram size range [min, max] |
 240 | | `language` | string | `"en"` | Language code for keyword extraction |
 241 | 
 242 | ### Token Reduction
 243 | 
 244 | ```toml
 245 | [token_reduction]
 246 | mode = "off"
 247 | preserve_important_words = true
 248 | ```
 249 | 
 250 | | Option | Type | Default | Description |
 251 | |--------|------|---------|-------------|
 252 | | `mode` | string | `"off"` | Mode: off, aggressive, moderate, minimal |
 253 | | `preserve_important_words` | boolean | `true` | Preserve important words during reduction |
 254 | 
 255 | ### Language Detection
 256 | 
 257 | ```toml
 258 | [language_detection]
 259 | enabled = true
 260 | min_confidence = 0.8
 261 | detect_multiple = false
 262 | ```
 263 | 
 264 | | Option | Type | Default | Description |
 265 | |--------|------|---------|-------------|
 266 | | `enabled` | boolean | `true` | Enable automatic language detection |
 267 | | `min_confidence` | float | `0.8` | Minimum confidence threshold for detection |
 268 | | `detect_multiple` | boolean | `false` | Detect multiple languages in document |
 269 | 
 270 | ### Post-Processor
 271 | 
 272 | ```toml
 273 | [postprocessor]
 274 | enabled = true
 275 | ```
 276 | 
 277 | | Option | Type | Default | Description |
 278 | |--------|------|---------|-------------|
 279 | | `enabled` | boolean | `true` | Enable post-processing of extracted content |
 280 | 
 281 | ## Naming Conventions
 282 | 
 283 | Kreuzberg uses consistent naming conventions across different contexts:
 284 | 
 285 | | Context | Convention | Example |
 286 | |---------|-----------|---------|
 287 | | Python | snake_case | `max_chars`, `pdf_options`, `use_cache` |
 288 | | Node.js / TypeScript | camelCase | `maxChars`, `pdfOptions`, `useCache` |
 289 | | Rust | snake_case | `max_chars`, `pdf_options`, `use_cache` |
 290 | | TOML / YAML / JSON | snake_case | `max_chars`, `pdf_options`, `use_cache` |
 291 | | CLI flags | kebab-case | `--max-chars`, `--pdf-options`, `--use-cache` |
 292 | 
 293 | When switching between languages, apply the appropriate conversion:
 294 | - Python → Node.js: `snake_case` to `camelCase`
 295 | - CLI → Python: `kebab-case` to `snake_case`
 296 | - TOML → Python: No conversion needed (both use `snake_case`)
 297 | 
 298 | ## Environment Variables
 299 | 
 300 | The following environment variables can override configuration:
 301 | 
 302 | | Variable | Purpose | Example |
 303 | |----------|---------|---------|
 304 | | `KREUZBERG_HOST` | Server bind address (serve command) | `127.0.0.1` |
 305 | | `KREUZBERG_PORT` | Server port (serve command) | `8080` |
 306 | 
 307 | ## Configuration Merging
 308 | 
 309 | Configuration sources are merged in priority order (highest to lowest):
 310 | 
 311 | 1. **CLI flags** (highest priority)
 312 | 2. **Inline JSON configuration** (programmatic)
 313 | 3. **Configuration file** (lowest priority)
 314 | 
 315 | Later sources override earlier ones. For example, a CLI flag `--max-chars 2000` overrides `max_chars = 1000` in the configuration file.
 316 | 
 317 | ## Example Configurations
 318 | 
 319 | ### Minimal Configuration
 320 | 
 321 | ```toml
 322 | use_cache = true
 323 | enable_quality_processing = true
 324 | 
 325 | [ocr]
 326 | backend = "tesseract"
 327 | language = "eng"
 328 | ```
 329 | 
 330 | ### High-Quality PDF Extraction
 331 | 
 332 | ```toml
 333 | use_cache = true
 334 | enable_quality_processing = true
 335 | force_ocr = false
 336 | 
 337 | [ocr]
 338 | backend = "tesseract"
 339 | language = "eng"
 340 | 
 341 | [ocr.tesseract_config]
 342 | psm = 3
 343 | oem = 3
 344 | enable_table_detection = true
 345 | table_min_confidence = 0.7
 346 | 
 347 | [pdf_options]
 348 | extract_images = true
 349 | extract_metadata = true
 350 | 
 351 | [pdf_options.hierarchy]
 352 | enabled = true
 353 | k_clusters = 6
 354 | 
 355 | [images]
 356 | extract_images = true
 357 | target_dpi = 300
 358 | ```
 359 | 
 360 | ### Semantic Search Configuration
 361 | 
 362 | ```toml
 363 | [chunking]
 364 | max_chars = 800
 365 | max_overlap = 150
 366 | 
 367 | [chunking.embedding]
 368 | batch_size = 32
 369 | normalize = true
 370 | cache_dir = "~/.cache/kreuzberg/embeddings"
 371 | 
 372 | [chunking.embedding.model]
 373 | type = "preset"
 374 | name = "accurate"
 375 | 
 376 | [keywords]
 377 | algorithm = "yake"
 378 | max_keywords = 15
 379 | ```
 380 | 
 381 | ## Field Name Reference
 382 | 
 383 | Critical field names to use in configuration files:
 384 | 
 385 | - `max_chars` (NOT `max_characters`)
 386 | - `max_overlap` (NOT `overlap`)
 387 | - `table_min_confidence`
 388 | - `table_column_threshold`
 389 | - `table_row_threshold_ratio`
 390 | - `ocr_coverage_threshold`
 391 | - `k_clusters`
 392 | - `include_bbox`
 393 | - `enable_table_detection`
 394 | - `auto_rotate`
 395 | - `auto_adjust_dpi`
 396 | - `show_download_progress`
 397 | - `min_confidence`
 398 | - `detect_multiple`
 399 | 
 400 | Always verify field names against the source configuration file when adding new options.
```

### File: `skills\kreuzberg\references\nodejs-api.md`

- Size: 32349 bytes
- Modified: SystemTime { intervals: 134176840062469194 }

```markdown
   1 | # Node.js/TypeScript API Reference
   2 | 
   3 | ## Overview
   4 | 
   5 | **Package**: `@kreuzberg/node` — A high-performance TypeScript SDK built on a Rust core for document intelligence and content extraction.
   6 | 
   7 | Supports both **ESM** (`import`) and **CommonJS** (`require`):
   8 | 
   9 | ```typescript
  10 | // ESM
  11 | import { extractFile, batchExtractFiles } from '@kreuzberg/node';
  12 | 
  13 | // CommonJS
  14 | const { extractFile, batchExtractFiles } = require('@kreuzberg/node');
  15 | ```
  16 | 
  17 | **Current Version**: 4.2.14
  18 | 
  19 | ---
  20 | 
  21 | ## Core Extraction Functions
  22 | 
  23 | All extraction functions return `ExtractionResult` containing extracted content, metadata, tables, and optional chunks/images.
  24 | 
  25 | ### Single File Extraction
  26 | 
  27 | #### `extractFile(filePath, mimeType?, config?): Promise<ExtractionResult>`
  28 | 
  29 | Extract content from a single file asynchronously.
  30 | 
  31 | ```typescript
  32 | import { extractFile } from '@kreuzberg/node';
  33 | 
  34 | // Auto-detect MIME type from file extension
  35 | const result = await extractFile('document.pdf');
  36 | console.log(result.content);
  37 | 
  38 | // Explicit MIME type
  39 | const result2 = await extractFile('document.pdf', 'application/pdf');
  40 | 
  41 | // With configuration
  42 | const result3 = await extractFile('document.pdf', null, {
  43 |   chunking: {
  44 |     maxChars: 1000,
  45 |     maxOverlap: 200,
  46 |   },
  47 | });
  48 | ```
  49 | 
  50 | **Parameters**:
  51 | - `filePath: string` — Path to the file to extract
  52 | - `mimeType?: string | null` — Optional MIME type hint (auto-detect if null)
  53 | - `config?: ExtractionConfig` — Optional extraction configuration
  54 | 
  55 | **Returns**: `Promise<ExtractionResult>`
  56 | 
  57 | **Throws**: `ParsingError`, `OcrError`, `ValidationError`, `KreuzbergError`
  58 | 
  59 | #### `extractFileSync(filePath, mimeType?, config?): ExtractionResult`
  60 | 
  61 | Extract content from a single file synchronously.
  62 | 
  63 | ```typescript
  64 | import { extractFileSync } from '@kreuzberg/node';
  65 | 
  66 | const result = extractFileSync('document.pdf');
  67 | console.log(result.content);
  68 | ```
  69 | 
  70 | **Parameters**: Same as `extractFile()`
  71 | 
  72 | **Returns**: `ExtractionResult`
  73 | 
  74 | ---
  75 | 
  76 | ### Raw Bytes Extraction
  77 | 
  78 | #### `extractBytes(data, mimeType, config?): Promise<ExtractionResult>`
  79 | 
  80 | Extract content from raw bytes (Buffer or Uint8Array) asynchronously.
  81 | 
  82 | ```typescript
  83 | import { extractBytes } from '@kreuzberg/node';
  84 | import { readFile } from 'fs/promises';
  85 | 
  86 | const data = await readFile('document.pdf');
  87 | const result = await extractBytes(data, 'application/pdf');
  88 | console.log(result.content);
  89 | ```
  90 | 
  91 | **Parameters**:
  92 | - `data: Buffer | Uint8Array` — Raw file content
  93 | - `mimeType: string` — MIME type (required)
  94 | - `config?: ExtractionConfig` — Optional configuration
  95 | 
  96 | **Returns**: `Promise<ExtractionResult>`
  97 | 
  98 | #### `extractBytesSync(data, mimeType, config?): ExtractionResult`
  99 | 
 100 | Extract content from raw bytes synchronously.
 101 | 
 102 | ```typescript
 103 | import { extractBytesSync } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 104 | import { readFileSync } from 'fs';
 105 | 
 106 | const data = readFileSync('document.pdf');
 107 | const result = extractBytesSync(data, 'application/pdf');
 108 | ```
 109 | 
 110 | **Parameters**: Same as `extractBytes()`
 111 | 
 112 | **Returns**: `ExtractionResult`
 113 | 
 114 | ---
 115 | 
 116 | ### Batch Extraction (Recommended)
 117 | 
 118 | For processing multiple documents, batch APIs provide superior performance and memory management.
 119 | 
 120 | #### `batchExtractFiles(paths, config?): Promise<ExtractionResult[]>`
 121 | 
 122 | Extract content from multiple files in parallel (asynchronous).
 123 | 
 124 | ```typescript
 125 | import { batchExtractFiles } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 126 | 
 127 | const files = ['doc1.pdf', 'doc2.docx', 'doc3.xlsx'];
 128 | const results = await batchExtractFiles(files);
 129 | 
 130 | results.forEach((result, i) => {
 131 |   console.log(`${files[i]}: ${result.content.substring(0, 100)}...`);
 132 | });
 133 | ```
 134 | 
 135 | **Parameters**:
 136 | - `paths: string[]` — Array of file paths
 137 | - `config?: ExtractionConfig` — Configuration (applied to all files)
 138 | 
 139 | **Returns**: `Promise<ExtractionResult[]>` — Results in same order as input
 140 | 
 141 | #### `batchExtractFilesSync(paths, config?): ExtractionResult[]`
 142 | 
 143 | Extract content from multiple files synchronously.
 144 | 
 145 | ```typescript
 146 | import { batchExtractFilesSync } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 147 | 
 148 | const files = ['doc1.pdf', 'doc2.docx', 'doc3.xlsx'];
 149 | const results = batchExtractFilesSync(files);
 150 | ```
 151 | 
 152 | **Parameters**: Same as `batchExtractFiles()`
 153 | 
 154 | **Returns**: `ExtractionResult[]`
 155 | 
 156 | #### `batchExtractBytes(dataList, mimeTypes, config?): Promise<ExtractionResult[]>`
 157 | 
 158 | Extract content from multiple byte arrays in parallel (asynchronous).
 159 | 
 160 | ```typescript
 161 | import { batchExtractBytes } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 162 | import { readFile } from 'fs/promises';
 163 | 
 164 | const files = ['doc1.pdf', 'doc2.docx'];
 165 | const dataList = await Promise.all(files.map(f => readFile(f)));
 166 | const mimeTypes = ['application/pdf', 'application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.wordprocessingml.document'];
 167 | 
 168 | const results = await batchExtractBytes(dataList, mimeTypes);
 169 | ```
 170 | 
 171 | **Parameters**:
 172 | - `dataList: Uint8Array[]` — Array of file contents
 173 | - `mimeTypes: string[]` — MIME types (one per item, must match length)
 174 | - `config?: ExtractionConfig` — Configuration (applied to all items)
 175 | 
 176 | **Returns**: `Promise<ExtractionResult[]>`
 177 | 
 178 | #### `batchExtractBytesSync(dataList, mimeTypes, config?): ExtractionResult[]`
 179 | 
 180 | Extract content from multiple byte arrays synchronously.
 181 | 
 182 | ```typescript
 183 | import { batchExtractBytesSync } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 184 | import { readFileSync } from 'fs';
 185 | 
 186 | const dataList = ['doc1.pdf', 'doc2.docx'].map(f => readFileSync(f));
 187 | const mimeTypes = ['application/pdf', 'application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.wordprocessingml.document'];
 188 | 
 189 | const results = batchExtractBytesSync(dataList, mimeTypes);
 190 | ```
 191 | 
 192 | **Parameters**: Same as `batchExtractBytes()`
 193 | 
 194 | **Returns**: `ExtractionResult[]`
 195 | 
 196 | ---
 197 | 
 198 | ## Worker Pool APIs
 199 | 
 200 | Worker pools enable concurrent extraction using Node.js worker threads for CPU-bound processing.
 201 | 
 202 | ### `createWorkerPool(size?): WorkerPool`
 203 | 
 204 | Create a worker pool for concurrent extraction.
 205 | 
 206 | ```typescript
 207 | import { createWorkerPool } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 208 | 
 209 | // Create pool with default size (number of CPU cores)
 210 | const pool = createWorkerPool();
 211 | 
 212 | // Create pool with specific size
 213 | const pool4 = createWorkerPool(4);
 214 | ```
 215 | 
 216 | **Parameters**:
 217 | - `size?: number` — Number of workers (defaults to CPU core count)
 218 | 
 219 | **Returns**: `WorkerPool` — Opaque handle for use with worker extraction functions
 220 | 
 221 | ### `extractFileInWorker(pool, filePath, mimeType?, config?): Promise<ExtractionResult>`
 222 | 
 223 | Extract a single file using a worker from the pool.
 224 | 
 225 | ```typescript
 226 | import { createWorkerPool, extractFileInWorker, closeWorkerPool } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 227 | 
 228 | const pool = createWorkerPool(4);
 229 | 
 230 | try {
 231 |   const files = ['doc1.pdf', 'doc2.docx', 'doc3.xlsx'];
 232 |   const results = await Promise.all(
 233 |     files.map(f => extractFileInWorker(pool, f))
 234 |   );
 235 | 
 236 |   results.forEach((r, i) => {
 237 |     console.log(`${files[i]}: ${r.content.substring(0, 100)}...`);
 238 |   });
 239 | } finally {
 240 |   await closeWorkerPool(pool);
 241 | }
 242 | ```
 243 | 
 244 | **Parameters**:
 245 | - `pool: WorkerPool` — Worker pool instance
 246 | - `filePath: string` — File path
 247 | - `mimeType?: string | null` — Optional MIME type
 248 | - `config?: ExtractionConfig` — Optional configuration
 249 | 
 250 | **Returns**: `Promise<ExtractionResult>`
 251 | 
 252 | ### `batchExtractFilesInWorker(pool, paths, config?): Promise<ExtractionResult[]>`
 253 | 
 254 | Extract multiple files using the worker pool for concurrent processing.
 255 | 
 256 | ```typescript
 257 | import { createWorkerPool, batchExtractFilesInWorker, closeWorkerPool } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 258 | 
 259 | const pool = createWorkerPool(4);
 260 | 
 261 | try {
 262 |   const files = ['invoice1.pdf', 'invoice2.pdf', 'invoice3.pdf'];
 263 |   const results = await batchExtractFilesInWorker(pool, files, {
 264 |     ocr: { backend: 'tesseract', language: 'eng' }
 265 |   });
 266 | 
 267 |   const total = results.reduce((sum, r) => sum + extractAmount(r.content), 0);
 268 |   console.log(`Total: $${total}`);
 269 | } finally {
 270 |   await closeWorkerPool(pool);
 271 | }
 272 | ```
 273 | 
 274 | **Parameters**:
 275 | - `pool: WorkerPool` — Worker pool instance
 276 | - `paths: string[]` — File paths
 277 | - `config?: ExtractionConfig` — Configuration (applied to all files)
 278 | 
 279 | **Returns**: `Promise<ExtractionResult[]>`
 280 | 
 281 | ### `getWorkerPoolStats(pool): WorkerPoolStats`
 282 | 
 283 | Get statistics about a worker pool.
 284 | 
 285 | ```typescript
 286 | import { createWorkerPool, getWorkerPoolStats } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 287 | 
 288 | const pool = createWorkerPool(4);
 289 | const stats = getWorkerPoolStats(pool);
 290 | 
 291 | console.log(`Pool size: ${stats.size}`);
 292 | console.log(`Active workers: ${stats.activeWorkers}`);
 293 | console.log(`Queued tasks: ${stats.queuedTasks}`);
 294 | ```
 295 | 
 296 | **Parameters**:
 297 | - `pool: WorkerPool` — Worker pool instance
 298 | 
 299 | **Returns**: `WorkerPoolStats`
 300 | 
 301 | ### `closeWorkerPool(pool): Promise<void>`
 302 | 
 303 | Close a worker pool and shut down all worker threads.
 304 | 
 305 | ```typescript
 306 | import { createWorkerPool, closeWorkerPool } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 307 | 
 308 | const pool = createWorkerPool(4);
 309 | 
 310 | try {
 311 |   // Use pool
 312 | } finally {
 313 |   await closeWorkerPool(pool);
 314 | }
 315 | ```
 316 | 
 317 | **Parameters**:
 318 | - `pool: WorkerPool` — Worker pool instance to close
 319 | 
 320 | **Returns**: `Promise<void>`
 321 | 
 322 | ---
 323 | 
 324 | ## Configuration Interface
 325 | 
 326 | ### `ExtractionConfig`
 327 | 
 328 | Main configuration object controlling extraction behavior.
 329 | 
 330 | ```typescript
 331 | interface ExtractionConfig {
 332 |   // Caching and processing
 333 |   useCache?: boolean;                            // Default: true
 334 |   enableQualityProcessing?: boolean;            // Default: false
 335 | 
 336 |   // OCR configuration
 337 |   ocr?: OcrConfig;                              // OCR settings
 338 |   forceOcr?: boolean;                           // Default: false
 339 | 
 340 |   // Document processing
 341 |   chunking?: ChunkingConfig;                    // Break into chunks
 342 |   images?: ImageExtractionConfig;               // Image extraction
 343 |   pdfOptions?: PdfConfig;                       // PDF-specific options
 344 |   tokenReduction?: TokenReductionConfig;        // Token optimization
 345 |   languageDetection?: LanguageDetectionConfig;  // Language detection
 346 |   postprocessor?: PostProcessorConfig;          // Post-processing
 347 |   htmlOptions?: HtmlConversionOptions;          // HTML conversion
 348 |   keywords?: KeywordConfig;                     // Keyword extraction
 349 |   pages?: PageExtractionConfig;                 // Page extraction
 350 | 
 351 |   // Output control
 352 |   maxConcurrentExtractions?: number;            // Default: 4
 353 |   outputFormat?: 'plain' | 'markdown' | 'djot' | 'html';  // Default: 'plain'
 354 |   resultFormat?: 'unified' | 'element_based';  // Default: 'unified'
 355 | }
 356 | ```
 357 | 
 358 | ### `ChunkingConfig`
 359 | 
 360 | Configuration for breaking documents into chunks (useful for RAG and vector databases).
 361 | 
 362 | ```typescript
 363 | interface ChunkingConfig {
 364 |   maxChars?: number;          // Max characters per chunk (default: 4096)
 365 |   maxOverlap?: number;        // Overlap between chunks (default: 512)
 366 |   chunkSize?: number;         // Alternative unit (mutually exclusive with maxChars)
 367 |   chunkOverlap?: number;      // Alternative unit (mutually exclusive with maxOverlap)
 368 |   preset?: string;            // Named preset ('default', 'aggressive', 'minimal')
 369 |   embedding?: Record<string, unknown>;  // Embedding config
 370 |   enabled?: boolean;          // Enable chunking (default: true when config provided)
 371 | }
 372 | ```
 373 | 
 374 | **Key Point**: Use `maxChars` and `maxOverlap`, NOT `maxCharacters` or `overlap`.
 375 | 
 376 | ### `OcrConfig`
 377 | 
 378 | Configuration for optical character recognition.
 379 | 
 380 | ```typescript
 381 | interface OcrConfig {
 382 |   backend: string;              // OCR backend name (e.g., 'tesseract')
 383 |   language?: string;            // Language code (e.g., 'eng', 'deu')
 384 |   tesseractConfig?: TesseractConfig;
 385 | }
 386 | 
 387 | interface TesseractConfig {
 388 |   psm?: number;                 // Page Segmentation Mode (0-13)
 389 |   enableTableDetection?: boolean;
 390 |   tesseditCharWhitelist?: string;  // Character whitelist
 391 | }
 392 | ```
 393 | 
 394 | ### `ImageExtractionConfig`
 395 | 
 396 | Configuration for extracting and optimizing images.
 397 | 
 398 | ```typescript
 399 | interface ImageExtractionConfig {
 400 |   extractImages?: boolean;      // Default: true
 401 |   targetDpi?: number;          // Target DPI (default: 150)
 402 |   maxImageDimension?: number;  // Max width/height in pixels (default: 2000)
 403 |   autoAdjustDpi?: boolean;     // Auto-adjust DPI (default: true)
 404 |   minDpi?: number;             // Minimum DPI (default: 72)
 405 |   maxDpi?: number;             // Maximum DPI (default: 300)
 406 | }
 407 | ```
 408 | 
 409 | ### `PdfConfig`
 410 | 
 411 | PDF-specific extraction options.
 412 | 
 413 | ```typescript
 414 | interface PdfConfig {
 415 |   extractImages?: boolean;      // Default: true
 416 |   passwords?: string[];         // Passwords for encrypted PDFs
 417 |   extractMetadata?: boolean;    // Default: true
 418 |   hierarchy?: HierarchyConfig;  // Hierarchy extraction
 419 | }
 420 | ```
 421 | 
 422 | ### `LanguageDetectionConfig`
 423 | 
 424 | Configuration for automatic language detection.
 425 | 
 426 | ```typescript
 427 | interface LanguageDetectionConfig {
 428 |   enabled?: boolean;            // Default: true
 429 |   minConfidence?: number;       // Threshold 0.0-1.0 (default: 0.5)
 430 |   detectMultiple?: boolean;     // Detect multiple languages (default: false)
 431 | }
 432 | ```
 433 | 
 434 | ### `TokenReductionConfig`
 435 | 
 436 | Configuration for optimizing token usage.
 437 | 
 438 | ```typescript
 439 | interface TokenReductionConfig {
 440 |   mode?: string;                // 'aggressive' or 'conservative' (default: 'conservative')
 441 |   preserveImportantWords?: boolean;  // Default: true
 442 | }
 443 | ```
 444 | 
 445 | ### `KeywordConfig`
 446 | 
 447 | Configuration for keyword extraction.
 448 | 
 449 | ```typescript
 450 | interface KeywordConfig {
 451 |   algorithm?: 'yake' | 'rake';  // Default: 'yake'
 452 |   maxKeywords?: number;         // Maximum keywords (default: 10)
 453 |   minScore?: number;            // Minimum relevance score (default: 0.1)
 454 |   ngramRange?: [number, number];  // N-gram range (default: [1, 3])
 455 |   language?: string;            // Language code (default: 'en')
 456 |   yakeParams?: YakeParams;
 457 |   rakeParams?: RakeParams;
 458 | }
 459 | ```
 460 | 
 461 | ### `PageExtractionConfig`
 462 | 
 463 | Configuration for page-level content tracking.
 464 | 
 465 | ```typescript
 466 | interface PageExtractionConfig {
 467 |   extractPages?: boolean;       // Extract as separate pages array
 468 |   insertPageMarkers?: boolean;  // Insert page markers in content
 469 |   markerFormat?: string;        // Marker format with {page_num} placeholder
 470 | }
 471 | ```
 472 | 
 473 | ### `HtmlConversionOptions`
 474 | 
 475 | Configuration for HTML to Markdown conversion.
 476 | 
 477 | ```typescript
 478 | interface HtmlConversionOptions {
 479 |   headingStyle?: 'atx' | 'underlined' | 'atx_closed';
 480 |   listIndentType?: 'spaces' | 'tabs';
 481 |   listIndentWidth?: number;
 482 |   bullets?: string;
 483 |   strongEmSymbol?: string;
 484 |   escapeAsterisks?: boolean;
 485 |   escapeUnderscores?: boolean;
 486 |   escapeMisc?: boolean;
 487 |   escapeAscii?: boolean;
 488 |   codeLanguage?: string;
 489 |   autolinks?: boolean;
 490 |   defaultTitle?: boolean;
 491 |   brInTables?: boolean;
 492 |   hocrSpatialTables?: boolean;
 493 |   highlightStyle?: 'double_equal' | 'html' | 'bold' | 'none';
 494 |   extractMetadata?: boolean;
 495 |   whitespaceMode?: 'normalized' | 'strict';
 496 |   stripNewlines?: boolean;
 497 |   wrap?: boolean;
 498 |   wrapWidth?: number;
 499 |   convertAsInline?: boolean;
 500 |   subSymbol?: string;
 501 |   supSymbol?: string;
 502 |   newlineStyle?: 'spaces' | 'backslash';
 503 |   codeBlockStyle?: 'indented' | 'backticks' | 'tildes';
 504 |   keepInlineImagesIn?: string[];
 505 |   encoding?: string;
 506 |   debug?: boolean;
 507 |   stripTags?: string[];
 508 |   preserveTags?: string[];
 509 |   preprocessing?: HtmlPreprocessingOptions;
 510 | }
 511 | ```
 512 | 
 513 | ---
 514 | 
 515 | ## Result Types
 516 | 
 517 | ### `ExtractionResult`
 518 | 
 519 | Complete extraction result from document processing.
 520 | 
 521 | ```typescript
 522 | interface ExtractionResult {
 523 |   // Main content
 524 |   content: string;
 525 | 
 526 |   // Document type
 527 |   mimeType: string;
 528 | 
 529 |   // Metadata (format-specific)
 530 |   metadata: Metadata;
 531 | 
 532 |   // Extracted structures
 533 |   tables: Table[];
 534 | 
 535 |   // Optional processed data
 536 |   detectedLanguages: string[] | null;
 537 |   chunks: Chunk[] | null;        // From chunking config
 538 |   images: ExtractedImage[] | null;  // From image extraction
 539 |   elements?: Element[] | null;   // From element_based result format
 540 |   pages?: PageContent[] | null;  // From page extraction
 541 |   extractedKeywords?: ExtractedKeyword[] | null;  // Extracted keywords with scores
 542 |   qualityScore?: number | null;  // Overall extraction quality (0.0-1.0)
 543 |   processingWarnings?: ProcessingWarning[];  // Non-fatal warnings from pipeline
 544 | }
 545 | ```
 546 | 
 547 | ### `Table`
 548 | 
 549 | Extracted table data with cell structure.
 550 | 
 551 | ```typescript
 552 | interface Table {
 553 |   cells: string[][];    // 2D array of cell contents (rows × columns)
 554 |   markdown: string;     // Markdown representation
 555 |   pageNumber: number;   // 1-indexed page number
 556 | }
 557 | ```
 558 | 
 559 | ### `Chunk`
 560 | 
 561 | Text chunk for RAG or vector database indexing.
 562 | 
 563 | ```typescript
 564 | interface Chunk {
 565 |   content: string;
 566 |   embedding?: number[] | null;  // Vector embedding if computed
 567 |   metadata: ChunkMetadata;
 568 | }
 569 | 
 570 | interface ChunkMetadata {
 571 |   byteStart: number;      // UTF-8 byte offset in original text
 572 |   byteEnd: number;        // UTF-8 byte offset
 573 |   tokenCount?: number | null;
 574 |   chunkIndex: number;     // Zero-based index
 575 |   totalChunks: number;    // Total number of chunks
 576 |   firstPage?: number | null;   // 1-indexed, if page tracking enabled
 577 |   lastPage?: number | null;
 578 | }
 579 | ```
 580 | 
 581 | ### `ExtractedImage`
 582 | 
 583 | Image extracted from document.
 584 | 
 585 | ```typescript
 586 | interface ExtractedImage {
 587 |   data: Uint8Array;      // Raw image bytes
 588 |   format: string;        // Format (e.g., 'png', 'jpeg', 'tiff')
 589 |   imageIndex: number;    // Sequential index (0-indexed)
 590 |   pageNumber?: number | null;
 591 |   width?: number | null;
 592 |   height?: number | null;
 593 |   colorspace?: string | null;
 594 |   bitsPerComponent?: number | null;
 595 |   isMask: boolean;
 596 |   description?: string | null;
 597 |   ocrResult?: ExtractionResult | null;  // OCR result if processed
 598 | }
 599 | ```
 600 | 
 601 | ### `PageContent`
 602 | 
 603 | Per-page content when page extraction is enabled.
 604 | 
 605 | ```typescript
 606 | interface PageContent {
 607 |   pageNumber: number;    // 1-indexed
 608 |   content: string;       // Page text content
 609 |   tables: Table[];       // Tables on this page
 610 |   images: ExtractedImage[];  // Images on this page
 611 | }
 612 | ```
 613 | 
 614 | ### `ExtractedKeyword`
 615 | 
 616 | Extracted keyword with relevance score and position information.
 617 | 
 618 | ```typescript
 619 | interface ExtractedKeyword {
 620 |   text: string;           // Keyword text
 621 |   score: number;          // Relevance score (0.0-1.0)
 622 |   algorithm: string;      // Algorithm used ("tfidf", "textrank", "yake", etc.)
 623 |   positions?: number[] | null;  // Character positions in content (if available)
 624 | }
 625 | ```
 626 | 
 627 | ### `ProcessingWarning`
 628 | 
 629 | Non-fatal warning encountered during document processing.
 630 | 
 631 | ```typescript
 632 | interface ProcessingWarning {
 633 |   source: string;         // Component that generated the warning
 634 |   message: string;        // Warning message describing the issue
 635 | }
 636 | ```
 637 | 
 638 | ### `Metadata`
 639 | 
 640 | Extraction result metadata (format-specific).
 641 | 
 642 | ```typescript
 643 | interface Metadata {
 644 |   // Common fields
 645 |   language?: string | null;
 646 |   date?: string | null;
 647 |   subject?: string | null;
 648 |   format_type?: 'pdf' | 'excel' | 'email' | 'pptx' | 'archive' | 'image' | 'xml' | 'text' | 'html' | 'ocr';
 649 | 
 650 |   // PDF metadata
 651 |   title?: string | null;
 652 |   author?: string | null;
 653 |   creator?: string | null;
 654 |   producer?: string | null;
 655 |   creation_date?: string | null;
 656 |   modification_date?: string | null;
 657 |   page_count?: number;
 658 | 
 659 |   // Excel metadata
 660 |   sheet_count?: number;
 661 |   sheet_names?: string[];
 662 | 
 663 |   // Email metadata
 664 |   from_email?: string | null;
 665 |   from_name?: string | null;
 666 |   to_emails?: string[];
 667 |   cc_emails?: string[];
 668 |   bcc_emails?: string[];
 669 |   message_id?: string | null;
 670 |   attachments?: string[];
 671 | 
 672 |   // Image metadata
 673 |   width?: number;
 674 |   height?: number;
 675 |   exif?: Record<string, string>;
 676 | 
 677 |   // OCR metadata
 678 |   psm?: number;
 679 |   output_format?: string;
 680 |   table_count?: number;
 681 | 
 682 |   // HTML metadata
 683 |   canonical_url?: string | null;
 684 |   html_language?: string | null;
 685 |   text_direction?: 'ltr' | 'rtl' | 'auto' | null;
 686 |   open_graph?: Record<string, string>;
 687 |   twitter_card?: Record<string, string>;
 688 |   meta_tags?: Record<string, string>;
 689 |   html_headers?: HeaderMetadata[];
 690 |   html_links?: LinkMetadata[];
 691 |   html_images?: HtmlImageMetadata[];
 692 |   structured_data?: StructuredData[];
 693 | 
 694 |   // Text metadata
 695 |   line_count?: number;
 696 |   word_count?: number;
 697 |   character_count?: number;
 698 |   headers?: string[] | null;
 699 |   links?: [string, string][] | null;
 700 |   code_blocks?: [string, string][] | null;
 701 | 
 702 |   // Page structure
 703 |   page_structure?: PageStructure | null;
 704 | 
 705 |   // Additional typed fields
 706 |   category?: string | null;
 707 |   tags?: string[];
 708 |   document_version?: string | null;
 709 |   abstract_text?: string | null;
 710 | 
 711 |   // Custom fields from postprocessors
 712 |   [key: string]: unknown;
 713 | }
 714 | ```
 715 | 
 716 | ---
 717 | 
 718 | ## Error Handling
 719 | 
 720 | ### Error Classes
 721 | 
 722 | ```typescript
 723 | import {
 724 |   KreuzbergError,
 725 |   ParsingError,
 726 |   OcrError,           // Note: camelCase, not "OCRError"
 727 |   ValidationError,
 728 |   MissingDependencyError,
 729 |   CacheError,
 730 |   ImageProcessingError,
 731 |   PluginError,
 732 |   ErrorCode,
 733 | } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 734 | ```
 735 | 
 736 | **Error Hierarchy**:
 737 | - `KreuzbergError` — Base class for all Kreuzberg errors
 738 |   - `ParsingError` — Document format invalid or corrupted
 739 |   - `OcrError` — OCR processing failed
 740 |   - `ValidationError` — Extraction validation failed
 741 |   - `MissingDependencyError` — Required dependency unavailable
 742 |   - `CacheError` — Cache operation failed
 743 |   - `ImageProcessingError` — Image extraction or processing failed
 744 |   - `PluginError` — Plugin registration or execution failed
 745 | 
 746 | ### Error Diagnostics
 747 | 
 748 | ```typescript
 749 | import {
 750 |   classifyError,
 751 |   getErrorCodeDescription,
 752 |   getErrorCodeName,
 753 |   getLastErrorCode,
 754 |   getLastPanicContext,
 755 | } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 756 | 
 757 | try {
 758 |   const result = await extractFile('document.pdf');
 759 | } catch (error) {
 760 |   const classification = classifyError(error.message);
 761 |   console.log(`Error code: ${getErrorCodeName(classification.code)}`);
 762 |   console.log(`Description: ${getErrorCodeDescription(classification.code)}`);
 763 |   console.log(`Confidence: ${classification.confidence}`);
 764 | }
 765 | ```
 766 | 
 767 | ### `ErrorCode` Enum
 768 | 
 769 | ```typescript
 770 | enum ErrorCode {
 771 |   Success = 0,
 772 |   GenericError = 1,
 773 |   Panic = 2,
 774 |   InvalidArgument = 3,
 775 |   IoError = 4,
 776 |   ParsingError = 5,
 777 |   OcrError = 6,
 778 |   MissingDependency = 7,
 779 | }
 780 | ```
 781 | 
 782 | ---
 783 | 
 784 | ## Plugin System
 785 | 
 786 | ### Post-Processors
 787 | 
 788 | Custom post-processors can enrich extraction results without failing the extraction if they encounter errors.
 789 | 
 790 | #### `registerPostProcessor(processor): void`
 791 | 
 792 | Register a custom post-processor.
 793 | 
 794 | ```typescript
 795 | import { registerPostProcessor, extractFile } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 796 | 
 797 | const processor = {
 798 |   name() {
 799 |     return 'my_processor';
 800 |   },
 801 | 
 802 |   async process(result) {
 803 |     // Enrich result with custom metadata
 804 |     result.metadata['custom_field'] = 'value';
 805 |     return result;
 806 |   },
 807 | 
 808 |   processingStage() {
 809 |     return 'late';  // 'early', 'middle', or 'late'
 810 |   },
 811 | 
 812 |   async initialize() {
 813 |     // Called once when registered
 814 |   },
 815 | 
 816 |   async shutdown() {
 817 |     // Called when unregistered
 818 |   },
 819 | };
 820 | 
 821 | registerPostProcessor(processor);
 822 | const result = await extractFile('document.pdf');
 823 | ```
 824 | 
 825 | #### `unregisterPostProcessor(name): void`
 826 | 
 827 | Remove a registered post-processor.
 828 | 
 829 | ```typescript
 830 | import { unregisterPostProcessor } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 831 | 
 832 | unregisterPostProcessor('my_processor');
 833 | ```
 834 | 
 835 | #### `listPostProcessors(): string[]`
 836 | 
 837 | List all registered post-processor names.
 838 | 
 839 | ```typescript
 840 | import { listPostProcessors } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 841 | 
 842 | const processors = listPostProcessors();
 843 | console.log('Registered processors:', processors);
 844 | ```
 845 | 
 846 | #### `clearPostProcessors(): void`
 847 | 
 848 | Unregister all post-processors.
 849 | 
 850 | ```typescript
 851 | import { clearPostProcessors } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 852 | 
 853 | clearPostProcessors();
 854 | ```
 855 | 
 856 | ### Validators
 857 | 
 858 | Custom validators check extraction results and fail the extraction if validation fails (unlike post-processors).
 859 | 
 860 | #### `registerValidator(validator): void`
 861 | 
 862 | Register a custom validator.
 863 | 
 864 | ```typescript
 865 | import { registerValidator, extractFile } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 866 | 
 867 | const validator = {
 868 |   name() {
 869 |     return 'content_length_validator';
 870 |   },
 871 | 
 872 |   validate(result) {
 873 |     if (result.content.length < 10) {
 874 |       throw new Error('Content too short');
 875 |     }
 876 |   },
 877 | 
 878 |   priority() {
 879 |     return 100;  // Higher = runs first
 880 |   },
 881 | 
 882 |   shouldValidate(result) {
 883 |     return result.mimeType === 'application/pdf';  // Conditional validation
 884 |   },
 885 | 
 886 |   async initialize() {
 887 |     // Called once when registered
 888 |   },
 889 | 
 890 |   async shutdown() {
 891 |     // Called when unregistered
 892 |   },
 893 | };
 894 | 
 895 | registerValidator(validator);
 896 | const result = await extractFile('document.pdf');
 897 | ```
 898 | 
 899 | #### `unregisterValidator(name): void`
 900 | 
 901 | Remove a registered validator.
 902 | 
 903 | ```typescript
 904 | import { unregisterValidator } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 905 | 
 906 | unregisterValidator('content_length_validator');
 907 | ```
 908 | 
 909 | #### `listValidators(): string[]`
 910 | 
 911 | List all registered validator names.
 912 | 
 913 | ```typescript
 914 | import { listValidators } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 915 | 
 916 | const validators = listValidators();
 917 | ```
 918 | 
 919 | #### `clearValidators(): void`
 920 | 
 921 | Unregister all validators.
 922 | 
 923 | ```typescript
 924 | import { clearValidators } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 925 | 
 926 | clearValidators();
 927 | ```
 928 | 
 929 | ### OCR Backends
 930 | 
 931 | Custom OCR backends can be registered to handle image text extraction.
 932 | 
 933 | #### `registerOcrBackend(backend): void`
 934 | 
 935 | Register a custom OCR backend.
 936 | 
 937 | ```typescript
 938 | import { registerOcrBackend, extractFile } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 939 | 
 940 | const backend = {
 941 |   name() {
 942 |     return 'my-ocr';
 943 |   },
 944 | 
 945 |   supportedLanguages() {
 946 |     return ['eng', 'deu', 'fra'];
 947 |   },
 948 | 
 949 |   async processImage(imageBytes, language) {
 950 |     // imageBytes: Uint8Array or Base64 string
 951 |     const buffer = typeof imageBytes === 'string'
 952 |       ? Buffer.from(imageBytes, 'base64')
 953 |       : Buffer.from(imageBytes);
 954 | 
 955 |     // Process and extract text
 956 |     return {
 957 |       content: 'extracted text',
 958 |       mime_type: 'text/plain',
 959 |       metadata: { confidence: 0.95, language },
 960 |       tables: [],
 961 |     };
 962 |   },
 963 | 
 964 |   async initialize() {
 965 |     // Load models, setup resources
 966 |   },
 967 | 
 968 |   async shutdown() {
 969 |     // Cleanup resources
 970 |   },
 971 | };
 972 | 
 973 | registerOcrBackend(backend);
 974 | ```
 975 | 
 976 | #### `GutenOcrBackend`
 977 | 
 978 | Built-in OCR backend implementation using Guten-OCR.
 979 | 
 980 | ```typescript
 981 | import { GutenOcrBackend, registerOcrBackend, extractFile } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 982 | 
 983 | const backend = new GutenOcrBackend();
 984 | await backend.initialize();
 985 | registerOcrBackend(backend);
 986 | 
 987 | const result = await extractFile('scanned.pdf', null, {
 988 |   ocr: { backend: 'guten-ocr', language: 'eng' }
 989 | });
 990 | ```
 991 | 
 992 | #### `unregisterOcrBackend(name): void`
 993 | 
 994 | Remove a registered OCR backend.
 995 | 
 996 | ```typescript
 997 | import { unregisterOcrBackend } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 998 | 
 999 | unregisterOcrBackend('my-ocr');
1000 | ```
1001 | 
1002 | #### `listOcrBackends(): string[]`
1003 | 
1004 | List all registered OCR backend names.
1005 | 
1006 | ```typescript
1007 | import { listOcrBackends } from '@kreuzberg/node';
1008 | 
1009 | const backends = listOcrBackends();
1010 | ```
1011 | 
1012 | #### `clearOcrBackends(): void`
1013 | 
1014 | Unregister all OCR backends.
1015 | 
1016 | ```typescript
1017 | import { clearOcrBackends } from '@kreuzberg/node';
1018 | 
1019 | clearOcrBackends();
1020 | ```
1021 | 
1022 | ---
1023 | 
1024 | ## MIME Type Utilities
1025 | 
1026 | ### `detectMimeType(data): string | null`
1027 | 
1028 | Detect MIME type from file content (magic bytes).
1029 | 
1030 | ```typescript
1031 | import { detectMimeType } from '@kreuzberg/node';
1032 | import { readFileSync } from 'fs';
1033 | 
1034 | const data = readFileSync('document');
1035 | const mimeType = detectMimeType(data);
1036 | console.log(`Detected MIME type: ${mimeType}`);
1037 | ```
1038 | 
1039 | ### `detectMimeTypeFromPath(filePath): string | null`
1040 | 
1041 | Detect MIME type from file extension.
1042 | 
1043 | ```typescript
1044 | import { detectMimeTypeFromPath } from '@kreuzberg/node';
1045 | 
1046 | const mimeType = detectMimeTypeFromPath('document.pdf');
1047 | console.log(`MIME type: ${mimeType}`);  // 'application/pdf'
1048 | ```
1049 | 
1050 | ### `getExtensionsForMime(mimeType): string[]`
1051 | 
1052 | Get file extensions for a MIME type.
1053 | 
1054 | ```typescript
1055 | import { getExtensionsForMime } from '@kreuzberg/node';
1056 | 
1057 | const extensions = getExtensionsForMime('application/pdf');
1058 | console.log(`Extensions: ${extensions}`);  // ['.pdf']
1059 | ```
1060 | 
1061 | ### `validateMimeType(mimeType): boolean`
1062 | 
1063 | Check if a MIME type is valid.
1064 | 
1065 | ```typescript
1066 | import { validateMimeType } from '@kreuzberg/node';
1067 | 
1068 | if (validateMimeType('application/pdf')) {
1069 |   console.log('Valid MIME type');
1070 | }
1071 | ```
1072 | 
1073 | ---
1074 | 
1075 | ## Configuration Loading
1076 | 
1077 | ### `ExtractionConfig.fromFile(filePath): ExtractionConfig`
1078 | 
1079 | Load extraction configuration from a file (JSON, YAML, or TOML).
1080 | 
1081 | ```typescript
1082 | import { ExtractionConfig, extractFile } from '@kreuzberg/node';
1083 | 
1084 | const config = ExtractionConfig.fromFile('./kreuzberg.toml');
1085 | const result = await extractFile('document.pdf', null, config);
1086 | ```
1087 | 
1088 | ### `ExtractionConfig.discover(): ExtractionConfig | null`
1089 | 
1090 | Auto-discover extraction configuration file in current and parent directories.
1091 | 
1092 | ```typescript
1093 | import { ExtractionConfig, extractFile } from '@kreuzberg/node';
1094 | 
1095 | // Searches for kreuzberg.{toml,yaml,json} in current directory and parents
1096 | const config = ExtractionConfig.discover();
1097 | if (config) {
1098 |   const result = await extractFile('document.pdf', null, config);
1099 | }
1100 | ```
1101 | 
1102 | ---
1103 | 
1104 | ## Embeddings
1105 | 
1106 | ### `getEmbeddingPreset(name): EmbeddingPreset | null`
1107 | 
1108 | Get a named embedding model preset.
1109 | 
1110 | ```typescript
1111 | import { getEmbeddingPreset } from '@kreuzberg/node';
1112 | 
1113 | const preset = getEmbeddingPreset('default');
1114 | if (preset) {
1115 |   console.log(`Model: ${preset.modelName}`);
1116 |   console.log(`Dimensions: ${preset.dimensions}`);
1117 | }
1118 | ```
1119 | 
1120 | ### `listEmbeddingPresets(): string[]`
1121 | 
1122 | List all available embedding presets.
1123 | 
1124 | ```typescript
1125 | import { listEmbeddingPresets } from '@kreuzberg/node';
1126 | 
1127 | const presets = listEmbeddingPresets();
1128 | console.log('Available presets:', presets);
1129 | ```
1130 | 
1131 | ### `EmbeddingPreset`
1132 | 
1133 | Type definition for embedding model presets.
1134 | 
1135 | ```typescript
1136 | interface EmbeddingPreset {
1137 |   name: string;           // Preset name (e.g., "fast", "balanced", "quality", "multilingual")
1138 |   chunkSize: number;      // Recommended chunk size in characters
1139 |   overlap: number;        // Recommended overlap in characters
1140 |   modelName: string;      // Model identifier (e.g., "AllMiniLML6V2Q", "BGEBaseENV15")
1141 |   dimensions: number;     // Embedding vector dimensions
1142 |   description: string;    // Human-readable description
1143 | }
1144 | ```
1145 | 
1146 | ---
1147 | 
1148 | ## Plugin Protocols
1149 | 
1150 | ### `PostProcessorProtocol`
1151 | 
1152 | Interface for custom post-processors.
1153 | 
1154 | ```typescript
1155 | interface PostProcessorProtocol {
1156 |   name(): string;
1157 | 
1158 |   process(result: ExtractionResult): ExtractionResult | Promise<ExtractionResult>;
1159 | 
1160 |   processingStage?(): ProcessingStage;  // 'early' | 'middle' | 'late'
1161 | 
1162 |   initialize?(): void | Promise<void>;
1163 | 
1164 |   shutdown?(): void | Promise<void>;
1165 | }
1166 | ```
1167 | 
1168 | ### `ValidatorProtocol`
1169 | 
1170 | Interface for custom validators.
1171 | 
1172 | ```typescript
1173 | interface ValidatorProtocol {
1174 |   name(): string;
1175 | 
1176 |   validate(result: ExtractionResult): void | Promise<void>;
1177 | 
1178 |   priority?(): number;  // Higher = runs first
1179 | 
1180 |   shouldValidate?(result: ExtractionResult): boolean;
1181 | 
1182 |   initialize?(): void | Promise<void>;
1183 | 
1184 |   shutdown?(): void | Promise<void>;
1185 | }
1186 | ```
1187 | 
1188 | ### `OcrBackendProtocol`
1189 | 
1190 | Interface for custom OCR backends.
1191 | 
1192 | ```typescript
1193 | interface OcrBackendProtocol {
1194 |   name(): string;
1195 | 
1196 |   supportedLanguages(): string[];
1197 | 
1198 |   processImage(
1199 |     imageBytes: Uint8Array | string,
1200 |     language: string,
1201 |   ): Promise<{
1202 |     content: string;
1203 |     mime_type: string;
1204 |     metadata: Record<string, unknown>;
1205 |     tables: unknown[];
1206 |   }>;
1207 | 
1208 |   initialize?(): void | Promise<void>;
1209 | 
1210 |   shutdown?(): void | Promise<void>;
1211 | }
1212 | ```
1213 | 
1214 | ---
1215 | 
1216 | ## Supported Document Formats
1217 | 
1218 | - **Documents**: PDF, DOCX, PPTX, XLSX, DOC, PPT
1219 | - **Text**: Markdown, Plain Text, XML, JSON, YAML, TOML
1220 | - **Web**: HTML (converted to Markdown)
1221 | - **Email**: EML, MSG
1222 | - **Images**: PNG, JPEG, TIFF (with OCR support)
1223 | - **Archives**: ZIP, TAR, GZIP (file listing)
1224 |

1275 |   // ... and many more
1276 | };
1277 | ```
1278 | 
1279 | ---
1280 | 
1281 | ## Best Practices
1282 | 
1283 | 1. **Use batch APIs for multiple documents**: `batchExtractFiles()` provides superior performance vs. calling `extractFile()` in a loop.
1284 | 
1285 | 2. **Enable chunking for RAG/vector DB**: Set `chunking` config to automatically break documents into overlapping chunks.
1286 | 
1287 | 3. **Use worker pools for high-concurrency scenarios**: Distribute CPU-bound work across multiple threads for 4+ concurrent extractions.
1288 | 
1289 | 4. **Configure language detection**: Enable automatic language detection for multilingual documents.
1290 | 
1291 | 5. **Register validators early**: Set up validators before calling extraction functions to catch quality issues immediately.
1292 | 
1293 | 6. **Use specific MIME types**: Provide explicit MIME types when available to avoid detection overhead.
1294 | 
1295 | 7. **Clean up resources**: Always call `closeWorkerPool()` when done to prevent resource leaks.
1296 | 
1297 | 8. **Handle extraction errors gracefully**: Catch specific error types (`ParsingError`, `OcrError`, etc.) for appropriate error handling.
1298 | 
1299 | ---
1300 | 
1301 | ## Version
1302 | 
1303 | **Package Version**: 4.2.14
```
