```markdown
   1 | # Language Bindings Reference
   2 | 
   3 | Kreuzberg provides native bindings for multiple programming languages, each with precompiled binaries for x86_64 and aarch64 on Linux and macOS. This reference covers installation and basic usage for each binding.
   4 | 
   5 | ## Go
   6 | 
   7 | **Installation:**
   8 | ```bash
   9 | go get github.com/kreuzberg-dev/kreuzberg/packages/go/v4
  10 | ```
  11 | 
  12 | **Basic Extraction:**
  13 | ```go
  14 | package main
  15 | 
  16 | import (
  17 |     "context"
  18 |     "fmt"
  19 |     "github.com/kreuzberg-dev/kreuzberg/packages/go/v4/kreuzberg"
  20 | )
  21 | 
  22 | func main() {
  23 |     ctx := context.Background()
  24 |     result, err := kreuzberg.ExtractFile(ctx, "document.pdf", nil)
  25 |     if err != nil {
  26 |         panic(err)
  27 |     }
  28 |     fmt.Println(result.Content)
  29 | }
  30 | ```
  31 | 
  32 | See the [Go binding documentation](https://github.com/kreuzberg-dev/kreuzberg/tree/main/packages/go) for complete API reference.
  33 | 
  34 | ## Ruby
  35 | 
  36 | **Installation:**
  37 | ```bash
  38 | gem install kreuzberg
  39 | ```
  40 | 
  41 | Or in your Gemfile:
  42 | ```ruby
  43 | gem 'kreuzberg'
  44 | ```
  45 | 
  46 | **Basic Extraction:**
  47 | ```ruby
  48 | require 'kreuzberg'
  49 | 
  50 | result = Kreuzberg.extract_file_sync('document.pdf')
  51 | puts result.content
  52 | ```
  53 | 
  54 | See the [Ruby binding documentation](https://github.com/kreuzberg-dev/kreuzberg/tree/main/packages/ruby) for complete API reference.
  55 | 
  56 | ## Java
  57 | 
  58 | **Installation:**
  59 | Add to your Maven `pom.xml`:
  60 | ```xml
  61 | <dependency>
  62 |     <groupId>dev.kreuzberg</groupId>
  63 |     <artifactId>kreuzberg</artifactId>
  64 |     <version>4.2.x</version>
  65 | </dependency>
  66 | ```
  67 | 
  68 | **Basic Extraction:**
  69 | ```java
  70 | import dev.kreuzberg.Kreuzberg;
  71 | import dev.kreuzberg.ExtractionResult;
  72 | 
  73 | public class Example {
  74 |     public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
  75 |         ExtractionResult result = Kreuzberg.extractFile("document.pdf");
  76 |         System.out.println(result.getContent());
  77 |     }
  78 | }
  79 | ```
  80 | 
  81 | See the [Java binding documentation](https://github.com/kreuzberg-dev/kreuzberg/tree/main/packages/java) for complete API reference.
  82 | 
  83 | ## C#
  84 | 
  85 | **Installation:**
  86 | ```bash
  87 | dotnet add package Kreuzberg
  88 | ```
  89 | 
  90 | **Basic Extraction:**
  91 | ```csharp
  92 | using Kreuzberg;
  93 | 
  94 | var result = KreuzbergClient.ExtractFileSync("document.pdf");
  95 | Console.WriteLine(result.Content);
  96 | ```
  97 | 
  98 | See the [C# binding documentation](https://github.com/kreuzberg-dev/kreuzberg/tree/main/packages/csharp) for complete API reference.
  99 | 
 100 | ## PHP
 101 | 
 102 | **Installation:**
 103 | ```bash
 104 | composer require kreuzberg/kreuzberg
 105 | ```
 106 | 
 107 | **Basic Extraction:**
 108 | ```php
 109 | <?php
 110 | require 'vendor/autoload.php';
 111 | 
 112 | use Kreuzberg\Kreuzberg;
 113 | 
 114 | $kreuzberg = new Kreuzberg();
 115 | $result = $kreuzberg->extractFile('document.pdf');
 116 | echo $result->content;
 117 | ```
 118 | 
 119 | See the [PHP binding documentation](https://github.com/kreuzberg-dev/kreuzberg/tree/main/packages/php) for complete API reference.
 120 | 
 121 | ## Elixir
 122 | 
 123 | **Installation:**
 124 | Add to your `mix.exs` dependencies:
 125 | ```elixir
 126 | def deps do
 127 |   [
 128 |     kreuzberg: "~> 4.2"
 129 |   ]
 130 | end
 131 | ```
 132 | 
 133 | **Basic Extraction:**
 134 | ```elixir
 135 | {:ok, result} = Kreuzberg.extract_file("document.pdf")
 136 | IO.puts(result.content)
 137 | ```
 138 | 
 139 | See the [Elixir binding documentation](https://github.com/kreuzberg-dev/kreuzberg/tree/main/packages/elixir) for complete API reference.
 140 | 
 141 | ## WebAssembly (WASM)
 142 | 
 143 | **Installation:**
 144 | ```bash
 145 | npm install @kreuzberg/wasm
 146 | ```
 147 | 
 148 | **Basic Extraction:**
 149 | ```typescript
 150 | import { extractBytes } from '@kreuzberg/wasm';
 151 | 
 152 | const fileData = await fs.promises.readFile('document.pdf');
 153 | const result = await extractBytes(fileData, 'application/pdf');
 154 | console.log(result.content);
 155 | ```
 156 | 
 157 | Supports browsers, Deno, and Cloudflare Workers.
 158 | 
 159 | See the [WASM binding documentation](https://github.com/kreuzberg-dev/kreuzberg/tree/main/packages/typescript) for complete API reference.
 160 | 
 161 | ## Docker
 162 | 
 163 | **Installation:**
 164 | Pull the official image from GitHub Container Registry:
 165 | ```bash
 166 | docker pull ghcr.io/kreuzberg-dev/kreuzberg
 167 | ```
 168 | 
 169 | **API Server Mode:**
 170 | ```bash
 171 | docker run -p 8000:8000 ghcr.io/kreuzberg-dev/kreuzberg serve --host 0.0.0.0
 172 | ```
 173 | 
 174 | **CLI Mode:**
 175 | ```bash
 176 | docker run -v $(pwd):/data ghcr.io/kreuzberg-dev/kreuzberg extract /data/document.pdf
 177 | ```
 178 | 
 179 | **MCP Server Mode:**
 180 | ```bash
 181 | docker run -i ghcr.io/kreuzberg-dev/kreuzberg mcp
 182 | ```
 183 | 
 184 | Image sizes:
 185 | - Core image: 1.0-1.3GB
 186 | - Full image: ~1.0-1.3GB
 187 | 
 188 | See the [Docker guide](https://docs.kreuzberg.dev/guides/docker/) for deployment details.
 189 | 
 190 | ## Platform Support
 191 | 
 192 | All language bindings include precompiled binaries for x86_64 and aarch64 on Linux and macOS. Windows support varies by binding. Refer to the main [README](https://github.com/kreuzberg-dev/kreuzberg) for platform compatibility matrix.
```

### File: `skills\kreuzberg\references\python-api.md`

- Size: 41681 bytes
- Modified: SystemTime { intervals: 134176840065617604 }

```markdown
   1 | # Kreuzberg Python API Reference
   2 | 
   3 | Comprehensive documentation for the Kreuzberg Python API. All extraction logic and heavy lifting is implemented in high-performance Rust, with Python adding OCR backends (EasyOCR, PaddleOCR) and custom post-processor support.
   4 | 
   5 | ## Extraction Functions
   6 | 
   7 | ### Synchronous File Extraction
   8 | 
   9 | ```python
  10 | def extract_file_sync(
  11 |     file_path: str | Path,
  12 |     mime_type: str | None = None,
  13 |     config: ExtractionConfig | None = None,
  14 |     *,
  15 |     easyocr_kwargs: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
  16 |     paddleocr_kwargs: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
  17 | ) -> ExtractionResult
  18 | ```
  19 | 
  20 | Extract content from a file (synchronous).
  21 | 
  22 | **Parameters:**
  23 | - `file_path` (str | Path): Path to the file
  24 | - `mime_type` (str | None): Optional MIME type hint (auto-detected if None)
  25 | - `config` (ExtractionConfig | None): Extraction configuration (uses defaults if None)
  26 | - `easyocr_kwargs` (dict | None): EasyOCR initialization options (languages, use_gpu, beam_width, etc.)
  27 | - `paddleocr_kwargs` (dict | None): PaddleOCR initialization options (lang, use_angle_cls, show_log, etc.)
  28 | 
  29 | **Returns:** ExtractionResult with content, metadata, and tables
  30 | 
  31 | **Example:**
  32 | 
  33 | ```python
  34 | from kreuzberg import extract_file_sync, ExtractionConfig, OcrConfig, TesseractConfig
  35 | 
  36 | # Basic usage
  37 | result = extract_file_sync("document.pdf")
  38 | 
  39 | # With Tesseract configuration
  40 | config = ExtractionConfig(
  41 |     ocr=OcrConfig(
  42 |         backend="tesseract",
  43 |         language="eng",
  44 |         tesseract_config=TesseractConfig(psm=6, enable_table_detection=True),
  45 |     )
  46 | )
  47 | result = extract_file_sync("invoice.pdf", config=config)
  48 | 
  49 | # With EasyOCR custom options
  50 | config = ExtractionConfig(ocr=OcrConfig(backend="easyocr", language="eng"))
  51 | result = extract_file_sync("scanned.pdf", config=config, easyocr_kwargs={"use_gpu": True})
  52 | ```
  53 | 
  54 | ### Asynchronous File Extraction
  55 | 
  56 | ```python
  57 | async def extract_file(
  58 |     file_path: str | Path,
  59 |     mime_type: str | None = None,
  60 |     config: ExtractionConfig | None = None,
  61 |     *,
  62 |     easyocr_kwargs: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
  63 |     paddleocr_kwargs: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
  64 | ) -> ExtractionResult
  65 | ```
  66 | 
  67 | Extract content from a file (asynchronous). Same parameters and behavior as `extract_file_sync`.
  68 | 
  69 | ### Synchronous Bytes Extraction
  70 | 
  71 | ```python
  72 | def extract_bytes_sync(
  73 |     data: bytes | bytearray,
  74 |     mime_type: str,
  75 |     config: ExtractionConfig | None = None,
  76 |     *,
  77 |     easyocr_kwargs: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
  78 |     paddleocr_kwargs: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
  79 | ) -> ExtractionResult
  80 | ```
  81 | 
  82 | Extract content from bytes (synchronous).
  83 | 
  84 | **Parameters:**
  85 | - `data` (bytes | bytearray): File content as bytes or bytearray
  86 | - `mime_type` (str): MIME type of the data (required for format detection)
  87 | - `config` (ExtractionConfig | None): Extraction configuration
  88 | - `easyocr_kwargs` (dict | None): EasyOCR initialization options
  89 | - `paddleocr_kwargs` (dict | None): PaddleOCR initialization options
  90 | 
  91 | **Returns:** ExtractionResult with content, metadata, and tables
  92 | 
  93 | ### Asynchronous Bytes Extraction
  94 | 
  95 | ```python
  96 | async def extract_bytes(
  97 |     data: bytes | bytearray,
  98 |     mime_type: str,
  99 |     config: ExtractionConfig | None = None,
 100 |     *,
 101 |     easyocr_kwargs: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
 102 |     paddleocr_kwargs: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
 103 | ) -> ExtractionResult
 104 | ```
 105 | 
 106 | Extract content from bytes (asynchronous). Same parameters and behavior as `extract_bytes_sync`.
 107 | 
 108 | ### Batch File Extraction
 109 | 
 110 | ```python
 111 | async def batch_extract_files(
 112 |     paths: list[str | Path],
 113 |     config: ExtractionConfig | None = None,
 114 |     *,
 115 |     easyocr_kwargs: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
 116 |     paddleocr_kwargs: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
 117 | ) -> list[ExtractionResult]
 118 | ```
 119 | 
 120 | Extract content from multiple files in parallel (asynchronous).
 121 | 
 122 | **Parameters:**
 123 | - `paths` (list[str | Path]): List of file paths
 124 | - `config` (ExtractionConfig | None): Extraction configuration
 125 | - `easyocr_kwargs` (dict | None): EasyOCR initialization options
 126 | - `paddleocr_kwargs` (dict | None): PaddleOCR initialization options
 127 | 
 128 | **Returns:** List of ExtractionResults (one per file)
 129 | 
 130 | ### Batch File Extraction (Synchronous)
 131 | 
 132 | ```python
 133 | def batch_extract_files_sync(
 134 |     paths: list[str | Path],
 135 |     config: ExtractionConfig | None = None,
 136 |     *,
 137 |     easyocr_kwargs: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
 138 |     paddleocr_kwargs: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
 139 | ) -> list[ExtractionResult]
 140 | ```
 141 | 
 142 | Extract content from multiple files in parallel (synchronous).
 143 | 
 144 | ### Batch Bytes Extraction
 145 | 
 146 | ```python
 147 | async def batch_extract_bytes(
 148 |     data_list: list[bytes | bytearray],
 149 |     mime_types: list[str],
 150 |     config: ExtractionConfig | None = None,
 151 |     *,
 152 |     easyocr_kwargs: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
 153 |     paddleocr_kwargs: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
 154 | ) -> list[ExtractionResult]
 155 | ```
 156 | 
 157 | Extract content from multiple byte arrays in parallel (asynchronous).
 158 | 
 159 | **Parameters:**
 160 | - `data_list` (list[bytes | bytearray]): List of file contents as bytes/bytearray
 161 | - `mime_types` (list[str]): List of MIME types (one per data item)
 162 | - `config` (ExtractionConfig | None): Extraction configuration
 163 | - `easyocr_kwargs` (dict | None): EasyOCR initialization options
 164 | - `paddleocr_kwargs` (dict | None): PaddleOCR initialization options
 165 | 
 166 | **Returns:** List of ExtractionResults (one per data item)
 167 | 
 168 | ### Batch Bytes Extraction (Synchronous)
 169 | 
 170 | ```python
 171 | def batch_extract_bytes_sync(
 172 |     data_list: list[bytes | bytearray],
 173 |     mime_types: list[str],
 174 |     config: ExtractionConfig | None = None,
 175 |     *,
 176 |     easyocr_kwargs: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
 177 |     paddleocr_kwargs: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
 178 | ) -> list[ExtractionResult]
 179 | ```
 180 | 
 181 | Extract content from multiple byte arrays in parallel (synchronous).
 182 | 
 183 | ## Configuration Classes
 184 | 
 185 | ### ExtractionConfig
 186 | 
 187 | Main extraction configuration for document processing. All attributes are optional and use sensible defaults when not specified.
 188 | 
 189 | **Attributes:**
 190 | 
 191 | | Field | Type | Default | Description |
 192 | |-------|------|---------|-------------|
 193 | | `use_cache` | bool | True | Enable caching of extraction results to improve performance on repeated extractions |
 194 | | `enable_quality_processing` | bool | True | Enable quality post-processing to clean and normalize extracted text |
 195 | | `ocr` | OcrConfig \| None | None | OCR configuration for extracting text from images. None = OCR disabled |
 196 | | `force_ocr` | bool | False | Force OCR processing even for searchable PDFs that contain extractable text |
 197 | | `chunking` | ChunkingConfig \| None | None | Text chunking configuration for dividing content into manageable chunks. None = disabled |
 198 | | `images` | ImageExtractionConfig \| None | None | Image extraction configuration for extracting images FROM documents. None = no extraction |
 199 | | `pdf_options` | PdfConfig \| None | None | PDF-specific options like password handling and metadata extraction |
 200 | | `token_reduction` | TokenReductionConfig \| None | None | Token reduction configuration for reducing token count in extracted content |
 201 | | `language_detection` | LanguageDetectionConfig \| None | None | Language detection configuration for identifying document language(s) |
 202 | | `keywords` | KeywordConfig \| None | None | Keyword extraction configuration for identifying important terms and phrases |
 203 | | `postprocessor` | PostProcessorConfig \| None | None | Post-processor configuration for custom text processing |
 204 | | `max_concurrent_extractions` | int \| None | num_cpus * 2 | Maximum concurrent extractions in batch operations |
 205 | | `html_options` | HtmlConversionOptions \| None | None | HTML conversion options for converting documents to markdown |
 206 | | `pages` | PageConfig \| None | None | Page extraction configuration for tracking page boundaries |
 207 | | `security_limits` | dict[str, int] \| None | None | Security limits configuration |
 208 | | `result_format` | str | "unified" | Result format: "unified" or "element_based" |
 209 | | `output_format` | str | "plain" | Output content format: "plain", "markdown", "djot", or "html" |
 210 | 
 211 | **Example:**
 212 | 
 213 | ```python
 214 | from kreuzberg import ExtractionConfig, ChunkingConfig, OcrConfig
 215 | 
 216 | # Basic extraction with defaults
 217 | config = ExtractionConfig()
 218 | 
 219 | # Enable chunking with 512-char chunks and 100-char overlap
 220 | config = ExtractionConfig(chunking=ChunkingConfig(max_chars=512, max_overlap=100))
 221 | 
 222 | # Enable OCR with Tesseract
 223 | config = ExtractionConfig(ocr=OcrConfig(backend="tesseract", language="eng"))
 224 | 
 225 | # Multiple options
 226 | config = ExtractionConfig(
 227 |     use_cache=True,
 228 |     enable_quality_processing=True,
 229 |     output_format="markdown",
 230 |     result_format="unified"
 231 | )
 232 | ```
 233 | 
 234 | ### OcrConfig
 235 | 
 236 | OCR configuration for extracting text from images.
 237 | 
 238 | **Attributes:**
 239 | 
 240 | | Field | Type | Default | Description |
 241 | |-------|------|---------|-------------|
 242 | | `backend` | str | "tesseract" | OCR backend: "tesseract", "easyocr", or "paddleocr" |
 243 | | `language` | str | "eng" | Language code (ISO 639-3 three-letter: "eng", "deu", "fra" or ISO 639-1 two-letter: "en", "de", "fr") |
 244 | | `tesseract_config` | TesseractConfig \| None | None | Tesseract-specific configuration (only used when backend="tesseract") |
 245 | 
 246 | **Example:**
 247 | 
 248 | ```python
 249 | from kreuzberg import OcrConfig
 250 | 
 251 | # Tesseract with German language
 252 | config = OcrConfig(backend="tesseract", language="deu")
 253 | 
 254 | # EasyOCR for faster recognition
 255 | config = OcrConfig(backend="easyocr", language="eng")
 256 | 
 257 | # PaddleOCR for production deployments
 258 | config = OcrConfig(backend="paddleocr", language="chi_sim")
 259 | ```
 260 | 
 261 | ### TesseractConfig
 262 | 
 263 | Detailed Tesseract OCR configuration for advanced tuning. Fine-tune Tesseract OCR behavior for specific document types and quality levels.
 264 | 
 265 | **Attributes:**
 266 | 
 267 | | Field | Type | Default | Description |
 268 | |-------|------|---------|-------------|
 269 | | `language` | str | "eng" | OCR language (ISO 639-3 three-letter code) |
 270 | | `psm` | int | 3 | Page Segmentation Mode: 0 (detection only), 3 (auto), 6 (uniform block), 11 (sparse text) |
 271 | | `output_format` | str | "markdown" | Output format for OCR results |
 272 | | `oem` | int | 3 | OCR Engine Mode: 0 (legacy), 1 (LSTM), 2 (both), 3 (auto) |
 273 | | `min_confidence` | float | 0.0 | Minimum confidence threshold (0.0-1.0) for accepting OCR results |
 274 | | `preprocessing` | ImagePreprocessingConfig \| None | None | Image preprocessing configuration before OCR |
 275 | | `enable_table_detection` | bool | True | Enable automatic table detection and extraction |
 276 | | `table_min_confidence` | float | 0.0 | Minimum confidence for table detection (0.0-1.0) |
 277 | | `table_column_threshold` | int | 50 | Minimum pixel width between columns |
 278 | | `table_row_threshold_ratio` | float | 0.5 | Minimum row height ratio |
 279 | | `use_cache` | bool | True | Cache OCR results for improved performance |
 280 | | `classify_use_pre_adapted_templates` | bool | True | Use pre-adapted character templates |
 281 | | `language_model_ngram_on` | bool | False | Enable language model n-gram processing |
 282 | | `tessedit_dont_blkrej_good_wds` | bool | True | Don't block-reject good words |
 283 | | `tessedit_dont_rowrej_good_wds` | bool | True | Don't row-reject good words |
 284 | | `tessedit_enable_dict_correction` | bool | True | Enable dictionary-based spelling correction |
 285 | | `tessedit_char_whitelist` | str | "" | Whitelist of characters to recognize (empty = all) |
 286 | | `tessedit_char_blacklist` | str | "" | Blacklist of characters to ignore |
 287 | | `tessedit_use_primary_params_model` | bool | True | Use primary parameters model |
 288 | | `textord_space_size_is_variable` | bool | True | Allow variable space sizes |
 289 | | `thresholding_method` | bool | False | Thresholding method for binarization |
 290 | 
 291 | **Example:**
 292 | 
 293 | ```python
 294 | from kreuzberg import TesseractConfig, ImagePreprocessingConfig
 295 | 
 296 | # General document OCR
 297 | config = TesseractConfig(psm=3, oem=3)
 298 | 
 299 | # Invoice/form OCR with table detection
 300 | config = TesseractConfig(psm=6, oem=2, enable_table_detection=True, min_confidence=0.6)
 301 | 
 302 | # High-precision technical document OCR
 303 | config = TesseractConfig(
 304 |     psm=3,
 305 |     oem=2,
 306 |     preprocessing=ImagePreprocessingConfig(denoise=True, contrast_enhance=True, auto_rotate=True),
 307 |     min_confidence=0.7,
 308 |     tessedit_enable_dict_correction=True,
 309 | )
 310 | 
 311 | # Numeric-only OCR (for receipts, barcodes)
 312 | config = TesseractConfig(psm=6, tessedit_char_whitelist="0123456789.-,", min_confidence=0.8)
 313 | 
 314 | # Multiple language document
 315 | config = TesseractConfig(language="eng+fra+deu", psm=3, oem=2)
 316 | ```
 317 | 
 318 | ### ChunkingConfig
 319 | 
 320 | Text chunking configuration for dividing content into chunks. Chunking is useful for preparing content for embedding, indexing, or processing with length-limited systems (like LLM context windows).
 321 | 
 322 | **Attributes:**
 323 | 
 324 | | Field | Type | Default | Description |
 325 | |-------|------|---------|-------------|
 326 | | `max_chars` | int | 1000 | Maximum number of characters per chunk. Chunks larger than this will be split intelligently at sentence/paragraph boundaries |
 327 | | `max_overlap` | int | 200 | Overlap between consecutive chunks in characters. Creates context bridges between chunks for smoother processing |
 328 | | `embedding` | EmbeddingConfig \| None | None | Configuration for generating embeddings for each chunk using ONNX models. None = no embeddings |
 329 | | `preset` | str \| None | None | Use a preset chunking configuration (overrides individual settings if provided). Use list_embedding_presets() to see available presets |
 330 | 
 331 | **IMPORTANT:** The fields are `max_chars` and `max_overlap` (NOT `max_characters` or `overlap`).
 332 | 
 333 | **Example:**
 334 | 
 335 | ```python
 336 | from kreuzberg import ExtractionConfig, ChunkingConfig, EmbeddingConfig, EmbeddingModelType
 337 | 
 338 | # Basic chunking with defaults
 339 | config = ExtractionConfig(chunking=ChunkingConfig())
 340 | 
 341 | # Custom chunk size with overlap
 342 | config = ExtractionConfig(chunking=ChunkingConfig(max_chars=512, max_overlap=100))
 343 | 
 344 | # Chunking with embeddings
 345 | config = ExtractionConfig(
 346 |     chunking=ChunkingConfig(
 347 |         max_chars=512,
 348 |         embedding=EmbeddingConfig(model=EmbeddingModelType.preset("balanced"))
 349 |     )
 350 | )
 351 | 
 352 | # Using preset configuration
 353 | config = ExtractionConfig(chunking=ChunkingConfig(preset="semantic"))
 354 | ```
 355 | 
 356 | ### PdfConfig
 357 | 
 358 | PDF-specific extraction configuration.
 359 | 
 360 | **Attributes:**
 361 | 
 362 | | Field | Type | Default | Description |
 363 | |-------|------|---------|-------------|
 364 | | `extract_images` | bool | False | Extract images from PDF documents |
 365 | | `passwords` | list[str] \| None | None | List of passwords to try when opening encrypted PDFs. Try each password in order until one succeeds |
 366 | | `extract_metadata` | bool | True | Extract PDF metadata (title, author, creation date, etc.) |
 367 | | `hierarchy` | HierarchyConfig \| None | None | Document hierarchy detection configuration. None = no hierarchy detection |
 368 | 
 369 | **Example:**
 370 | 
 371 | ```python
 372 | from kreuzberg import ExtractionConfig, PdfConfig, HierarchyConfig
 373 | 
 374 | # Basic PDF configuration
 375 | config = ExtractionConfig(pdf_options=PdfConfig())
 376 | 
 377 | # Extract metadata and images from PDF
 378 | config = ExtractionConfig(pdf_options=PdfConfig(extract_images=True, extract_metadata=True))
 379 | 
 380 | # Handle encrypted PDFs
 381 | config = ExtractionConfig(pdf_options=PdfConfig(passwords=["password123", "fallback_password"]))
 382 | 
 383 | # Enable hierarchy detection
 384 | config = ExtractionConfig(pdf_options=PdfConfig(hierarchy=HierarchyConfig(k_clusters=6)))
 385 | ```
 386 | 
 387 | ### ImageExtractionConfig
 388 | 
 389 | Configuration for extracting images FROM documents. This is NOT for preprocessing images before OCR.
 390 | 
 391 | **Attributes:**
 392 | 
 393 | | Field | Type | Default | Description |
 394 | |-------|------|---------|-------------|
 395 | | `extract_images` | bool | True | Enable image extraction from documents |
 396 | | `target_dpi` | int | 300 | Target DPI for image normalization. Images are resampled to this DPI for consistency |
 397 | | `max_image_dimension` | int | 4096 | Maximum width or height for extracted images. Larger images are downscaled to fit |
 398 | | `auto_adjust_dpi` | bool | True | Automatically adjust DPI based on image content quality |
 399 | | `min_dpi` | int | 72 | Minimum DPI threshold. Images with lower DPI are upscaled |
 400 | | `max_dpi` | int | 600 | Maximum DPI threshold. Images with higher DPI are downscaled |
 401 | 
 402 | **Example:**
 403 | 
 404 | ```python
 405 | from kreuzberg import ExtractionConfig, ImageExtractionConfig
 406 | 
 407 | # Basic image extraction
 408 | config = ExtractionConfig(images=ImageExtractionConfig())
 409 | 
 410 | # Extract images with custom DPI settings
 411 | config = ExtractionConfig(
 412 |     images=ImageExtractionConfig(target_dpi=150, max_image_dimension=2048, auto_adjust_dpi=False)
 413 | )
 414 | ```
 415 | 
 416 | ### EmbeddingConfig
 417 | 
 418 | Embedding generation configuration for text chunks. Configures embedding generation using ONNX models via fastembed-rs.
 419 | 
 420 | **Attributes:**
 421 | 
 422 | | Field | Type | Default | Description |
 423 | |-------|------|---------|-------------|
 424 | | `model` | EmbeddingModelType | Preset "balanced" | The embedding model to use (preset, fastembed, or custom) |
 425 | | `normalize` | bool | True | Whether to normalize embedding vectors to unit length (recommended for cosine similarity) |
 426 | | `batch_size` | int | 32 | Number of texts to process simultaneously. Higher values use more memory but may be faster |
 427 | | `show_download_progress` | bool | False | Display progress during embedding model download |
 428 | | `cache_dir` | str \| None | None | Custom directory for caching downloaded models (defaults to ~/.cache/kreuzberg/embeddings/) |
 429 | 
 430 | **Example:**
 431 | 
 432 | ```python
 433 | from kreuzberg import EmbeddingConfig, EmbeddingModelType
 434 | 
 435 | # Basic preset embedding (recommended)
 436 | config = EmbeddingConfig()
 437 | 
 438 | # Specific preset with settings
 439 | config = EmbeddingConfig(
 440 |     model=EmbeddingModelType.preset("balanced"),
 441 |     normalize=True,
 442 |     batch_size=64
 443 | )
 444 | 
 445 | # Custom ONNX model
 446 | config = EmbeddingConfig(
 447 |     model=EmbeddingModelType.custom(model_id="sentence-transformers/all-MiniLM-L6-v2", dimensions=384)
 448 | )
 449 | 
 450 | # With custom cache directory
 451 | config = EmbeddingConfig(cache_dir="/path/to/model/cache")
 452 | ```
 453 | 
 454 | ### EmbeddingModelType
 455 | 
 456 | Embedding model type selector with multiple configurations.
 457 | 
 458 | **Static Methods:**
 459 | 
 460 | ```python
 461 | @staticmethod
 462 | def preset(name: str) -> EmbeddingModelType
 463 | ```
 464 | Use a preset configuration (recommended for most use cases). Available presets: balanced, compact, large.
 465 | 
 466 | ```python
 467 | @staticmethod
 468 | def fastembed(model: str, dimensions: int) -> EmbeddingModelType
 469 | ```
 470 | Use a specific fastembed model by name.
 471 | 
 472 | ```python
 473 | @staticmethod
 474 | def custom(model_id: str, dimensions: int) -> EmbeddingModelType
 475 | ```
 476 | Use a custom ONNX model from HuggingFace (e.g., sentence-transformers/*).
 477 | 
 478 | **Example:**
 479 | 
 480 | ```python
 481 | from kreuzberg import EmbeddingModelType, list_embedding_presets
 482 | 
 483 | # Using the balanced preset (recommended for general use)
 484 | model = EmbeddingModelType.preset("balanced")
 485 | 
 486 | # Using a specific fast embedding model
 487 | model = EmbeddingModelType.fastembed(model="BAAI/bge-small-en-v1.5", dimensions=384)
 488 | 
 489 | # Using a custom HuggingFace model
 490 | model = EmbeddingModelType.custom(
 491 |     model_id="sentence-transformers/all-MiniLM-L6-v2",
 492 |     dimensions=384
 493 | )
 494 | 
 495 | # Listing available presets
 496 | presets = list_embedding_presets()
 497 | print(f"Available presets: {presets}")
 498 | ```
 499 | 
 500 | ### TokenReductionConfig
 501 | 
 502 | Configuration for reducing token count in extracted content. Reduces token count to lower costs when working with LLM APIs.
 503 | 
 504 | **Attributes:**
 505 | 
 506 | | Field | Type | Default | Description |
 507 | |-------|------|---------|-------------|
 508 | | `mode` | str | "off" | Token reduction mode: "off", "light", "moderate", "aggressive", or "maximum" |
 509 | | `preserve_important_words` | bool | True | Preserve capitalized words, technical terms, and proper nouns even in aggressive reduction modes |
 510 | 
 511 | **Example:**
 512 | 
 513 | ```python
 514 | from kreuzberg import ExtractionConfig, TokenReductionConfig
 515 | 
 516 | # Moderate token reduction
 517 | config = ExtractionConfig(
 518 |     token_reduction=TokenReductionConfig(mode="moderate", preserve_important_words=True)
 519 | )
 520 | 
 521 | # Maximum reduction for large batches
 522 | config = ExtractionConfig(
 523 |     token_reduction=TokenReductionConfig(mode="maximum", preserve_important_words=True)
 524 | )
 525 | 
 526 | # No reduction (default)
 527 | config = ExtractionConfig(
 528 |     token_reduction=TokenReductionConfig(mode="off")
 529 | )
 530 | ```
 531 | 
 532 | ### LanguageDetectionConfig
 533 | 
 534 | Configuration for detecting document language(s).
 535 | 
 536 | **Attributes:**
 537 | 
 538 | | Field | Type | Default | Description |
 539 | |-------|------|---------|-------------|
 540 | | `enabled` | bool | True | Enable language detection for extracted content |
 541 | | `min_confidence` | float | 0.8 | Minimum confidence threshold (0.0-1.0) for language detection |
 542 | | `detect_multiple` | bool | False | Detect multiple languages in the document. When False, only the most confident language is returned |
 543 | 
 544 | **Example:**
 545 | 
 546 | ```python
 547 | from kreuzberg import ExtractionConfig, LanguageDetectionConfig, extract_file_sync
 548 | 
 549 | # Basic language detection
 550 | config = ExtractionConfig(language_detection=LanguageDetectionConfig())
 551 | 
 552 | # Detect multiple languages with lower confidence threshold
 553 | config = ExtractionConfig(
 554 |     language_detection=LanguageDetectionConfig(detect_multiple=True, min_confidence=0.6)
 555 | )
 556 | 
 557 | # Access detected languages in result
 558 | result = extract_file_sync("multilingual.pdf", config=config)
 559 | print(f"Languages: {result.detected_languages}")
 560 | ```
 561 | 
 562 | ### KeywordConfig
 563 | 
 564 | Keyword extraction configuration.
 565 | 
 566 | **Attributes:**
 567 | 
 568 | | Field | Type | Default | Description |
 569 | |-------|------|---------|-------------|
 570 | | `algorithm` | KeywordAlgorithm | - | Keyword extraction algorithm (KeywordAlgorithm.Yake or KeywordAlgorithm.Rake) |
 571 | | `max_keywords` | int | 10 | Maximum number of keywords to extract |
 572 | | `min_score` | float | 0.0 | Minimum score threshold |
 573 | | `ngram_range` | tuple[int, int] | (1, 3) | N-gram range for keyword extraction |
 574 | | `language` | str \| None | "en" | Optional language hint |
 575 | | `yake_params` | YakeParams \| None | None | YAKE-specific tuning parameters |
 576 | | `rake_params` | RakeParams \| None | None | RAKE-specific tuning parameters |
 577 | 
 578 | ### PageConfig
 579 | 
 580 | Page extraction and tracking configuration.
 581 | 
 582 | **Attributes:**
 583 | 
 584 | | Field | Type | Default | Description |
 585 | |-------|------|---------|-------------|
 586 | | `extract_pages` | bool | False | Enable page tracking and per-page extraction |
 587 | | `insert_page_markers` | bool | False | Insert page markers into content |
 588 | | `marker_format` | str | "\\n\\n<!-- PAGE {page_num} -->\\n\\n" | Marker template containing {page_num} |
 589 | 
 590 | **Example:**
 591 | 
 592 | ```python
 593 | from kreuzberg import ExtractionConfig, PageConfig
 594 | 
 595 | config = ExtractionConfig(pages=PageConfig(extract_pages=True))
 596 | ```
 597 | 
 598 | ### PostProcessorConfig
 599 | 
 600 | Configuration for post-processors in the extraction pipeline.
 601 | 
 602 | **Attributes:**
 603 | 
 604 | | Field | Type | Default | Description |
 605 | |-------|------|---------|-------------|
 606 | | `enabled` | bool | True | Enable post-processors in the extraction pipeline |
 607 | | `enabled_processors` | list[str] \| None | None | Whitelist of processor names to run. None = run all enabled |
 608 | | `disabled_processors` | list[str] \| None | None | Blacklist of processor names to skip. None = none disabled |
 609 | 
 610 | **Example:**
 611 | 
 612 | ```python
 613 | from kreuzberg import ExtractionConfig, PostProcessorConfig
 614 | 
 615 | # Basic post-processing with defaults
 616 | config = ExtractionConfig(postprocessor=PostProcessorConfig())
 617 | 
 618 | # Enable only specific processors
 619 | config = ExtractionConfig(
 620 |     postprocessor=PostProcessorConfig(
 621 |         enabled=True,
 622 |         enabled_processors=["normalize_whitespace", "fix_encoding"]
 623 |     )
 624 | )
 625 | 
 626 | # Disable specific processors
 627 | config = ExtractionConfig(
 628 |     postprocessor=PostProcessorConfig(
 629 |         enabled=True,
 630 |         disabled_processors=["experimental_cleanup"]
 631 |     )
 632 | )
 633 | 
 634 | # Disable all post-processing
 635 | config = ExtractionConfig(postprocessor=PostProcessorConfig(enabled=False))
 636 | ```
 637 | 
 638 | ### ImagePreprocessingConfig
 639 | 
 640 | Configuration for preprocessing images before OCR. This is NOT for extracting images from documents.
 641 | 
 642 | **Attributes:**
 643 | 
 644 | | Field | Type | Default | Description |
 645 | |-------|------|---------|-------------|
 646 | | `target_dpi` | int | 300 | Target DPI for image normalization before OCR |
 647 | | `auto_rotate` | bool | True | Automatically detect and correct image rotation |
 648 | | `deskew` | bool | True | Correct skewed images to improve OCR accuracy |
 649 | | `denoise` | bool | False | Apply denoising filters to reduce noise in images |
 650 | | `contrast_enhance` | bool | False | Enhance contrast to improve text readability |
 651 | | `binarization_method` | str | "otsu" | Method for converting images to black and white |
 652 | | `invert_colors` | bool | False | Invert colors (white text on black background) |
 653 | 
 654 | **Example:**
 655 | 
 656 | ```python
 657 | from kreuzberg import TesseractConfig, ImagePreprocessingConfig
 658 | 
 659 | # Basic preprocessing for OCR
 660 | config = TesseractConfig(preprocessing=ImagePreprocessingConfig())
 661 | 
 662 | # Aggressive preprocessing for low-quality scans
 663 | config = TesseractConfig(
 664 |     preprocessing=ImagePreprocessingConfig(
 665 |         target_dpi=300,
 666 |         denoise=True,
 667 |         contrast_enhance=True,
 668 |         auto_rotate=True,
 669 |         deskew=True
 670 |     )
 671 | )
 672 | ```
 673 | 
 674 | ## ExtractionResult
 675 | 
 676 | Result object returned by extraction functions.
 677 | 
 678 | **Attributes:**
 679 | 
 680 | | Field | Type | Description |
 681 | |-------|------|-------------|
 682 | | `content` | str | Main extracted text content in the specified output_format |
 683 | | `mime_type` | str | MIME type of the processed document |
 684 | | `metadata` | Metadata | Extracted document metadata (title, author, created_at, format_type, etc.) |
 685 | | `tables` | list[ExtractedTable] | Extracted tables from the document |
 686 | | `detected_languages` | list[str] \| None | Detected language codes (e.g., ["en", "de"]) if language detection is enabled |
 687 | | `chunks` | list[Chunk] \| None | Text chunks if chunking is enabled (each chunk has content, embedding, metadata) |
 688 | | `images` | list[ExtractedImage] \| None | Extracted images if image extraction is enabled |
 689 | | `pages` | list[PageContent] \| None | Per-page content and metadata if page extraction is enabled |
 690 | | `elements` | list[Element] \| None | Semantic elements if result_format="element_based" |
 691 | | `output_format` | str \| None | Format of the content field (plain, markdown, djot, html) |
 692 | | `result_format` | str \| None | Result format used (unified or element_based) |
 693 | | `extracted_keywords` | list[ExtractedKeyword] \| None | Extracted keywords with relevance scores if keyword extraction enabled |
 694 | | `quality_score` | float \| None | Overall quality score for the extraction result (0.0-1.0) |
 695 | | `processing_warnings` | list[ProcessingWarning] | Non-fatal warnings encountered during extraction pipeline |
 696 | 
 697 | **Methods:**
 698 | 
 699 | ```python
 700 | def get_page_count(self) -> int
 701 | ```
 702 | Get the total number of pages in the document.
 703 | 
 704 | ```python
 705 | def get_chunk_count(self) -> int
 706 | ```
 707 | Get the total number of chunks if chunking is enabled.
 708 | 
 709 | ```python
 710 | def get_detected_language(self) -> str | None
 711 | ```
 712 | Get the most confident detected language code.
 713 | 
 714 | ```python
 715 | def get_metadata_field(self, field_name: str) -> Any | None
 716 | ```
 717 | Get a specific metadata field by name.
 718 | 
 719 | **Example:**
 720 | 
 721 | ```python
 722 | from kreuzberg import extract_file_sync, ExtractionConfig, ChunkingConfig
 723 | 
 724 | config = ExtractionConfig(
 725 |     chunking=ChunkingConfig(max_chars=512),
 726 |     output_format="markdown"
 727 | )
 728 | result = extract_file_sync("document.pdf", config=config)
 729 | 
 730 | print(f"Content preview: {result.content[:200]}")
 731 | print(f"MIME type: {result.mime_type}")
 732 | print(f"Page count: {result.get_page_count()}")
 733 | print(f"Chunk count: {result.get_chunk_count()}")
 734 | print(f"Detected language: {result.get_detected_language()}")
 735 | 
 736 | if result.tables:
 737 |     print(f"Found {len(result.tables)} tables")
 738 | 
 739 | if result.chunks:
 740 |     first_chunk = result.chunks[0]
 741 |     print(f"First chunk: {first_chunk.content[:100]}")
 742 |     if first_chunk.embedding:
 743 |         print(f"Embedding dimensions: {len(first_chunk.embedding)}")
 744 | ```
 745 | 
 746 | ## Error Classes
 747 | 
 748 | All exceptions inherit from `KreuzbergError`, the base exception class.
 749 | 
 750 | ### KreuzbergError
 751 | 
 752 | Base exception class for all Kreuzberg errors.
 753 | 
 754 | ```python
 755 | class KreuzbergError(Exception):
 756 |     """Base exception for all Kreuzberg errors."""
 757 | ```
 758 | 
 759 | ### ParsingError
 760 | 
 761 | Raised when document parsing fails.
 762 | 
 763 | ```python
 764 | class ParsingError(KreuzbergError):
 765 |     """Document parsing failed (corrupt, malformed, etc.)."""
 766 | ```
 767 | 
 768 | ### OCRError
 769 | 
 770 | Raised when OCR processing fails.
 771 | 
 772 | ```python
 773 | class OCRError(KreuzbergError):
 774 |     """OCR operation failed."""
 775 | ```
 776 | 
 777 | ### ValidationError
 778 | 
 779 | Raised when validation fails.
 780 | 
 781 | ```python
 782 | class ValidationError(KreuzbergError):
 783 |     """Validation failed (invalid parameters, constraints, format mismatches)."""
 784 | ```
 785 | 
 786 | ### MissingDependencyError
 787 | 
 788 | Raised when required dependencies are not available.
 789 | 
 790 | ```python
 791 | class MissingDependencyError(KreuzbergError):
 792 |     """Required dependency not available (easyocr, paddleocr, tesseract, etc.)."""
 793 | 
 794 |     @staticmethod
 795 |     def create_for_package(dependency_group: str, functionality: str, package_name: str) -> MissingDependencyError
 796 | ```
 797 | 
 798 | **Example:**
 799 | 
 800 | ```python
 801 | from kreuzberg import extract_file_sync, MissingDependencyError, OCRError, ParsingError
 802 | 
 803 | try:
 804 |     result = extract_file_sync("document.pdf")
 805 | except ParsingError as e:
 806 |     print(f"Failed to parse document: {e}")
 807 | except OCRError as e:
 808 |     print(f"OCR failed: {e}")
 809 | except MissingDependencyError as e:
 810 |     print(f"Missing dependency: {e}")
 811 | ```
 812 | 
 813 | ## Utility Functions
 814 | 
 815 | ### MIME Type Detection
 816 | 
 817 | ```python
 818 | def detect_mime_type(data: bytes | bytearray) -> str
 819 | ```
 820 | 
 821 | Detect MIME type from file bytes using magic number detection.
 822 | 
 823 | **Parameters:**
 824 | - `data` (bytes | bytearray): File content as bytes or bytearray
 825 | 
 826 | **Returns:** Detected MIME type (e.g., "application/pdf", "image/png")
 827 | 
 828 | ```python
 829 | def detect_mime_type_from_path(path: str | Path) -> str
 830 | ```
 831 | 
 832 | Detect MIME type from file path by reading the file and detecting its MIME type.
 833 | 
 834 | **Parameters:**
 835 | - `path` (str | Path): Path to the file
 836 | 
 837 | **Returns:** Detected MIME type
 838 | 
 839 | **Raises:**
 840 | - `OSError`: If file cannot be read (file not found, permission denied, etc.)
 841 | - `RuntimeError`: If MIME type detection fails
 842 | 
 843 | **Example:**
 844 | 
 845 | ```python
 846 | from kreuzberg import detect_mime_type, detect_mime_type_from_path
 847 | 
 848 | # From bytes
 849 | pdf_bytes = b"%PDF-1.4\n"
 850 | mime_type = detect_mime_type(pdf_bytes)
 851 | 
 852 | # From path
 853 | mime_type = detect_mime_type_from_path("document.pdf")
 854 | ```
 855 | 
 856 | ### MIME Type Validation
 857 | 
 858 | ```python
 859 | def validate_mime_type(mime_type: str) -> str
 860 | ```
 861 | 
 862 | Validate a MIME type string and return the canonical form.
 863 | 
 864 | ```python
 865 | def get_extensions_for_mime(mime_type: str) -> list[str]
 866 | ```
 867 | 
 868 | Get file extensions associated with a MIME type.
 869 | 
 870 | **Example:**
 871 | 
 872 | ```python
 873 | from kreuzberg import validate_mime_type, get_extensions_for_mime
 874 | 
 875 | canonical = validate_mime_type("application/pdf")
 876 | extensions = get_extensions_for_mime("application/pdf")  # Returns ["pdf"]
 877 | ```
 878 | 
 879 | ### Configuration Loading
 880 | 
 881 | ```python
 882 | def load_extraction_config_from_file(path: str | Path) -> ExtractionConfig
 883 | ```
 884 | 
 885 | Load extraction configuration from a specific file.
 886 | 
 887 | **Parameters:**
 888 | - `path` (str | Path): Path to the configuration file (.toml, .yaml, or .json)
 889 | 
 890 | **Returns:** ExtractionConfig parsed from the file
 891 | 
 892 | **Raises:**
 893 | - `FileNotFoundError`: If the configuration file does not exist
 894 | - `RuntimeError`: If the file cannot be read or parsed
 895 | - `ValueError`: If the file format is invalid or unsupported
 896 | 
 897 | ```python
 898 | def discover_extraction_config() -> ExtractionConfig | None
 899 | ```
 900 | 
 901 | Discover extraction configuration from the environment (deprecated).
 902 | 
 903 | Attempts to locate a Kreuzberg configuration file using:
 904 | 1. KREUZBERG_CONFIG_PATH environment variable
 905 | 2. Search for kreuzberg.toml, kreuzberg.yaml, or kreuzberg.json in current and parent directories
 906 | 
 907 | **Returns:** ExtractionConfig if found, None otherwise
 908 | 
 909 | **Note:** Deprecated in favor of `load_extraction_config_from_file` for more predictable behavior.
 910 | 
 911 | **Example:**
 912 | 
 913 | ```python
 914 | from kreuzberg import load_extraction_config_from_file, extract_file_sync
 915 | 
 916 | # Load from specific file
 917 | config = load_extraction_config_from_file("kreuzberg.toml")
 918 | result = extract_file_sync("document.pdf", config=config)
 919 | 
 920 | # Auto-discover configuration
 921 | import os
 922 | os.environ["KREUZBERG_CONFIG_PATH"] = "config/kreuzberg.yaml"
 923 | # Then extraction will use the discovered config
 924 | ```
 925 | 
 926 | ## Plugin System
 927 | 
 928 | ### Registering Post-Processors
 929 | 
 930 | ```python
 931 | def register_post_processor(processor: Any) -> None
 932 | ```
 933 | 
 934 | Register a Python PostProcessor with the Rust core. Once registered, the processor will be called automatically after extraction to enrich results.
 935 | 
 936 | **Required Methods:**
 937 | - `name() -> str`: Return processor name (must be non-empty)
 938 | - `process(result: ExtractionResult) -> ExtractionResult`: Process and enrich the extraction result
 939 | - `processing_stage() -> str`: Return "early", "middle", or "late"
 940 | 
 941 | **Optional Methods:**
 942 | - `initialize() -> None`: Called when processor is registered
 943 | - `shutdown() -> None`: Called when processor is unregistered
 944 | 
 945 | **Example:**
 946 | 
 947 | ```python
 948 | from kreuzberg import register_post_processor, ExtractionResult
 949 | 
 950 | class EntityExtractor:
 951 |     def name(self) -> str:
 952 |         return "entity_extraction"
 953 | 
 954 |     def processing_stage(self) -> str:
 955 |         return "early"
 956 | 
 957 |     def process(self, result: ExtractionResult) -> ExtractionResult:
 958 |         entities = {"PERSON": ["John Doe"], "ORG": ["Microsoft"]}
 959 |         result.metadata["entities"] = entities
 960 |         return result
 961 | 
 962 | register_post_processor(EntityExtractor())
 963 | ```
 964 | 
 965 | ### Registering OCR Backends
 966 | 
 967 | ```python
 968 | def register_ocr_backend(backend: Any) -> None
 969 | ```
 970 | 
 971 | Register a Python OCR backend with the Rust core.
 972 | 
 973 | **Required Methods:**
 974 | - `name() -> str`: Return backend name (must be non-empty)
 975 | - `supported_languages() -> list[str]`: Return list of supported language codes
 976 | - `process_image(image_bytes: bytes, language: str) -> OcrResult`: Process image and return OCR result
 977 | - `process_file(path: str, language: str) -> OcrResult`: Process file and return OCR result
 978 | - `initialize() -> None`: Called when backend is registered
 979 | - `shutdown() -> None`: Called when backend is unregistered
 980 | - `version() -> str`: Return backend version string
 981 | 
 982 | **Example:**
 983 | 
 984 | ```python
 985 | from kreuzberg import register_ocr_backend
 986 | 
 987 | class MyOcrBackend:
 988 |     def name(self) -> str:
 989 |         return "my-ocr"
 990 | 
 991 |     def supported_languages(self) -> list[str]:
 992 |         return ["eng", "deu", "fra"]
 993 | 
 994 |     def process_image(self, image_bytes: bytes, language: str) -> dict:
 995 |         return {
 996 |             "content": "extracted text",
 997 |             "metadata": {"confidence": 0.95},
 998 |             "tables": []
 999 |         }
1000 | 
1001 | register_ocr_backend(MyOcrBackend())
1002 | ```
1003 | 
1004 | ### Registering Validators
1005 | 
1006 | ```python
1007 | def register_validator(validator: Any) -> None
1008 | ```
1009 | 
1010 | Register a Python Validator with the Rust core. Validators are called automatically after extraction to validate results.
1011 | 
1012 | **Required Methods:**
1013 | - `name() -> str`: Return validator name (must be non-empty)
1014 | - `validate(result: ExtractionResult) -> None`: Validate the extraction result (raise error to fail)
1015 | 
1016 | **Optional Methods:**
1017 | - `should_validate(result: ExtractionResult) -> bool`: Check if validator should run (defaults to True)
1018 | - `priority() -> int`: Return priority (defaults to 50, higher runs first)
1019 | 
1020 | **Example:**
1021 | 
1022 | ```python
1023 | from kreuzberg import register_validator, ValidationError, ExtractionResult
1024 | 
1025 | class MinLengthValidator:
1026 |     def name(self) -> str:
1027 |         return "min_length_validator"
1028 | 
1029 |     def priority(self) -> int:
1030 |         return 100
1031 | 
1032 |     def validate(self, result: ExtractionResult) -> None:
1033 |         if len(result.content) < 100:
1034 |             raise ValidationError("Content too short")
1035 | 
1036 | register_validator(MinLengthValidator())
1037 | ```
1038 |

1086 | ## Format Enums
1087 | 
1088 | ### OutputFormat
1089 | 
1090 | Output format for extraction results.
1091 | 
1092 | ```python
1093 | class OutputFormat(str, Enum):
1094 |     PLAIN = "plain"         # Plain text format
1095 |     MARKDOWN = "markdown"   # Markdown format
1096 |     DJOT = "djot"          # Djot lightweight markup format
1097 |     HTML = "html"          # HTML format
1098 | ```
1099 | 
1100 | ### ResultFormat
1101 | 
1102 | Result format controlling extraction output structure.
1103 | 
1104 | ```python
1105 | class ResultFormat(str, Enum):
1106 |     UNIFIED = "unified"                # All content in `content` field
1107 |     ELEMENT_BASED = "element_based"   # Unstructured-compatible output with semantic elements
1108 | ```
1109 | 
1110 | ## Error Handling
1111 | 
1112 | ### Error Code Functions
1113 | 
1114 | ```python
1115 | def get_last_error_code() -> int
1116 | ```
1117 | 
1118 | Get the last error code from the FFI layer.
1119 | 
1120 | **Returns:**
1121 | - 0 (SUCCESS): No error occurred
1122 | - 1 (GENERIC_ERROR): Generic unspecified error
1123 | - 2 (PANIC): A panic occurred in the Rust core
1124 | - 3 (INVALID_ARGUMENT): Invalid argument provided
1125 | - 4 (IO_ERROR): I/O operation failed
1126 | - 5 (PARSING_ERROR): Document parsing failed
1127 | - 6 (OCR_ERROR): OCR operation failed
1128 | - 7 (MISSING_DEPENDENCY): Required dependency not available
1129 | 
1130 | ```python
1131 | def get_error_details() -> dict[str, Any]
1132 | ```
1133 | 
1134 | Get detailed error information from the FFI layer.
1135 | 
1136 | **Returns:** dict with keys:
1137 | - `message` (str): Human-readable error message
1138 | - `error_code` (int): Numeric error code (0-7)
1139 | - `error_type` (str): Error type name (e.g., "validation", "ocr")
1140 | - `source_file` (str | None): Source file path if available
1141 | - `source_function` (str | None): Function name if available
1142 | - `source_line` (int): Line number (0 if unknown)
1143 | - `context_info` (str | None): Additional context if available
1144 | - `is_panic` (bool): Whether error came from a panic
1145 | 
1146 | ```python
1147 | def classify_error(message: str) -> int
1148 | ```
1149 | 
1150 | Classify an error message into a Kreuzberg error code.
1151 | 
1152 | **Parameters:**
1153 | - `message` (str): The error message to classify
1154 | 
1155 | **Returns:** int error code (0-7) representing the classification
1156 | 
1157 | ```python
1158 | def error_code_name(code: int) -> str
1159 | ```
1160 | 
1161 | Get the human-readable name of an error code.
1162 | 
1163 | **Parameters:**
1164 | - `code` (int): Numeric error code (0-7)
1165 | 
1166 | **Returns:** Human-readable error code name (e.g., "validation", "ocr")
1167 | 
1168 | **Example:**
1169 | 
1170 | ```python
1171 | from kreuzberg import get_error_details, get_last_error_code, error_code_name, classify_error
1172 | 
1173 | try:
1174 |     result = extract_file_sync("document.pdf")
1175 | except Exception as e:
1176 |     code = get_last_error_code()
1177 |     if code:
1178 |         print(f"Error code: {code} ({error_code_name(code)})")
1179 | 
1180 |     details = get_error_details()
1181 |     print(f"Error: {details['message']}")
1182 |     print(f"Type: {details['error_type']}")
1183 | 
1184 |     classified = classify_error(str(e))
1185 |     print(f"Classified as: {error_code_name(classified)}")
1186 | ```
1187 |

1294 | if preset:
1295 |     print(f"Balanced preset: {preset.description}")
1296 |     print(f"Dimensions: {preset.dimensions}")
1297 |     print(f"Recommended chunk size: {preset.chunk_size}")

1300 | ## Configuration Utilities
1301 | 
1302 | ### Config Manipulation
1303 | 
1304 | ```python
1305 | def config_to_json(config: ExtractionConfig) -> str
1306 | ```
1307 | Convert ExtractionConfig to JSON string.
1308 | 
1309 | ```python
1310 | def config_get_field(config: ExtractionConfig, field_name: str) -> Any | None
1311 | ```
1312 | Get a specific field value from ExtractionConfig.
1313 | 
1314 | ```python
1315 | def config_merge(base: ExtractionConfig, override: ExtractionConfig) -> None
1316 | ```
1317 | Merge override config into base config (mutates base).
1318 | 
1319 | **Example:**
1320 | 
1321 | ```python
1322 | from kreuzberg import ExtractionConfig, config_to_json, config_get_field, config_merge
1323 | 
1324 | config = ExtractionConfig(use_cache=True, enable_quality_processing=False)
1325 | 
1326 | # Convert to JSON
1327 | json_str = config_to_json(config)
1328 | print(json_str)
1329 | 
1330 | # Get field
1331 | use_cache = config_get_field(config, "use_cache")
1332 | print(f"use_cache: {use_cache}")
1333 | 
1334 | # Merge configs
1335 | override = ExtractionConfig(use_cache=False)
1336 | config_merge(config, override)
1337 | ```

### File: `skills\kreuzberg\references\rust-api.md`

- Size: 19679 bytes
- Modified: SystemTime { intervals: 134176840067035184 }

```markdown
   1 | # Kreuzberg Rust API Reference
   2 | 
   3 | Complete API reference for the Kreuzberg document extraction library in Rust.
   4 | 
   5 | ## Setup
   6 | 
   7 | Add to your `Cargo.toml`:
   8 | 
   9 | ```toml
  10 | [dependencies]
  11 | kreuzberg = { version = "4", features = [
  12 |     "tokio-runtime",
  13 |     "pdf",
  14 |     "ocr",
  15 |     "chunking",
  16 |     "embeddings",
  17 |     "language-detection",
  18 |     "keywords-yake",
  19 |     "keywords-rake",
  20 |     "api",
  21 |     "mcp"
  22 | ] }
  23 | tokio = { version = "1", features = ["full"] }
  24 | ```
  25 | 
  26 | ### Core Features
  27 | 
  28 | - **tokio-runtime**: Enables async/sync extraction (default). Required for `extract_file_sync`, `batch_extract_file_sync`, `batch_extract_file`
  29 | - **pdf**: PDF extraction with PDFium
  30 | - **ocr**: Tesseract-based OCR for scanned documents
  31 | - **chunking**: Text chunking for RAG pipelines
  32 | - **embeddings**: Vector embeddings generation
  33 | - **language-detection**: Detect document language
  34 | - **keywords-yake** / **keywords-rake**: Extract keywords using YAKE or RAKE
  35 | - **api**: HTTP API with Axum
  36 | - **mcp**: Model Context Protocol support
  37 | 
  38 | ---
  39 | 
  40 | ## Core Extraction Functions
  41 | 
  42 | ### `extract_file` (async)
  43 | 
  44 | Extract content from a file path.
  45 | 
  46 | ```rust
  47 | pub async fn extract_file(
  48 |     path: impl AsRef<Path>,
  49 |     mime_type: Option<&str>,
  50 |     config: &ExtractionConfig,
  51 | ) -> Result<ExtractionResult>
  52 | ```
  53 | 
  54 | **Always available.** Requires async context (`#[tokio::main]`, `tokio::spawn`, etc.).
  55 | 
  56 | ```rust
  57 | use kreuzberg::{extract_file, ExtractionConfig};
  58 | use std::path::Path;
  59 | 
  60 | #[tokio::main]
  61 | async fn main() -> kreuzberg::Result<()> {
  62 |     let config = ExtractionConfig::default();
  63 |     let result = extract_file("document.pdf", None, &config).await?;
  64 |     println!("Content: {}", result.content);
  65 |     Ok(())
  66 | }
  67 | ```
  68 | 
  69 | ### `extract_bytes` (async)
  70 | 
  71 | Extract content from byte data.
  72 | 
  73 | ```rust
  74 | pub async fn extract_bytes(
  75 |     data: &[u8],
  76 |     mime_type: &str,
  77 |     config: &ExtractionConfig,
  78 | ) -> Result<ExtractionResult>
  79 | ```
  80 | 
  81 | **Always available.** Requires async context.
  82 | 
  83 | ```rust
  84 | #[tokio::main]
  85 | async fn main() -> kreuzberg::Result<()> {
  86 |     let config = ExtractionConfig::default();
  87 |     let pdf_bytes = std::fs::read("document.pdf")?;
  88 |     let result = extract_bytes(&pdf_bytes, "application/pdf", &config).await?;
  89 |     Ok(())
  90 | }
  91 | ```
  92 | 
  93 | ### `extract_file_sync` (sync)
  94 | 
  95 | Synchronous wrapper around `extract_file`.
  96 | 
  97 | ```rust
  98 | pub fn extract_file_sync(
  99 |     path: impl AsRef<Path>,
 100 |     mime_type: Option<&str>,
 101 |     config: &ExtractionConfig,
 102 | ) -> Result<ExtractionResult>
 103 | ```
 104 | 
 105 | **Requires tokio-runtime feature.** Blocks the current thread using a global Tokio runtime.
 106 | 
 107 | ```rust
 108 | use kreuzberg::{extract_file_sync, ExtractionConfig};
 109 | 
 110 | fn main() -> kreuzberg::Result<()> {
 111 |     let config = ExtractionConfig::default();
 112 |     let result = extract_file_sync("document.pdf", None, &config)?;
 113 |     println!("Content: {}", result.content);
 114 |     Ok(())
 115 | }
 116 | ```
 117 | 
 118 | ### `extract_bytes_sync` (sync)
 119 | 
 120 | Synchronous wrapper around `extract_bytes`.
 121 | 
 122 | ```rust
 123 | pub fn extract_bytes_sync(
 124 |     content: &[u8],
 125 |     mime_type: &str,
 126 |     config: &ExtractionConfig,
 127 | ) -> Result<ExtractionResult>
 128 | ```
 129 | 
 130 | **Always available.** Works in sync and async contexts.
 131 | 
 132 | ```rust
 133 | fn main() -> kreuzberg::Result<()> {
 134 |     let config = ExtractionConfig::default();
 135 |     let bytes = b"Hello, world!";
 136 |     let result = extract_bytes_sync(bytes, "text/plain", &config)?;
 137 |     Ok(())
 138 | }
 139 | ```
 140 | 
 141 | ### `batch_extract_file` (async, parallel)
 142 | 
 143 | Extract multiple files concurrently.
 144 | 
 145 | ```rust
 146 | pub async fn batch_extract_file(
 147 |     paths: Vec<impl AsRef<Path>>,
 148 |     config: &ExtractionConfig,
 149 | ) -> Result<Vec<ExtractionResult>>
 150 | ```
 151 | 
 152 | **Requires tokio-runtime feature.** Processes files in parallel with automatic concurrency management (defaults to `num_cpus * 1.5`).
 153 | 
 154 | ```rust
 155 | #[tokio::main]
 156 | async fn main() -> kreuzberg::Result<()> {
 157 |     let config = ExtractionConfig::default();
 158 |     let paths = vec!["doc1.pdf", "doc2.pdf", "doc3.pdf"];
 159 |     let results = batch_extract_file(paths, &config).await?;
 160 |     println!("Processed {} files", results.len());
 161 |     Ok(())
 162 | }
 163 | ```
 164 | 
 165 | ### `batch_extract_bytes` (async, parallel)
 166 | 
 167 | Extract multiple byte arrays concurrently.
 168 | 
 169 | ```rust
 170 | pub async fn batch_extract_bytes(
 171 |     contents: Vec<(Vec<u8>, String)>,
 172 |     config: &ExtractionConfig,
 173 | ) -> Result<Vec<ExtractionResult>>
 174 | ```
 175 | 
 176 | **Requires tokio-runtime feature.** Each tuple is `(bytes, mime_type)`.
 177 | 
 178 | ```rust
 179 | #[tokio::main]
 180 | async fn main() -> kreuzberg::Result<()> {
 181 |     let config = ExtractionConfig::default();
 182 |     let contents = vec![
 183 |         (b"PDF content".to_vec(), "application/pdf".to_string()),
 184 |         (b"Text content".to_vec(), "text/plain".to_string()),
 185 |     ];
 186 |     let results = batch_extract_bytes(contents, &config).await?;
 187 |     Ok(())
 188 | }
 189 | ```
 190 | 
 191 | ### `batch_extract_file_sync` (sync, parallel)
 192 | 
 193 | Synchronous wrapper for batch file extraction.
 194 | 
 195 | ```rust
 196 | pub fn batch_extract_file_sync(
 197 |     paths: Vec<impl AsRef<Path>>,
 198 |     config: &ExtractionConfig,
 199 | ) -> Result<Vec<ExtractionResult>>
 200 | ```
 201 | 
 202 | **Requires tokio-runtime feature.** Uses global runtime for concurrency.
 203 | 
 204 | ```rust
 205 | fn main() -> kreuzberg::Result<()> {
 206 |     let config = ExtractionConfig::default();
 207 |     let paths = vec!["doc1.pdf", "doc2.pdf"];
 208 |     let results = batch_extract_file_sync(paths, &config)?;
 209 |     Ok(())
 210 | }
 211 | ```
 212 | 
 213 | ### `batch_extract_bytes_sync` (sync, parallel)
 214 | 
 215 | Synchronous wrapper for batch byte extraction.
 216 | 
 217 | ```rust
 218 | pub fn batch_extract_bytes_sync(
 219 |     contents: Vec<(Vec<u8>, String)>,
 220 |     config: &ExtractionConfig,
 221 | ) -> Result<Vec<ExtractionResult>>
 222 | ```
 223 | 
 224 | **Always available.** Each tuple is `(bytes, mime_type)`.
 225 | 
 226 | ```rust
 227 | fn main() -> kreuzberg::Result<()> {
 228 |     let config = ExtractionConfig::default();
 229 |     let contents = vec![
 230 |         (b"content 1".to_vec(), "text/plain".to_string()),
 231 |         (b"content 2".to_vec(), "text/plain".to_string()),
 232 |     ];
 233 |     let results = batch_extract_bytes_sync(contents, &config)?;
 234 |     Ok(())
 235 | }
 236 | ```
 237 | 
 238 | ---
 239 | 
 240 | ## Configuration
 241 | 
 242 | ### `ExtractionConfig`
 243 | 
 244 | Main configuration struct for all extraction operations.
 245 | 
 246 | ```rust
 247 | pub struct ExtractionConfig {
 248 |     /// Enable caching (default: true)
 249 |     pub use_cache: bool,
 250 | 
 251 |     /// Enable quality post-processing (default: true)
 252 |     pub enable_quality_processing: bool,
 253 | 
 254 |     /// OCR configuration (None = OCR disabled)
 255 |     pub ocr: Option<OcrConfig>,
 256 | 
 257 |     /// Force OCR even for searchable PDFs (default: false)
 258 |     pub force_ocr: bool,
 259 | 
 260 |     /// Text chunking configuration (None = disabled)
 261 |     pub chunking: Option<ChunkingConfig>,
 262 | 
 263 |     /// Image extraction configuration (None = disabled)
 264 |     pub images: Option<ImageExtractionConfig>,
 265 | 
 266 |     /// PDF-specific options (requires pdf feature)
 267 |     #[cfg(feature = "pdf")]
 268 |     pub pdf_options: Option<PdfConfig>,
 269 | 
 270 |     /// Token reduction configuration (None = disabled)
 271 |     pub token_reduction: Option<TokenReductionConfig>,
 272 | 
 273 |     /// Language detection configuration (None = disabled)
 274 |     pub language_detection: Option<LanguageDetectionConfig>,
 275 | 
 276 |     /// Page extraction configuration (None = disabled)
 277 |     pub pages: Option<PageConfig>,
 278 | 
 279 |     /// Keyword extraction configuration (requires keywords-yake or keywords-rake)
 280 |     #[cfg(any(feature = "keywords-yake", feature = "keywords-rake"))]
 281 |     pub keywords: Option<KeywordConfig>,
 282 | 
 283 |     /// Post-processor configuration (None = use defaults)
 284 |     pub postprocessor: Option<PostProcessorConfig>,
 285 | 
 286 |     /// HTML to Markdown conversion options (requires html feature)
 287 |     #[cfg(feature = "html")]
 288 |     pub html_options: Option<ConversionOptions>,
 289 | 
 290 |     /// Maximum concurrent extractions in batch (None = num_cpus * 1.5)
 291 |     pub max_concurrent_extractions: Option<usize>,
 292 | 
 293 |     /// Result structure format (default: Unified)
 294 |     /// Uses types::OutputFormat (Unified | ElementBased)
 295 |     pub result_format: types::OutputFormat,
 296 | 
 297 |     /// Security limits for archives (requires archives feature)
 298 |     #[cfg(feature = "archives")]
 299 |     pub security_limits: Option<SecurityLimits>,
 300 | 
 301 |     /// Content output format (default: Plain)
 302 |     /// Uses config::OutputFormat (Plain | Markdown | Djot | Html)
 303 |     pub output_format: OutputFormat,
 304 | }
 305 | ```
 306 | 
 307 | #### Creating Configs
 308 | 
 309 | ```rust
 310 | use kreuzberg::{ExtractionConfig, OcrConfig, ChunkingConfig, OutputFormat};
 311 | 
 312 | // Default configuration
 313 | let config = ExtractionConfig::default();
 314 | 
 315 | // With OCR
 316 | let config = ExtractionConfig {
 317 |     ocr: Some(OcrConfig {
 318 |         backend: "tesseract".to_string(),
 319 |         ..Default::default()
 320 |     }),
 321 |     ..Default::default()
 322 | };
 323 | 
 324 | // With chunking
 325 | let config = ExtractionConfig {
 326 |     chunking: Some(ChunkingConfig {
 327 |         max_characters: 512,
 328 |         overlap: 50,
 329 |         ..Default::default()
 330 |     }),
 331 |     output_format: OutputFormat::Markdown,
 332 |     ..Default::default()
 333 | };
 334 | ```
 335 | 
 336 | ---
 337 | 
 338 | ## Output Formats
 339 | 
 340 | There are two separate enums both named `OutputFormat` in different modules:
 341 | 
 342 | ### Content `OutputFormat` (`core::config::formats::OutputFormat`)
 343 | 
 344 | Controls the format of the `content` field text. Used by `ExtractionConfig::output_format`.
 345 | 
 346 | ```rust
 347 | pub enum OutputFormat {
 348 |     /// Plain text (default)
 349 |     Plain,
 350 |     /// Markdown formatted
 351 |     Markdown,
 352 |     /// Djot markup format
 353 |     Djot,
 354 |     /// HTML format
 355 |     Html,
 356 | }
 357 | ```
 358 | 
 359 | ### Result `OutputFormat` (`types::extraction::OutputFormat`)
 360 | 
 361 | Controls the result structure. Used by `ExtractionConfig::result_format`.
 362 | 
 363 | ```rust
 364 | pub enum OutputFormat {
 365 |     /// Unified format with all content in `content` field (default)
 366 |     Unified,
 367 |     /// Element-based format with semantic element extraction
 368 |     ElementBased,
 369 | }
 370 | ```
 371 | 
 372 | ```rust
 373 | use kreuzberg::{ExtractionConfig, OutputFormat};
 374 | 
 375 | let config = ExtractionConfig {
 376 |     output_format: OutputFormat::Markdown,  // content format (Plain/Markdown/Djot/Html)
 377 |     // result_format uses types::OutputFormat (Unified/ElementBased) — defaults to Unified
 378 |     ..Default::default()
 379 | };
 380 | ```
 381 | 
 382 | ---
 383 | 
 384 | ## Extraction Result
 385 | 
 386 | ### `ExtractionResult`
 387 | 
 388 | Result returned by all extraction functions.
 389 | 
 390 | ```rust
 391 | pub struct ExtractionResult {
 392 |     /// Main extracted content
 393 |     pub content: String,
 394 | 
 395 |     /// Document MIME type
 396 |     pub mime_type: Cow<'static, str>,
 397 | 
 398 |     /// Metadata about extraction
 399 |     pub metadata: Metadata,
 400 | 
 401 |     /// Extracted tables (HTML/Markdown)
 402 |     pub tables: Vec<Table>,
 403 | 
 404 |     /// Detected languages (if language-detection enabled)
 405 |     pub detected_languages: Option<Vec<String>>,
 406 | 
 407 |     /// Text chunks (if chunking enabled)
 408 |     pub chunks: Option<Vec<Chunk>>,
 409 | 
 410 |     /// Extracted images (if image extraction enabled)
 411 |     pub images: Option<Vec<ExtractedImage>>,
 412 | 
 413 |     /// Per-page content (if page extraction enabled)
 414 |     pub pages: Option<Vec<PageContent>>,
 415 | 
 416 |     /// Semantic elements (if element-based format enabled)
 417 |     pub elements: Option<Vec<Element>>,
 418 | 
 419 |     /// Djot document structure (if extracting Djot)
 420 |     pub djot_content: Option<DjotContent>,
 421 | 
 422 |     /// Extracted keywords with relevance scores (if keyword extraction enabled)
 423 |     pub extracted_keywords: Option<Vec<ExtractedKeyword>>,
 424 | 
 425 |     /// Quality score for extraction result (0.0-1.0)
 426 |     pub quality_score: Option<f64>,
 427 | 
 428 |     /// Non-fatal warnings during processing pipeline
 429 |     pub processing_warnings: Vec<ProcessingWarning>,
 430 | }
 431 | ```
 432 | 
 433 | ### `ExtractedKeyword`
 434 | 
 435 | Extracted keyword with relevance score and position information.
 436 | 
 437 | ```rust
 438 | pub struct ExtractedKeyword {
 439 |     /// Keyword text
 440 |     pub text: String,
 441 | 
 442 |     /// Relevance score (0.0-1.0)
 443 |     pub score: f32,
 444 | 
 445 |     /// Algorithm used for extraction ("tfidf", "textrank", "yake", etc.)
 446 |     pub algorithm: String,
 447 | 
 448 |     /// Character positions in content (if available)
 449 |     pub positions: Option<Vec<usize>>,
 450 | }
 451 | ```
 452 | 
 453 | ### `ProcessingWarning`
 454 | 
 455 | Non-fatal warning encountered during document processing.
 456 | 
 457 | ```rust
 458 | pub struct ProcessingWarning {
 459 |     /// Component that generated the warning
 460 |     pub source: String,
 461 | 
 462 |     /// Warning message describing the issue
 463 |     pub message: String,
 464 | }
 465 | ```
 466 | 
 467 | ### `Chunk`
 468 | 
 469 | Text chunk with optional embedding.
 470 | 
 471 | ```rust
 472 | pub struct Chunk {
 473 |     /// Chunk text content
 474 |     pub content: String,
 475 | 
 476 |     /// Optional embedding vector
 477 |     pub embedding: Option<Vec<f32>>,
 478 | 
 479 |     /// Chunk metadata
 480 |     pub metadata: ChunkMetadata,
 481 | }
 482 | 
 483 | pub struct ChunkMetadata {
 484 |     pub byte_start: usize,
 485 |     pub byte_end: usize,
 486 |     pub token_count: Option<usize>,
 487 |     pub chunk_index: usize,
 488 |     pub total_chunks: usize,
 489 |     pub first_page: Option<usize>,
 490 |     pub last_page: Option<usize>,
 491 | }
 492 | ```
 493 | 
 494 | ### `ExtractedImage`
 495 | 
 496 | Image extracted from document.
 497 | 
 498 | ```rust
 499 | pub struct ExtractedImage {
 500 |     /// Raw image bytes
 501 |     pub data: Bytes,
 502 | 
 503 |     /// Format: "jpeg", "png", "webp", etc.
 504 |     pub format: Cow<'static, str>,
 505 | 
 506 |     /// Zero-indexed position
 507 |     pub image_index: usize,
 508 | 
 509 |     /// Page number (1-indexed)
 510 |     pub page_number: Option<usize>,
 511 | 
 512 |     /// Image dimensions
 513 |     pub width: Option<u32>,
 514 |     pub height: Option<u32>,
 515 | 
 516 |     /// Colorspace: "RGB", "CMYK", "Gray"
 517 |     pub colorspace: Option<String>,
 518 | 
 519 |     /// Bits per component
 520 |     pub bits_per_component: Option<u32>,
 521 | 
 522 |     /// Whether this is a mask image
 523 |     pub is_mask: bool,
 524 | 
 525 |     /// Image description
 526 |     pub description: Option<String>,
 527 | 
 528 |     /// Nested OCR result (if OCRed)
 529 |     pub ocr_result: Option<Box<ExtractionResult>>,
 530 | }
 531 | ```
 532 | 
 533 | ---
 534 | 
 535 | ## Error Handling
 536 | 
 537 | ### `KreuzbergError` enum
 538 | 
 539 | ```rust
 540 | pub enum KreuzbergError {
 541 |     /// File system errors (always bubble up)
 542 |     Io(std::io::Error),
 543 | 
 544 |     /// Document parsing errors
 545 |     Parsing {
 546 |         message: String,
 547 |         source: Option<Box<dyn std::error::Error + Send + Sync>>,
 548 |     },
 549 | 
 550 |     /// OCR processing errors
 551 |     Ocr {
 552 |         message: String,
 553 |         source: Option<Box<dyn std::error::Error + Send + Sync>>,
 554 |     },
 555 | 
 556 |     /// Configuration/input validation errors
 557 |     Validation {
 558 |         message: String,
 559 |         source: Option<Box<dyn std::error::Error + Send + Sync>>,
 560 |     },
 561 | 
 562 |     /// Cache operation errors
 563 |     Cache {
 564 |         message: String,
 565 |         source: Option<Box<dyn std::error::Error + Send + Sync>>,
 566 |     },
 567 | 
 568 |     /// Image processing errors
 569 |     ImageProcessing {
 570 |         message: String,
 571 |         source: Option<Box<dyn std::error::Error + Send + Sync>>,
 572 |     },
 573 | 
 574 |     /// Serialization errors (JSON, MessagePack)
 575 |     Serialization {
 576 |         message: String,
 577 |         source: Option<Box<dyn std::error::Error + Send + Sync>>,
 578 |     },
 579 | 
 580 |     /// Missing system dependency (e.g. Tesseract)
 581 |     MissingDependency(String),
 582 | 
 583 |     /// Plugin-specific errors
 584 |     Plugin {
 585 |         message: String,
 586 |         plugin_name: String,
 587 |     },
 588 | 
 589 |     /// Mutex/RwLock poisoning
 590 |     LockPoisoned(String),
 591 | 
 592 |     /// Unsupported MIME type or format
 593 |     UnsupportedFormat(String),
 594 | 
 595 |     /// Other errors
 596 |     Other(String),
 597 | }
 598 | ```
 599 | 
 600 | #### Error Constructors
 601 | 
 602 | ```rust
 603 | use kreuzberg::KreuzbergError;
 604 | 
 605 | // Create errors
 606 | let err = KreuzbergError::parsing("invalid PDF");
 607 | let err = KreuzbergError::ocr("Tesseract failed");
 608 | let err = KreuzbergError::validation("config invalid");
 609 | let err = KreuzbergError::unsupported_format("application/unknown");
 610 | let err = KreuzbergError::missing_dependency("tesseract");
 611 | 
 612 | // With source
 613 | let source = std::io::Error::new(std::io::ErrorKind::NotFound, "file missing");
 614 | let err = KreuzbergError::parsing_with_source("corrupt PDF", source);
 615 | ```
 616 | 
 617 | #### Handling Errors
 618 | 
 619 | ```rust
 620 | use kreuzberg::extract_file;
 621 | 
 622 | match extract_file("doc.pdf", None, &config).await {
 623 |     Ok(result) => println!("Success: {}", result.content),
 624 |     Err(kreuzberg::KreuzbergError::Io(e)) => {
 625 |         println!("File error: {}", e);
 626 |     }
 627 |     Err(kreuzberg::KreuzbergError::UnsupportedFormat(fmt)) => {
 628 |         println!("Unsupported: {}", fmt);
 629 |     }
 630 |     Err(e) => println!("Other error: {}", e),
 631 | }
 632 | ```
 633 | 
 634 | ---
 635 | 
 636 | ## MIME Type Detection
 637 | 
 638 | ### `detect_mime_type`
 639 | 
 640 | Detect MIME type from file path.
 641 | 
 642 | ```rust
 643 | pub fn detect_mime_type(path: impl AsRef<Path>) -> Result<String>
 644 | ```
 645 | 
 646 | ```rust
 647 | use kreuzberg::detect_mime_type;
 648 | 
 649 | let mime = detect_mime_type("document.pdf")?;
 650 | assert_eq!(mime, "application/pdf");
 651 | ```
 652 | 
 653 | ### `detect_mime_type_from_bytes`
 654 | 
 655 | Detect MIME type from byte data.
 656 | 
 657 | ```rust
 658 | pub fn detect_mime_type_from_bytes(data: &[u8]) -> Result<String>
 659 | ```
 660 | 
 661 | ### `validate_mime_type`
 662 | 
 663 | Check if a MIME type is supported.
 664 | 
 665 | ```rust
 666 | pub fn validate_mime_type(mime_type: &str) -> Result<()>
 667 | ```
 668 | 
 669 | ```rust
 670 | use kreuzberg::validate_mime_type;
 671 | 
 672 | validate_mime_type("application/pdf")?;  // OK
 673 | validate_mime_type("application/unknown")?;  // Error
 674 | ```
 675 | 
 676 | ### `get_extensions_for_mime`
 677 | 
 678 | Get file extensions for a MIME type.
 679 | 
 680 | ```rust
 681 | pub fn get_extensions_for_mime(mime_type: &str) -> Vec<String>
 682 | ```
 683 | 
 684 | ```rust
 685 | use kreuzberg::get_extensions_for_mime;
 686 | 
 687 | let exts = get_extensions_for_mime("application/pdf");
 688 | // ["pdf"]
 689 | 
 690 | let exts = get_extensions_for_mime("text/plain");
 691 | // ["txt", "text"]
 692 | ```
 693 | 
 694 | ### MIME Type Constants
 695 | 
 696 | ```rust
 697 | use kreuzberg::{
 698 |     PDF_MIME_TYPE,
 699 |     PLAIN_TEXT_MIME_TYPE,
 700 |     HTML_MIME_TYPE,
 701 |     MARKDOWN_MIME_TYPE,
 702 |     JSON_MIME_TYPE,
 703 |     XML_MIME_TYPE,
 704 |     DOCX_MIME_TYPE,
 705 |     POWER_POINT_MIME_TYPE,
 706 |     EXCEL_MIME_TYPE,
 707 | };
 708 | 
 709 | assert_eq!(PDF_MIME_TYPE, "application/pdf");
 710 | assert_eq!(PLAIN_TEXT_MIME_TYPE, "text/plain");
 711 | ```
 712 |

 715 | ## Plugin Registry
 716 | 
 717 | Access extractors, OCR backends, and validators.
 718 | 
 719 | ### `get_document_extractor_registry`
 720 | 
 721 | Get all available document extractors.
 722 | 
 723 | ```rust
 724 | pub fn get_document_extractor_registry() -> Arc<RwLock<DocumentExtractorRegistry>>
 725 | ```
 726 | 
 727 | ### `get_ocr_backend_registry`
 728 | 
 729 | Get all available OCR backends.
 730 | 
 731 | ```rust
 732 | pub fn get_ocr_backend_registry() -> Arc<RwLock<OcrBackendRegistry>>
 733 | ```
 734 | 
 735 | ### `get_post_processor_registry`
 736 | 
 737 | Get all available post-processors.
 738 | 
 739 | ```rust
 740 | pub fn get_post_processor_registry() -> Arc<RwLock<PostProcessorRegistry>>
 741 | ```
 742 | 
 743 | ### `get_validator_registry`
 744 | 
 745 | Get all available validators.
 746 | 
 747 | ```rust
 748 | pub fn get_validator_registry() -> Arc<RwLock<ValidatorRegistry>>
 749 | ```
 750 | 
 751 | ---
 752 | 
 753 | ## Complete Example
 754 | 
 755 | ```rust
 756 | use kreuzberg::{
 757 |     extract_file, ExtractionConfig, OutputFormat,
 758 |     ChunkingConfig, OcrConfig, LanguageDetectionConfig,
 759 | };
 760 | 
 761 | #[tokio::main]
 762 | async fn main() -> kreuzberg::Result<()> {
 763 |     // Configure extraction
 764 |     let config = ExtractionConfig {
 765 |         output_format: OutputFormat::Markdown,
 766 |         chunking: Some(ChunkingConfig {
 767 |             max_characters: 512,
 768 |             overlap: 50,
 769 |             ..Default::default()
 770 |         }),
 771 |         language_detection: Some(LanguageDetectionConfig::default()),
 772 |         ocr: Some(OcrConfig {
 773 |             backend: "tesseract".to_string(),
 774 |             ..Default::default()
 775 |         }),
 776 |         force_ocr: false,
 777 |         ..Default::default()
 778 |     };
 779 | 
 780 |     // Extract from file
 781 |     let result = extract_file("document.pdf", None, &config).await?;
 782 | 
 783 |     // Use results
 784 |     println!("Content:\n{}", result.content);
 785 |     println!("MIME: {}", result.mime_type);
 786 | 
 787 |     if let Some(langs) = result.detected_languages {
 788 |         println!("Languages: {:?}", langs);
 789 |     }
 790 | 
 791 |     if let Some(chunks) = result.chunks {
 792 |         println!("Chunks: {}", chunks.len());
 793 |         for chunk in chunks {
 794 |             println!("  - {}", &chunk.content[..50.min(chunk.content.len())]);
 795 |         }
 796 |     }
 797 | 
 798 |     if let Some(images) = result.images {
 799 |         println!("Images: {}", images.len());
 800 |     }
 801 | 
 802 |     if let Some(pages) = result.pages {
 803 |         println!("Pages: {}", pages.len());
 804 |     }
 805 | 
 806 |     Ok(())
 807 | }
 808 | ```
 809 | 
 810 | ---
 811 | 
 812 | ## Result Type Alias
 813 | 
 814 | ```rust
 815 | pub type Result<T> = std::result::Result<T, KreuzbergError>;
 816 | ```
 817 | 
 818 | All fallible operations return `Result<T>` where errors are `KreuzbergError`.
 819 | 
 820 | ---
 821 | 
 822 | ## Feature Flags Summary
 823 | 
 824 | | Feature | Availability | Dependencies |
 825 | |---------|--------------|--------------|
 826 | | tokio-runtime | Default | Tokio runtime for async/sync |
 827 | | pdf | Default | PDFium |
 828 | | ocr | Optional | Tesseract |
 829 | | chunking | Optional | text-splitter |
 830 | | embeddings | Optional | FastEmbed, requires tokio-runtime |
 831 | | language-detection | Optional | whatlang |
 832 | | keywords-yake | Optional | yake-rust |
 833 | | keywords-rake | Optional | rake |
 834 | | api | Optional | Axum, requires tokio-runtime |
 835 | | mcp | Optional | Model Context Protocol, requires tokio-runtime |
 836 | 
 837 | ---
 838 | 
 839 | ## Version
 840 | 
 841 | This reference is for Kreuzberg 4.x.
```
