```markdown
   1 | # Supported Formats Reference
   2 | 
   3 | Kreuzberg supports 75+ file formats across 8 major categories with intelligent format detection and comprehensive metadata extraction. All formats support text and metadata extraction. Additional capabilities like OCR and table detection are noted per format.
   4 | 
   5 | ## Office Documents
   6 | 
   7 | ### Word Processing
   8 | 
   9 | | Format | Extensions | MIME Type | Capabilities |
  10 | |--------|-----------|-----------|--------------|
  11 | | Microsoft Word | `.docx` | `application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.wordprocessingml.document` | Full text extraction, tables, embedded images, metadata, styles |
  12 | | OpenDocument Text | `.odt` | `application/vnd.oasis.opendocument.text` | Full text extraction, tables, embedded images, metadata, styles |
  13 | 
  14 | ### Spreadsheets
  15 | 
  16 | | Format | Extensions | MIME Type | Capabilities |
  17 | |--------|-----------|-----------|--------------|
  18 | | Excel Workbook | `.xlsx` | `application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.spreadsheetml.sheet` | Sheet data, cell values, formulas, cell metadata, charts |
  19 | | Excel Macro-Enabled | `.xlsm` | `application/vnd.ms-excel.sheet.macroEnabled.12` | Sheet data, formulas, macros (text only), metadata |
  20 | | Excel Binary | `.xlsb` | `application/vnd.ms-excel.sheet.binary.macroEnabled.12` | Binary sheet data extraction, metadata |
  21 | | Excel Legacy | `.xls` | `application/vnd.ms-excel` | Legacy sheet data extraction, metadata |
  22 | | Excel Add-in | `.xla` | `application/vnd.ms-excel` | Add-in data extraction |
  23 | | Excel Macro Add-in | `.xlam` | `application/vnd.ms-excel.addin.macroEnabled.12` | Macro add-in metadata |
  24 | | Excel Template | `.xltm` | `application/vnd.ms-excel.template.macroEnabled.12` | Template data and metadata |
  25 | | OpenDocument Spreadsheet | `.ods` | `application/vnd.oasis.opendocument.spreadsheet` | Sheet data, cell values, formulas, metadata |
  26 | 
  27 | ### Presentations
  28 | 
  29 | | Format | Extensions | MIME Type | Capabilities |
  30 | |--------|-----------|-----------|--------------|
  31 | | PowerPoint Presentation | `.pptx` | `application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.presentationml.presentation` | Slide text, speaker notes, embedded images, metadata |
  32 | | PowerPoint Legacy | `.ppt` | `application/vnd.ms-powerpoint` | Legacy slide text extraction, metadata |
  33 | | PowerPoint Slideshow | `.ppsx` | `application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.presentationml.slideshow` | Slideshow content, speaker notes, metadata |
  34 | 
  35 | ### PDF
  36 | 
  37 | | Format | Extensions | MIME Type | Capabilities |
  38 | |--------|-----------|-----------|--------------|
  39 | | Portable Document Format | `.pdf` | `application/pdf` | Text extraction, tables, embedded images, metadata, OCR (when needed), password protection support |
  40 | 
  41 | ### eBooks
  42 | 
  43 | | Format | Extensions | MIME Type | Capabilities |
  44 | |--------|-----------|-----------|--------------|
  45 | | EPUB | `.epub` | `application/epub+zip` | Chapter text, metadata, embedded resources, navigation |
  46 | | FictionBook | `.fb2` | `application/x-fictionbook+xml` | Book content, metadata, chapter structure |
  47 | 
  48 | ## Images (OCR-Enabled)
  49 | 
  50 | ### Raster Images
  51 | 
  52 | | Format | Extensions | MIME Type | Capabilities |
  53 | |--------|-----------|-----------|--------------|
  54 | | PNG | `.png` | `image/png` | OCR text extraction, table detection, EXIF metadata, dimensions, color space |
  55 | | JPEG | `.jpg`, `.jpeg` | `image/jpeg` | OCR text extraction, table detection, EXIF metadata, color profile |
  56 | | GIF | `.gif` | `image/gif` | OCR text extraction, animation metadata, dimensions |
  57 | | WebP | `.webp` | `image/webp` | OCR text extraction, metadata, lossy/lossless detection |
  58 | | Bitmap | `.bmp` | `image/bmp` | OCR text extraction, dimensions, color depth |
  59 | | TIFF | `.tiff`, `.tif` | `image/tiff` | OCR text extraction, multi-page support, EXIF metadata, compression info |
  60 | 
  61 | ### Advanced Image Formats
  62 | 
  63 | | Format | Extensions | MIME Type | Capabilities |
  64 | |--------|-----------|-----------|--------------|
  65 | | JPEG 2000 | `.jp2` | `image/jp2` | OCR via pure Rust decoder (hayro-jpeg2000), table detection, resolution metadata |
  66 | | JPEG 2000 Extended | `.jpx` | `image/jpx` | Advanced JPEG 2000 features, high-resolution content, metadata |
  67 | | JPEG 2000 Compound | `.jpm` | `image/jpm` | Compound image support, mixed content |
  68 | | Motion JPEG 2000 | `.mj2` | `video/mj2` | JPEG 2000 video/sequence metadata |
  69 | | JBIG2 | `.jbig2`, `.jb2` | `image/jbig2` | Bi-level image OCR, high compression, technical documents |
  70 | | Portable PixMap | `.pnm`, `.pbm`, `.pgm`, `.ppm` | `image/x-portable-pixmap` | OCR for plain image formats, raw pixel data |
  71 | 
  72 | ### Vector Graphics
  73 | 
  74 | | Format | Extensions | MIME Type | Capabilities |
  75 | |--------|-----------|-----------|--------------|
  76 | | Scalable Vector Graphics | `.svg` | `image/svg+xml` | DOM parsing, embedded text extraction, graphics metadata, vector elements |
  77 | 
  78 | ## Web & Data
  79 | 
  80 | ### Markup & Structured Text
  81 | 
  82 | | Format | Extensions | MIME Type | Capabilities |
  83 | |--------|-----------|-----------|--------------|
  84 | | HyperText Markup | `.html`, `.htm` | `text/html` | DOM parsing, text extraction, metadata (Open Graph, Twitter Card), link extraction |
  85 | | XHTML | `.xhtml` | `application/xhtml+xml` | XHTML parsing, metadata extraction, semantic structure |
  86 | | XML | `.xml` | `application/xml` | DOM parsing, namespace handling, text extraction, structure analysis |
  87 | 
  88 | ### Structured Data Formats
  89 | 
  90 | | Format | Extensions | MIME Type | Capabilities |
  91 | |--------|-----------|-----------|--------------|
  92 | | JSON | `.json` | `application/json` | Schema detection, nested structure parsing, validation |
  93 | | YAML | `.yaml`, `.yml` | `application/x-yaml` | Hierarchical data parsing, custom tags, nested structures |
  94 | | TOML | `.toml` | `application/toml` | Configuration parsing, table structures, type preservation |
  95 | | CSV | `.csv` | `text/csv` | Delimiter detection, header inference, type detection |
  96 | | TSV | `.tsv` | `text/tab-separated-values` | Tab-separated value parsing, header detection |
  97 | 
  98 | ### Text & Markup Languages
  99 | 
 100 | | Format | Extensions | MIME Type | Capabilities |
 101 | |--------|-----------|-----------|--------------|
 102 | | Plain Text | `.txt` | `text/plain` | Raw text extraction, encoding detection |
 103 | | Markdown | `.md`, `.markdown` | `text/markdown` | CommonMark parsing, GFM extensions, front matter |
 104 | | Djot | `.djot` | `text/djot` | Djot format parsing, semantic structure |
 105 | | reStructuredText | `.rst` | `text/x-rst` | RST parsing, directive handling, role extraction |
 106 | | Org Mode | `.org` | `text/org` | Org mode structure, outline parsing, metadata |
 107 | | Rich Text Format | `.rtf` | `application/rtf` | Text with formatting extraction, font information |
 108 | 
 109 | ## Email & Archives
 110 | 
 111 | ### Email Formats
 112 | 
 113 | | Format | Extensions | MIME Type | Capabilities |
 114 | |--------|-----------|-----------|--------------|
 115 | | Email Message | `.eml` | `message/rfc822` | Headers (from, to, subject, date), body (HTML/plain text), attachments, threading info |
 116 | | Microsoft Outlook | `.msg` | `application/vnd.ms-outlook` | Outlook headers, body content, attachments, recipient metadata |
 117 | 
 118 | ### Archive Formats
 119 | 
 120 | | Format | Extensions | MIME Type | Capabilities |
 121 | |--------|-----------|-----------|--------------|
 122 | | ZIP Archive | `.zip` | `application/zip` | File listing, nested archive support, compression metadata |
 123 | | Tar Archive | `.tar` | `application/x-tar` | File listing, permission metadata, nested archives |
 124 | | Gzip Tar | `.tgz` | `application/gzip` | Compressed archive listing, metadata |
 125 | | Gzip | `.gz` | `application/gzip` | Compressed file metadata |
 126 | | 7-Zip | `.7z` | `application/x-7z-compressed` | File listing, compression info, nested archives |
 127 | 
 128 | ## Academic & Scientific
 129 | 
 130 | ### Citation Formats
 131 | 
 132 | | Format | Extensions | MIME Type | Capabilities |
 133 | |--------|-----------|-----------|--------------|
 134 | | BibTeX | `.bib` | `text/bibtex` | Structured parsing, entry types, field extraction |
 135 | | BibLaTeX | `.biblatex` | `text/bibtex` | Extended BibTeX format, advanced field support |
 136 | | RIS | `.ris` | `application/x-research-info-systems` | Structured RIS format parsing, type detection |
 137 | | NIH RIS | `.nbib` | `application/x-research-info-systems` | NIH/PubMed format, structured citation data |
 138 | | EndNote | `.enw` | `application/x-endnote` | EndNote XML format, citation metadata |
 139 | | Citation Style Language | `.csl` | `application/vnd.citationstyles.csl+xml` | CSL JSON/XML parsing, style definitions |
 140 | 
 141 | ### Scientific & Technical Formats
 142 | 
 143 | | Format | Extensions | MIME Type | Capabilities |
 144 | |--------|-----------|-----------|--------------|
 145 | | LaTeX | `.tex`, `.latex` | `application/x-latex` | LaTeX source parsing, commands, document structure |
 146 | | Typst | `.typ` | `text/plain` | Typst markup parsing, document structure |
 147 | | JATS XML | `.jats` | `application/xml` | PubMed JATS parsing, article structure, metadata |
 148 | | Jupyter Notebook | `.ipynb` | `application/x-ipynb+json` | Cell extraction (code + markdown), output parsing, metadata |
 149 | | DocBook | `.docbook` | `application/docbook+xml` | DocBook XML parsing, semantic structure |
 150 | 
 151 | ### Documentation Formats
 152 | 
 153 | | Format | Extensions | MIME Type | Capabilities |
 154 | |--------|-----------|-----------|--------------|
 155 | | OPML | `.opml` | `application/x-opml+xml` | Outline parsing, hierarchy extraction, metadata |
 156 | | Perl POD | `.pod` | `text/x-pod` | Perl documentation parsing, section extraction |
 157 | | Manual Page | `.mdoc` | `text/plain` | UNIX manual page parsing, section structure |
 158 | | Troff/Groff | `.troff` | `text/troff` | Typesetting markup parsing, document structure |
 159 | 
 160 | ## Format Capabilities Summary
 161 | 
 162 | ### Text Extraction
 163 | All 75+ formats support full or partial text extraction. Document structure and encoding are automatically detected.
 164 | 
 165 | ### Metadata Support
 166 | Comprehensive metadata extraction includes:
 167 | - Document properties (title, author, subject, creation date, modification date)
 168 | - Format-specific metadata (page count, dimensions, encoding, language)
 169 | - EXIF data (for images)
 170 | - Document statistics (word count, character count)
 171 | 
 172 | ### OCR (Optical Character Recognition)
 173 | OCR is available for image formats:
 174 | - **Raster Images**: PNG, JPEG, GIF, WebP, BMP, TIFF
 175 | - **Advanced Formats**: JPEG 2000, JBIG2, PNM/PBM/PGM/PPM
 176 | - **Configurable Backends**: Tesseract (all languages), EasyOCR, PaddleOCR (Python), Guten (Node.js)
 177 | 
 178 | ### Table Detection
 179 | Smart table detection and reconstruction available for:
 180 | - PDF documents (native tables and scanned content with OCR)
 181 | - Office documents (Excel, Word)
 182 | - Images (via OCR backends)
 183 | - HTML/XML (from markup structure)
 184 | 
 185 | ### Archive & Nested Document Support
 186 | Archives and nested formats support file listing and sequential extraction:
 187 | - ZIP, TAR, TGZ, 7Z archives
 188 | - Email attachments
 189 | - Nested archives within archives
 190 | 
 191 | ## Getting Started
 192 | 
 193 | For language-specific examples and detailed API documentation, see the [API Reference](https://docs.kreuzberg.dev/reference/api-python/).
 194 | 
 195 | For OCR configuration and backend selection, see the [OCR Backends Guide](https://docs.kreuzberg.dev/guides/ocr/).
 196 | 
 197 | For comprehensive format details and format detection, see the [Complete Format Reference](https://docs.kreuzberg.dev/reference/formats/).
```
